### [1] [Derivation of height field theory for the two-dimensional classical dimer model from a Grassmann-integral representation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17154)
*Stephen Powell*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从Grassmann积分表示出发，构造性地推导了方格和蜂巢晶格上经典二聚体模型（classical dimer model）的长波场论。通过将二聚体模型精确表示为无质量Dirac费米子，再经由路径积分玻色化（bosonization），严格映射到连续高度场理论，并导出了二聚体可观测量与高度场的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二聚体模型在二分晶格上具有Coulomb相，其特征为代数关联和拓扑序（topological order），其长波性质可由零散度矢量场描述。本文旨在从精确的Grassmann积分表示出发，对方格和蜂巢晶格上的这一场论进行构造性推导，填补从微观模型到场论描述之间的严格推导链条。

Method: 从二聚体模型的Grassmann积分精确表示出发，取连续极限得到二维欧几里得空间中的无质量Dirac费米子（massless Dirac fermion）；利用路径积分表示中的玻色化技术，将该费米子理论精确映射到高度场理论，并纳入边界间断（“tilt”）与通量之间的关联。

Result: 推导出描述二聚体可观测量（dimer observables）的高度场表达式；识别出通量密度（flux density）和局域价键固体序参量（local valence-bond-solid order parameter）是描述渐近长程关联所需的唯二源项。

Conclusion: 本文建立了从Grassmann积分到高度场理论之间的严格映射，为二聚体模型中的Coulomb相提供了构造性的场论基础。

Abstract: The classical dimer model on bipartite lattices hosts a Coulomb phase, characterized by algebraic correlations and topological order. Its long-wavelength properties can be described by the fluctuations of a vector field with zero divergence, which, in two dimensions, is equivalent to a continuum height model. We show how this field theory can be derived constructively for both square and honeycomb lattices, starting from an exact representation of the dimer model in terms of Grassmann integrals. Taking the continuum limit gives a massless Dirac fermion in two-dimensional Euclidean space, which, using bosonization in the path integral representation, maps exactly to the well-known height field theory, incorporating the relationship between its boundary discontinuity (or "tilt") and the flux. By including source terms coupling to the flux density and the local valence-bond-solid order parameter, which we show are the only ones required to describe the asymptotic long-distance correlations, we derive expressions for the dimer observables in terms of the height.

</details>


### [2] [Why dimensional analysis works: general classification of self-similarity based on scale-invariance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17179)
*Hirokazu Maruoka*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从尺度不变性（scale invariance）出发重新形式化自相似性（self-similarity），论证量纲分析（dimensional analysis）源于单位和物理参数之间共享的部分尺度不变性，并据此将自相似解分为三种类型，提供了一个统一的理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自相似性概念缺乏统一的数学形式化定义，量纲分析与自相似性之间的深层联系尚未被系统地阐明。本文旨在建立一种基于尺度不变性视角的统一框架，以厘清不同种类自相似解的分类及其与量纲分析的关系。

Method: 首先将自相似性定义为函数在尺度变换下形式不变的性质；然后将该形式化应用于由数值和单位组成的物理参数，证明量纲分析之所以有效，是因为单位与物理参数之间共享部分尺度不变性；最后依据单位诱导的尺度函数与物理参数关联的尺度函数是否等价，区分第一类相似性（similarity of the first kind）与第二类相似性（similarity of the second kind），并进一步根据相似参数的幂指数是否包含无量纲数（dimensionless numbers）的函数，对第二类自相似解进行再分类。

Result: 推导出三类自相似解（three kinds of self-similar solutions）的分类体系：第一类相似性、第二类相似性（其中幂指数不含无量纲数函数）以及第二类相似性（其中幂指数包含无量纲数函数）。

Conclusion: 该研究为理解量纲分析提供了一个统一框架，并建立了物理问题中自相似性的普适分类体系。

Abstract: In this work, we formulate self-similarity from the perspective of scale invariance, where a self-similar form is understood as the transformation of a function into a form invariant under scale transformations. By applying this formulation to physical parameters, which consist of numerical values and units, it is demonstrated that dimensional analysis works for physical problems because scale invariance is partially shared between units and physical parameters. This naturally leads to the distinction between similarity of the first kind and similarity of the second kind according to whether the scale functions induced by units and those associated with physical parameters are equivalent or not. Self-similar solutions of the second kind can be further classified according to whether the power exponents of the similarity parameters include functions of dimensionless numbers. This leads to the conclusion that there are three kinds of self-similar solutions. The present work provides a unified framework for understanding dimensional analysis and a universal classification of self-similarity in physical problems.

</details>


### [3] [Making complex CFTs real: The two-dimensional Potts model for $Q>4$ and complex $Q$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18125)
*Jesper Lykke Jacobsen,Kay Joerg Wiese*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过将二维 Q 态 Potts 模型映射为环模型（loop model），在连续 Q 参数下研究了其一阶相变区域（Q>4）的临界现象。研究表明，在 Q=4 处一个临界固定点（critical fixed point）与一个三重临界固定点（tricritical fixed point）碰撞，随后在 Q>4 或复数 Q 下作为一对复数共形不变理论（complex conformally invariant theories）出现。作者推测所有共形数据（conformal data）可通过 Q≤4 精确结果的分析延拓（analytic continuation）获得，并利用传递矩阵（transfer-matrix）计算和 Q=5 的已有研究验证了这一猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维实数耦合 Potts 模型在 Q>4 时呈现一级相变（first-order transition），其临界行为的理论描述尚不完整。本文旨在通过将模型映射为具有连续参数 Q 的环模型，揭示 Q>4 区域中临界固定点与三重临界固定点的碰撞机制，并探索复数共形场论（conformal field theory）的描述可能性。

Method: 从具有两体和三体自旋相互作用的三角晶格 Potts 模型出发，研究与之等价的环模型，其中 Q 被视为连续参数。结合解析论证与数值计算，分析固定点的碰撞行为；利用传递矩阵方法进行大规模数值计算，并将结果与已知的 Q≤4 精确结果通过分析延拓进行比较。

Result: 在 Q=4 处，临界固定点与三重临界固定点碰撞，并在 Q>4 或复数 Q 下作为一对复数共形不变理论涌现。对于实数 Q>4 和复数 Q，传递矩阵计算结果与基于 Q≤4 精确结果的分析延拓猜想一致，并在 Q=5 时与既有研究吻合。

Conclusion: 作者提出，对于 Q>4 甚至复数 Q 的复数耦合常数，所有共形数据（如中心荷（central charge）、临界指数（critical exponents）和三点结构常数（three-point structure constants））均可通过 Q≤4 环模型已知精确结果的分析延拓获得。数值验证支持了这一猜想，表明复数共形场论可描述原本一级相变区域的临界行为。

Abstract: The two-dimensional $Q$-state Potts model with real couplings has a first-order transition for $Q>4$. Starting from a triangular-lattice Potts model with two- and three-spin interactions, we study an equivalent loop model in which $Q$ is a continuous parameter. By a combination of analytical and numerical arguments, we show that this loop model allows for the collision of a critical and a tricritical fixed point at $Q=4$. These then emerge as a pair of complex conformally invariant theories at $Q>4$, or even complex $Q$, for suitable complex coupling constants. We conjecture that all conformal data (such as the central charge, critical exponents, and three-point structure constants) can be obtained by analytic continuation of known exact results for the loop model with $Q \le 4$. This conjecture is checked, both for real $Q>4$ and for $Q \in \mathbb{C}$, by extensive transfer-matrix computations and comparison to previous studies for $Q=5$.

</details>


### [4] [Brownian gyration of an inertial ellipsoid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17554)
*Soham Dutta,Arnab Saha*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过惯性朗之万动力学（inertial Langevin dynamics）研究了非球形椭圆微粒在欠阻尼（underdamped）条件下的布朗回旋（Brownian gyration），揭示了粒子形状、轴向取向和惯性等因素对非平衡稳态中回旋行为的影响，并比较了球体与非球体在过阻尼和欠阻尼条件下的差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对布朗回旋（Brownian gyration）的研究主要集中在过阻尼（overdamped）条件下的球对称粒子，缺乏对欠阻尼（underdamped）条件下非球形粒子回旋行为的理解。

Method: 采用惯性朗之万动力学（inertial Langevin dynamics）方法，模拟一个在球不对称势阱（spherically asymmetric trap）中受限的微观椭球体，同时与两个不同热库（thermal reservoirs）耦合，从而驱动系统进入非平衡稳态（nonequilibrium steady state, NESS）。

Result: 研究发现微观回旋不仅依赖于势阱不对称性和温差，还显著受到粒子固有物理性质（如形状、轴向取向）和惯性的影响。球体与非球体在过阻尼和欠阻尼条件下均表现出根本性差异。

Conclusion: 为在更广泛的实验可调参数（experimentally tuneable parameters）空间中优化布朗回旋（Brownian gyration）提供了关键见解。

Abstract: Recent studies on Brownian gyration (BG) have focused primarily on spherically symmetric particles under overdamped conditions. To explore BG in the underdamped regime with a spherically asymmetric particle, we investigate the inertial dynamics of a microscopic ellipsoid in a dissipative medium. The particle is confined in a spherically asymmetric trap and simultaneously coupled to two distinct thermal reservoirs. This configuration drives the system into a nonequilibrium steady state (NESS) characterised by BG, which is quantified by the mean and fluctuation of the particle's specific angular momentum. Using inertial Langevin dynamics, we systematically analyze how this microscopic gyration depends not merely on the trap asymmetry and temperature difference, but also on the particle's intrinsic physical properties like shape and axial orientation, besides inertia. Our study uncovers fundamental differences between the gyration of spherical and non-spherical particles in overdamped as well as underdamped conditions, at microscopic scales. These findings provide key insights for optimizing Brownian gyration across a broader landscape of experimentally tuneable parameters.

</details>


### [5] [Work Extraction via Backward Motion in Optimal Closed-Loop Stochastic Control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17624)
*Luis Frieder Reinalter,Emanuele Panizon,Lokesh Muruga,Clemens Bechinger*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文利用实时光镊结合原位强化学习（RL），在过阻尼胶体系统中实验实现了有限时间反馈控制。通过改变光学陷阱位移的协议持续时间 tf，RL 识别的优化策略显示出从确定性拖拽到利用热涨落的反馈辅助的交叉，降低并最终克服了能量成本。该策略与精确最优闭环解定量吻合。将方法扩展到空间局域外力后，RL 能在异质随机环境中识别出最优反馈策略，而此类环境的直接解析控制设计极具挑战性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在过阻尼胶体系统中，如何通过有限时间反馈控制有效利用热涨落来降低甚至克服能量成本，仍缺乏实验验证。本文的动机是在实验层面探索强化学习能否在有限时间协议中识别出最优反馈策略，并超越传统解析方法的适用范围。

Method: 采用实时光镊作为控制执行器，结合原位强化学习（RL）进行在线策略优化。实验系统为过阻尼胶体系统，通过改变光学陷阱位移的协议持续时间 tf，在预设位置间移动光阱。进一步将方法扩展到包含空间局域外力的异质随机环境。

Result: RL 识别的最优策略表现出从确定性拖拽到反馈辅助利用热涨落的交叉行为；随着协议持续时间 tf 变化，该策略能降低并最终克服能量成本。所得策略与精确最优闭环解（exact optimal closed-loop solution）定量吻合。在异质随机环境中，RL 同样能识别出最优反馈策略。

Conclusion: 强化学习能够在过阻尼胶体系统中实验实现有限时间反馈控制，其优化策略与理论解析解一致，并能拓展到难以直接解析设计的异质随机环境，证明了 RL 在复杂控制问题中的有效性和泛化能力。

Abstract: We experimentally realize finite-time feedback control in an overdamped colloidal system using real-time optical tweezers with in situ reinforcement learning (RL). By varying the protocol duration tf for displacing the optical trap between prescribed positions, the optimal strategies identified by RL reveal a crossover from deterministic dragging toward the target to feedback-assisted exploitation of thermal fluctuations, reducing and eventually overcoming the energetic cost. The resulting policies agree quantitatively with the exact optimal closed-loop solution. By extending the approach to spatially localized external forcing, we further show that RL can identify optimal feedback strategies in heterogeneous stochastic environments where direct analytical control design is challenging.

</details>


### [6] [First-order phase transitions in the three-dimensional Blume-Capel ferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17691)
*D. Mataragkas,A. Vasilopoulos,Z. D. Vatansever,Y. Kim,D. -H. Kim,N. G Fytas*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过结合多正则模拟（multicanonical simulations）与双参数Wang-Landau采样（two-parameter Wang-Landau sampling），系统研究了三维简单立方晶格上Blume-Capel铁磁体（Blume-Capel ferromagnet）中的一级相变（first-order phase transitions），分析了共存区、有限尺寸标度行为以及界面张力，并评估了场混合分析方法在三维体系中的适用性界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在深入表征三维Blume-Capel模型中从三相点（tricritical point）附近到强一级相变区域内，温度与晶体场耦合（crystal-field couplings）宽广范围内的共存区特性，并检验场混合分析（field-mixing analysis）方法在三维体系中的有效性。

Method: 采用多正则模拟结合双参数Wang-Landau采样；通过分析能量概率密度函数（energy probability density function）、自由能势垒（free-energy barriers）和界面性质（interfacial properties）等热力学量的有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）行为进行研究。利用联合态密度（joint density of states）进行场混合分析以定位一级相变点并探测三相点行为。

Result: 双峰能量分布的演化揭示了从弱一级相变到强一级相变的逐渐交叉；通过对自由能势垒的标度确定了沿共存线的界面张力（interface tension）及其在三相点附近的消失行为。在三维体系中，场混合分析在三相点区域附近变得敏感，因相关标度变量分布结构平缓，限制了当前可及系统尺寸下对共存条件的分辨能力。

Conclusion: 研究勾勒了该方法在三维体系中的适用性范围，并为该模型一级相变区域提供了一致的刻画，同时揭示了场混合分析在三维中相对于二维实现时的局限性。

Abstract: We investigate first-order phase transitions in the three-dimensional Blume-Capel ferromagnet on the simple cubic lattice by combining multicanonical simulations with two-parameter Wang-Landau sampling. The generalized-ensemble approach enables a detailed characterization of the coexistence region over a broad range of temperatures and crystal-field couplings, extending from the vicinity of the tricritical point deep into the first-order regime. We analyze the finite-size scaling behavior of thermodynamic observables, with particular emphasis on the energy probability density function, free-energy barriers, and interfacial properties. The evolution of the double-peaked energy distributions reveals a gradual crossover from weak to strong first-order behavior as the temperature is lowered. From the scaling of the free-energy barrier we determine the interface tension along the coexistence line and characterize its approach to the tricritical region through its vanishing behavior. In parallel, a field-mixing analysis based on the joint density of states obtained from two-parameter Wang-Landau simulations is employed to locate first-order transition points and probe tricritical behavior. While this approach has been highly successful in two-dimensional realizations of the Blume-Capel model, we find that in three dimensions its practical implementation becomes increasingly sensitive in the vicinity of the tricritical region, where the shallow structure of the relevant scaling variable distribution limits the ability to resolve coexistence conditions for the system sizes currently accessible. These results delineate the range of applicability of the method in three dimensions and provide a consistent picture of the first-order regime of the model.

</details>


### [7] [Thermodynamic description of wealth inequality in the world](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17965)
*Klaus M. Frahm,Leonardo Ermann,Dima L. Shepelyansky*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文基于财富热化假说（Wealth Thermalization Hypothesis, WTH），提出瑞利-金斯（Rayleigh-Jeans, RJ）热分布能够统一描述全球财富不平等现象，并通过多类实证数据验证了这一理论的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释全球财富不平等的普遍规律，并验证财富热化假说（WTH）是否能够通过瑞利-金斯（RJ）热分布对不同层面的财富分布数据进行统一描述。

Method: 将社会财富分层类比为非线性动力系统中的能级，引入总能量与概率范数两个运动积分（integrals of motion）；分析多个真实数据集（包括国家及全球家庭财富洛伦兹曲线（Lorenz curve）与帕累托曲线（Pareto curve）、国家间GDP、多地股市市值、比特币交易及全球贸易）的分布特征。

Result: WTH理论较好地拟合了所有分析对象的洛伦兹曲线与帕累托曲线；观察到瑞利-金斯冷凝（RJ condensation）现象——即形成占据社会财富绝大部分的极小寡头阶段（oligarchic phase）和巨大的贫困阶段（poverty phase）。

Conclusion: 瑞利-金斯（RJ）热分布为全球财富不平等提供了一种普适性描述（universal description），其机制与多模光纤中的自清洁（self cleaning）及其他物理系统中的约束驱动冷凝（constraint driven condensation）具有相似性。

Abstract: According to the recent Wealth Thermalization Hypothesis (WTH) the wealth inequality in the world is described by the Rayleigh-Jeans (RJ) thermal distribution of interacting agents in a society with social stratification. In this concept, the wealth layers of society are associated with energy levels from a nonlinear dynamical system conserving two integrals of motion being total energy and probability norm. This leads to RJ condensation and the formation of a huge poverty phase of low wealth and a tiny oligarchic phase that captures a main part of total society wealth. This RJ phenomenon has similarities with self cleaning in multimode optical fibers and constraint driven condensation in various physical systems. We analyze real Lorenz and Pareto curves for wealth of households in countries and the world, Gross Domestic Product of countries, market capitalization of companies at stock exchange of Hong Kong, Shanghai, London, bitcoin transactions, world trade between countries and show that the WTH theory gives a good description of these curves. On the basis of this comparison we argue that the RJ thermal distribution provides a universal description of wealth inequality in the world.

</details>


### [8] [Equilibrium cluster statistics of cooperative and anticooperative binding on finite one-dimensional rings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18020)
*Thomas Alfonsi,Jérôme Dorignac,John Palmeri,Nils-Ole Walliser*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文针对周期边界条件下的一维有限格点气（lattice gas）模型，推导了平均占据数、畴壁数、团簇数及团簇大小分布等可观测量的精确有限尺寸表达式，并提出了一种基于团簇的组合方法，将状态空间规模从指数级 $2^L$ 缩减至整数分划（integer partitions）尺度 $\approx e^{\sqrt{L}}$，为有限周期系统提供了精确基准，尤其适用于环状生物底物上的吸附与结合研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究有限一维周期格点气中平衡团簇（equilibrium clustering）的形成，作为小环状底物上吸附与结合的最小模型，旨在理解吸引（合作）与排斥（反合作）相互作用下空间组织的变化规律，并揭示有限尺寸与宇称效应对系统行为的影响。

Method: 采用巨正则系综（grand-canonical formulation）结合最近邻耦合（nearest-neighbor coupling），推导平均占据数、畴壁（domain walls）数、团簇（clusters）数等物理量的精确有限尺寸表达式。利用精确 $k$-位点关联函数（$k$-site correlation functions）进一步推导大小为 $k$ 的团簇平均数目、团簇大小分布（cluster-size distribution）和位点加权团簇大小分布（site-weighted cluster-size distribution）。为处理更大格点，提出基于团簇的组合方法，按团簇计数和大小对构型进行分类，将有效状态空间规模从 $2^L$ 压缩至整数分划尺度 $\approx e^{\sqrt{L}}$。

Result: 得到了平均占据数、畴壁数、团簇数以及团簇大小相关统计量的精确有限尺寸表达式。研究发现空间组织在吸引与排斥相互作用下呈现不同特征，并凸显了有限尺寸效应和宇称依赖效应（parity-dependent effects），后者在半填充（half filling）附近的小系统中尤为显著。

Conclusion: 本文结果为有限周期系统提供了精确基准，并提出了具有实验相关性的团簇可观测量，可作为占据数型合作性（occupancy-based cooperativity）测量方法的补充，特别适用于生物组装体中环状底物上的结合研究。

Abstract: We study equilibrium clustering in a finite one-dimensional lattice gas of $L$ sites with periodic boundary conditions, as a minimal model for adsorption and binding on small ring-like substrates. Using a grand-canonical formulation with nearest-neighbor coupling, we derive exact finite-size expressions for the mean occupancy, the mean number of domain walls, and the mean number of clusters. Building on exact $k$-site correlation functions, we further derive expressions for the mean number of clusters of size $k$ and for two complementary size statistics: the cluster-size distribution, and the site-weighted cluster-size distribution. These observables characterize how spatial organization changes across attractive (cooperative) and repulsive (anticooperative) interactions, and highlight finite-size and parity-dependent effects of the underlying lattice, the latter being particularly pronounced near half filling in small systems. To access larger lattices without enumerating all $2^L$ microstates, we also develop a cluster-based combinatorial formulation in which configurations are classified by cluster counts and sizes, reducing the effective state space to a set whose size scales with integer partitions, $\approx e^{\sqrt{L}}$, rather than with $\approx e^{L}$. Taken together, our results provide exact benchmarks for finite periodic systems and suggest experimentally relevant cluster observables that complement occupancy-based measures of cooperativity, with particular relevance for binding on ring-like substrates for biological assemblies.

</details>

### [9] [Chiral Phonons Enable Ultrafast Magnetization Switching via Magnetoelastic Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17124)
*Weiwei He,Muhammad Hamza Asim,Mara Strungaru,Roy Chantrel,Min Yi,Oksana Chubykalo-Fesenko*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究表明，太赫兹驱动的手性声子（chiral phonon）通过纯磁弹耦合（magnetoelastic coupling）同时传递能量和角动量，能够比线性声子实现更快的磁化翻转。手性声子的单一旋向能有效转移角动量至自旋系统，该现象可由一个巨大的假想运动学Barnett-like场（fictitious kinematic Barnett-like field）解释。通过分析自旋波谱的不同区域，发现近Γ点（Γ-point）和P点（P-point）分别适用于不同的磁化翻转条件。研究结果确立声子手性（phonon chirality）作为自旋-晶格动力学中一个决定性的、此前被忽视的参数，为超快低能耗自旋电子学器件提供了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无电流的高效自旋操纵（spin manipulation）是自旋电子学的重要目标，利用手性声子的手性实现超快磁化翻转（magnetization switching）仍是该领域积极追求的方向。作者旨在探究太赫兹驱动的手性声子是否能够以及如何通过纯磁弹耦合机制实现比线性声子更快的磁化翻转。

Method: 通过将太赫兹驱动的手性声子与线性声子进行对比，研究纯磁弹耦合作用下能量与角动量向自旋系统的传递过程。引入一个巨大的假想运动学Barnett-like场来分析不同手性声子对自旋进动（spin precession）的稳定性影响，并考察自旋波谱（spinwave spectrum）中近Γ点与近P点的不同区域特性。

Result: 发现只有单一旋向的手性声子能够高效地将角动量转移至自旋系统，而相反手性的声子可通过THz频率下的巨大假想Barnett-like场使自旋进动失稳。在自旋波谱的近Γ点，强能量传递与自旋波激发（spinwave excitation）占主导，可实现磁化翻转；在近P点，能量损失最小，同样可实现开关条件。

Conclusion: 声子手性在磁弹耦合机制的自旋-晶格动力学（spin-lattice dynamics）中是一个决定性但此前被忽略的关键参数。该发现为开发超快、低能耗的自旋电子学器件（spintronic devices）提供了有前景的研究方向。

Abstract: Phonons are desirable for current-free energy-efficient spin manipulation and harnessing their chirality to achieve ultrafast magnetization switching remains actively pursued. Here we demonstrate that terahertz-driven chiral phonons enable faster magnetization switching than linear phonons through the purely magnetoelastic coupling that transfers both energy and angular momentum. Only one phonon handedness efficiently transfers angular momentum to the spin system, which we explain by a large fictitious kinematic Barnett-like field at THz frequencies that destabilizes spin precession for the opposite chirality. Considering different regions of the spinwave spectrum, we find that switching conditions can be realized near the Γ-point where strong energy transfer and spinwave excitation dominate, and near the P-point which offers minimal energy loss. Our results establish phonon chirality as a decisive and previously overlooked parameter in spin-lattice dynamics within the magnetoelastic coupling mechanism, offering a promising avenue for ultrafast low-energy spintronic devices.

</details>


### [10] [Machine learning insights into band gap properties in halide-based perovskites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17186)
*Chadawan Khamdang,Mengen Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究基于原子与结构性质，开发了多种机器学习模型（包括随机森林回归、梯度提升回归树、极限梯度提升等集成树方法），用于预测多种卤化物钙钛矿（halide perovskites）的带隙能量（band gap energies），并分析了特征重要性，识别出B位和X位元素性质以及A位和B位原子数量为关键描述符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 卤化物钙钛矿在光电器件中具有广阔应用前景，无铅钙钛矿因低毒性而备受关注，这推动了对替代组分与结构的探索。准确预测带隙能量对设计新材料至关重要，同时需要建立结构与元素描述符与带隙能量之间的直接关系。

Method: 基于原子和结构性质，开发机器学习模型来预测多种卤化物钙钛矿的带隙能量。所用算法包括集成树方法（ensemble tree-based methods）：随机森林回归（random forest regression, RFR）、梯度提升回归树（gradient boosted regression trees, GBRT）和极限梯度提升（extreme gradient boosting, XGB）。

Result: 随机森林回归、梯度提升回归树和极限梯度提升等集成树算法均展现出较强的预测精度。特征重要性分析识别出B位和X位元素性质以及A位和B位原子数量是影响带隙能量的主要因素。

Conclusion: 该研究加深了对机器学习模型的理解，并为设计新型卤化物钙钛矿材料提供了指导。

Abstract: Halide perovskites show great promise for applications in optoelectronic devices. The lead-free perovskites are attracting increasing interest due to their low toxicity and motivate the exploration of alternative compositions and structures, including A$_2$BX$_6$, A$_2$BB$^\prime$X$_6$, A$_3$B$_2$X$_9$, and A$_4$BX$_6$. Accurate predictions of a wide range of band gap energies are important for designing new materials. It is also desired to generate a direct relationship between the structural and elemental descriptors and the band gap energies. In this work, we develop machine learning models to predict band gap energies across various types of halide perovskites based on atomic and structural properties. Algorithms including ensemble tree-based methods, random forest regression (RFR), gradient boosted regression trees (GBRT), and extreme gradient boosting (XGB) showed strong predictive accuracy. We also analyzed feature importance to identify key descriptors, including B-site and X-site elemental properties, as well as the number of A- and B-site atoms, as primary factors influencing band gap energies. These results improve our understanding of the ML models and provide guidance for designing new halide perovskite materials.

</details>


### [11] [Physics-Informed Attention Mechanism and Generalization Capability of Deep Learning-Based Grain Growth Evolution Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17235)
*Pungponhavoan Tep,Marc Bernacki*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究评估了先前训练的机器学习模型在晶粒生长预测中的分布外（OOD）泛化能力，并提出了一种边界掩码注意力机制（boundary-masked attention mechanism）以提升模型鲁棒性。该物理启发的注意力模型在不经重新训练的情况下成功泛化至三种测试场景（实验微观组织、双峰晶粒尺寸分布微观组织、异常晶粒生长），尤其在双峰分布案例中，结构相似性指数（SSIM）从0.6221提升至0.7609，平均晶粒尺寸误差从8.75%降至3.57%。注意力热力图分析表明，该模型自发学习到与大晶界对齐的注意力模式，与曲率驱动晶粒生长物理一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 用于晶粒生长预测的机器学习模型通常在理想化的合成数据上训练，但实际应用要求模型能够泛化到训练分布之外的条件（Out-Of-Distribution, OOD）。本研究旨在检验先前训练的模型在多种OOD场景下的泛化能力，并探究物理启发的架构设计（如边界掩码注意力机制）是否能进一步提升鲁棒性。

Method: 研究基于先前训练的模型，提出了一种专门针对晶粒生长问题的边界掩码注意力机制（boundary-masked attention mechanism），将注意力限制在晶界像素上。基线模型与此物理启发的注意力模型均在不经重新训练或微调（fine-tuning）的条件下，在三种OOD测试案例（实验微观组织、双峰晶粒尺寸分布微观组织、异常晶粒生长）上进行评估。

Result: 两种模型均成功泛化至三种OOD测试案例。边界掩码注意力机制在所有案例中均显著提升性能，其中双峰晶粒尺寸分布微观组织案例的改进最为显著：SSIM从0.6221提升至0.7609，平均晶粒尺寸（$\overline{R}$）误差从8.75%降至3.57%。注意力热力图分析显示，该模型学会将注意力集中在与曲率驱动晶粒生长物理（curvature-driven grain growth physics）一致的大晶界上。

Conclusion: 在合成数据上训练的模型能够在无需重新训练的条件下泛化至多种分布外条件，而物理启发的注意力机制（当边界形态与训练域匹配时）可进一步提升预测精度。注意力模式的自发涌现表明，物理先验的融入并不需要显式编码到架构中。

Abstract: Machine Learning (ML) models for grain growth prediction are typically trained on idealized synthetic data, yet practical applications require generalization to conditions outside the training distribution. This study evaluated the Out-Of-Distribution (OOD) generalization capability of the trained model from our previous study across three test cases, including experimental microstructures, microstructures characterized by a bimodal grain size distribution, and abnormal grain growth. To further probe whether physics-informed architectural design could improve robustness under these different conditions, a boundary-masked attention mechanism was proposed specifically for grain growth, constraining attention to grain boundary pixels. Both the baseline and the proposed physics-informed attention model were evaluated without retraining or fine-tuning on the OOD data. Both models successfully generalized to all three test cases, yet the boundary-masked attention mechanism provided substantial improvements, with the most notable gains for microstructures characterized by a bimodal grain size distribution, where Structural Similarity Index Measure (SSIM) improved from \num{0.6221} to \num{0.7609} and mean grain size ($\overline{R}$) error decreased from \SI{8.75}{\percent} to \SI{3.57}{\percent}. The attention heatmap analysis revealed that the boundary-masked attention model learned to concentrate attention on large grain boundaries in a manner consistent with curvature-driven grain growth physics, emerging from training without being explicitly encoded into the architecture. These results indicate that models trained on synthetic data can generalize to diverse OOD conditions without retraining, and that physics-informed attention may improve accuracy when the boundary morphology matches the training domain.

</details>


### [12] [General Method for Evaluation of Stop-Bands of Periodic Structures with Symmetric Unit Cells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17265)
*Alexander Hvatov,Mariia Krasikova,Aleksandra Pavliuk,Steffen Marburg*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用周期单胞的镜像对称性，将布里渊区高对称顶点处的驻波本征问题分解为四分之一单胞上的四个独立子问题，每种子问题由诺伊曼（Neumann）或狄利克雷（Dirichlet）边界条件控制。通过沿不可约布里渊区边界各段按指标排序和配对所得本征频率，可无需计算完整色散图而直接得到阻带（stop-band）间隔的显式公式。该分解基于小群（little group）表示论，适用于材料分布在垂直于单胞面的镜像下不变的单胞。在两种声子晶体构型（环氧树脂基体中的铅柱圆柱声子晶体、耦合C形亥姆霍兹谐振器晶格）上验证，重构的阻带边界与完整Floquet色散计算在最低频带偏差低于1%，且仅需三个离散波矢的本征值解。文中识别了导致配对规则失效的能带非单调行为及谱条件，并将两种边界条件共有的平带（flat band）识别为连续谱束缚态（bound state in the continuum）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上计算声子晶体或光子晶体的色散关系（dispersion relation）需要求解完整布里渊区（Brillouin zone）上的本征值问题，计算成本高昂。本文的动机是通过对称性约化，仅需少量离散波矢即可精确获得阻带边界信息，从而大幅降低计算开销。

Method: 利用周期单胞的镜像对称性，将布里渊区高对称顶点处的驻波本征问题分解为一个四分之一单胞上的四个独立子问题，分别施加诺伊曼（Neumann）或狄利克雷（Dirichlet）边界条件；随后沿不可约布里渊区（irreducible Brillouin zone）边界各段，按本征频率的指标排序与配对，导出阻带间隔的显式公式。该分解基于高对称点处小群（little group）的表示论（representation theory）。

Result: 在两种构型（环氧树脂基体中的铅柱声子晶体、耦合C形亥姆霍兹谐振器晶格）上验证了该方法：重构的阻带边界与完整Floquet色散计算在最低频带偏差在1%以内，且仅需求解三个离散波矢的本征值问题。同时指出，当布里渊区段内出现回避交叉（avoided crossing）导致能带非单调时，配对规则仅为近似，并识别了相应的谱条件。此外，两种边界条件共有的平带被识别为连续谱束缚态。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一种基于对称性约化的高效阻带预测框架，无需计算完整色散图即可精确获得阻带边界，适用于具有相应镜像对称性的周期结构。文中同时明确了配对规则近似的适用范围及失效条件。

Abstract: The mirror symmetries of a periodic unit cell are exploited to decompose the standing-wave eigenproblem at the high-symmetry vertices of the Brillouin zone into four independent sub-problems on a quarter-cell, each governed by Neumann (sound-hard) or Dirichlet (sound-soft) boundary conditions. Sorting and pairing the resulting eigenfrequencies by index along each segment of the irreducible Brillouin zone boundary yields an explicit formula for the stop-band intervals without computing the full dispersion diagram. The decomposition is exact, following directly from the representation theory of the little group at each high-symmetry point. It applies to any unit cell whose material distribution is invariant under the mirrors normal to the cell faces. The method is validated on two configurations: a phononic crystal of lead cylinders in an epoxy matrix, analyzed using the plane-wave expansion, and a lattice of coupled C-shaped Helmholtz resonators, analyzed using finite-element analysis. For both systems, the reconstructed stop-band boundaries agree with the full Floquet dispersion calculation to within 1% for the lowest bands, requiring eigenvalue solutions at only three discrete wavevectors. Avoided crossings within a Brillouin zone segment can cause bands to exhibit non-monotone behavior, rendering the pairing rule approximate; the spectral conditions for this are identified. Flat bands common to both boundary-condition types are identified as bound states in the continuum.

</details>


### [13] [Dislocation-templated antiferromagnetic domains in epitaxial NiO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17302)
*Alexandra Fonseca Montenegro,Justin Michel,Fengyuan Yang,Roberto C. Myers*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本论文利用扫描电子显微镜电子通道衬度成像（ECCI）技术，在NiO/MgO(001)外延薄膜中发现了反铁磁畴壁被界面位错网络确定性钉扎的结构记忆效应；通过热循环、衍射矢量分析和厚度系列实验，揭示了磁致伸缩应变场与位错网络演化对反铁磁畴结构的控制机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）畴的控制对自旋电子学（spintronics）至关重要，但由于反铁磁材料缺乏净磁化强度（net magnetization），实现确定性操控仍然极具挑战。

Method: 利用扫描电子显微镜电子通道衬度成像（scanning electron microscopy electron channeling contrast imaging, ECCI）技术，对NiO/MgO(001)外延薄膜进行热循环实验（跨越奈尔温度（Néel temperature））、衍射矢量（diffraction-vector）依赖的ECCI分析，并对23–60 nm厚度系列薄膜进行定量图像分析。

Result: 发现反铁磁孪晶畴壁（twin-domain walls, DWs）在纳米尺度上被界面位错网络（interface dislocation networks）确定性钉扎；热循环后畴壁在相同空间位置重现；畴对比度源于局域菱方磁致伸缩应变场（rhombohedral magnetostrictive strain fields）；揭示了从23到60 nm厚度范围氧化物弛豫机制的显式转变：薄层中以沿<100>方向的界面失配位错（misfit dislocations, MDs）主导，厚层中临界应变引发位错段交滑移至次级或高阶晶面，形成偏向<110>方向的锯齿形位错网络。

Conclusion: 畴壁面积分数直接追踪位错网络（MD networks）的局域密度和空间构型，为利用一维缺陷（one-dimensional defects）进行反铁磁织构的缺陷工程（defect-engineering）提供了框架。

Abstract: Controlling antiferromagnetic domains is essential for spintronics, yet deterministic manipulation remains challenging due to their lack of net magnetization. Here, we utilize scanning electron microscopy electron channeling contrast imaging (ECCI) to demonstrate a robust structural memory effect in epitaxial NiO/MgO(001), where antiferromagnetic twin-domain walls (DWs) are deterministically pinned at the nanoscale by interface dislocation networks. Thermal cycling across the Neel temperature reveals that while DW contrast completely vanishes in the paramagnetic phase, the features re-emerge at identical spatial locations upon cooling. Diffraction-vector-dependent ECCI demonstrates that domain contrast stems from localized rhombohedral magnetostrictive strain fields. By tracking a film thickness series from 23 to 60 nm, we resolve an explicit transition in oxide relaxation mechanics. A primary slip system initiates strain relaxation via interface misfit dislocations (MDs) tracking along <100>. At greater thicknesses, rising critical strain prompts threading segments to cross-slip onto secondary or higher-index planes, depositing a wavy network of zig-zag MD lines deviated toward <110>. Quantitative image analysis reveals that DW area fractions directly track the local density and spatial configuration of the evolving MD networks, providing a framework for defect-engineering antiferromagnetic textures using one-dimensional defects.

</details>


### [14] [Bridging the continuum and the kinetic-Boltzmann theories of heat flow through generalized Knudsen numbers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17829)
*Nikhil Malviya,Navaneetha K. Ravichandran*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过引入广义克努森数（generalized Knudsen numbers）框架，系统地将线性化Peierls-Boltzmann方程（LPBE）约化为多种连续介质热输运模型，并基于LPBE的本征模分析（eigenmode analysis）提出了一个统一的温度场连续方程，从而在23种半导体材料中揭示了若干此前未被识别的非傅里叶热流特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半导体晶体的热传导根本上由声子（phonon）输运的线性化Peierls-Boltzmann方程（LPBE）描述，但实验上常使用傅里叶热扩散、弱准弹道（weakly quasiballistic）和流体动力学（hydrodynamic）热方程等连续介质理论来解释。这些不同的理论之间缺乏系统的联系，因此需要建立一个统一框架来桥接粒子描述与连续介质描述，并澄清各热流区域的边界与特征。

Method: 基于LPBE的本征模分析，引入一组广义克努森数（generalized Knudsen numbers）作为尺度参数，系统地将LPBE约化为各种连续介质热输运方程的极限形式，并推导出一个统一的温度场连续方程，涵盖从弹道（ballistic）到扩散（diffusive）的所有热流区域。

Result: 在23种技术重要的半导体材料中，该框架识别出四种此前未被揭示的非傅里叶热流特征：（1）弱准弹道区域与流体动力学热流区域相互排斥；（2）流体动力学第二声（second sound）温度波的传播速度具有长度依赖性，且存在一个特征加热长度（characteristic heating length）使第二声效应最强；（3）频域温度响应可区分流体动力学第二声与弹道热流；（4）瞬态流体动力学热流中存在一种新的非振荡（non-oscillatory）特征信号。

Conclusion: 该工作正式桥接了热流的连续介质描述与粒子描述，为不同热流区域的温度动力学提供了关键特征信号，有助于未来对这些热流区域进行明确的实验观测。

Abstract: Heat conduction in semiconductor crystals is fundamentally governed by the linearized Peierls-Boltzmann equation (LPBE) for phonon transport, that arises out of a kinetic theory for phonon quasiparticles. Yet, continuum theories such as the Fourier's heat diffusion, weakly quasiballistic and hydrodynamic heat equations are often used to explain the experimental observations of heat flow in these materials. Here, we show that a systematic reduction of the LPBE into such equivalent continuum descriptions are possible only for the limiting values of a set of generalized Knudsen numbers. We further show that all of these continuum heat flow regimes, along with the ballistic heat flow, can be described by a single continuum equation for the temperature field that originates from the eigenmode analysis of the LPBE, thus offering a unified picture of all possible heat flow regimes in semiconducting crystals. Using quantitative examples on twenty three technologically important semiconductors, we show that several previously-unidentified features of the non-Fourier heat flow regimes emerge from this generalized Knudsen number framework such as (1) the mutual exclusivity of the weakly quasiballistic and the hydrodynamic heat flow regimes, (2) length-dependent velocity of the hydrodynamic second sound temperature wave and a characteristic heating length for the strongest hydrodynamic second sound, (3) characteristic frequency-domain temperature response distinguishing the hydrodynamic second sound from the ballistic heat flow regime and, (4) a new non-oscillatory signature of transient hydrodynamic heat flow. Our work formally bridges the continuum and the particulate descriptions of heat flow, and provides insights into the important signatures of temperature dynamics in each of these heat flow regimes, that will aid in their unambiguous experimental observations in the future.

</details>


### [15] [Robust Spin Splitting and Strain-Controlled Optical Response in Monolayer CrC2N4 for Valleytronic and Optoelectronic Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17329)
*Md. Samrat,Vivek Chowdhury,Sake Wang,Ahmed Zubair*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）研究原始和双轴应变（biaxial strain）下单层CrC₂N₄的电子结构、谷性质、电荷转移和光学性质。

Result: 单层CrC₂N₄在K/K'谷处呈现直接带隙；SOC产生了谷对比面外自旋极化，价带自旋分裂为51.9 meV，导带分裂为1.7 meV；-4%至+4%双轴应变可将带隙从1.987 eV调至1.421 eV，并在约-1%应变处发生间接-直接带隙转变；拉伸应变增强贝里曲率（Berry curvature）并将光学响应红移至可见-近红外区域。

Abstract: Monolayer CrC2N4 recently emerged as a promising two-dimensional semiconductor, yet its spin-orbit-coupled (SOC) physics and strain-tunable optical response remained largely unexplored. Here, we investigated the electronic, valley, charge-transfer, and optical properties of pristine and biaxially strained monolayer CrC2N4 using first-principles calculations. The monolayer exhibited a direct band gap at the K/K' valleys. SOC produced valley contrasting out-of-plane spin polarization, yielding a moderate valence band spin splitting of 51.9 meV and a small conduction band spin splitting of 1.7 meV. Orbital-resolved analysis showed that the edge states were mainly governed by Cr-d and N-p hybridization, while Bader analysis indicated polar-covalent bonding through charge transfer toward N atoms. Biaxial strain in the range of -4% to +4% tuned the band gap from 1.987 to 1.421 eV and drove an indirect-to-direct gap transition near -1% strain. Tensile strain enhanced the Berry curvature and red-shifted the optical response toward the visible-near-infrared region. These results suggested monolayer CrC2N4 as a promising platform for strain-engineered valleytronic and optoelectronic device applications.

Here we use hard x-ray photoemission spectroscopy (HAXPES) to probe hydrogen-related electronic structure in as-grown and post-annealed InN thin films prepared at different grown temperatures. Post annealing, which reduces the concentration of hydrogen impurities in the films, shifts the core-level spectra toward lower binding energy, consistent with a chemical-potential shift associated with the passivation of electron carriers. This infrastructure allows the automated capture, curation, analysis and dissemination of data ranging from experimental materials synthesis parameters and characterization, to theoretical first-principles and ReaxFF molecular dynamics modeling1. The system currently hosts synthesis and property data (accessible via a REST API) on approximately twenty thousand samples produced by the 2DCC grown using a variety of techniques from bulk crystal growth to metal-organic chemical vapor deposition (MOCVD) and molecular beam epitaxy (MBE), among others. Data used in publications can easily be grouped by the system into data packages that are given digital object identifiers (DOIs) for inclusion with each publication. The LiST platform is now being used by groups outside of the 2DCC as a solution for data curation in materials science. Data management tools such as LiST support the materials development process by allowing a closed loop iteration between synthesis, characterization, theory, and targeted materials design. This also enables machine learning (ML) research, artificial intelligence (AI) analysis, and the potential for autonomous synthesis in the future.

### [19] [Hybrid Electronic-Ionic Ferroelectricity in Superlubric van der Waals Heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17502)
*Jing Huang,Jun Kang,Daniel Bennett*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文揭示了超润滑滑动铁电体（SL-sFE）中极化并非仅由滑动驱动，而是依赖层间滑动与间隔层面外屈曲之间的耦合，产生一种混合电子-离子极化，并呈现多种铁电迟滞行为，从而将SL-sFE确立为一类新型铁电体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在滑动铁电体（sliding ferroelectric, sFE）中降低开关势垒的一种策略是插入非公度间隔层以减少滑动摩擦，从而构造超润滑滑动铁电体（superlubric sliding ferroelectric, SL-sFE）。然而，极化如何在有效解耦的外层之间保持稳定仍是一个未解问题，这构成了本文的研究动机。

Method: 通过理论分析，研究了SL-sFE中极化与层间滑动及间隔层面外屈曲（out-of-plane buckling）之间的耦合机制，揭示了由此产生的不对称轨道杂化（asymmetric orbital hybridization）所驱动的混合电子-离子极化。

Result: 研究发现SL-sFE与传统sFE存在根本性差异：极化并非仅由滑动单独驱动，而是由层间滑动与间隔层屈曲之间的复杂耦合所决定。这种耦合导致极化呈现出混合的一阶和二阶相变、多步开关以及反铁电体（antiferroelectric-like）行为等多种铁电迟滞类型。

Conclusion: SL-sFE中极化机制与传统sFE不同，是一种由滑动与屈曲耦合产生的混合电子-离子极化，并表现出丰富的相变与开关行为，应将SL-sFE视为一类独立的铁电体。

Abstract: One strategy to lower the switching barrier in a sliding ferroelectric (sFE) is to insert an incommensurate spacer to reduce sliding friction, creating a superlubric sliding ferroelectric (SL-sFE). However, how polarization survives across the effectively decoupled outer layers remains an open question. We show that SL-sFEs are fundamentally different from conventional sFEs: polarization is not driven by sliding alone, but by an intricate coupling between interlayer sliding and the out-of-plane buckling of the spacer layer. This coupling results in a unique hybrid electronic-ionic polarization arising from asymmetric orbital hybridization. The interplay of these order parameters generates several distinct types of ferroelectric hysteresis, including mixed first- and second-order transitions, multi-step switching, and antiferroelectric-like behavior, establishing SL-sFEs as a distinct class of ferroelectrics.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We report the crystal structure and magnetic properties of a $S=3/2$ anisotropic triangular lattice compound Na$_3$Cr(PO$_4$)$_2$ employing single-crystal and powder x-ray diffraction, magnetization, heat capacity, and $^{31}$P nuclear magnetic resonance (NMR) experiments, supported by the band structure calculations. Magnetic susceptibility exhibits a broad maximum around 3.5 K, indicating the presence of a short-range antiferromagnetic order, typical of a low-dimensional spin system. Magnetization and heat capacity manifest an antiferromagnetic long-range ordering at around $T_{\rm N} \simeq 2.6$ K. This was further confirmed by the drastic NMR line broadening and a peak in the nuclear spin-lattice and spin-spin relaxation rates. The isothermal magnetization data exhibit a field-induced spin-flop transition at around $μ_0H_{\rm SF} \simeq 1.7$ T reminiscent of an anisotropic two-dimensional magnet, before saturating above $μ_0H_{\rm sat} \simeq 4.5$ T. The saturation field was further upheld by the field-dependent NMR relaxation measurements at low temperatures. The $^{31}$P NMR spectral shape confirms the commensurate antiferromagnetic nature of the ordering below $T_{\rm N}$. \textit{Ab initio} calculations reveal a significant deformation of the triangular spin lattice, resulting in triangles with two antiferromagnetic couplings of similar strength and a much weaker coupling along the third side of the triangle.

### [21] [Surface Induced Magnetism of CdSe Quantum Dots: A DFT Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17681)
*G. Kurian,D. Subedi,A. Aniagboso,M. D. Mochena*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过自旋极化密度泛函理论（spin-polarized density functional theory）计算，系统研究了量子点（quantum dots）的表面重构对诱导磁性的影响，发现双配位（bi-coordinated）表面原子而非三配位（tri-coordinated）原子是自旋极化表面态的主要来源，并预测钝化后残留的悬挂键（dangling bonds）可能导致可调谐的表面磁性（tunable surface magnetism）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子点的表面诱导磁性（surface induced magnetism）由于表面化学的复杂性及磁性本身涉及的多自由度，理解不充分且存在争议，亟需系统性地澄清表面重构与磁性之间的关联。

Method: 采用自旋极化共线密度泛函理论（spin-polarized colinear density functional theory）计算裸量子点及钝化量子点的电荷密度和自旋密度，以受控方式确定表面重构状态。

Result: 三配位表面原子弛豫后不贡献悬挂键；双配位原子发生二聚化（dimerize），减少悬挂键数量从而影响诱导磁性；双配位而非三配位原子是自旋极化表面态的成因。

Conclusion: 预测在具有双配位原子的低指数晶面（low index facets）上，即使经过钝化处理，残留的悬挂键仍可能产生可调谐的表面磁性；该结果有助于解释文献中相互矛盾的实验现象。

Abstract: Surface induced magnetism of quantum dots is not well understood and has been a subject of considerable controversy because of the complexity of surface chemistry of quantum dot facets coupled with the many degrees of freedom inherently involved in magnetism. We performed spin-polarized colinear density functional theory calculations to study charge and spin densities to determine surface reconstructions in bare as well as passivated quantum dots in controlled way. We find that tricoordinated surface atoms relax contributing no dangling bonds and bi-coordinated atoms dimerize, reducing the population of the dangling bonds affecting the induced magnetism. As a result, bicoordinated rather than tricoordinated surface atoms are responsible for spin polarized surface states. In light of recent advanced experimental tools, we predict dangling bonds that remain, despite passivation, on low index facets with bicoordinated atoms could result in tunable surface magnetism. Our results also shed light on the contradicting experimental results in the literature.

</details>

Abstract: Activated carbons are promising adsorbents for post-combustion CO2 capture due to their high surface area, tunable microporosity, and resistance to moisture and flue-gas impurities. Despite extensive equilibrium adsorption studies, the dynamic behavior of activated carbons under fixed-bed operating conditions relevant to post-combustion CO2/N2 remains insufficiently understood, particularly for renewable materials. In this work, the adsorption and separation behavior of CO2/N2 mixtures on a commercial coal-derived activated carbon (WS-480) and a biomass-based activated carbon (MSP700-A900CO2) is comparatively evaluated by combining experimental measurements and simulations. We employ atomistic activated carbon models, augmented with surface functional groups as representations of WS-480 and MSP700-A900CO2, achieving close agreement with experimental adsorption data. The validated models are subsequently used to predict CO2/N2 separation under equilibrium and dynamic conditions, reproducing the experimental breakthrough behavior while providing molecular-level insight into the influence of pore structure and surface chemistry on adsorption performance.

### [23] [Hydrogen s-electrons as the origin of crystal magnetism beyond spin-orbit coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17902)
*Baiqiang Liu,Zhen Gong,Rui Liu,Siyang Liu,Yue Feng,Zhigang Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用第一性原理计算方法，设计并研究了一种将十三个氢原子封装在 (BN)12 笼内的低 Z 铁磁晶体 H13@(BN)12，通过化学预压缩实现常压稳定性，并分析电子结构与磁性质。

Abstract: Magnetism has long been attributed to localized d, f, and even p electrons with strong correlations, whereas s electrons exemplified by hydrogen are reactive and tend to have their spins quenched, making s-electron-derived magnetism and long-range ordered magnetic crystals seem unattainable. Here we report a low-Z ferromagnetic crystal H13@(BN)12 using first-principles calculations, where thirteen hydrogen atoms are encapsulated within a (BN)12 cage and magnetism originates from the 1s electron of the central hydrogen atom. Interestingly, under 16 GPa compression, the system transforms into a nonmagnetic metallic state driven by delocalized electrons of the central hydrogen atom. This study opens a pathway for constructing s-electron-driven magnetic materials and lays the foundation for developing low-energy consumption magnetic devices without SOC.

Here, we revisit this problem using DFT and machine-learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs). We show that while quantum effects do contribute to dislocation glide at low temperature, their magnitude is much lower than previously reported, and insufficient to reconcile atomistic predictions with experiments. The YIAG exchange-decouples the YIG layers while enabling lattice coherence, maintaining the low damping of the YIG. ### [26] [Tunable Electronic and Transport Properties of Biphenylene via Fluorination and Disorder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18083)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 关联氟化（correlated fluorination）可作为主动调控电子输运的有效机制，为二维碳同素异形体的能带与输运工程设计提供新策略。

Abstract: Biphenylene (BPN) network is a newly synthesized 2D carbon allotrope hosting anisotropic Dirac electronic states. Here, we investigate how fluorination and correlated chemical disorder modify the electronic structure and charge transport of fluorinated biphenylene (F/BPN) using density functional theory, Wannier-based tight-biding Hamiltonian, and quantum transport simulations. We show that fluorination reshapes the transport response of BPN, producing concentration-dependent anisotropic conduction regimes. For pristine and ordered fluorinated systems, we identified the emergence of negative differential resistance (NDR) and a bias-induced inversion of the preferred transport direction, from armchair to zigzag and vice versa. In contrast, disorder suppresses the NDR, driving the system toward an approximately Ohmic transport regime. At high fluorine coverage, we further observed a nonmonotonic dependence of the armchair current on adatom concentration, which we attribute to the formation of correlated quasi-linear fluor conformation that promote armchair-oriented C-$π$ transport channels while simultaneously suppressing transport along the zigzag direction. Our results demonstrate that correlated fluorination can be used as an active mechanism to engineer electronic transport.

### [27] [Impact of dynamic electrostatic disorder on hole mobility in rubrene: a nonadiabatic molecular dynamics investigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18090)
*Jan Elsner,Samuele Giannini,Jochen Blumberger*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过将阻尼移位力（damped shifted-force, DSF）实空间静电求和方法与高效的加减方案相结合，在基于片段轨道的表面跳跃（fragment orbital-based surface hopping, FOB-SH）模拟中纳入了动态静电无序，从而实现了对红荧烯（rubrene）中室温空穴传输的定量预测描述。结果表明，静电相互作用显著增大了重组能（reorganization energy）、增强了位能无序（site energy disorder），使空穴波函数的空间扩展减小，并将沿高迁移率方向的理论迁移率从35 cm² V⁻¹ s⁻¹下调至21 cm² V⁻¹ s⁻¹，与实验值高度吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高迁移率有机分子晶体（如红荧烯）是有机电子学的重要材料，但其电荷传输性质的定量预测性描述仍具挑战性。先前针对非极性分子晶体的大规模模拟通常忽略动态静电无序，因为静电能计算开销大且对非极性体系似乎合理，但这一近似是否合理尚待验证。

Method: 采用阻尼移位力（DSF）实空间静电求和方法，结合高效的加减方案，在基于片段轨道的表面跳跃（FOB-SH）模拟中引入动态静电无序，对红荧烯在室温下的空穴传输进行非绝热分子动力学（nonadiabatic molecular dynamics）模拟。

Result: 静电相互作用使（假设的）最近邻跳跃的重组能在a方向和b方向分别增加29 meV和39 meV（基线值为152 meV）。在FOB-SH模拟中，静电能导致位能无序增大，使得空穴波函数的空间扩展减小（逆参与比从13降至9），沿高迁移率方向的理论迁移率从35 cm² V⁻¹ s⁻¹降低至21 cm² V⁻¹ s⁻¹，与实验结果高度一致。

Conclusion: 动态静电无序对非极性有机分子晶体的电荷传输具有不可忽略的影响；将DSF静电求和方法纳入FOB-SH框架能够实现与实验高度吻合的迁移率定量预测，从而为有机电子材料的电荷传输理论研究提供了更精确的计算方案。

Abstract: High-mobility organic molecular crystals such as rubrene are important materials for organic electronics, yet a quantitatively predictive description of their charge transport properties remains challenging. Direct mixed quantum-classical nonadiabatic molecular dynamics simulations provide a promising route by explicitly propagating the charge carrier wavefunction, without assuming a specific transport mechanism. However, previous large-scale simulations of apolar molecular crystals have commonly neglected dynamic electrostatic disorder, since evaluation of electrostatic interactions is computationally demanding and the approximation appears plausible for apolar systems. Here, we use the damped shifted-force (DSF) real-space electrostatic summation method, combined with an efficient addition-subtraction scheme, to include dynamic electrostatic disorder in fragment orbital-based surface hopping (FOB-SH) simulations of room-temperature hole transport in rubrene. We find that electrostatic interactions increase the reorganization energy for (hypothetical) nearest neighbour hopping by 29 and 39 meV along the a and b-directions, respectively, relative to a baseline value of 152 meV obtained without electrostatics. In FOB-SH simulations, electrostatic interactions lead to increased site energy disorder, reducing the spatial extent of the hole wavefunction, as measured by a decrease in the inverse participation ratio from 13 to 9, and lowering the predicted mobility along the high-mobility direction from $35$ to $21~\mathrm{cm^2 V^{-1}s^{-1}}$, in close agreement with experiment.

### [28] [Double quantum spin Hall phase in bilayer ZrTe$_5$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18130)
*Chao Chen Ye,Gábor Kalla,Jianting Ye,Jagoda Sławińska*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算发现，双层ZrTe₅在其最稳定结构中可实现双重量子自旋霍尔态（double quantum spin Hall phase），具有两对受保护的螺旋边缘态（helical edge states）和量子化自旋霍尔响应（quantized spin Hall response），可通过单轴应变（uniaxial strain）调控转变为常规单对边缘态的量子自旋霍尔相，从而在单一材料中连接了传统$\mathbb{Z}_2$分类框架内外的拓扑相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超出传统$\mathbb{Z}_2$拓扑分类（topological classification）的双量子自旋霍尔相（double QSH phase）的可实验实现体系，特别是在具有可观带隙（sizeable band gaps）的材料中寻找这类相，并研究其在外界调控下的相变行为。

Method: 基于第一性原理计算（first principles calculations），对最稳定结构下的双层ZrTe₅进行电子结构分析，并研究单轴应变（uniaxial strain）对其拓扑相的影响。

Result: 双层ZrTe₅在其最稳定结构中实现了双重量子自旋霍尔相，该相拥有两对螺旋边缘态（two pairs of helical edge states），产生增强的边缘电导（enhanced edge conductance）和量子化自旋霍尔响应（quantized spin Hall response），且该响应在高达约100 meV的能量窗口内保持鲁棒性。单轴应变可驱动该相转变为常规单对边缘态QSH相（$\mathbb{Z}_2=1$）。

Conclusion: 双层ZrTe₅作为可调谐平台（tunable platform），能够在单一材料中连接常规QSH相和双重QSH相；此外，非扭曲范德华双层体系（untwisted van der Waals bilayers）有能力承载超越传统$\mathbb{Z}_2$分类（conventional $\mathbb{Z}_2$ classification）的拓扑相。

Abstract: Quantum spin Hall insulators (QSH) are topological materials that host helical edge states protected against backscattering, making them ideal candidates for dissipationless spin transport. Within the conventional $\mathbb{Z}_2$ classification, only phases with an odd number of edge state pairs ($\mathbb{Z}_2 = 1$) are topologically nontrivial, whereas even-channel systems ($\mathbb{Z}_2 = 0$) lie beyond this framework but can host robust edge transport characterized by a spin Chern number. Experimentally accessible realizations of such phases remain rare, particularly in systems with sizeable band gaps. Here, we show that bilayer ZrTe$_5$ realizes a double quantum spin Hall phase in its energetically most stable structure. Using first principles calculations, we demonstrate that uniaxial strain drives a transition from this phase to a conventional single pair QSH phase with $\mathbb{Z}_2 = 1$. The double QSH phase hosts two pairs of helical edge states, resulting in enhanced edge conductance and a quantized spin Hall response that remains robust over an energy window of up to $\sim$100 meV. These results establish bilayer ZrTe$_5$ as a tunable platform connecting conventional and double QSH phases within a single material. More broadly, they demonstrate that untwisted van der Waals bilayers can host topological phases beyond the conventional $\mathbb{Z}_2$ classification.

</details>


### [29] [Anisotropic Short-Range Order Modulates Ferroelectric Switching in Wurtzite ScAlN Alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18213)
*Shunda Chen,Xianchao Dong,Xiaochen Jin,Tianshu Li*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文发现纤锌矿（wurtzite）铁电合金中的短程有序（short-range order, SRO）会显著影响本征翻转势垒（intrinsic switching barrier）。通过第一性原理正则采样，研究揭示ScAlN中存在强各向异性SRO，它抑制面内Sc–N–Sc构型并增强沿极轴方向的柱状混合阳离子链，从而系统性地提高翻转势垒。柱状Sc–N–Al–N–Sc构型的数量被确定为控制势垒变化的关键结构描述符，表明SRO可作为独立于组分的自由度来调控铁电翻转。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对纤锌矿铁电合金翻转行为的理解通常基于组分、应变、缺陷和界面等因素，而忽略了局域化学有序（local chemical order）或仅将其视为次要扰动。本文旨在证明短程有序（SRO）实际上是一个被忽视的微观变量，它对本征翻转势垒具有实质性影响。

Method: 采用第一性原理正则采样（first-principles canonical sampling）方法，结合构型基元分析（motif-resolved analysis），对纤锌矿ScAlN合金中的短程有序及其对铁电翻转势垒的影响进行系统研究。

Result: ScAlN在原子尺度上形成了强各向异性的短程有序（SRO），抑制了面内Sc–N–Sc构型并增强了沿极轴c方向的柱状混合阳离子链，打破了传统随机合金模型的假设。SRO在较宽的组分范围内系统性地提高了本征翻转势垒。柱状Sc–N–Al–N–Sc构型的数量被识别为解释不同局域有序构型间势垒变化的主要结构描述符。

Conclusion: 各向异性短程有序（SRO）可作为独立于组分的自由度来调控铁电翻转行为，揭示了局域化学有序如何与极性半导体晶格的对称性区分方向耦合以改变功能性质。该发现为在不改变合金组分的前提下定制翻转势垒的SRO工程（SRO engineering）奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: Ferroelectric switching in wurtzite alloys is typically understood in terms of composition, strain, defects, and interfaces, while local chemical order is often neglected or treated as a secondary perturbation. Here we show that short-range order (SRO) is a previously overlooked microscopic variable that substantially influences the intrinsic switching barrier. Using first-principles canonical sampling, we find that wurtzite ScAlN develops a robust, highly anisotropic SRO that challenges the conventional random-alloy picture. This ordering suppresses in-plane Sc--N--Sc motifs while enhancing columnar mixed-cation chains along the polar $c$ axis, reflecting the symmetry-distinct polar and basal directions of the wurtzite lattice and reorganizing its polar connectivity. Relative to random-alloy structures, SRO systematically increases the intrinsic switching barrier across a broad composition range. Motif-resolved analysis further identifies the population of columnar Sc--N--Al--N--Sc motifs as the primary structural descriptor underlying switching-barrier variations among configurations with different local order. These results establish anisotropic SRO as an independent degree of freedom for tuning ferroelectric switching. More broadly, they reveal how local chemical order can couple to the symmetry-distinct directions of a polar semiconductor lattice to modify functional behavior. Our findings lay a foundation for SRO engineering as a route to tailoring switching barriers without changing alloy composition.

</details>

### [30] [Defect Localization by Stress Anisotropy in Active Nematic Turbulence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17595)
*Sameer Kumar,Manas Khan*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过活性向列相（active nematics）模型研究细胞单层中的集体应力产生机制，发现主应力方向与向列指向矢（nematic director）存在垂直（平行）对齐关系，并识别出湍流状态下由各向异性应力分量定义的特征等值线（isoline），该等值线稳定地定位所有±1/2缺陷（defects），且不随活性强度与类型变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 细胞单层中的集体应力产生（collective stress generation）是调控协调迁移与涌现多细胞动力学（emergent multicellular dynamics）的关键现象过程，但其应力产生机制及相关性质尚需系统研究。

Method: 采用通用活性向列相模型（generic active nematics model）模拟细胞单层，通过分析不同活性强度（activity strengths）下的最大主应力（maximal principal stress）及其与向列指向矢（nematic director）的相关性进行研究。

Result: 主应力在伸展活性（extensile activity）下垂直于向列指向矢对齐，在收缩活性（contractile activity）下平行对齐。在湍流态（turbulent regime）中，识别出一条由各向异性应力分量（anisotropic stress components）定义的等值线（isoline），沿该等值线所有±1/2缺陷（包括向列缺陷与应力缺陷）均被局域化，且该特征在活性大小和类型变化下保持鲁棒。

Conclusion: 这些发现为探测汇合细胞层（confluent cell layers）的力学与流变学性质提供了新路径，尤其是在应力测量比详细的细胞形状或尺寸表征更易获取的情况下。

Abstract: Collective stress generation in cellular monolayers is a key phenomenological process governing coordinated migration and emergent multicellular dynamics. We employ a generic active nematics model to investigate stress generation and its associated properties. By analyzing the maximal principal stress and its correlation with the nematic director across different activity strengths, we find that the principal stress aligns perpendicular (parallel) to the nematic director for extensile (contractile) activity. In the turbulent regime, we identify a distinct isoline derived from anisotropic stress components along which all $\pm 1/2$ defects (both nematic and stress) are localized. This feature is robust and remains unchanged with variations in both the magnitude and nature (extensile or contractile) of activity. Our findings provide a new route to probe the mechanical and rheological properties of confluent cell layers, where stress measurements are more accessible than detailed cell shape or size characterization.

</details>


### [31] [Using fast-reactive crosslinkers to modulate the internal structure of thermoresponsive microgels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17701)
*Ballin Elisa,Brasili Francesco,Sztucki Michael,Rovigatti Lorenzo,Sennato Simona,Zaccarelli Emanuela*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过实验（动态光散射、小角X射线散射）和单体分辨数值模拟，系统研究了表面活性剂和交联剂含量如何调控聚（N-异丙基丙烯酰胺）（PNIPAM）微凝胶的内部结构，揭示了表面活性剂对星形微凝胶结构的关键作用，并建立了合成-结构之间的直接关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解聚（N-异丙基丙烯酰胺）（PNIPAM）微凝胶的内部结构——即当标准交联剂BIS被EGDMA替换时从模糊球（fuzzy-sphere）结构转变为星形（star-like）结构——如何受到表面活性剂和交联剂含量的调控，从而为软星形微凝胶的理性设计提供指导。

Method: 采用动态光散射（Dynamic Light Scattering, DLS）、小角X射线散射（Small-angle X-ray Scattering, SAXS）和单体分辨数值模拟（monomer-resolved numerical simulations），系统考察表面活性剂与交联剂含量对微凝胶内部结构的影响。

Result: 表面活性剂是获得星形微凝胶结构的关键；当EGDMA浓度超过某一阈值时，微凝胶结构从星形区（star-like regime）转变为以核为主导的结构（core-dominated structure）。单体分辨模拟揭示了表面活性剂在EGDMA交联与BIS交联微凝胶中的作用差异。

Conclusion: 建立了直接的合成-结构关系（synthesis-structure relationship），为具有超软相互作用（ultra-soft interactions）的软星形微凝胶的理性设计提供了明确指导，并加强了微凝胶与模型星形聚合物（model star polymers）之间的联系。

Abstract: The internal architecture of poly(N-isopropylacrylamide) (PNIPAM) microgels, which switches from fuzzy-sphere to star-like when the standard N,N'-methylenebis(acrylamide) (BIS) crosslinker is replaced with ethylene glycol dimethacrylate (EGDMA), critically determines their interactions and swelling behavior. Here, we systematically investigate the role of the surfactant and crosslinker content in modulating the internal structure of the microgels using Dynamic Light Scattering, Small-angle X-ray Scattering and monomer-resolved numerical simulations. We reveal that the presence of the surfactant is crucial for obtaining the star-like architecture, and that the transition from the star-like regime to a more core-dominated structure occurs above a threshold EGDMA concentration. Monomer-resolved simulations capture how the role of surfactant differs between EGDMA-crosslinked and BIS-crosslinked microgels. Our findings establish a direct synthesis-structure relationship, providing a clear guidance for the rational design of soft, star-like microgels with ultra-soft interactions, strenghtening the connection between microgels and model star polymers.

### [32] [Electronic access to glass transition in supercooled ionic liquids using ambipolar transistor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17763)
*Tanima Kundu,Rahul Paramanik,Aishee Saha,Shibnath Mandal,Antarik Sarkar,Bipul Karmakar,Subhadeep Datta*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文利用双极性PdSe₂场效应晶体管作为电学探针，在器件运行环境中解析了脆性离子玻璃形成体中与离子种类相关的弛豫动力学，并半定量推断了流变学参数。通过转移曲线滞后和电流瞬态的温度演化，观察到非阿伦尼乌斯（non-Arrhenius）脆性减慢行为，并利用电学可测量量 p_eq(T) 量化了可弛豫迁移离子的比例，从而追踪了动态平衡液体区域在玻璃化转变过程中的连续缩小。该方法能够在传统流变学不适用的固态器件架构中实现粘度的温度依赖性标度和特征温度的提取。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过冷液体在接近玻璃态停滞（glassy arrest）时的弛豫动力学是集成电子架构中的一个核心挑战，因为传统流变学方法在此类环境中不相容。因此，需要开发一种能够在器件内部环境中直接探测离子弛豫动力学并推断流变学参数的新型电学方法。

Method: 采用双极性PdSe₂场效应晶体管（field-effect transistor）作为电学探针，测量离子栅极脉冲下的转移曲线滞后（transfer curve hysteresis）和时域电流瞬态（time-resolved current transients）随温度的变化。引入电学可测量量 p_eq(T)，定义为在实验时间尺度内能够弛豫的迁移离子比例，用于追踪动态平衡液体区域的尺寸变化。

Result: 温度降低时，p_eq(T) 急剧下降，表明移动离子区域碎裂为逾渗分形团簇（percolating fractal clusters），符合脆性玻璃形成体中组态熵（configurational entropy）减少的预期。该方法成功实现了粘度的温度依赖性标度，并提取了标志遍历-非遍历交叉（ergodic-to-nonergodic crossover）的特征温度。此外，离子液体的聚合物受限（polymer confinement）会使这些特征温度升高，表明方法对聚合物基体施加的结构约束具有敏感性。

Conclusion: 该电学探针方法能够在传统流变学不可行的固态器件架构中半定量地推断离子玻璃形成体的弛豫动力学和流变学参数，为集成电子环境下玻璃态动力学研究提供了新途径。该方法对聚合物约束的敏感性进一步扩展了其在复杂结构环境中的应用潜力。

Abstract: Relaxation dynamics of supercooled liquids approaching glassy arrest remain a central challenge in integrated electronic architectures, where conventional rheometry becomes incompatible. Here, we demonstrate that an ambipolar PdSe$_2$ field-effect transistor functions as an electrical probe capable of resolving ion-specific relaxation dynamics in fragile ionic glass formers and semiquantitatively inferring rheological parameters within an operating device environment. Temperature evolution of the transfer curve hysteresis and time-resolved current transients under ionic-gate pulse reveal a non-Arrhenius fragile slowdown. We track the continuous reduction of dynamically equilibrated liquid regions approaching the glass transition through an electrically accessible quantity $p_\text{eq}(T)$, quantifying the fraction of the mobile ions able to relax within the experimental timescale. Upon cooling, $p_\text{eq}$ collapses sharply as mobile regions fragment into percolating fractal clusters, consistent with a reduction of configurational entropy predicted for fragile glass formers. This approach enables temperature-dependent scaling of viscosity and extraction of characteristic temperatures marking the ergodic-to-nonergodic crossover, within a solid-state device architecture where conventional rheological characterization is inapplicable. Further, polymer confinement of the ionic liquid shifts these characteristic temperatures upward, demonstrating the sensitivity of this method to structural constraints imposed by the polymer matrix.

</details>


### [33] [Dynamical properties of ab initio water from machine-learning potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18163)
*P. Montero de Hijes,L. Neubeck,G. Kresse,C. Dellago*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究使用机器学习原子间势（machine-learning interatomic potentials）评估了多种密度泛函（density functionals）对液态水动力学性质的预测能力。通过比较时间相关函数（time-correlation functions）和长期动力学系数，发现RPBE-D3/zd泛函与实验数据整体吻合最佳，并在宽温-压范围内对该泛函进行了进一步验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）被广泛用于水的模拟，但不同泛函对液态水动力学性质的预测差异尚不明确。本文旨在系统评估多种泛函的动力学表现，并寻找与实验最一致的泛函。

Method: 使用MACE模型针对SCAN、RPBE-D3/zd、revPBE-D3/zd、revPBE0-D3/BJ、PBE0-D3/zd和PBE0-D3/BJ六种泛函训练机器学习原子间势（machine-learning interatomic potentials）；通过时间相关函数（time-correlation functions）比较平动、转动和粘性动力学；对表现最佳的RPBE-D3/zd使用Behler–Parrinello神经网络势（Behler–Parrinello neural-network potential）在宽温度、密度和压力范围内进行验证。

Result: 扩散系数、二阶取向弛豫时间（second-rank orientational relaxation time）和剪切粘度在不同泛函间表现出系统性差异。标准化至各泛函的熔化温度后，动力学观测值的离散程度降低。RPBE-D3/zd整体与实验吻合最佳，该模型能再现扩散系数的大小和反常压力依赖性，提供较好的粘度值，并捕捉转动弛豫时间的温度依赖性。

Conclusion: 在不同密度泛函中，RPBE-D3/zd对液态水动力学性质的预测最接近实验结果，且在更广泛的温度-压力条件下表现稳定，适合用于液态水的动力学模拟。

Abstract: We assess the dynamical properties of liquid water predicted by several density functionals using machine-learning interatomic potentials. MACE models were trained for SCAN, RPBE-D3/zd, revPBE-D3/zd, revPBE0-D3/BJ, PBE0-D3/zd, and PBE0-D3/BJ using previously reported ab initio datasets. We compare translational, rotational, and viscous dynamics through time-correlation functions, which resolve relaxation processes across different timescales, and through the corresponding long-time kinetic coefficients. The diffusion coefficient, second-rank orientational relaxation time, and shear viscosity reveal systematic differences among functionals. Part of these differences can be rationalized as shifts along the phase diagram, as comparisons relative to each functionals melting temperature reduce the spread in the dynamical observables. Among the functionals considered, RPBE-D3/zd provides the best overall agreement with experiment. We therefore perform a broader validation of RPBE-D3/zd using a Behler--Parrinello neural-network potential over a wide range of temperatures, densities, and pressures. The model reproduces the magnitude and anomalous pressure dependence of the diffusion coefficient, gives generally good viscosities, and captures the temperature dependence of the rotational relaxation time.

### [34] [Vector peakon equations and isospectral flows in Clifford algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17238)
*Andrew N. W. Hone,Vladimir S. Novikov,Jacek Szmigielski*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类定义在克利福德代数（Clifford algebra）上的可积偏微分方程组（PDEs），该方程组可视为带有正交对称性的Camassa–Holm方程的向量扰动。文中分析了双分量情形下的行波解、可积扰动分类，以及任意分量数下的短脉冲极限与测度值解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从克利福德代数（Clifford algebra）中的谱问题出发，研究一类可积的耦合PDE系统，该系统可作为Camassa–Holm方程（Camassa–Holm equation）的向量扰动，并保留正交对称性（orthogonal symmetry）。

Method: 利用互逆变换（reciprocal transformation）将耦合PDE系统与Hirota–Satsuma系统（Hirota–Satsuma system）的对称性联系起来，进而证明双分量情形下的行波解对应一个具有两个自由度的Liouville可积哈密顿系统（Liouville integrable Hamiltonian system）。

Result: 在双分量情形下，展示了行波解与Liouville可积哈密顿系统的对应关系；完成了所有可积双分量Camassa–Holm扰动的对称性分类（symmetry classification），发现除了已知的耦合2CH系统及Miura变换（Miura transformation）相关的方程外，还获得了一个此前未见报道的新系统。在任意分量数下，研究了短脉冲（高频率）极限，其极限动力学由向量值Hunter–Saxton型系统（vector-valued Hunter-Saxton type system）支配。

Conclusion: 对于任意分量数d的情形，进一步分析了与该向量值Hunter–Saxton型系统相关的测度值（弱）解（measure-valued (weak) solutions）。

Abstract: Starting from a spectral problem posed in a Clifford algebra with $d$ generators and Euclidean signature, we study an integrable, coupled system of PDEs that can be viewed as a vector perturbation of the Camassa--Holm equation with residual orthogonal symmetry. In the two-component case $d=2$, we show that the travelling wave solutions correspond to a Liouville integrable Hamiltonian system with two degrees of freedom, making use of a reciprocal transformation linking the coupled PDEs to a symmetry of the Hirota--Satsuma system. We also present a symmetry classification of all integrable two-component perturbations of Camassa--Holm, and find that besides the $d=2$ system analyzed here, the coupled 2CH system studied by Olver and Rosenau (as well as by Chen, Liu and Zhang, and Falqui), and equations related to either of those systems by Miura transformations, we also obtain a new system that (to the best of our knowledge) has not been reported previously. For the case of an arbitrary number of components $d$, we additionally investigate the short-pulse (high-frequency) regime, in which the limiting dynamics are governed by a vector-valued Hunter-Saxton type system. Furthermore, we provide a detailed analysis of the corresponding measure-valued (weak) solutions associated with this system.

</details>

### [35] [Superconductivity from emergent dipolar interactions in a fractionalized Fermi liquid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17159)
*Mina-Lou Schleith,Arthur Bril,Nick Bultinck*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文基于自旋-费米子模型或 Hertz-Millis 理论，发展了一种描述分数量子化费米液体（fractionalized Fermi liquid）向 d_{x^2-y^2} 超导态转变的理论，揭示了由自旋子（spinon）和荷子（chargon）束缚态构成的掺杂电子通过投影平移对称性产生偶极排斥作用，进而在反铁磁波矢处诱导 d 波配对的微观机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解分数量子化费米液体向 d 波超导态的转变机制，特别是在半满态上轻微电子掺杂的情形下，探索超导配对的微观起源。

Method: 从描述电子耦合反铁磁（anti-ferromagnetic）自旋涨落的自旋-费米子模型或 Hertz-Millis 理论出发，将掺杂电子视为自旋子-荷子束缚态，分析其在 U(1) 规范对称性下的中性特征和偶极两体相互作用（dipolar two-body potential），并利用平移对称性（translation symmetry）在自旋子和荷子上的投影作用推导相互作用傅里叶分量的峰值位置。

Result: 偶极排斥相互作用的傅里叶分量在反铁磁波矢处达到峰值，从而为分数量子化金属（fractionalized metal）中的 d_{x^2-y^2} 配对提供了稳健的微观机制。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了一种由分数量子化费米液体通过投影平移对称性驱动 d 波超导的理论路径，为强关联电子体系中的非常规超导机制提供了新的微观理解。

Abstract: Starting from the spin-fermion model or Hertz-Millis theory describing electrons coupled to anti-ferromagnetic spin fluctuations we develop a theory to describe the transition from a fractionalized Fermi liquid into a $d_{x^2-y^2}$ superconductor. We focus on small electron doping on top of the half-filled state. The doped electrons enter the system as spinon-chargon bound states, which form a small, reconstructed Fermi surface. The bound states are neutral under the emergent U(1) gauge symmetry of the fractionalized Fermi liquid, but interact via a dipolar two-body potential. We show that because of the projective action of translation symmetry on the spinons and chargons, the Fourier components of this repulsive dipolar interaction are peaked at the anti-ferromagnetic wave vector, thereby providing a robust microscopic mechanism for $d_{x^2-y^2}$ pairing in a fractionalized metal.

### [36] [Hybrid Ferromagnet-SNSPDs: Single photon induced order-to-disorder transition in ferromagnets coupled to thin film superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17177)
*Leif Bauer,Daien He,Sathwik Bharadwaj,Zubin Jacob*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于铁磁/超导双层膜中混合相变的涡旋工程方法，将中波和长波红外单光子探测器的工作温度从0.08-0.9K提升至3.25-3.75K，从而显著降低对复杂低温冷却系统的依赖。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中波和长波红外单光子探测器在光谱学、遥感、系外行星探测和自由空间量子通信等领域具有重要应用前景，但现有器件需要工作在极低温度（0.08-0.9K）以降低暗噪声，必须依赖稀释制冷机或³He制冷等先进低温技术，严重限制了实际应用。

Method: 提出一种基于铁磁体/超导体双层膜中混合相变的涡旋工程（vortex-engineering）方法：铁磁层产生的局域磁场抑制超导层中的涡旋穿越以降低暗噪声；当单个光子入射时，光子诱导的热点（hotspot）引发铁磁层中有序-无序相变，进而触发超导层中的涡旋诱导相变。通过调控铁磁层的居里温度（Curie temperature）使其接近器件工作温度，可在更高工作温度下实现单光子灵敏度。

Result: 预测在中波/长波红外波段（3–14 μm）的工作温度可提升至3.25–3.75K。

Conclusion: 该方法可使红外单光子探测器工作温度显著升高，从而能够采用更简单的冷却系统，有望推动相关应用的发展。

Abstract: The development of midwave and longwave infrared single photon detectors is crucial for their emerging applications in spectroscopy, remote sensing, exoplanet detection, and free space quantum communications. However, existing sensors need to be operated at extremely low temperatures (0.08-0.9K) to reduce dark noise and hence require the use of advanced cryogenics such as dilution refrigerators or $^3$He cryogens, significantly limiting applications. Here we propose a vortex-engineering approach based on a hybrid phase transition in a ferromagnet/superconductor bilayer to increase the operating temperature of infrared single photon detectors up to 3.75K. We show that the introduction of a ferromagnetic layer produces a local magnetic field which impedes vortex crossing in the superconductor, reducing dark noise. When a single photon is incident, the photon-induced hotspot causes an order-to-disorder transition in the ferromagnet, leading to a vortex-induced phase transition in the superconducting layer. By engineering the ferromagnet's Curie temperature to be close to the device's operating temperature, single photon sensitivity can be achieved at increased operating temperatures. We predict at midwave/longwave infrared wavelengths (3-14$μ$m) the operating temperature can be raised to 3.25-3.75K, enabling significantly simpler cooling systems.

### [37] [How twist angle inhomogeneity masks the BKT transition and the order parameter symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17191)
*Ilaria Maccari,Louk Rademaker,Giulia Venditti*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文通过弹性理论和随机阻抗网络模型，论证了摩尔系统（moiré systems）中由于扭转角不均匀性导致的空间关联无序（spatially correlated disorder）会显著改变二维超导体的BKT转变（BKT transition）行为，使其退化为渗流转变（percolative transition），并掩盖节状（nodal）与完全能隙（gapped）序参量对称性之间的区别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维超导体（如扭曲多层石墨烯）理论上应表现出BKT转变（BKT transition），且超流刚度（superfluid stiffness）的温度依赖性可用于区分节状（nodal）与有能隙（gapped）序参量对称性。然而，空间关联无序（spatially correlated disorder）会从根本上改变这一图景，而这种关联无序在摩尔系统（moiré systems）中因扭转角不均匀性而自然存在，亟需理论建模来阐明其影响。

Method: 采用弹性理论（elasticity theory）对摩尔系统中的扭转角不均匀性进行建模；构建基于局域临界温度（local \(T_c\)）随机涨落的随机阻抗网络（random impedance network），以模拟空间关联无序的有效作用。

Result: 有限频率电导率（finite-frequency conductance）揭示出一个被抹平的渗流转变（percolative transition），而非BKT转变（BKT transition）。在低温下，无序可以有效掩盖节状（nodal）与完全能隙（fully gapped）超导序参量之间的区别。

Conclusion: 提出电导率的实部（real part of the conductivity）可作为关键诊断可观测量，用于探测关联无序（correlated disorder）在二维超导体中的实际影响。

Abstract: Two-dimensional superconductors, including twisted multilayer graphene, should exhibit a BKT transition, and the $T$-dependence of the superfluid stiffness should distinguish between nodal or gapped order parameter symmetries. However, this picture dramatically changes when spatially correlated disorder is taken into account. Such correlations naturally arise in moiré systems due to twist angle inhomogeneities, which we model using elasticity theory. Using a random impedance network based on realistic disorder in the local $T_c$, we show that the finite-frequency conductance reveals a smeared percolative transition instead of a BKT transition. At low temperatures, the disorder can effectively obscure the distinction between nodal and fully gapped superconducting order parameters. We propose that the real part of the conductivity can be used as a key diagnostic observable to probe the relevance of correlated disorder.

### [38] [Tunable Superconductivity in 1313-La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$: Suppressed under Compression and Possible $s^{\pm}$ Pairing under Tension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17273)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受近期1313-La₃Ni₂O₇镍酸盐薄膜（nickelate thin films）研究进展的启发（Nie et al., Nature 652, 628 (2026)），旨在系统探究压缩应变（compressive strain）和拉伸应变（tensile strain）对该体系的影响。

Method: 采用随机相位近似（random-phase approximation, RPA）方法，对单层（single-layer, SL）与三层（trilayer, TL）区块间的自掺杂效应（self-doping effects）及配对不稳定性进行分析。

Result: 拉伸应变下，TL子系统中出现稳健的s±波配对态（s±-wave pairing state），其Γ点的小电子型σ口袋与M点的小空穴型γ口袋之间存在符号反转，两者由接近(π,π)的波矢连接；超导性需要优化尺寸的γ口袋，过大的γ口袋会抑制配对形成。

Conclusion: 预测了1313-La₃Ni₂O₇中存在应变依赖的电子重构（strain-dependent electronic reconstruction），并为常压条件下工程化超导性提供了指导原则。

Abstract: Motivated by recent progress in the 1313-La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ nickelate thin films (Nie et al., Nature {\bf 652}, 628 (2026)), we systematically investigate the effects of both compressive and tensile strain in this system. Self-doping effects between the single-layer (SL) and trilayer (TL) blocks are observed in our studies in both cases, but are most pronounced under tensile strain. We find that superconductivity is unlikely to emerge in the 1313 film on the LSAO substrate even with further hole doping. Remarkably, within the random-phase approximation, under {\it tensile} strain, a robust $s^{\pm}$-wave pairing state emerges in the TL subsystem with sign changes between the small electron-like $σ$ pocket at the $Γ$ point and the small hole-like $γ$ pocket at the M point. These pockets are connected by a wave vector close to $(π,π)$. Our calculations also suggest that superconductivity in 1313-LNO requires an optimally sized $γ$ pocket, because an oversized $γ$ pocket suppresses pairing formation. Overall, our results predict strain-dependent electronic reconstruction in 1313-La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ and provide guiding principles for engineering superconductivity under ambient pressure conditions.

### [39] [Distinguishing Majorana zero modes from trivial defect states on the surface of the iron-based superconductor Fe(Te,Se)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17499)
*Dongfei Wang,Jon Ortuzar,Freek Massee,Ruidan Zhong,Genda Gu,Wende Xiao,Yugui Yao,Roland Wiesendanger*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过自旋极化扫描隧道谱（spin-polarized scanning tunneling spectroscopy）对铁基超导体Fe(Te,Se)表面的局域态进行研究，发现结构缺陷上的近零能局域态本质上是拓扑平庸的Yu-Shiba-Rusinov态，而非马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero modes），强调了自旋分辨测量在鉴别马约拉纳零模中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁基超导体Fe(Te,Se)被认为是本征拓扑超导体（intrinsic topological superconductor），可能承载遵循非阿贝尔交换统计（non-Abelian exchange statistics）的马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero modes），但其表面缺陷产生的近零能局域态可能被误判，因此需要更严格的验证手段来区分真伪马约拉纳态。

Method: 采用自旋极化扫描隧道谱（spin-polarized scanning tunneling spectroscopy）技术，对Fe(Te,Se)表面的多种结构缺陷（包括台阶边缘和线缺陷）进行空间分辨和磁场依赖的自旋分辨隧穿谱分析。

Result: 实验发现，结构缺陷（台阶边缘和线缺陷）上的近零能局域态源自拓扑平庸的Yu-Shiba-Rusinov态（Yu-Shiba-Rusinov states）。同时，在无表面缺陷区域也观测到零能束缚态（zero-energy bound states），但结合空间分布和磁场依赖的自旋分辨谱分析，这些零能态无法归因于马约拉纳束缚态（Majorana bound states）。

Conclusion: 这些发现强调了在寻找马约拉纳零模时，对低能态进行自旋依赖研究（spin-dependent studies）的重要性和必要性，传统的非自旋分辨测量可能因缺陷诱导的平庸态而产生误判。

Abstract: Majorana zero modes, which obey non-Abelian exchange statistics, are promising candidates for topological quantum computation due to their robustness against environmental perturbations. The iron-based superconductor Fe(Te,Se) has been identified as an intrinsic topological superconductor, possibly hosting Majorana zero modes. In this paper, we report the observation of near-zero-energy localized states at multiple structural defects on the Fe(Te,Se) surface, which could be misidentified as Majorana zero modes without additional verification. By using spin-polarized scanning tunneling spectroscopy, we demonstrate that the near-zero-energy localized states on step edges and line defects originate from topologically trivial Yu-Shiba-Rusinov states. In addition, zero-energy bound states are also observed for regions without surface defects. A combined spatial and magnetic field dependent analysis of the spin-resolved tunneling spectra in these regions reveals that this type of zero-energy states cannot be attributed to the presence of Majorana bound states. These findings emphasize the importance of spin-dependent studies of low-energy states for pursuing Majorana zero modes.

### [40] [Graphene Josephson diodes from inherent asymmetric disorder](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17673)
*Ivan Villani,Luca Chirolli,Matteo Carrega,Alessandro Crippa,Elia Strambini,Francesco Giazotto,Vaidotas Miseikis,Camilla Coletti,Fabio Beltram,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Stefan Heun,Sergio Pezzini*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文展示石墨烯约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）可实现超过20%的超流整流效率，在毫特斯拉量级的垂直磁场下发生，并在夫琅禾费干涉图样（Fraunhofer interference pattern）节点附近增强。理论模型指出长程散射势（long-range scattering potential）是导致超流整流的对称性破缺机制，且清洁二维系统中不可避免的残余无序足以促成该效应。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 实验上对石墨烯约瑟夫森结施加毫特斯拉量级的垂直面外磁场（out-of-plane magnetic field），并在夫琅禾费干涉图样节点附近测量不同电流方向下的开关电流差异。理论上通过建立包含长程散射势的理论模型，分析了高透明结（highly transparent junction）中超流整流的对称性破缺机制。

Result: 石墨烯约瑟夫森结实现了超过20%的超流整流效率。该效应在施加mT量级的垂直磁场时出现，并在夫琅禾费干涉图样节点附近得到增强。理论模型表明，长程散射势作为对称性破缺机制，在高透明结中导致了超流整流。

Conclusion: 尽管石墨烯本身是超洁净的传输介质，但清洁二维系统中不可避免的残余无序（residual disorder）足以推动超流整流效应。通过外部栅极（external gate）的合理设计，有望实现反转（镜面）对称性的可控剪裁。

Abstract: Josephson diodes are non-reciprocal superconducting devices characterized by different switching currents depending on the current flow direction. They recently attracted considerable theoretical and experimental attention, in view of their possible application as rectifying elements in the field of superconducting electronics, and as probes to investigate symmetry breaking mechanisms in mesoscopic systems. In this work, we show that graphene Josephson junctions provide rectification of supercurrent with an efficiency exceeding 20%. The effect appears applying a mT out-of-plane magnetic field and is enhanced close to the nodes of the Fraunhofer interference pattern. Our theoretical model identifies long-range scattering potentials in the junction as the symmetry-breaking mechanism, which yields supercurrent rectification in highly transparent junctions. While graphene stands as an ultra-clean transmission medium, our work shows that unavoidable residual disorder in a clean two-dimensional system is sufficient to promote this effect. Tailoring of the inversion (mirror) symmetry breaking could be obtained via proper design of external gates.
