### [41] [AC-flux-driven SQUID diode spectroscopy as a probe of current-phase relations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17704)
*Yuriy Yerin,Iman Askerzade,Alexey Fedorchenko,Ali Gencer,Oleksandr Dobrovolskiy*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出通过交流磁通驱动的非对称直流超导量子干涉仪（dc SQUID）中的二极管效应来探测约瑟夫森结的电流-相位关系（CPR）各次谐波，利用Kapitza型微扰理论和Jacobi–Anger平均方法揭示各谐波被贝塞尔函数调制的特征，并通过数值模拟验证了不同CPR分量在二极管效率中产生独特的弱、稀疏、密集或互调弧图案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 约瑟夫森结的电流-相位关系（current-phase relation, CPR）包含高阶和分数次谐波，能揭示超导态的微观信息，但不同CPR分量在静态干涉图案中几乎相同，且受到器件不对称性、阻尼和动力学效应的干扰，难以明确提取。

Method: 采用两种互补的快速驱动动力学约化方法：针对常规结的Kapitza型微扰理论（Kapitza-type perturbation theory）和针对一般CPR的Jacobi–Anger平均方法（Jacobi–Anger averaging）；结合耦合动力学方程的数值解，分析含$\sin\varphi$、$\sin(\varphi/2)$和$\sin 2\varphi$项（$\varphi$为超导相位差）的CPR，构建二极管效率$\eta(\varphi_{\rm ac},\omega)$的相图。

Result: 交流磁通调制使各CPR谐波被不同的贝塞尔函数（Bessel function）修饰，在二极管效率$\eta(\varphi_{\rm ac},\omega)$中产生特征性信号。不同CPR分量在相图中呈现弱、稀疏、密集或互调弧图案（weak, sparse, dense, or intermodulated arc patterns），且这些图案在过阻尼和欠阻尼（overdamped and underdamped）情况下均保持稳健。

Conclusion: 交流磁通驱动的超导量子干涉仪二极管光谱学（ac-flux-driven SQUID diode spectroscopy）可作为探测拓扑材料、多带系统及其他非常规超导体中电流-相位关系的有效探针。

Abstract: The current-phase relation (CPR) of a Josephson junction encodes microscopic information on superconducting states through higher-order and fractional harmonics. However, their unambiguous extraction is challenging, as different CPR components produce nearly identical static interference patterns that are further obscured by device asymmetries, damping, and dynamical effects. Here, we propose probing individual CPR harmonics via the ac magnetic-flux-driven diode effect in asymmetric dc SQUIDs with unequal junction critical currents. Using two complementary reductions of the fast-driven dynamics -- a Kapitza-type perturbation theory for the conventional junction and a Jacobi--Anger averaging for a general CPR -- we show that ac flux modulation dresses each harmonic with a distinct Bessel function, yielding characteristic signatures in the diode efficiency $η(φ_{\rm ac},ω)$ as a function of ac flux amplitude $φ_{\rm ac}$ and frequency $ω$. We verify and extend these predictions by numerical solutions of the coupled dynamical equations for CPRs containing $\sin\varphi$, $\sin(\varphi/2)$, and $\sin 2\varphi$ terms ($\varphi$: superconducting phase difference), and construct phase diagrams of $η(φ_{\rm ac},ω)$. Distinct CPR components are revealed to produce characteristic weak, sparse, dense, or intermodulated arc patterns that remain robust in both overdamped and underdamped regimes. This suggests ac-flux-driven SQUID diode spectroscopy as a probe of current-phase relations in topological materials, multiband systems, and other unconventional superconductors.

### [42] [AC calorimetric study of magneto-quantum oscillations in anisotropic multiband V$_2$Ga$_5$ superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17750)

TL;DR: 本文利用高灵敏度交流量热法在V₂Ga₅单晶中观测到热容量磁量子振荡（MQO），确认了位于布里渊区Z点附近的γ费米面椭球口袋的体态起源，并精确提取了有效回旋质量、Dingle温度、量子弛豫时间、载流子迁移率和电子平均自由程等关键参数，同时证明了净贝里通量（net Berry flux）在磁场方向旋转下保持不变。

Method: 采用高灵敏度交流量热法（ac calorimetry）对V₂Ga₅单晶进行测量，通过快速傅里叶变换（FFT）解析主导振荡频率，并结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）验证γ口袋的各向异性。

Abstract: Unlike de Haas--van Alphen measurements, heat-capacity magneto-quantum oscillations directly probe the oscillatory bulk quasiparticle density of states. Here, we report the observation of MQOs in V$_2$Ga$_5$ single crystals studied via highly sensitive ac calorimetry. The strongest MQO signal is observed for a magnetic field applied along the vanadium chains, in excellent agreement with de Haas--van Alphen magnetization data. A single dominant frequency of 126.6 T resolved by fast Fourier transform confirms the true bulk origin of the elliptical $γ$ Fermi-surface pocket located near the Z point of the Brillouin zone. The angular dependence of the FFT frequency closely tracks the anisotropy of the $γ$ pocket, as supported by first-principles calculations. Analysis of the temperature- and field-dependent MQO amplitudes allows the precise determination of the effective cyclotron mass, Dingle temperature, quantum relaxation time, carrier mobility, and electron mean free path. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the net Berry flux is invariant with respect to the magnetic-field orientation, as a consequence of a conserved hybridization phase twist within the $γ$ pocket. These findings establish ac calorimetry as a powerful macroscopic probe of topological orbital hybridization in complex intermetallics.

### [43] [Cavity-enhanced superconducting response in an underdoped cuprate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18084)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将欠掺杂YBa₂Cu₃O₇₋δ薄膜置于由半透明金镜构成的可调谐太赫兹腔（terahertz cavity）中，通过温度依赖的太赫兹透射测量获取超导响应，并结合腔耦合相位涨落超导体模型进行理论计算。

Result: 腔体增强了临界温度以下的超导响应，推算出超流权重（superfluid weight）增大；该效应在更小腔长时更为显著，并伴随着超导起始温度（superconducting onset temperature）的上移。

Conclusion: 实验结果与腔增强相位刚度（cavity-enhanced phase stiffness）的解释一致，展示了腔工程在关联电子体系中设计涌现功能（emergent functionalities）的潜力。

Abstract: Superconductors carry electrical current without resistance when paired electrons condense into a coherent macroscopic quantum state. In underdoped cuprates, evidence suggests that pairing-related correlations and superconducting fluctuations can survive above the temperature at which global coherence is lost, pointing to phase fluctuations as a key limitation on superconductivity in this regime. Motivated by recent demonstrations of cavity-modified collective states in quantum materials, we investigate whether superconducting coherence can be stabilized by engineering the electromagnetic environment of the superconductor. We study an underdoped YBa$_2$Cu$_3$O$_{7-δ}$ thin film in a tunable terahertz cavity formed with a semi-transparent gold mirror. From temperature-dependent terahertz transmission measurements, we find that the cavity enhances the superconducting response below the critical temperature, with an increase of the inferred superfluid weight. The effect becomes more pronounced at smaller cavity lengths and is accompanied by an upward shift of the superconducting onset temperature. Calculations based on a cavity-coupled model for phase-fluctuating superconductors capture these trends and support an interpretation in terms of cavity-enhanced phase stiffness. These results showcase the potential of cavity engineering for designing emergent functionalities in correlated systems.

</details>


### [44] [Superconductivity from interband coupling to ferroelectric quantum critical fluctuations in two dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18251)
*Sudip Kumar Saha,Jonathan Ruhman,Avraham Klein*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文为铁电量子临界点附近由有效双声子耦合（effective two-phonon coupling）驱动的超导增强机制建立了量子临界Eliashberg理论（quantum critical Eliashberg theory），发现临界温度$T_c$在二维系统中相比传统BCS理论显著增强，且增强幅度取决于带间能隙（interband gap）的大小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁电量子相变（ferroelectric quantum phase transitions）附近的软临界涨落（soft critical fluctuations）通常具有横向极性特征，导致传统的密度-密度电子-声子耦合（density-density electron-phonon coupling）被强烈抑制，然而众多材料却在铁电性附近表现出增强的超导电性，这一矛盾亟需寻找替代耦合机制并加以解释。

Method: 构建了二维系统在量子临界点（quantum critical point）附近、跨越广泛带间能隙范围的量子临界Eliashberg理论（quantum critical Eliashberg theory），通过分析双声子配对（two-phonon pairing）的红外截止（infrared cutoff）动力学来研究超导增强的机制。

Result: 在大量隙极限下，配对核（pairing kernel）呈现出高阶对数贡献，$T_c$由三次和二次对数项主导而参数式增强；在小带隙区域，配对标度呈现修正的BCS形式，对无量纲耦合常数的逆平方根具有增强的依赖性。二维系统中的$T_c$相比三维系统显著增强，因为前者的红外截止由$T_c$本身设定，而后者由费米能（Fermi energy）设定。

Conclusion: 本文阐明了有效双声子相互作用的独特动力学性质，揭示了二维系统在铁电量子临界点附近超导增强的机制，可能对层状化合物Td-MoTe$_2$和掺杂SrTiO$_3$薄膜等材料具有参考意义。

Abstract: Soft critical fluctuations associated with ferroelectric quantum phase transitions are typically transverse owing to their polar nature. This implies that the conventional density--density electron--phonon coupling to these modes is strongly suppressed, which is puzzling as a variety of materials exhibit enhanced superconductivity in the vicinity of ferroelectricity. An alternative coupling mechanism is an interband ``Stark''-like coupling that connects bands of opposite parity. In the limit where one of the bands is far in energy, these processes generate an effective quadratic (two-phonon) coupling. In contrast, when both bands lie close to the Fermi energy, the resulting interaction develops singular behavior due to the additional gapless electronic states, motivating a detailed study into the dynamics of this effective two-phonon coupling. To this end, we construct the quantum critical Eliashberg theory for a two-dimensional system across a wide range of interband gap magnitudes, near the quantum critical point. We find that the critical temperature $T_c$ is strongly enhanced relative to conventional BCS expectations. In the large-gap limit, the pairing kernel acquires higher-order logarithmic contributions, leading to a parametrically enhanced $T_c$ governed by cubic and quadratic logarithmic terms. In the small-gap regime, the pairing scale exhibits a modified BCS-like form with an enhanced dependence on the inverse square root of the dimensionless coupling constant. The enhancement is due to the dynamics of the two-phonon pairing whose infrared cutoff is set by $T_c$, resulting in a significant enhancement of superconductivity compared to three-dimensional systems, where it is set by the Fermi energy. Our results elucidate the unique dynamical properties of effective two-phonon interactions, and may be relevant to layered compounds like Td-MoTe$_2$ and doped SrTiO$_3$ membranes.

</details>

### [45] [Optimized filtering for pulse-shape based pile-up rejection applied to $0νββ$ search with $^{100}$Mo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17948)
*V. Berest,M. Buchynska,P. Carniti,A. Giuliani,C. Gotti,H. Khalife,P. Loaiza,P. de Marcillac,C. Nones,M. Pageot,E. Olivieri,G. Pessina,D. V. Poda,J. A. Scarpaci,B. Schmidt,A. S. Zolotarova*

TL;DR: 提出了一种用于鉴别堆积事件（pile-up events）的优化数字滤波器（optimized digital filter），可将堆积引起的本底降低31%（在90%效率下），适用于低温量热探测器（cryogenic calorimetric detectors）如CUPID实验中的无中微子双贝塔衰变（neutrinoless double beta decay）搜索。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 堆积事件会扭曲可观测物理量、降低能量分辨率并产生本底（background），在稀有或低计数率过程（如无中微子双贝塔衰变搜索）中构成重大挑战，尤其是CUPID实验中来自100Mo双中微子双贝塔衰变（2νββ）的堆积本底被视为主要本底贡献。

Method: 针对具有已知信号响应（known signal response）和平稳噪声功率谱密度（stationary noise power spectral density）的探测器，推导了一种优化的数字滤波器（optimized digital filter），用于堆积事件的鉴别（discrimination）。

Result: 在90%效率下，该滤波器将堆积诱导的本底相比参考文献（Eur. Phys. J. C 83(5), 373 (2023)）中的参考方法降低了31%。

Conclusion: 虽然讨论基于低温量热探测器，但所提出的概念和方法广泛适用于多种探测器技术和实验场景。

Abstract: Pile-up events, arising from the partial or complete temporal overlap of distinct signals, represent a major challenge in many areas of experimental physics where rare or low-rate processes are targeted. If not properly identified, pile-up can distort reconstructed observables, degrade energy resolution, and generate backgrounds that mimic genuine events of interest. This work presents an algorithm to obtain an optimized digital filter for the discrimination of pile-up events for detectors with known signal response and stationary noise power spectral density. It is developed in the context of the search for neutrinoless double beta decay with cryogenic Li$_{2}$$^{100}$MoO$_4$ detectors like CUPID, where pile-up induced background from $^{100}$Mo $2νββ$ is expected to be the leading background contribution. For this application, the new filter discriminant reduces the pile-up induced background (at 90% efficiency) by 31%, compared to an analysis with a reference method previously presented in Eur. Phys. J. C 83(5), 373 (2023). While the discussion is grounded in cryogenic calorimetric detectors, the concepts and methods described are broadly applicable to a wide class of detector technologies and experimental contexts.

### [46] [Coupled-Mode Equations with Arbitrary Mode Combinations for Kinetic-Inductance Superconducting Traveling-Wave Parametric Devices: Theory and Experimental Validation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17264)
*F. Patricio Mena,Camilo Espinoza,Ryan O. Berriel,Ricardo Finger,David J. Thoen*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了耦合模方程（coupled-mode equations, CMEs）在行波超导参量放大器中的应用，提出了一个系统地包含损耗（losses）的修正公式，并通过独立实验测量非线性参数 $I'_*$ 与线性仿真相结合，实现了无自由参数的理论验证，发现 $I'_* \approx 27$ mA 与理论解对电流（depairing current）成比例而非与器件的临界电流（critical current）一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 耦合模方程（CMEs）在非线性光学参量过程中已被证明非常成功，并已推广至微波超导参量放大器与倍频器。然而，在微波频段，原有假设部分失效且损耗作用更为显著，因此需要重新审视并修正 CME 公式以准确描述行波超导放大器。

Method: 作者重新推导了包含损耗的 CME 框架，使其能系统性地适用于任意行波组合；随后利用超导共面波导（coplanar waveguide, CPW）人工传输线，通过独立实验测定非线性参数 $I'_*$，并结合线性特性的仿真，实现了无自由参数的公式验证。

Result: 非线性参数 $I'_*$ 测定为约 27 mA，该值意外地与理论解对电流（depairing current）成比例，而非与更小的器件临界电流（critical current）成比例。多谐波产生（multiple-harmonic generation）的测量结果与理论预测高度一致。若不恰当处理损耗及不需要的谐波和交调产物，器件性能会显著偏离理想情况。

Conclusion: 该研究为行波超导参量放大器的设计提供了更准确的建模方法，并指出 $I'_* \gg I_C$ 这一发现对器件设计具有直接的重要影响。

Abstract: The coupled-mode equations (CMEs) have proven very successful in describing parametric processes in nonlinear optics. More recently, the same formulation has been used to model microwave superconducting parametric amplifiers and frequency multipliers. However, when applied to the microwave regime, not all assumptions remain valid and losses play a more dramatic role. Here, we revisit the CMEs applied to traveling-wave superconducting amplifiers to include losses and provide a formulation that enables their systematic derivation for any combination of traveling waves. As examples, we discuss the impact of unwanted harmonics and intermodulation products on parametric amplification, as well as harmonic generation. We verify that, if not properly accounted for, device performance can deviate considerably from the ideal case. Furthermore, using a superconducting CPW-based artificial transmission line and combining an independent experimental determination of its nonlinear parameter $I'_*$ with simulations of its linear properties, we obtain a parameter-free validation of this formulation. The nonlinear parameter was determined to be $I'_* \approx 27$ mA which, surprisingly, scales with the theoretical depairing current and not with the much smaller critical current of the device. For the validation, we measured multiple-harmonic generation and found excellent agreement between theory and experiment. The fact that $I'_* \gg I_C$ has direct implications for device design.

### [47] [Impulsive Hydrodynamic Exfoliation into Monolayer Graphene and Nanofragments by Transonic Flow Focusing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17083)
*A. Ponce-Torres,A. Rubio-González,J. M. Montanero,M. A. Herrada,F. J. Galindo-Rosales*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文提出利用跨音速流动聚焦（Transonic Flow Focusing, TFF）技术，在无表面活性剂或氧化化学处理条件下，通过纯机械自上而下（top-down）方式从石墨烯纳米片悬浮液中高效剥离出单层石墨烯薄片（横向尺寸约300-400 nm）和单层石墨烯纳米碎片（横向尺寸约10-15 nm，与量子点兼容），单层产率在异丙醇中超过99%、在纯水中达到92.9%。理论分析表明，在弯月面-射流过渡区的微秒级停留时间内，剪切和拉伸应变率高达10^6 s^{-1}，粘性功率密度达10^{10} W/m^3。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有石墨烯剥离方法常需添加表面活性剂或使用氧化化学处理，工艺复杂且可能引入杂质。本文旨在探索一种纯机械、溶剂适应性广且高效剥离石墨烯纳米材料的新方法。

Method: 采用跨音速流动聚焦（TFF）技术将液体悬浮液聚焦为高速微米级射流，在受限且无接触的区域中施加极高的剪切和拉伸应力；实验以异丙醇和纯水为溶剂处理石墨烯纳米片悬浮液，并结合理论分析计算弯月面-射流过渡区的应变率和功率密度。

Result: 单步TFF处理同时获得横向尺寸约300-400 nm的单层石墨烯薄片和约10-15 nm（与量子点兼容）的单层石墨烯纳米碎片。高分辨透射电子显微镜和原子力显微镜显示，单层比例在异丙醇中超过99%，在纯水中达92.9%。理论分析揭示过渡区剪切和拉伸应变率约10^6 s^{-1}，粘性功率密度约10^{10} W/m^3。

Conclusion: TFF技术能够在无需表面活性剂或氧化化学的条件下，以纯机械自上而下（top-down）方式高效剥离出高单层产率的石墨烯纳米材料，且溶剂适应性良好（异丙醇和纯水均适用）。这为二维和零维纳米材料的制备提供了一种绿色、通用的新途径。

Abstract: We propose using Transonic Flow Focusing (TFF) to produce 2D and 0D nanomaterials. This technique focuses liquid suspensions into high-speed micrometer-scale jets, combining extremely high shear and elongational stresses in a confined, contact-free zone. For the Graphene Nanoplatelets suspensions and TFF operating conditions investigated here, the process promoted exfoliation without added surfactants or oxidative chemistry. Both graphene monolayer flakes ($\sim 300-400$ nm in lateral size) and monolayer graphene nanofragments with lateral sizes compatible with quantum dots ($\sim 10-15$ nm) were obtained in a single TFF step using isopropanol and pure water. Our theoretical analysis reveals that, during microsecond residence times at the meniscus-jet transition, shear and extensional stresses of the order of $10^6$ s$^{-1}$ act on the suspended particles, yielding viscous power densities of the order of $10^{10}$ $\mathrm{W/m^{3}}$. High-resolution transmission electron microscopy and atomic force microscopy show that the monolayer fraction exceeded 99\% for isopropanol and 92.9\% for water. These results suggest that TFF can combine solvent versatility with a high monolayer fraction in a purely mechanical top-down process.

### [48] [Exotic magnetism and persistent spin dynamics in a frustrated Jeff = 1/2 triangular lattice antiferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17166)
*M. Barman,K. Jaksetič,M. Pregelj,M. D. Le. P. J. Baker,A. Zorko,P. Khuntia*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本论文通过热力学、非弹性中子散射（INS）和 μSR 实验对三角晶格阻挫磁体 K₃NdTe₂O₉ 进行研究，发现其在 50 mK 以下不存在长程磁有序或自旋冻结，而是表现出持续的量子自旋涨落和奇异磁性，为阻挫稀土三角晶格反铁磁体中的新奇量子态提供了实验平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在赝自旋 J_eff=1/2 稀土三角晶格反铁磁体中，竞争自由度（competing degrees of freedom）、各向异性（anisotropy）以及阻挫（frustration）诱导的强量子涨落之间存在微妙的相互作用，这为实验上实现具有非平庸低能激发的奇异量子态提供了有前景的平台。因此，本文旨在寻找并表征这类材料，以探索其低能自旋动力学行为。

Method: 本文采用了三种实验方法：（1）热力学测量；（2）非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering, INS）；（3）μ 子自旋弛豫（muon spin relaxation, μSR）技术。研究对象为 K₃NdTe₂O₉，其中 Nd³⁺离子构成结构完美的三角晶格，且未检测到位点无序。

Result: 实验发现 Nd³⁺离子形成具有 J_eff=1/2 的 Kramers 二重态基态（Kramers doublet ground state），与第一激发态能隙很大；三角平面内 Nd³⁺离子间的反铁磁交换相互作用约为 0.6 K。零场 μSR 弛豫在 50 mK 下未出现振荡和 1/3 平台，排除了长程磁有序（long-range magnetic ordering）和自旋冻结（spin freezing）。零场 μSR 弛豫率的温度依赖性很好地符合 Orbach 弛豫机制（Orbach relaxation mechanism），表明基态中存在涨落磁矩。

Conclusion: 该材料在 50 mK 以下表现出奇异磁性和持续的自旋动力学，表明这一新型阻挫稀土三角晶格反铁磁家族是实现具有新奇低能激发的非平庸量子态的理想候选体系。

Abstract: The delicate interplay between competing degrees of freedom, anisotropy, and frustration-induced strong quantum fluctuations in pseudospin-$J_{\rm eff}=1/2$ rare-earth triangular-lattice antiferromagnets offers a promising platform for the experimental realization of exotic states with nontrivial low-energy excitations. Here, we present thermodynamic, inelastic neutron scattering (INS), and muon spin relaxation ($μ$SR) investigations of the frustrated magnet K$_3$NdTe$_2$O$9$, in which Nd$^{3+}$ ions constitute a structurally perfect triangular lattice with no detectable site disorder. The experiments reveal the realization of a Kramers doublet ground state with $J{\rm eff}=1/2$ moments, well separated from the first excited state, which interact antiferromagnetically with an exchange interaction of $\sim$0.6 K between the Nd$^{3+}$ moments in the triangular plane. The absence of oscillations and the so-called 1/3 plateau in the zero-field $μ$SR asymmetry down to 50 mK rules out long-range magnetic ordering and spin freezing on the $μ$SR time scale, respectively. The temperature dependence of the zero-field $μ$SR relaxation rate is well described by the Orbach relaxation mechanism, indicating the existence of fluctuating moments in the ground state of this frustrated magnet. Our results demonstrate exotic magnetism and persistent spin dynamics down to 50 mK. These observations establish this new family of frustrated rare-earth triangular-lattice antiferromagnets as a promising venue for the experimental realization of nontrivial quantum states with exotic low-energy excitations.

### [49] [Antisite-disorder driven tuning of magnetic properties and exchange-bias in Nd$_{2-x}$Sr$_{x}$CoMnO$_{6-δ}$ $(0 \leq x \leq 1)$ ($δ\sim 0.5$) double perovskites](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17244)
*Kazi Parvez Islam,Jayjit Kumar Dey,Sourav Chowdhury,Samyabrata Paria,Flora Banerjee,Suryakanta Mishra,Suman Kalyan Samanta,Moritz Hoesch,Robert Dankelman,Indu Dhiman,Debraj Choudhury*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 通过Sr²⁺空穴掺杂，在Nd₂₋ₓSrₓCoMnO₆₋δ双钙钛矿体系中实现了交换偏置（exchange bias, EB）从正常态到反常态的精确调控，并在x=0.75处观察到显著的团簇玻璃行为（cluster-glass behavior）和高达~4 kOe的反常交换偏置（inverse EB），归因于掺杂诱导的结构相变与磁性竞争。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索通过Sr²⁺空穴掺杂调控稀土双钙钛矿体系的交换偏置行为，揭示正常与反常EB状态之间的转变机制，为设计先进磁性材料提供新思路。

Method: 采用中子粉末衍射（neutron powder diffraction）和X射线吸收谱（X-ray absorption spectroscopy）表征晶体结构与元素价态；使用直流（DC）磁化测量和交流（AC）磁化率测量分析磁性能。

Result: 随x增加，体系从B位有序的单斜（P2₁/n）相演变为无序的菱方（R\overline{3}c）相；Co有效价态从+2升至+3，Mn价态基本不变；铁磁性逐渐被抑制；x=0.75时呈现团簇玻璃行为，并在8 K、6 T冷却场下获得~4 kOe的最高EB场；校正小回线效应后确认存在稳健的反常交换偏置。

Conclusion: 掺杂诱导的结构与磁性竞争在调控交换偏置行为中起关键作用，竞争性铁磁-反铁磁及铁磁-玻璃界面是反常EB的物理根源，相关机制与强磁阻挫及稀土4f电子的磁晶各向异性有关。

Abstract: We demonstrate precise control of exchange bias (EB) in the Nd$_{2-x}$Sr$_x$CoMnO$_{6-δ}$ ($0 \leq x \leq 1$) double-perovskite series through Sr$^{2+}$ induced hole doping, unveiling a remarkable transition between normal and inverse EB states. Employing neutron powder diffraction and X-ray absorption spectroscopy, we reveal a structural evolution from a B-site-ordered monoclinic ($P2_1/n$) phase to a disordered rhombohedral ($R\overline{3}c$) phase with increasing $x$, accompanied by a shift in the effective Co valence from +2 toward +3, while the Mn valence remains essentially unchanged. DC magnetization measurements indicate a gradual suppression of ferromagnetism with hole doping, whereas AC susceptibility measurements at $x = 0.75$ reveal pronounced cluster-glass behavior and the highest EB field of $\sim 4$ kOe at 8 K under a 6 T cooling field. After correcting for minor-loop effects, we identify robust inverse EB at $x = 0.75$, persisting even under a cooling field of 6 T. We attribute this phenomenon to competing ferromagnetic--antiferromagnetic and ferromagnetic--glassy interfaces, governed by strong magnetic frustration and the magnetocrystalline anisotropy associated with rare-earth 4$f$ electrons. These findings elucidate the pivotal role of doping-induced structural and magnetic competition in tailoring EB behavior in rare-earth double perovskites, providing new insights for the design of advanced magnetic materials.

</details>


### [50] [II. Exploring the role of the Crystal Electric Field in the vicinity of a Quantum Critical Point](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17305)
*Julian G. Sereni,Ivan Curlik,Slavo Gabani,Mauro Giovannini*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文分析了Yb$T_4M$家族化合物在极低温下的热力学性质，涵盖了从磁性基态到量子临界点（QCP）再到费米液体基态的广泛行为。通过考虑晶体电场（CEF）劈裂改进了Doniach-Lavagna相图，并基于化学掺杂调控，识别出三种基态行为类型，绘制了一个更真实的围绕QCP的相图，其中低能量子涨落主导，比热值在极限低温下不发散而出现明显下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Doniach-Lavagna相图在描述Yb$T_4M$族化合物时存在局限性，未充分考虑晶体电场（CEF）劈裂对基态行为的影响，因此需要改进相图以更准确地描述从磁性基态到费米液体基态之间的量子临界点（QCP）区域。

Method: 以Yb$T_{5-x}M_x$（$T$ = Ni, Cu; $M$ = Cd, Mg, Pd, Au, Zn, Ag）合金为研究对象，以化学掺杂为控制参数，测量极低温下的比热（$C_{4f}/T$）等热力学性质，系统观测基态行为穿过QCP区域的演化过程。

Result: 识别出三种基态行为类型：i) 磁性区域，其双态基态具有极低Kondo温度，在$T_m \leq 1$ K以下出现弱相互作用，比热$C_{4f}/T (T \geq T_q)$呈幂律依赖，$T_q \approx 0.3$ K以下出现重费米子平台；ii) 越过QCP后呈现典型的非费米液体对数温度依赖 $C_{4f}/T \propto \ln(T/T_0)$；iii) 非磁性极限下表现为价涨落系统，Kondo温度$T_K$超过CEF劈裂。

Conclusion: 基于实验数据，可以绘制出一个更真实的围绕QCP的相图。在该相图中，低能量子涨落主导物理场景，$C_{4f}/T$在低温极限下不发散，而是出现明显下降，这与传统理论预期有所不同。

Abstract: Very low temperature thermdynamic properties of the Yb$T_4M$ family of compounds are analyzed in a broad range of behavior including a quantum critical point QCP between magnetic and Fermi-liquid ground states GS. Doniach-Lavagna phase diagram limitations are improved by taking into account crystal electric field CEF splittings. The studied alloys: Yb$T_{5-x}M_x$ (with $T$= Ni, Cu, and $M$= Cd, Mg, Pd, Au, Zn, Ag), allow to gain insight into the evolution of the GS behavior undergoing the QCP region as a function of chemical doping as control parameter. Three types of behaviors are recognized in this system: i) a magnetic one, with weak interactions at $T_m\leq 1$\,K and very low Kondo temperature of their respective doublets GS. Between $T_m$ and $T_q\approx 0.3$\,K, quantum fluctuations start to dominate the scenario with the specific heat $C_{4f}/T(T\geq T_q)$ showing $T$ power law dependencies and a very heavy-fermion {\it plateau} below $T_q$. ii) beyond the QCP the typical non-fermi-liquid logarithmic $T$ dependence: $C_{4f}/T \propto \ln(T/T_0)$ and iii) at the non-magnetic limit, the alloys behave as valence-fluctuation systems with $T_K$ overcoming the CEF splitting. With this experimental information, a more realistic phase diagram can be drawn around the QCP where the scenario is dominated by low lying quantum fluctuations, without $C_{4f}/T|_{Lim T\to 0}$ divergences but a clear drop of its value.

### [51] [Emergent Antiphase Stacking in a Transient Charge Density Wave](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17326)
*Jade Stanton,Gal Orenstein,Ryan A. Duncan,Gilberto A. de la Peña Muñoz,Yijing Huang,Viktor Krapivin,Quynh Le Nguyen,Samuel Teitelbaum,Anisha G. Singh,Roman Mankowsky,Henrik Lemke,Mathias Sander,Yunpei Deng,Christopher Arrell,Ian R. Fisher,David A. Reis,Mariano Trigo*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用红外泵浦-X射线探针散射技术，在自由电子激光器上以高动量和高时间分辨率研究了LaTe₃中光诱导的瞬态电荷密度波（CDW）。研究发现该瞬态CDW具有高度无序性，其有序波矢为(2/7, 0, 0)，与平衡态下的a序和c序截然不同，表明光激发可产生平衡态中不存在的全新量子态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光激发可以在材料中诱导出平衡态无法达到的新型量子态，近期在LaTe₃中观察到的光诱导电荷密度波（charge density wave, CDW）即为一个典型案例。本文旨在深入探究这一瞬态CDW的微观结构特性及其与平衡态CDW的本质区别。

Method: 采用红外泵浦- X射线探针散射（infrared-pump x-ray-probe scattering）技术，在自由电子激光器（free-electron laser）上开展实验，实现了高动量分辨率和高时间分辨率的测量。

Result: 瞬态CDW的布拉格峰在倒易空间中展宽，表明该状态具有高度无序性；其有序波矢位于(2/7, 0, 0)附近，而平衡态的a序和c序分别位于≈(5/7, 0, 0)和(0, 0, 2/7)；瞬态CDW与平衡态a序在常规单胞内两个等效近正方形Te-Te网之间的CDW位移相对相位上存在差异。

Conclusion: 光激发能够产生平衡态中不存在的新奇量子态，瞬态CDW是一种与平衡态CDW在波矢和相对相位上都截然不同的高度无序态；X射线散射技术为揭示此类难以捉摸的微观相提供了有力工具。

Abstract: Photoexcitation can induce novel states in materials that are inaccessible in equilibrium, a recent example being the light-induced charge density wave (CDW) observed in $\text{LaTe}_3$. Here, we investigate this transient CDW using infrared-pump x-ray-probe scattering at a free-electron laser, with high momentum and time resolution. We find that the transient CDW Bragg peak is broad in reciprocal space, indicating a highly disordered state. The ordering wavevector of the transient state is different from the equilibrium orders that develop in this class of materials - the transient peak appears near (2/7, 0, 0) reciprocal lattice units, whereas the equilibrium $a$ order and $c$ order occur at $\approx (5/7, 0, 0)$ and $(0, 0, 2/7)$, respectively. The transient CDW is therefore distinct from the equilibrium $a$ order, differing in the relative phase of the CDW displacement between the two equivalent nearly-square Te-Te nets in the conventional unit cell. Our work highlights how photoexcitation can access states with no equilibrium analog, and how x-ray scattering can provide microscopic insight into such elusive phases.

### [52] [Flat-Band Stoner Instability and Peierls-Phase Origin of the Transdimensional Anomalous Hall Effect in Rhombohedral Graphite](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17535)
*Yang Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出一种微观理论，将九层菱方石墨烯中观测到的"跨维度反常霍尔效应"（TDAHE）归因于平带Stoner不稳定性与Peierls相位隙调制的耦合，并通过自洽Hartree-Fock计算和动力学平均场理论重现了实验观测的关键特征，给出了可检验的理论预言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验上在九层菱方石墨烯（rhombohedral graphite）中观测到了一种新型的"跨维度反常霍尔效应"（transdimensional anomalous Hall effect, TDAHE），即面内和面外磁场均能产生具有滞回特性的霍尔信号，但缺乏对其微观机制的理论解释。

Method: 基于平带Stoner不稳定性（Stoner instability）与Peierls相位隙调制（Peierls-phase gap modulation）的耦合建立微观理论，采用自洽$2N$能带Hartree-Fock计算（Hartree-Fock calculation）求解平均场，并引入二维Ising临界涨落修正，同时利用动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory）验证本征反常霍尔电导的层数无关性。

Result: 理论成功重现了实验观测的反常霍尔电阻$R_{xy}\approx 1.5$ kΩ、临界温度$T_c\approx 1.6$ K及相窗口；完整谷极化（$η\to 1$）发生于平均场临界温度$T_c^{\mathrm{MF}}\approx 2.2$ K以下；预言了谷极化在$N=7$到$N=9$之间的突然出现、新月形费米面锁定在$m=1$向列通道以及跨维度与常规霍尔效应的比值与$η$和$U$无关。

Conclusion: TDAHE的两种霍尔响应由同一序参量$η$（谷极化）承载，因此共享单一$T_c$，该温度由Stoner积$Uρ$主导而对谷间交换作用不敏感；理论不再将交换强度作为可调参数，并给出了多个可实验检验的定量预言。

Abstract: A ``transdimensional'' anomalous Hall effect (TDAHE), where both in-plane ($\Bpar$) and out-of-plane magnetic fields produce hysteretic Hall signals, was recently observed in nine-layer rhombohedral graphite~\cite{Li2026Nature}. We present a microscopic theory attributing the TDAHE to a flat-band Stoner instability coupled to Peierls-phase gap modulation. The flat-band density of states satisfies the Stoner criterion $Uρ(\varepsilon_F) > 1$~\cite{Bultinck2020}, driving a spin-valley-locked ferromagnet whose valley polarization $η$ breaks time-reversal symmetry and generates an intrinsic anomalous Hall conductivity (AHC). The orbital $g$-factor $g_{\mathrm{orb}} = e d_0 v_F (N{-}1)/2 \propto (N{-}1)$ then lets $\Bpar$ modulate the gap, producing the transdimensional response $\propto η$. A self-consistent $2N$-band Hartree-Fock calculation yields complete valley polarization ($η\to 1$) below a mean-field transition $T_c^{\mathrm{MF}} \approx 2.2$~K, reduced by 2D-Ising critical fluctuations to the experimental $T_c \approx 1.6$~K, with $R_{xy} \approx 1.5$~k$Ω$. Because both Hall responses are carried by one order parameter $η$, they share a single $T_c$, as observed; $T_c$ is governed by the Stoner product $Uρ$ and is insensitive to the intervalley exchange, which only gates whether the valley-polarized phase forms, so the exchange strength is not a fitted parameter. Beyond reproducing $R_{xy}$, $T_c$, and the phase window, the theory predicts a sharp onset of valley polarization between $N = 7$ and $N = 9$, a symmetry selection rule fixing the crescent Fermi surface to the $m{=}1$ nematic channel, and a transdimensional-to-conventional Hall ratio $\sigmaPHE/\sigmaAHE^{\mathrm{tot}} = g_{\mathrm{orb}}\Bpar/m$ independent of $η$ and $U$. The $Z$-independence of the intrinsic AHC is verified within dynamical mean-field theory.

TL;DR: 本研究通过比较La₃Ni₂O₇、Nd₃Ni₂O₇和LaNiO₃的Ni 2p与Ni 1s芯能级光电子能谱，揭示了Ni 2p谱与La 3d谱存在严重的能量重叠问题，而深层的Ni 1s芯能级能够提供更清晰的电子激发信息，有助于解析Ruddlesden-Popper系列镍氧化物中电子结构的细微差异。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 对La₃Ni₂O₇、Nd₃Ni₂O₇和LaNiO₃三种镍氧化物同时采集Ni 2p和Ni 1s芯能级的光电子能谱，通过对比分析评估两种芯能级在分辨率上的优劣，并利用深层Ni 1s芯能级来规避表面与重叠干扰。

Result: Ni 2p谱确实受到La 3d谱的严重能量重叠干扰，导致其本征电子激发信息难以区分。相比之下，深层的Ni 1s芯能级（deep Ni 1s core level）能提供一个洁净的视角来观察本征电子激发，并能够分辨出La₃Ni₂O₇、Nd₃Ni₂O₇及LaNiO₃之间电子结构的细微差异。

Conclusion: Ni 1s芯能级光电子能谱是研究强关联Ruddlesden-Popper系列镍氧化物（如Laₙ₊₁NiₙO₃ₙ₊₁）电子结构的有效探针，能够弥补Ni 2p谱因与La 3d重叠而导致的解析困难，在未来对这一体系的电子结构研究中具有重要潜力。

Abstract: We present a comparative Ni core level photoemission study of La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$, Nd$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$, and LaNiO$_3$ using both the Ni $2p$ and the Ni $1s$. We address the challenges in analyzing the widely investigated Ni $2p$ spectra arising from the substantial overlap in energy of the Ni $2p$ with the La $3d$. We show that on the other hand the deep Ni $1s$ core level does provide a clean view on the intrinsic electronic excitations and we highlight its potential to resolve detailed differences in the electronic structure within the strongly correlated Ruddlesden-Popper series La$_{n+1}$Ni$_n$O$_{3n+1}$.

Method: 采用中子衍射（neutron diffraction）和同步辐射X射线衍射（synchrotron X-ray diffraction）实验技术，结合不可约表示（irreducible representation, irrep）分析和对称性分析，研究β-Fe₂O₃中由温度驱动的磁相变。

Using neutron and synchrotron X-ray diffraction, we investigate the temperature-driven magnetic transition in $β$-Fe$_2$O$_3$. A noncollinear antiferromagnetic structure sets in abruptly via activation of irrep $mH_1^{+}$ at the H-point [$\mathbf{k}=(1,1,1)$] together with antitranslation $(1'|\tfrac{1}{2},\tfrac{1}{2},\tfrac{1}{2})$. Below $T_{\mathrm{N}}$, the magnetic cell becomes primitive $(P_I a \bar{3})$, yielding two interpenetrating primitive cubic subcells with inverted moments and non-polar type-IV symmetry. All Fe$^{3+}$-O-Fe$^{3+}$ exchanges are antiferromagnetic, and the bixbyite structure promotes geometric frustration and noncollinear magnetism through coexisting magnetic sublattices with distinct symmetries and easy axes. Its frustration index $f \simeq 7.6$ is among the highest reported for binary magnetic oxides. In $\{111\}$ planes, distorted Fe2O$_6$ octahedra form hexagonal rings interconnected by triangular units. Notably, hexagonal Fe2 rings host a central Fe1 ion with strong Ising-like anisotropy, which could act as a switching element for the rings' magnetic state. These features point to routes for functional design.

TL;DR: 本文报道在中心对称的交替磁体（altermagnet）CoF₂中观测到电偶极和磁偶极禁戒的光学二次谐波产生（SHG），发现该信号源于铁性磁八极矩（ferroic magnetic octupole）这一反铁磁有序参量，并通过偏振分辨SHG实验与对称性分析揭示了交替磁体自旋结构诱发的非线性极化机制。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Altermagnetism as a new concept in condensed matter physics is currently being thoroughly investigated. Despite the absence of macroscopic magnetization, altermagnets host a hidden spin order whose direct detection remains a challenge. Here we report on the observation of electric and magnetic dipole forbidden optical second-harmonic generation (SHG) in the altermagnet CoF$_2$ with a centrosymmetric lattice and spin order. We demonstrate that below the Néel temperature $T_N = 38$ K the SHG signal is sensitive to the ferrotype magnetic octupole $\mathbf{\mathcal{O}}^M$ which is the order parameter in the antiferromagnetic phase. By combining polarization-resolved SHG experimental data and a phenomenological symmetry analysis, we show that the altermagnetic spin structure of CoF$_2$ enables a ferroic-octupole-induced electric-quadrupolar nonlinear polarization $\mathbf{P}^{2ω} = \mathrm i\varepsilon_{0}{ }^c\mathbfχ^{(3)}(\mathbf{\mathcal{O}}^M) :\mathbf{E}^ω \nabla \mathbf{E}^ω$. The temperature dependence of SHG reveals a phase transition at $T_N$ confirming the spin origin of the observed signal. The SHG response is resonantly enhanced by a coherent three-photon process caused by the electronic $d$-$d$ transitions of the Co$^{2+}$ ion. Model calculations of SHG polarization rotational anisotropies and temperature dependencies give a reasonable agreement with experimental data, proving the disclosed nonlinear contribution. Our results establish SHG as a novel sensitive tool of ferroic-octupolar spin ordering and highlight the potential of CoF$_2$ and other altermagnets for further nonlinear optical investigations and applications.

### [56] [Three-dimensional repulsive Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17933)
*Alexei Sherman*

Motivation: 三维排斥哈伯德模型是强关联电子体系的重要模型，但对其有限温度相图及金属-绝缘体转变的精确描述仍具挑战。本文旨在通过强耦合图解法系统研究该模型的顺磁-反铁磁相边界、莫特转变（Mott transition）及奈尔温度（Néel temperature）的掺杂依赖性。

Method: 采用强耦合图解法（strong-coupling diagram technique）进行分析。该方法适用于中等至强耦合区间（U≥4t），通过图解微扰技术处理电子关联。

Result: 半填充下顺磁-反铁磁边界在4t≤U≤12t范围内确定，密度态（density of states）计算显示莫特转变发生在U≈9t。U≥6t时密度态呈现强电子排斥特征，U=4t时则表现为弱耦合特征。U=4t时奈尔温度随电子浓度单调下降；U=12t时在\bar{n}≈0.87附近出现平台，归因于电子退占据有效削弱耦合引起的密度态重构。U=12t半填充时磁临界指数γ≈1.4，接近海森堡模型（Heisenberg model）的值。

Conclusion: 强耦合图解法定量描述了三维哈伯德模型的顺磁-反铁磁相变与莫特转变，揭示了电子掺杂对奈尔温度的非单调影响（强耦合下出现平台）。临界指数表明半填充强耦合极限下体系行为接近海森堡模型。此外，有限晶体中观察到类似一级相变（first-order phase transition）的特征。

Abstract: The three-dimensional repulsive Hubbard model is investigated using the strong-coupling diagram technique. For half-filling, the boundary between paramagnetic and antiferromagnetic states is determined for the range of the Hubbard repulsion $4t\leq U\leq12t$, where $t$ is the hopping integral between neighboring sites. Along this boundary, the density of states is calculated, and it demonstrates the Mott transition at $U\approx9t$. For $U\geq6t$ and half-filling, the density of states has the shape inherent in the strong electron repulsion, while for $U=4t$, its shape points to weak coupling. The dependence of the Néel temperature $T_{\rm N}$ on the electron concentration $\bar{n}$ is investigated for the cases $U=4t$ and $12t$. In the former case, $T_{\rm N}$ decreases monotonously with $\bar{n}$, while in the latter case, there is a plateau in the dependence near $\bar{n}=0.87$. The plateau is connected to a reconstruction of the density of states caused by an effective weakening of electron coupling due to electron depopulation. For $U=12t$ and half-filling, the magnetic critical exponent $γ\approx1.4$, which is close to the value in the Heisenberg model. Some features resembling the first-order phase transition, revealing themselves in a finite crystal, are discussed.

</details>


### [57] [Theory of clusterization in orbitally degenerate transition-metal compounds driven by lattice instabilities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18014)
*Soshun Ozaki,Kota Mitsumoto,Chisa Hotta*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文针对过渡金属化合物，推导出一个包含量子 S=1 自由度的有效轨道-晶格模型（effective orbital-lattice model），揭示了自旋、轨道和晶格自由度协同作用驱动团簇形成的微观机制。研究发现，仅靠轨道驱动的交换相互作用不能稳定实验观测的三聚化（trimerized）相；引入离子晶格位移调节交换耦合后，该模型得以在全量子框架下稳定三聚化基态。简化模型还复现了微观模型的基本基态性质，并揭示了包含一级、二级和Kosterlitz-Thouless相变（Kosterlitz-Thouless transition）的丰富热相变序列。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受LiVS₂和LiVO₂中观测到的三聚化相的启发，本文旨在从微观模型出发，理解过渡金属化合物中自旋、轨道与晶格自由度之间协同相互作用如何驱动团簇的形成。

Method: 从多轨道Kanamori-Hubbard哈密顿量出发，将低能部分投影到局域S=1三重态流形（triplet manifold）上，该流形中两个电子根据洪德耦合（Hund's coupling）占据不同轨道。随后引入离子晶格位移（ionic lattice displacements），该位移调制跃迁积分并在缩短和伸长的键上诱导与键相关的交换耦合（bond-dependent exchange coupling）。此外，提出一个简化轨道-晶格模型，将自旋交换能替换为有效键能（effective bond energy）。

Result: 轨道驱动的交换相互作用单独无法稳定实验观测的三聚化相。引入晶格位移后，相竞争被定性改变，三聚化基态在全量子框架下得到稳健稳定。简化模型忠实复现了微观模型的基本基态性质，并在有限温度大尺度模拟中揭示出包含一级相变（first-order transition）、二级相变（second-order transition）和Kosterlitz-Thouless相变的丰富热相变序列，分别进入自旋、轨道和晶格有序相。

Conclusion: 自旋-轨道-晶格三者之间的协同作用对于过渡金属化合物中三聚化团的稳定至关重要，单纯的轨道交换机制不足以解释实验现象。简化轨道-晶格模型为研究该体系的有限温度热力学行为提供了有效途径。

Abstract: We derive an effective orbital-lattice model with quantum $S=1$ degrees of freedom for transition-metal compounds, providing a microscopic understanding of cluster formation driven by the cooperative interplay of spin, orbital, and lattice degrees of freedom. Motivated by the trimerized phases observed in LiVS$_2$ and LiVO$_2$, we consider a triangular-lattice three-orbital system with two electrons per site occupying the threefold-degenerate $t_{2g}$ manifold. Starting from a multiorbital Kanamori-Hubbard Hamiltonian, we project the low-energy sector onto the local $S=1$ triplet manifold, in which two electrons occupy different orbitals according to Hund's coupling. The resulting effective model exhibits exchange networks whose geometry is determined by the orbital configuration. However, the orbital-driven exchange interactions alone do not stabilize the experimentally observed trimer phase. We find that by incorporating ionic lattice displacements that modulate transfer integrals and induce bond-dependent exchange couplings on shortened and elongated bonds, the phase competition is qualitatively altered, leading to the robust stabilization of a trimerized ground state within a fully quantum-mechanical framework. We further show that a simplified orbital-lattice model, in which the spin-exchange energy is replaced by effective bond energies, faithfully reproduces the essential ground-state properties of the microscopic model. This reduced description enables large-scale finite-temperature simulations and reveals a rich sequence of thermal phase transitions, including first-order, second-order, and Kosterlitz-Thouless transitions into distinct spin-, orbital-, and lattice-ordered phases.

### [58] [High-temperature ferromagnetism and antiferromagnetism in monolayer \ce{CrTe2}: Roles of strong spin-lattice coupling and charge doping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18148)
*Anupama S,Mukul Kabir*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算与海森堡蒙特卡洛模拟，揭示了二维磁体 CrTe₂ 中晶格应变与载流子浓度调控下丰富的磁相图，阐明了结构、电子与磁自由度的耦合机制，并预测了新型双条纹反铁磁相及室温铁磁/反铁磁性的实现路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维磁体中结构、电子与磁自由度的相互耦合决定了相稳定性与临界温度，理解并控制这一耦合对基础研究与自旋电子学（spintronics）应用至关重要。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）结合海森堡蒙特卡洛模拟（Heisenberg Monte Carlo simulations）进行系统研究。

Result: 揭示了由晶格应变（lattice strain）与载流子密度（carrier density）共同调控的丰富磁相图；预测了通过电子掺杂可稳定的新型双条纹反铁磁相；实现了室温铁磁性与反铁磁性；发现该磁演化源于直接交换与配体介导交换相互作用（ligand-mediated exchange interactions）在鲁德曼-基特尔-胜矢-芳田耦合（RKKY coupling）下的竞争；定量了巨磁弹性响应并识别了可作相鉴定实验指纹的区折叠拉曼模式（zone-folded Raman modes）。

Conclusion: CrTe₂ 被确立为一种通用的二维自旋电子学平台，其磁序与转变温度可通过结构工程与电学工程进行定制化调控。

Abstract: The interplay of structural, electronic, and magnetic degrees of freedom governs phase stability and critical temperatures in two-dimensional magnets. Controlling this coupling is essential for advancing fundamental understanding and spintronic applications. Combining first-principles calculations with Heisenberg Monte Carlo simulations, we reveal a rich magnetic phase diagram governed by the interplay of lattice strain and carrier density. These results provide a unified framework that reconciles diverse experimental reports on epitaxial layers and predicts a novel double-stripe antiferromagnetic phase, further stabilized by electron doping. Moreover, structural and electronic perturbations enable room-temperature ferromagnetism and antiferromagnetism. This magnetic evolution arises from competing, highly tunable direct and ligand-mediated exchange interactions in the presence of Ruderman-Kittel-Kasuya-Yosida coupling. By disentangling their individual contributions, we elucidate the underlying microscopic mechanisms, which transcends the conventional conduction electron picture. Finally, we quantify the colossal magnetoelastic response and identify zone-folded Raman modes that serve as unique experimental fingerprints for phase identification. Together, these results establish \ce{CrTe2} as a versatile platform for two-dimensional spintronics, where magnetic order and transition temperatures are tailorable via structural and electrical engineering.

### [59] [Skew column RSK dynamics and the box-ball system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17525)
*Takashi Imamura,Matteo Mucciconi,Tomohiro Sasamoto,Travis Scrimshaw*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种称为“倾斜列RSK动力学”的确定性动力系统，它是经典盒球系统的二维推广，通过显式双射实现时间演化的线性化，并建立了与经典盒球系统、KRR构型及变换Hall-Littlewood多项式恒等式之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Fomin关于Schensted列插入的局部规则可被视为一种双车道盒球系统（two-lane box-ball system），其中载子（carrier）将粒子向前或横向移动。将这种双车道动力学并行运行在周期格点上，自然产生了盒球系统的二维推广，即本文所研究的倾斜列RSK动力学。

Method: 本文利用倾斜半标准Young表对上的两个交换的仿射晶体结构（affine crystal structures）以及关于Kirillov-Reshetikhin晶体张量积中特定子图的新连通性定理（connectivity theorem），构造了显式双射(P,Q) ↔ (H₁,H₂,κ,ν)，将时间演化线性化；同时通过末次穿越渗流（last-passage percolation）导出孤子长度的Greene型公式。

Result: 证明了该动力学具有孤子行为（solitonic behavior）；构造的线性化坐标包括两个水平弱表（horizontally weak tableaux）H₁、H₂、整数riggings κ以及弱递减整数序列 ν。建立了倾斜列RSK动力学到经典盒球系统的显式投影，其中κ恰好对应于关联盒球构型的Kerov-Kirillov-Reshetikhin rigging。通过线性化坐标的生成函数，获得了变换Hall-Littlewood多项式（transformed Hall-Littlewood polynomials）的Cauchy型与Kawanaka-Littlewood型恒等式的双射证明。

Conclusion: 本文系统建立了倾斜列RSK动力学的孤子结构，并揭示了其与经典盒球系统、晶体理论及对称函数恒等式之间的深层联系。

Abstract: The Fomin local rules for Schensted column insertion can be seen as a two-lane box-ball system, in which a carrier moves particles forward or laterally. Running such two-lane dynamics in parallel on a periodic lattice gives rise to a two-dimensional generalization of the box-ball system, which we call the \emph{skew column RSK dynamics}. Equivalently, this is a deterministic dynamics on pairs of skew semistandard Young tableaux $(P_t,Q_t)_{t \in \mathbb{Z}}$. We prove that this dynamics exhibits solitonic behavior and construct an explicit bijection $(P,Q) \leftrightarrow (H_1,H_2,κ,ν)$ that linearizes the time evolution. The resulting coordinates consist of two horizontally weak tableaux $H_1,H_2$ recording the asymptotic soliton data, integer riggings $κ$, and a weakly decreasing sequence of integers $ν$. A key feature of the construction is an explicit projection from the skew column RSK dynamics to the classical box-ball system; under this projection, the rigging $κ$ is precisely the Kerov--Kirillov--Reshetikhin rigging of the associated box-ball configuration. Our proof uses two commuting affine crystal structures on pairs of skew tableaux and a novel connectivity theorem for distinguished subgraphs of tensor products of Kirillov--Reshetikhin crystals. We also derive Greene-type formulas for the soliton lengths in terms of last-passage percolation on the associated cylindrical environment. Finally, by taking generating functions in the linearizing coordinates, we obtain bijective proofs of Cauchy and Kawanaka--Littlewood-type identities for transformed Hall--Littlewood polynomials.

### [60] [QPO-like Signatures and Hydrodynamical Variability in Accretion around a JNW-type Compact Spacetime in Freund-Nambu Scalar-Tensor Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17157)
*Orhan Donmez,M. Yousaf,G. Mustafa*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文在Freund-Nambu标量-张量引力（FNST）框架下构建了一个新的精确解（FNST度规），并数值求解了相对论流体动力学方程，研究了围绕该时空的Bondi-Hoyle-Lyttleton吸积激波锥机制。结果表明，更强的标量-张量偏离会改变激波锥形态、增加吸积物质积累并增强振荡行为；提取的准周期振荡（QPO）模式频率范围（几Hz至约100 Hz）与恒星质量黑洞候选体（如GRS 1915+105）的观测特征重叠，提示FNST时空的流体动力学变异性可作为标量场偏离Schwarzschild引力的现象学诊断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标量-张量引力理论通过引入标量自由度扩展了广义相对论，但现有研究对强引力场景下标量场偏离的流体动力学特征（如吸积激波锥及其可观测信号）尚缺乏系统探讨。本文旨在通过构造FNST精确解并数值分析其Bondi-Hoyle-Lyttleton吸积动力学，探索标量-张量偏离是否产生可观测的准周期振荡特征，从而为区分不同引力理论提供现象学诊断。

Method: 首先在Freund-Nambu标量-张量引力框架下解析构造了一个新的精确解——FNST度规，它是Janis-Newman-Winicour裸奇点几何的非平凡标量-张量推广，包含一个额外的标量区耦合参数q。随后在赤道面上数值求解了广义相对论流体动力学（general relativistic hydrodynamic）方程，模拟围绕该FNST时空的Bondi-Hoyle-Lyttleton吸积过程，并计算功率谱密度（power spectral density）以提取Lorentzian类峰对应的QPO模。

Result: 更强的标量-张量偏离（即耦合参数q的增大）显著改变激波锥形态、增加中心致密天体附近累积的物质质量，并增强激波锥的振荡行为。数值功率谱密度呈现Lorentzian类峰，可解释为流体动力学产生的类QPO模，来源于激波锥振荡以及锥内等离子体的压缩与稀疏。对于质量参数M=10M_sun的致密天体，提取的频率主要在几Hz至约100 Hz范围内，与恒星质量黑洞候选体（如GRS 1915+105）的QPO观测范围重叠；其中FNST2-FNST4模型对应的频率落入GRS 1915+105的时间特征范围。

Conclusion: FNST致密时空的外部流体动力学变异性可能提供标量场诱导的Schwarzschild偏离的现象学诊断手段。本文结果提示，通过分析吸积激波锥的QPO特征频率，有望在观测上区分标量-张量引力与广义相对论。

Abstract: Scalar tensor theories of gravity provide a broad as well as physically rich extension of general theory of relativity by allowing the gravitational interaction to be mediated not only by the spacetime metric but also by scalar degrees of freedom. In this manuscript, we present a new exact solution in the Freund-Nambu scalar-tensor (FNST) gravity scenario, representing a nontrivial scalar-tensor generalization of the Janis-Newman-Winicour naked-singularity geometry, characterized by an additional coupling parameter q in the scalar sector. We also numerically solve the general relativistic hydrodynamic equations in order to investigate the shock-cone mechanism formed by Bondi-Hoyle-Lyttleton accretion around this compact spacetime on the equatorial plane. We show that stronger scalar-tensor deviations modify the shock-cone morphology, significantly increase the amount of matter accumulated near the central compact object, and enhance the oscillatory behavior of the shock cone. The Lorentzian-like peaks obtained from the numerically computed power spectral density are interpreted as hydrodynamically generated QPO-like modes. These modes are driven by shock cone oscillations and by the compression and rarefaction of the plasma trapped inside the cone. Finally, for a compact object with mass parameter M = 10M_sun, the numerically extracted frequencies are found mainly in the range from a few Hz up to approximately 100 Hz. These frequencies overlap with the QPO ranges reported in stellar-mass black-hole-candidate systems. In particular, the frequencies obtained for the FNST2-FNST4 models fall within the range of timing features reported for the source GRS 1915+105. These results suggest that the exterior hydrodynamical variability of FNST compact spacetimes may provide phenomenological diagnostics of scalar-field-induced deviations from the Schwarzschild reference case.

### [61] [Can a Slow and Strong Phase Transition in Neutron Stars Relieve Major Compact-Star Observation Tensions?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17231)
*Chen Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过引入强一级强子-夸克相变（first-order hadron–quark phase transition）且相变速度慢于径向振荡的慢速稳定混合分支（extended stable hybrid branches），检验了中子星（neutron star）能否同时解释HESS J1731--347的低质量小半径、XTE J1814--338的异常小半径以及GW190814次级组分的过高质量，同时与GW170817和NICER约束一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来几个异常致密天体观测——HESS J1731--347和XTE J1814--338的低质量小半径，以及GW190814次级组分高于常规中子星最大质量上限——对传统中子星图像构成补充性挑战，亟需统一的物态方程（equation of state, EOS）解释方案。

Method: 采用分段多方位（piecewise-polytropic, PP）基准模型，并辅以独立的速度-声速（speed-of-sound, CS）参数化进行对照，在强子分支和混合分支上开展广泛参数扫描，寻找与多重观测一致的物态方程模式。

Result: 发现两种可行方案：情景1使用同一物态方程，纯强子分支同时兼容GW190814量级质量和HESS J1731--347，慢速稳定混合分支到达XTE J1814--338；情景2保留GW190814量级强子分支，但在不同相变强度区间内通过慢速稳定分支分别到达XTE J1814--338和HESS J1731--347。

Conclusion: 强一级相变导致的慢速稳定混合分支为调和当前多个异常致密天体观测提供了一条有前景的物态方程途径。

Abstract: Recent anomalous compact-star observations challenge the conventional neutron-star interpretation in complementary ways: HESS J1731--347 and XTE J1814--338 favor unusually small radii at low mass, while the secondary component of GW190814 appears too massive for an ordinary neutron star under GW170817-based maximum-mass inferences. We examine whether neutron stars with a strong first-order hadron--quark phase transition can address these tensions via the extended stable hybrid branches that arise when the phase conversion is slow compared to radial oscillations, while remaining consistent with GW170817 and NICER constraints. Using a piecewise-polytropic (PP) benchmark, supplemented by an independent speed-of-sound (CS) parametrization comparison, we find two viable patterns in a general parameter scan over both the hadronic and hybrid branches. Scenario 1 realizes an all-at-once solution: the same EOS has a pure hadronic branch compatible with both the GW190814-scale mass and HESS J1731--347, while its slow stable hybrid branch reaches XTE J1814--338. Scenario 2 retains the GW190814-scale hadronic branch but reaches XTE J1814--338 and HESS J1731--347 on slow stable branches in different transition-strength regimes.

### [62] [Effective description of lensed gravitational waves diffracted by stellar fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17765)
*Miguel Zumalacárregui,Xikai Shan*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出降阶随机衍射（Reduced-Order Stochastic Diffraction, ROSD）模型，通过奇异值分解（singular value decomposition）数值模拟的波光学微透镜效应，构建优化正交基与系数概率密度函数，用于描述引力波（gravitational waves）因恒星场微透镜（microlensing）产生的频率依赖畸变，并支持贝叶斯参数估计中的注入与恢复分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波在经星系和星系团放大时，会受到大量恒星及残骸天体（微透镜，microlenses）的干扰，产生频率依赖的波光学效应，现有方法难以同时处理大规模小尺度透镜与波动衍射效应。

Method: 对恒星场波光学透镜效应的数值模拟实施奇异值分解（singular value decomposition），从中综合出降阶有效描述，得到优化正交基（orthonormal basis）描述微透镜畸变，并估计系数的概率密度函数。

Result: 给出了SVD-stellar-I5-aLIGO作为模型实例，讨论了截断阶数（truncation order）的作用，并通过贝叶斯参数估计（Bayesian parameter estimation）中的注入与恢复演示了模型在引力波数据上的应用能力。

Conclusion: ROSD模型可根据探测器灵敏度和源类型进行定制，可扩展至不同微透镜种群和外势场，为探测恒星级致密天体及其残骸、暗物质候选体以及发现最遥远致密双星并合提供了新途径。

Abstract: As natural telescopes, Gravitational lenses enable the observation of sources that would otherwise be too distant and faint. Stellar-mass objects, or microlenses, act as impurities in the lens, producing subtle distortions of the source. These effects are necessary to correctly interpret observations, and may in some cases be themselves evidence of gravitational magnification. Gravitational waves (GWs) observed by ground detectors and magnified by galaxies and clusters will undergo microlensing by fields of stars and remnants: describing these systems requires not only considering a large number of small-scale lenses (microlenses), but also including wave-optics effects, leading to frequency dependent modulations of the signal. Here we present novel models for Reduced-Order Stochastic Diffraction (ROSD), which overcome these challenges in the search for GW lensing signatures: an effective description is synthesized from numerical simulations of wave-optics lensing by stellar fields via a singular value decomposition. The procedure yields an optimized orthonormal basis to describe microlensing distortions and a probability density function for the coefficients, which can be used as priors or to verify the consistency with stellar-field lensing. We present SVD-stellar-I5-aLIGO as an example of this model category, discuss the role of truncation order and demonstrate how it can be applied to GW data via injection and recovery in Bayesian parameter estimation. ROSD can be tailored to account for detector sensitivity and the type of source under analysis, and extended to different microlens populations and external potentials. ROSD models open a new window to probe small-scale objects (stars, remnants and potentially dark matter) and facilitate the discovery of the most distant compact binary mergers.

</details>


### [63] [A Semi-Analytical Loss Cone Theory for Tidal Disruption Event Rates Around Kerr Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18050)
*Wenkang Xin*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个将自旋相关的损失锥边界纳入潮汐瓦解事件（TDE）率理论的半解析框架，发现虽然黑洞自旋对瓦解边界产生一阶偏向（倾向于瓦解逆行星），但全局TDE率对自旋不敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有TDE处理方法要么假设黑洞不自旋，要么依赖对自旋黑洞的数值模拟，缺乏能够解析描述自旋效应与轨道倾角影响的半解析框架。

Method: 利用新型潮汐张量形式（tidal tensor formalism）计算倾角依赖的潮汐瓦解与直接捕获阈值；将经典一维损失锥问题推广到嵌套瓦解与捕获边界的情形，推导出闭合形式的捕获分数；建立描述角动量大小与方向同时扩散的二维Fokker-Planck方程，并采用微扰方法进行分析。

Result: Kerr黑洞的瓦解边界导致一阶偏向，优先瓦解逆行星（retrograde stars）；但全局TDE率对黑洞自旋表现出显著的鲁棒性（insensitivity）。

Conclusion: 该半解析框架为在群体级TDE研究中纳入黑洞自旋和轨道倾角效应提供了可行的途径。

Abstract: A tidal disruption event (TDE) occurs when a star is scattered onto a near-radial orbit and is torn apart by a black hole (BH)'s tidal field. The angular momentum threshold for disruption is set by general relativistic tidal dynamics, while the supply of stars to the disruption zone is governed by Newtonian stellar dynamics. A spinning BH breaks the spherical symmetry of the disruption boundary, so a star's survival depends on both the magnitude and the orientation of its angular momentum. Existing treatments either assume a non-spinning BH or rely on numerical simulations of spinning BHs. We develop the first semi analytical framework that incorporates spin-dependent loss cone boundaries into TDE rate theory. Using a novel tidal tensor formalism, we compute inclination-dependent thresholds for tidal disruption and direct capture by the event horizon. We then revisit the classical one dimensional loss cone problem with nested disruption and capture boundaries, deriving a closed form capture fraction valid across all loss cone regimes. Finally, we formulate a two dimensional Fokker--Planck equation describing simultaneous diffusion in angular momentum magnitude and orientation. Through a perturbative treatment, we demonstrate that while the Kerr disruption boundary induces a first-order bias favouring the disruption of retrograde stars, the global TDE rate is remarkably insensitive to black hole spin. This approach offers a tractable route to including spin and orbital inclination in population-level TDE studies.

</details>


### [64] [Polarized emission of orbiting hot-spots near Sagittarius A*: effects of electromagnetic interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18107)
*Abylaikhan Tlemissov,Arman Tursunov,Maciek Wielgus*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文研究了施瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）周围带电热斑（hot-spot）在外磁场中的极化特征，发现电磁相互作用参数会显著改变极化环的对称性与时间比，并可能导致系统参数（如轨道倾角、热斑速度）估计中的歧义性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑洞热斑模型多忽略热斑与黑洞外部磁场的电磁相互作用，可能遗漏重要的极化信号特征；本文旨在揭示这一相互作用如何影响极化观测，并评估其对人马座A*（Sagittarius A*）毫米波观测数据解释的影响。

Method: 采用广义相对论模型，结合同步辐射（synchrotron emission）和光线追踪（ray-tracing）计算光传播，分析电磁相互作用参数对电场矢量位置角（electric vector position angle, EVPA）及$Q$-$U$平面极化环演化的影响；并将模型应用于ALMA对人马座A*的毫米波观测，通过探索参数空间拟合极化环的不对称性、时间比和面积比。

Result: 小的正相互作用参数使极化环对称性增强、时间比增加；而负的磁参数会导致强不对称性，无法复现观测数据。

Conclusion: 电磁相互作用可能引入系统参数（如轨道倾角或热斑速度）估计中的歧义性，在解释实际观测时需予以考虑。

Abstract: We investigate the polarimetric signatures of orbiting hot-spots around a Schwarzschild black hole in the presence of an external magnetic field, accounting for the electromagnetic interaction between the charged emitter and the field. Using a general-relativistic model that incorporates synchrotron emission and ray-tracing of light propagation, we analyze how the electromagnetic interaction parameter modifies the observed polarization patterns, with particular emphasis on the behavior of the electric vector position angle (EVPA) and the time-evolving polarization loops in the $Q$-$U$ plane. Applying the model to millimeter wavelength ALMA observations of Sagittarius~A*, we explore the parameter space that best reproduces the asymmetry, time ratio, and area ratio of the observed polarization loops. We find that the inclusion of a small positive interaction parameter increases the symmetry of the loops and the time ratio, while a negative magnetic parameter introduces strong asymmetry and fails to reproduce the data. Our results indicate that electromagnetic interaction can lead to ambiguity in the estimation of the system parameters such as orbital inclination or hot-spot velocity.

### [65] [A Joint Optimal Search for Gravitational Waves from Resolved and Unresolved Supermassive Binary Black Holes with Pulsar Timing Arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18241)
*Boris Goncharov,Gabriela Sato-Polito,Xiaoming Bi,Matias Zaldarriaga*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文从第一性原理出发，构建了一个联合模型，同时描述引力波背景（gravitational wave background, GWB）和可被脉冲星计时阵（Pulsar Timing Array, PTA）单独解析的超大质量黑洞双星（supermassive black hole binary, SMBHB）源。引入SMBHB源的特征数 $N_{\rm c}$ 作为GWB天体物理起源的探测统计量，并应用于模拟的NANOGrav 15年数据，给出了可分辨SMBHB的应变振幅的天体物理上限，揭示了21个候选源与观测结果的冲突，并预测了未来20年数据中的探测概率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有PTA搜索面临引力波背景与可分辨单源之间的统计区分难题，缺乏自洽的联合建模方法。本文旨在建立从第一性原理出发的统一框架，以区分GWB的起源是由大量SMBHB的泊松叠加（Poissonian superposition）构成，还是存在可单独解析的明亮源，并定量评估这些源与现有观测的兼容性。

Method: 本文从第一性原理推导出一个联合模型，将GWB和可单独分辨的明亮SMBHB源统一描述。提出 $N_{\rm c}$（SMBHB源的特征数）作为检测统计量，用于区分GWB的泊松起源。利用该模型对模拟的NANOGrav 15年数据（复刻了真实数据的所有已知噪声、观测特征和推断的GWB功率谱）进行分析，推导可分辨SMBHB的应变振幅上限，并计算探测概率。

Result: 在114个来自活动星系核（active galactic nuclei, AGN）观测的SMBHB候选源中，21个与NANOGrav观测存在张力（tension），而依据原始分析的上限报告，仅1个候选源存在张力。在模拟NANOGrav 15年数据中，以信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio, SNR）=5为阈值，从孤立SMBHB探测到引力波的概率为2%；在预期的20年数据中，该概率升至5%。同时，在20年数据中发现SNR=2的离群值（outlier）的概率为40%。

Conclusion: 本文提出的联合模型和 $N_{\rm c}$ 统计量为区分GWB的天体物理起源提供了新工具。分析表明，现有NANOGrav数据对可分辨SMBHB源的应变振幅施加了比原始上限更严格的约束。对未来NANOGrav 20年数据的预测显示，探测到孤立SMBHB源的概率虽仍较低，但发现中低信噪比离群信号的概率可观，有望推动对SMBHB群体性质（population properties）的理解。

Abstract: We introduce, from first principles, a joint model of the gravitational wave background (GWB) and brightest supermassive black hole binary (SMBHB) sources that may be individually resolvable in Pulsar Timing Array (PTA) searches for gravitational waves. We propose the characteristic number of SMBHB sources, $N_{\rm c}$, as a detection statistic for the astrophysical origin of the GWB. We then demonstrate how the brightest SMBHBs assist in resolving $N_{\rm c}$. Applying our method to the simulated NANOGrav 15-year data, which replicates all aspects of real data's known noise, observations, and the inferred GWB power spectrum, we demonstrate direct astrophysical limits on the strain amplitude of individually resolvable SMBHBs. We find that 21 of 114 SMBHB candidates from active galactic nuclei observations are in tension with the NANOGrav's observations. In contrast, only one candidate is in tension with the NANOGrav data based on the upper limits reported in the original analysis. Constraining the Poisson-specific characteristic number of SMBHBs, $N_{\rm c}$, at ${\rm yr}^{-1}$, we outline implications for the population properties of SMBHBs. Based on our new model applied to the simulated NANOGrav data, we calculate the probability of detecting GWs from isolated SMBHB in the 15-year data to be 2\% at the ${\rm SNR}=5$ level. Our projection towards the expected NANOGrav 20-year data suggests an increase to 5\%. With this, we estimate the probability of finding an outlier with an SNR of 2 in the NANOGrav 20-year data to be $40\%$.

### [66] [Creating squeezed and non-classical collective motional many-body states through stroboscopic Rydberg dressing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17849)

Main category: physics.atom-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现量子计算和量子模拟所需的条件性量子操作（如量子门）依赖于粒子间的受控相互作用，而这类相互作用通常依赖于粒子间距离；相对位置的量子不确定性会导致门操作保真度下降。因此，需要一种方法有效降低原子间距离的量子涨落。

Method: 该方法基于中性原子阵列平台，利用原子运动与随机激发的里德伯态（Rydberg states）之间的耦合，集体压缩所有对应于原子间位移的运动模式，从而将距离波动抑制到运动真空态（motional vacuum state）以下。

Result: 该方法可将所有原子间距离的不确定性降低至运动真空态的分数量级，并能够制备具有显著维格纳负性（Wigner negativity）的非经典关联态。

Conclusion: 这些压缩态和非经典关联态有望降低运动退相干（motional decoherence）、提高量子门保真度，并可能成为量子增强计量（quantum-enhanced metrology）的资源。

Abstract: Realizing conditional quantum operations, e.g., quantum gates, for quantum computing and simulation requires controlled interactions between particles. Often, these interactions depend on the interparticle distance, and accordingly, an uncertainty of the relative particle position may translate into gate infidelities. We consider here a quantum computing platform based on an array of neutral atoms and present a method that allows to reduce the uncertainty of all interatomic distances. Our approach exploits the coupling between atomic motion and stroboscopically excited atomic Rydberg states. It allows to collectively squeeze the modes corresponding to interatomic displacements, thereby reducing distance fluctuations down to a fraction of the motional vacuum state. Furthermore, the method permits the creation of non-classical states with substantial Wigner negativity. These correlated states may allow reducing motional decoherence, increasing gate fidelity, and potentially yield a resource for quantum-enhanced metrology.

Method: 采用扩散量子蒙特卡罗方法（diffusion quantum Monte Carlo method）对零温下的一维电子-空穴双线系统（electron-hole biwire system）进行数值模拟，计算对关联函数（pair correlation functions）和凝聚体分数（condensate fraction），并在广泛的载流子密度rs和线间距d范围内构建相图。

Abstract: We study a mass-asymmetric one-dimensional electron-hole biwire system at zero temperature using the diffusion quantum Monte Carlo method. Pair correlation functions and condensate fraction are obtained over a wide range of carrier densities $r_{\rm s}$ and interwire separations $d$, allowing us to construct the phase diagram. We identify regimes corresponding to a two-component electron-hole plasma, an excitonic fluid with quasicondensation, and a Wigner-correlated phase at various densities. Owing to reduced dimensionality, strong electron-hole correlations favor excitonic quasicondensation even in the high-density limit, persisting down to $r_{\rm s} = 0.3$ a.u. These results provide a microscopic characterization of correlation-driven phases in electron-hole systems in one dimension.

### [68] [Kohn--Luttinger Superconductivity in Flat Chern Bands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17205)
*Nianlong Zou,Cheng Xu,Yafis Barlas,Yang Zhang*

TL;DR: 本文揭示了一种几何驱动的Kohn-Luttinger机制：在平带体系中，类朗道能级（Landau-level-like）形状因子使RPA屏蔽库仑相互作用的吸引瓣与形状因子峰值对齐，从而在局域能带极值附近产生异常强的吸引通道。基于斯格明子晶格模型，研究发现自旋非极化配对时形状因子幅度驱动动量空间平移对称性并选择扩展-s波失稳，自旋极化配对时形状因子相位驱动手性p波和f波序。该机制在高温屏蔽和BKT相涨落下仍有效，建立了量子几何（quantum geometry）作为平带陈带中非常规配对的关键组织原则。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平带体系中超导与关联拓扑相共存的最新观测暗示平带几何（flat-band geometry）与电子配对之间存在某种联系，但具体的微观机制尚不清楚。本文旨在揭示这一几何效应如何驱动非常规配对，而非依赖传统的自旋涨落或电子-声子耦合。

Method: 作者提出了一种几何驱动的Kohn-Luttinger机制，其中类朗道能级形状因子（form factor）重新调整RPA屏蔽库仑相互作用的角分布，使吸引瓣对准形状因子峰值。以斯格明子晶格（Skyrmion lattice）模型作为最小实现，分别对自旋非极化和自旋极化配对情形进行分析。

Result: 自旋非极化配对中，形状因子幅度强制产生动量空间平移对称性，导致在费米小口袋处选择扩展-s波失稳；自旋极化配对中，形状因子相位直接驱动手性p波和f波序，无需依赖自旋涨落。该增强效应在更高朗道能级类似物中持续存在，并能抵御有限温度屏蔽和BKT相涨落（Berezinskii--Kosterlitz--Thouless phase fluctuations）。

Conclusion: 量子几何（quantum geometry）是平带陈带（flat Chern bands）中非常规配对的一个核心组织原则，本工作为理解平带超导中几何与配对之间的内在关联提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Recent observations of superconductivity near correlated topological phases in flat bands suggest a facile link between flat-band geometry and electron pairing. In this work, we reveal a geometry-driven Kohn--Luttinger mechanism in which Landau-level-like form factors align the attractive lobe of the RPA-screened Coulomb interaction with the form-factor peak, generating an anomalously strong attractive channel near local band extrema. Using the Skyrmion lattice model as a minimal realization, we show that for spin-unpolarized pairing the form-factor magnitude enforces an emergent momentum-space translational symmetry and selects an extended-$s$ instability concentrated at small Fermi pockets, while for spin-polarized pairing the form-factor phase drives chiral $p$- and $f$-wave order without invoking spin fluctuations. The band-extrema enhancement persists in higher Landau-level analogs and survives finite-temperature screening and Berezinskii--Kosterlitz--Thouless phase fluctuations. Our work establishes quantum geometry as a key organizing principle for unconventional pairing in flat Chern bands.

### [69] [Room-temperature tuning and probing of Fermi polarons in atomically thin semiconductors on a plasmonic metasurface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17278)

Abstract: The Fermi polaron, arising from interactions between a mobile impurity and a degenerate Fermi sea, is a many-body quasiparticle that provides a sensitive probe of strongly correlated electronic phases in atomically thin semiconductors. In doped transition-metal dichalcogenides, the attractive and repulsive polaron branches are well established in monolayers. However, extending active control and quantitative, branch-resolved probing to stacked geometries has remained elusive because spectral quenching and weak optical contrast restrict access to Fermi polaron signatures. Here, we integrate electron-doped WS$_2$ flakes from monolayer to quadrilayer with a strain-tunable plasmonic metasurface, enabling high-contrast scattering readout at room temperature through coupling between Fermi polaron resonances and surface plasmons. This platform enables quantitative extraction of polaron branch spectral weights and coupling strengths across different layer numbers. We uncover a systematic thickness dependence of the spectral-weight distribution and demonstrate continuous and fully reversible spectral-weight transfer between attractive and repulsive branches in bilayers and quadrilayers, with near-complete transfer achieved in bilayers. By identifying layer number and strain as complementary control parameters for Fermi polarons, our results establish metasurface-enabled scattering spectroscopy as a practical route to resolve and manipulate many-body resonances in stacked van der Waals semiconductors, bridging idealized monolayer polaron physics and device-relevant architectures.

### [70] [Vortex-Beam-Driven Dirac Materials: Impurity and Polarization Effects on Light-Induced Vortex and Edge States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17341)
*Trevor W. Walsh,Eric E. Caldwell,Nancy P. Sandler,Mahmoud M. Asmar*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解有限几何结构中圆偏振涡旋光（circularly polarized vortex light）驱动的狄拉克系统中，杂质散射与偏振失谐对拓扑边缘态（topological edge states）和光诱导多量子化涡旋态（photoinduced multiply quantized vortex states）的影响。

Method: 通过分析准能量谱（quasienergy spectrum）、实空间态（real-space states）和局域态密度（local density of states），研究了有限尺寸效应、涡度（vorticity）和有效粒子-空穴对称性（effective particle-hole symmetry）的表现，并考察了局域杂质与杂质团簇导致的角动量混合效应。

Result: 局域杂质与杂质团簇引起的角动量混合（angular-momentum mixing）会重塑涡旋态；而圆偏振产生的角动量混合则导致动态能隙（dynamical gap）被体衍生态逐渐填充。在杂质与偏振偏差存在时，涡旋态与边缘态信号仍可观测。

Conclusion: 涡旋与边缘态在杂质与偏振失谐条件下仍保持可观测性，为相关实验的可行性与鲁棒性提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We study impurity scattering and polarization detuning in finite-size vortex-light-beam-driven massive Dirac systems. In finite geometries, circularly polarized vortex light opens a dynamical gap where topological edge states coexist with photoinduced multiply quantized vortex states. We analyze how finite-size effects, vorticity, and effective particle-hole symmetry manifest in the quasienergy spectrum, real-space states, and local density of states. We show that angular-momentum mixing due to localized impurities and impurity clusters reshape vortex states, while when produced by circular polarization, it leads to a gradual filling of the dynamical gap with bulk-derived states. Our results indicate that both vortex and edge signatures remain observable in the presence of impurities and realistic polarization deviations, providing guidance for experimental realizations.

### [71] [Operator ordering as an emergent gauge field in twisted bilayer graphene: singular spectral signatures at the magic angle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17349)
*C. A. S. Almeida*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文指出，魔角扭曲双层石墨烯（magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene）的AB和BA堆叠点扫描隧道谱（STM）应呈现两个不对称的Van Hove峰，峰间距约为171 meV，这一特征在标准Bistritzer–MacDonald光谱中不存在。作者证明，该信号源自Dirac哈密顿量在空间变化质量下的Hermitian排序修正，该修正产生了有效质量零点处h/(2e)的Aharonov–Bohm通量；排序修正项在AB/BA点产生1/r奇异性，分裂能标随√θ变化且与栅压无关，空间局域化在~2.1 nm范围内，且零模具有抛物柱面函数特征D_{-1/2}。该预测可通过现有STM数据的空间分辨谱进行检验，其元胞平均展宽~14 meV与已有实验的16 meV偏差吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Bistritzer–MacDonald模型给出的魔角扭曲双层石墨烯（magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene）光谱在AB和BA堆叠点处缺少实验上预期的两个不对称Van Hove峰结构。本文旨在从理论层面揭示这一分裂信号的物理起源，并解释其与现有实验数据的差异。

Method: 作者引入带有空间变化质量项（spatially varying mass）的Dirac哈密顿量的Hermitian排序修正（Hermitian ordering correction），该修正项在有效质量m_eff(r)的零点处产生一个h/(2e)的Aharonov–Bohm（AB）通量。在手征极限（chiral limit）下，通过空间依赖的幺正变换（unitary transformation）局域对角化层间耦合，排序项H_ord在AB/BA堆叠点处（m_eff=0）发展出1/r奇异性。此外，作者基于局部渐近理论（local asymptotic theory）分析了零点附近的零模（zero mode）结构。

Result: 排序修正产生的Van Hove峰分裂Δ_split ≈ 171 meV，其标度行为为√θ，区别于关联驱动能隙的θ或1/θ依赖；该分裂不依赖于栅压（gate-voltage independent），且空间局域在AB/BA堆叠点周围~2.1 nm范围内。零模在渐近形式下呈现抛物柱面函数D_{-1/2}特征。元胞平均展宽~14 meV与已有STM实验与BM紧束缚模型预测之间的16 meV偏差一致。

Conclusion: 所述排序修正自然解释了AB/BA堆叠点处不对称Van Hove峰的出现及其定量特征。该预测可通过分析现有STM空间分辨谱来验证，为魔角扭曲双层石墨烯中电子结构的微观物理机制提供了可检验的理论框架。

Abstract: Scanning-tunnelling spectroscopy at the AB and BA stacking points of magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene should reveal two asymmetric Van~Hove peaks separated by $Δ_{\mathrm{split}}\approx 171$~meV -- a splitting absent from the standard Bistritzer--MacDonald spectrum. We show this signature arises naturally from the Hermitian ordering correction of the Dirac Hamiltonian with spatially varying mass, which generates an emergent Aharonov--Bohm flux of $h/(2e)$ at each zero of the effective mass $m_{\mathrm{eff}}(\mathbf{r})=w|f(\mathbf{r})|$. In the chiral limit, the interlayer coupling is locally diagonalised by a spatially dependent unitary transformation; the ordering term $H_{\mathrm{ord}}=-\tfrac{i}{2}\boldsymbolσ\cdot \nabla\ln m_{\mathrm{eff}}$ then develops a $1/r$ singularity at the AB/BA stacking points, where $m_{\mathrm{eff}}$ vanishes. The splitting scales as $\sqrtθ$ -- distinguishing it from correlation-driven gaps ($\proptoθ$ or $\propto 1/θ$) -- is gate-voltage independent, and is spatially localised within $r_c\approx 2.1$~nm of each AB/BA point. Within the local asymptotic theory near the zeros of $\mathrm{eff}$, the ordering-corrected zero mode acquires parabolic-cylinder character $D_{-1/2}$. The spatially resolved AB/BA spectrum reported in recent STM studies of magic-angle TBG has not been analysed for two-peak structure and constitutes an immediate experimental test; the predicted cell-averaged broadening of $\approx 14$~meV is consistent with the $16$~meV discrepancy between existing STM data and the BM tight-binding prediction.

Abstract: Dispersive coupling between vibrational modes with different frequencies is a major nonlinear dynamical effect. We show that in $p$-doped semiconductors such coupling is strongly enhanced. Moreover, the coupling parameters increase with the order of the nonlinearity. The doping-induced dispersive coupling becomes much stronger than the intrinsic one already for moderately strong doping. Its dependence on the hole density is nonmonotonic, and the temperature dependence becomes nonmonotonic for higher densities. Relevant mesoscopic frequency fluctuations are briefly discussed. The results are applied to Si resonators, where doping is used to compensate the temperature dependence of a clock mode, whereas another low-frequency mode is used as a thermometer to enable temperature stabilization.

Abstract: Weyl semimetals host topologically protected surface states, known as Fermi arcs, which connect bulk Weyl nodes in momentum space. Both bulk Weyl nodes and Fermi arcs are anticipated to be chiral. The chirality of bulk bands has been confirmed through observations of the chiral anomaly and Weyl orbits. In contrast, despite their discovery more than a decade ago, the chiral nature of Fermi arcs has remained unresolved. Here we report Fermi-arc-induced nonlinear transport in the archetypal Weyl semimetal TaAs. While linear transport remains dominated by bulk conduction, nonlinear transport uncovers surface-specific contributions, including an exceptionally large third-order nonreciprocal response that exceeds conventional expectations and highlights the crucial role of the singular arc endpoints. Our findings unambiguously demonstrate the chiral nature of Fermi arcs and establish nonlinear transport as a direct probe of these topological surface states. Given the abundance of natural materials predicted to host topological semimetal states, these results open opportunities for exploring nonlinear transport phenomena and device concepts across a broad class of systems.

### [74] [Anomalous Pairing Currents and a Second Topological Edge Channel in Bosonic Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17538)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于连续性方程在kagome晶格上导出跳跃电流和反常配对电流；引入整数para-幺正Chern数描述体隙拓扑相；定义相位敏感泄漏比Λ_ℐ刻画缺陷周围的配对电流行为。

Result: 玻色子配对在kagome晶格上产生了第二手性电流通道；预测了体隙相中的手性循环以及缺陷周围可调的配对电流泄漏比；发现跳跃电流与配对电流分别由键上单粒子相干性和非局域反常相干性驱动，后者的空间范围由BdG配对隙决定。

Conclusion: 体拓扑与反常边缘响应存在共存区域，该区域在粒子数守恒物质中无对应物，且预言可在驱动光子晶格和超导电路阵列等实验平台上直接验证。

Abstract: We show that bosonic pairing opens a second chiral current channel on a 2D kagome lattice, absent from any particle-conserving model. From the continuity equation, we derive both a hopping current and an anomalous pairing current on the lattice, and predict chiral circulation in bulk-gapped phases with integer para-unitary Chern numbers, as well as a phase-sensitive leakage ratio, $Λ_{\cal I}$, for the pairing current around a defect. This ratio can be tuned from confined to strongly anomalous regimes at fixed topology. The two channels differ microscopically: the hopping current is sourced by the on-bond single-particle coherence, whereas the pairing current is sourced by the off-site anomalous coherence, whose spatial range is governed by the BdG pairing gap rather than by the single-particle gap. This separation produces distinct defect-induced signatures in real space, identifies a regime in which bulk topology and anomalous edge response coexist with no analogue in particle-conserving matter, and is directly testable in driven photonic lattices and superconducting-circuit arrays.

### [75] [Beyond the interface: Persistent Hopping Transport and Frequency Dispersion in Strong-inversion Cryogenic MOSFETs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17547)
*Keito Yoshinaga,Wataru Miyagi,Ryo Toyoshima,Munehiro Tada,Ken Uchida*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文报道了低温MOSFET（cryo-MOSFET）沟道阻抗中存在的本征频率色散现象（intrinsic frequency dispersion），通过Cole-Cole分析将其归因于电离杂质诱导的带尾局域态（band-tail localized states）中的变程跳跃（variable-range hopping）机制，并基于此提出了一个新的物理模型，解释了强反型区下的阻抗频率依赖性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低温CMOS（cryo-CMOS）技术是量子计算接口的关键，需要精确建模器件的动态行为。然而，传统模型将MOSFET输出阻抗的频率依赖性归因于外部寄生效应，忽略了沟道内部可能存在的本征色散机制，这限制了高频小信号建模的准确性。

Method: 采用Cole-Cole分析法（Cole-Cole analysis）在阻抗平面上表征频率色散特征，将其识别为压低半圆（depressed semicircle），并结合变程跳跃（variable-range hopping）机制通过带尾局域态（band-tail localized states）进行物理解释。与传统将带尾态局限于氧化层界面的模型不同，本文提出高沟道掺杂MOSFET中的带尾态由电离杂质（ionized impurities）诱导并分布于整个耗尽区（depletion region）。

Result: 在强反型区（strong-inversion region）深处仍观察到沟道阻抗的本征频率色散；Cole-Cole图中的阻抗轨迹呈现典型的压低半圆特征；该色散行为由电离杂质诱导的变程跳跃主导，即使在漂移传导（drift conduction）占主导的条件下仍然存在。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了电离杂质诱导的跳跃传导（hopping conduction）支配着低温MOSFET沟道阻抗的动态响应，即便在漂移电流主导情况下亦不例外，为精确的小信号建模（small-signal modeling）和高温频低温CMOS电路设计（high-frequency cryo-CMOS circuit design）提供了关键理论指导。

Abstract: Cryogenic complementary metal-oxide-semiconductor (cryo-CMOS) technology is essential for quantum computing interfaces, which require precise modeling of dynamic device behavior. The output impedance of MOS field-effect transistors (MOSFETs) is frequency dependent, which has been conventionally attributed to extrinsic parasitics. Here, we report an intrinsic frequency dispersion in the channel impedance of cryogenic MOSFETs that persists deep into the strong-inversion region. Through a Cole-Cole analysis, we characterize this dispersion as a depressed semicircle in the impedance plane and attribute its behavior to variable-range hopping through band-tail localized states. Unlike conventional models where band-tail states are confined to the oxide interface, we demonstrate that in MOSFETs with high channel doping the band-tail states are induced by ionized impurities and distributed throughout the depletion region. Our paradigm accounts for frequency dispersion under strong inversion. This work demonstrates that ionized-impurities-induced hopping governs the dynamic response of cryo-MOSFETs channel impedance even when drift conduction dominates, offering critical insights for accurate small-signal modeling and high-frequency cryo-CMOS circuit design.

Abstract: Atomic-scale insights into light-matter interaction can be obtained using light-assisted scanning probe microscopy techniques. The observed sub-molecular contrast suggests the involvement of a long-lived quadruplet excited state. Motivation: ν=2/5分数量子霍尔态的对撞机实验中观测到反常的负Fano因子，与现有理论预测相矛盾，亟需新的理论机制来解释这一现象。

Method: 作者在多模分数量子霍尔对撞机（multi-mode FQH collider）模型中引入边缘间相互作用（inter-edge interactions），分析由此导致的分数化效应，并将任意子束分解为关联（correlated）与非关联（uncorrelated）两个分量，分别考察它们在时域编织（time-domain braiding）中的行为。

Result: 在长结极限（long-junction limit）下，非关联分量占据主导地位，导致隧穿电流符号反转，从而成功复现ν=2/5态中观测到的负Fano因子。

Conclusion: 研究结果凸显了相互作用在多模系统中的关键作用，并为任意子编织（anyonic braiding）的实验观测提供了一种不与现有理论框架冲突的稳健解释。

Abstract: Fractional quantum Hall (FQH) colliders measure anyon exchange phases via time-domain braiding, but the $ν=2/5$ state exhibits an intriguing negative Fano factor, challenging theoretical predictions. Here, we study the effect of inter-edge interactions in a multi-mode FQH collider. We demonstrate that the resulting fractionalization into eigenmodes causes the anyon beam to decompose into correlated and uncorrelated components, which have very distinct behavior in terms of time-domain braiding. We show that the uncorrelated part dominates in the long-junction limit, reversing the tunneling current sign and reproducing the observed negative Fano factor at $ν=2/5$. Our results highlight the role of interactions and provide a robust interpretation of anyonic braiding in multi-mode systems.

</details>


### [78] [Spin-Wave Phase Shifter Controlled by a Domain Wall Racetrack](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17804)
*Uladzislau Makartsou,Olena Tartakivska,Paweł Gruszecki,Anton Lutsenko,Sebastiaan van Dijken,Volodymyr V. Kruglyak,Maciej Krawczyk*
