TL;DR: 本文提出了一种由磁畴壁赛道（domain-wall racetrack）控制的自旋波移相器。通过微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulation）展示了在钇铁石榴石（YIG）薄膜上方放置坡莫合金（Permalloy）磁畴壁赛道。赛道中钉扎的畴壁产生的杂散场（stray field）会改变YIG区域中的内磁场，导致自旋波波长局部变化，从而控制通过该区域的Damon-Eshbach自旋波累积的相位。通过移动赛道上的畴壁，同一物理结构可在不改变波导几何形状的情况下提供高达±90度的相移。基于半经典近似的模型证实相移主要由畴壁诱导的杂散场主导。这些结果表明了一条通向紧凑可编程自旋波移相器的路径，可用于基于干涉的磁振子电路（magnonic circuits）进行信息处理。此外，所展示的磁振子器件与磁畴壁赛道的集成可促进其在存内计算（in-memory computing）中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现一种不改变波导几何形状、可编程且紧凑的自旋波移相器，以支持基于干涉的磁振子电路（magnonic circuits）用于信息处理。

Method: 利用微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulation）在YIG薄膜上方构建坡莫合金（Permalloy）磁畴壁赛道（domain-wall racetrack）。通过赛道中钉扎畴壁（pinned domain walls）产生的杂散场（stray field）改变YIG区域的内磁场，从而局部改变自旋波波长以控制相位。采用半经典近似（semiclassical approximation）模型验证相移机制。

Result: 移动赛道上的畴壁可在不改变波导几何形状的条件下实现高达±90度的相移。半经典近似模型证实相移主要由畴壁诱导的杂散场主导。

Conclusion: 研究结果指向一种紧凑可编程自旋波移相器的实现路径，适用于基于干涉的磁振子电路进行信息处理。器件与磁畴壁赛道的集成还有望应用于存内计算（in-memory computing）。

Abstract: We propose a spin-wave phase shifter controlled using a domain-wall racetrack. The concept is demonstrated using micromagnetic simulations of a Permalloy domain-wall racetrack placed above a YIG film. The stray field from pinned domain walls modifies the internal magnetic field in the YIG region under the racetrack. This leads to a local change of the spin-wave wavelength and thereby enables control of the phase accumulated by Damon-Eshbach spin waves propagating through the region. Moving domain walls on the racetrack, the same physical structure can provide phase shifts of up to +/-90 degrees, without changing the waveguide geometry. A model based on the semiclassical approximation confirms that the phase shift is dominated by the domain-wall-induced stray field. These results suggest a route toward a compact programmable spin-wave phase shifter for interference-based magnonic circuits for information processing. Moreover, the demonstrated magnonic device integration with a magnetic domain-wall racetrack can lead to its application in in-memory computing.

### [79] [Tunneling amplifies chirality-induced spin selectivity and explains its current-direction invariance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17823)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者提出一个最小模型，以量子隧穿（quantum tunneling）为输运机制，并引入相互作用诱导的自旋分裂（interaction-induced spin splitting），具体实现为粒子自旋与电流感应磁场之间的弱塞曼相互作用（weak Zeeman interaction）。

Result: 模型表明，量子隧穿与耗散（dissipation）的协同作用能够显著放大微小的自旋依赖微扰效应，使自旋极化率（spin polarization）在较宽偏压范围内达到约100%。该模型自然复现了CISS特有的电流-电压对称性，即自旋极化符号在电流方向反转时保持不变，并完全符合昂萨格倒易关系（Onsager's reciprocity relations）。

Conclusion: 该最小模型成功解释了绝缘手性分子中CISS效应的核心实验现象，揭示了量子隧穿与耗散在放大微弱自旋效应中的关键作用，为理解CISS的微观机制提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We propose a minimal model for chirality-induced spin selectivity (CISS) in dc transport through insulating chiral molecules, based on quantum tunneling and interaction-induced spin splitting. As a concrete realization of the latter, we consider a weak Zeeman interaction of the particle spin with the current-induced magnetic field, recently shown to occur in helical molecules. We show that quantum tunneling, combined with dissipation, amplifies the effect, so that even such a small spin-dependent perturbation can yield spin polarizations on the order of 100\% across a wide range of applied bias voltages. Furthermore, our tunneling scenario naturally reproduces the characteristic CISS symmetry of the current-voltage dependence -- namely, the invariance of the spin-polarization sign under reversal of the current direction -- while fully respecting Onsager's reciprocity relations.

Method: 提出一种由开口谐振环（split-ring resonators）组成的超表面（metasurface）结构，利用偶极模式（dipole mode）与四极模式（quadrupole mode）之间的耦合实现射频光子HOTI。通过数值模拟和1.5-1.7 GHz频段的实验测量验证其拓扑特性，采用印刷电路板（printed circuit board, PCB）技术制作样品。

Result: 数值模拟和实验共同证实，所提出的超表面在1.5-1.7 GHz频段内支持角局域态（corner-localized states）和边缘局域态（edge-localized states），验证了高阶拓扑绝缘体的特征态层级结构。

Conclusion: 该研究展示了一种基于印刷电路板技术的可扩展、易重构GHz频段平台，为光子HOTI的进一步实验研究和微波应用开发迈出了关键步骤。

Abstract: Photonic higher-order topological insulators (HOTI) are characterized by a hierarchy of topologically-protected states with different dimensionalities, making them especially interesting for potential applications that combine strong localization of electromagnetic fields and their robust waveguiding. However, their practical implementation often requires expensive processing techniques and is limited by accessible material parameters. In this paper, we demonstrate that a radio-frequency photonic HOTI can be implemented as a metasurface composed of split-ring resonators with couplings between dipole and quadrupole modes. We verify, by numerical simulations and experimentally at frequencies of 1.5-1.7 GHz, that a proposed metasurface supports corner- and edge-localized states. Our results reveal a scalable and easily reconfigurable GHz-range platform that employs printed circuit board technology, thus making crucial steps required for further experimental studies of photonic HOTI and the development of their microwave applications.

### [81] [Chirality-induced spin selectivity without intrinsic spin-orbit coupling: Role of current-induced molecular orbital moment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17865)
*Sumit Ghosh,Angela Wittmann,Frank Matthes,Daniel E. Bürgler*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于分子轨道矩（molecular orbital moment, MOM）的新理论，以解释螺旋分子中手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）的微观起源。该理论通过分子环流产生的轨道矩与分子手性的关联，成功解释了CISS磁电阻和磁手征电导不对称性，并阐明了电学磁手征各向异性的起源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于界面或散射的CISS理论忽略了分子本身的贡献，而近期实验表明分子自身上存在显著CISS效应，因此亟需建立一种能包含分子贡献的新理论。

Method: 通过分子环中的电荷循环产生分子轨道矩（MOM），其方向由分子结构畸变产生的规范场（gauge field）决定，并与分子手性相关联。

Result: 该MOM能产生有限CISS磁电阻和磁手征电导不对称性（magnetochiral conductance asymmetries），且这些效应在偏压中呈偶函数，不违反昂萨格-卡西米尔互易关系（Onsager-Casimir reciprocity relations）；MOM可通过费米能级和偏压进行外部调控，导致对映体电流-电压（I-V）曲线的额外交叉。

Conclusion: 在同一框架下解释了电学磁手征各向异性（electrical magnetochiral anisotropy）的起源，证明了该理论的普适适用性。

Abstract: The microscopic origin of the chirality-induced spin selectivity (CISS) in helical molecules remains an open question. Recent experiments suggest that a significant contribution to CISS arises from the molecule itself, which is disregarded in existing interfacial or scattering based theories. Here we present an alternative theory of CISS to address this molecular contribution. The mechanism is based on the circulation of charge current in molecular loops that generates a molecular orbital moment (MOM). The direction of the MOM is governed by the gauge field arising from the structural distortion of the molecule and is associated with the handedness of the molecule. Such a MOM can produce finite CISS magnetoresistance and magnetochiral conductance asymmetries that are even in bias voltage, without violating the Onsager-Casimir reciprocity relations. Depending on the Fermi level and bias voltage, the MOM can be controlled externally, which can result in additional crossings of the enantiomer $I-V$ curves. Finally we explain the origin of the electrical magnetochiral anisotropy within the same framework, which establishes its generic applicability.

### [82] [Robust Signatures of Fragile Topology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17870)
*Viktor Könye,Ihor Nimyi,Oleg Janson,Jeroen van den Brink,Jasper van Wezel,Cosma Fulga*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明，虽然脆弱拓扑相（fragile topological phases）通常不具有受保护的边界态，但它们在二维材料中会强制产生体态狄拉克锥（bulk Dirac cones），并提供了一种可通过第一性原理计算和实验直接验证的稳健光谱学特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脆弱拓扑相（fragile topology）被认为缺乏像强拓扑相那样的鲁棒边界态，并且可以通过添加额外价带而被平凡化，因此其是否具有任何可观测的稳健特征尚不明确。本文旨在揭示脆弱拓扑相仍然具有不容忽视的物理可观测后果。

Method: 在具有时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）和二重旋转对称性（twofold rotation symmetry）的系统中，定义了一个脆弱拓扑指标（fragile topological index），该指标保证能带结构中存在能隙闭合点（gap closing points）。通过第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）对五种材料进行了验证。

Result: 所有五种测试材料中均观测到狄拉克点（Dirac points），表明脆弱拓扑导致的体态狄拉克锥是一种普遍现象（widespread phenomenon）。该结果为实验直接探测脆弱拓扑相提供了稳健的光谱学特征（spectroscopic signature），也为在从头算模拟（ab-initio simulations）中寻找狄拉克锥提供了替代方法。

Conclusion: 脆弱拓扑相虽然不具有受保护边界态，但在二维材料中强制产生体态狄拉克锥，这构成一种可直接实验测量的稳健信号。该发现还可用于识别具有非线性输运性质（nonlinear transport properties）的材料。

Abstract: Some topological phases of matter are called fragile. They do not generically host protected gapless boundary states and they can be trivialized by adding additional valence bands. Here we show that fragile topology nevertheless has robust signatures: it yields bulk Dirac cones in two-dimensional materials with arbitrarily many bands. In systems with time-reversal and twofold rotation symmetry, we establish a fragile topological index which guarantees the presence of gap closing points in the band structure. We test this prediction using first-principles calculations in five materials and find that all of them host such Dirac points, suggesting that this is a widespread phenomenon. Our results provide a robust spectroscopic signature of fragile topology which can be directly accessed in experiment. Further, they enable an alternate method for finding Dirac cones in ab-initio simulations, and may be used as a route towards identifying materials with nonlinear transport properties.

### [83] [Torsion-controlled spin transport and tunable intersubband absorption in a screw-dislocated semiconductor nanowire](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17943)
*Carlos Magno O. Pereira,Edilberto O. Silva*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文发展了一套有限半导体纳米线中自旋分辨输运与子带间光学吸收的有效质量理论，揭示了螺位错诱导扭转（torsion）对能带底部、自旋选择区间以及太赫兹共振吸收的调控机制，并在开放量子线模型中统一描述了几何扭转、自旋分辨介观输运、自旋热电势与可调子带间吸收。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 建立能够同时描述有限半导体纳米线中自旋分辨输运与子带间光学吸收的统一理论框架，特别是考察螺位错诱导扭转对能带结构、自旋选择输运及光学共振的调制作用，并纳入有限尺寸效应（如表面边界条件、法布里-珀罗干涉等）的影响。

Method: 采用有效质量理论（effective-mass theory）构建有限半导体纳米线的模型，将活性区域处理为长度为L、半径为R的开放散射区，引入法布里-珀罗干涉（Fabry-Perot interference）、径向边界条件（radial boundary conditions）及表面诱导线宽展宽（surface-induced linewidth broadening）。通过极化率（polarization）和电导对比度（conductance-contrast）图像量化自旋分辨响应的有效线宽判据。

Result: 扭转降低了一维子带的能带底部，轴向磁场解开了两个塞曼分支（Zeeman branches），当费米能级位于两分支极小值之间时形成自旋选择扭转区间（spin-selective torsion interval）；在小塞曼分裂极限下，该区间宽度与塞曼分裂呈线性关系。有限半径子带间吸收在太赫兹（THz）波段产生扭转可调的共振；表面边界条件改变绝对共振频率并修正振子强度（oscillator strength），但主导单位跃迁的扭转斜率∂ω/∂τ≈ℏk_F/m^*保持不变。

Conclusion: 本文提出的理论框架将几何扭转、自旋分辨介观输运、自旋热电势（spin thermopower）与可调子带间吸收统一在单个开放量子线模型（open-quantum-wire model）中，为纳米线中自旋-扭转耦合效应的分析与设计提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We develop an effective-mass theory for spin-resolved transport and intersubband optical absorption in a finite semiconductor nanowire containing a uniform screw-dislocation-induced torsion. The central transport quantity is the band bottom of each torsion-dependent one-dimensional subband: torsion lowers this band bottom while an axial magnetic field resolves the two Zeeman branches, so that a spin-selective torsion interval opens when the Fermi level lies between the two branch minima. We distinguish this band-bottom transport threshold from the fixed-momentum transverse energy that governs the vertical intersubband optical transition, and obtain a design rule for the width of the spin-selective torsion interval that is linear in the Zeeman splitting in the small-splitting limit. Finite-size effects are incorporated by treating the active region as an open scattering region of length $L$ and radius $R$, with Fabry-Perot interference, radial boundary conditions, and surface-induced linewidth broadening. The spin-resolved response remains well defined when the effective linewidth satisfies $Γ_{\mathrm{eff}}\llΔ_Z$, a criterion quantified through polarization and conductance-contrast maps. In the optical sector, finite-radius intersubband absorption gives a torsion-tunable resonance in the THz range; surface boundary conditions shift the absolute resonance frequency and modify the oscillator strength, while, for the dominant unit-branch transition, the leading fixed-momentum torsional slope $\partialω/\partialτ\simeq\hbar k_F/m^*$ is preserved. The resulting framework connects geometric torsion, spin-resolved mesoscopic transport, spin thermopower, and tunable intersubband absorption within a single open-quantum-wire model.

### [84] [Highly nonlinear Moiré exciton and trion polaritons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18077)
*Arnab Barman Ray,Trevor Ollis,Fei Cheng,Adam L. Freidman,Aubrey T. Hanbicki,Anthony Nickolas Vamivakas*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本工作通过在n掺杂MoSe₂/WS₂异质双层的光学微腔中强耦合层杂化激子与三离子（trion），观察到由掺杂电子的Lindhard屏蔽和三离子形成导致的显著非单调非线性响应，并实现了标称扩散长度接近100微米的高速度热极化激元（hot polaritons）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将n掺杂MoSe₂/WS₂异质双层中的层杂化激子与三离子强耦合至光学微腔（optical microcavity）中，通过实验测量其光学非线性响应和极化激元（polariton）的扩散特性。

Result: 掺杂电子的Lindhard屏蔽（Lindhard screening）与三离子的形成导致显著的非单调非线性响应；莫尔超晶格（Moiré superlattice）中电子捕获的缺失对实现非常大的二阶非线性（second-order nonlinearities）至关重要；得到的trion极化激元表现为高速度热极化激元，标称扩散长度（nominal diffusion length）接近100微米。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了掺杂电子与三离子在微腔耦合下对非线性光响应的独特贡献，表明莫尔超晶格中无电子捕获效应是获得强二阶非线性的关键，并通过高迁移率trion极化激元展示了长距离传播的潜力。

Abstract: Moiré multi-layers of transition metal dichalcogenides have been shown to exhibit optical responses that are endowed with a richness that is absent in single monolayers. Much of this can be attributed to the Moiré superlattice that modulates the electronic landscape of these heterostructures. Strongly coupled layer-hybridized excitons in MoSe2/WS2 heterobilayers have been shown to exhibit enhanced optical nonlinearities. In this work we strongly couple layer hybridized excitons and trions in n-doped $\text{MoSe}_2 / \text{WS}_2$ heterobilayers inside an optical microcavity. We find that the additional Lindhard screening from dopant electrons and the formation of trions result in a strikingly non-monotonic nonlinear response. The absence of electron capture in the Moiré superlattice plays a crucial role, promising very large second-order nonlinearities. In this work, trion polaritons manifest as high velocity hot polaritons, reaching nominal diffusion lengths approaching 100 microns.

### [85] [Coherent effects in quantum transport models and their classical counterparts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18224)

Result: 所研究的量子系统中的时间依赖概率分布函数（PDF）展现出与经典连续时间随机游走（CTRW）模型（如 Lévy 行走或扩散扩散率）类似的行为。

### [86] [Stochastic Thermodynamics of Score Matching in Diffusion Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17252)
*Xuehao Ding,H. T. Quan,Yuhai Tu*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文为基于分数（score）的扩散模型（diffusion models）建立了随机热力学（stochastic thermodynamics）框架，揭示了时间不对称熵产生（TAEP）与分数匹配目标（score-matching objective）之间的严格定量关系，阐明了扩散模型优越采样多样性的热力学机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型作为一类强大的生成式AI系统，其动力学包含正向扩散与逆向重建过程，但缺乏对其底层统计力学（statistical mechanics）原理的统一理解。本文旨在建立扩散模型的热力学理论框架，揭示分数匹配目标（score-matching objective）的熵本质。

Method: 引入轨迹依赖量——时间不对称熵产生（time-asymmetry entropy production, TAEP），基于正向与逆向扩散动力学（forward and reverse diffusion dynamics）定义，并证明其满足精确的涨落定理（fluctuation theorems）。分析TAEP的平均值与涨落特性，将其与Hyvärinen隐式分数匹配核（implicit score-matching kernel）和分数匹配目标建立联系。

Result: Hyvärinen的隐式分数匹配核作为TAEP的涨落成分自然出现；平均TAEP与分数匹配目标严格成正比；TAEP的涨落可量化采样的不均匀性（sampling unevenness）并提供数据流形覆盖（data-manifold coverage）的热力学度量。

Conclusion: 定量解释了扩散模型优越的采样多样性；揭示了随机梯度下降（stochastic gradient descent）偏好更平坦、更具泛化性解的热力学机制；建立了扩散生成式AI（diffusion-based generative AI）的基础统计力学原理。

Abstract: Score-based diffusion models are a powerful class of generative AI systems capable of sampling from complex, high-dimensional probability distributions. Their dynamics consist of a forward diffusion process that transforms data into noise and a learned reverse process that reconstructs data by reversing the probability flow. Here, we develop a stochastic thermodynamic framework for diffusion models and their score-matching objective. We introduce a trajectory-dependent quantity, time-asymmetry entropy production (TAEP), defined from the forward and reverse diffusion dynamics, and show that it obeys exact fluctuation theorems. Remarkably, Hyvärinen's implicit score-matching kernel emerges naturally as a fluctuating component of TAEP, while the average TAEP is exactly proportional to the score-matching objective. We further show that fluctuations of TAEP quantify sampling unevenness and provide a thermodynamic measure of data-manifold coverage. These results yield a quantitative explanation for the superior sampling diversity of diffusion models and reveal a thermodynamic mechanism by which stochastic gradient descent favors flatter, more generalizable solutions. By uncovering the entropic nature of score matching, our work establishes fundamental statistical-mechanical principles underlying diffusion-based generative AI.

</details>


### [87] [Hyperuniform charge distributions and phase transitions in a generalized Aubry-André model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17532)
*Lujia Xiang,Junmo Jeon,Shiro Sakai*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该论文通过广义Aubry-André模型研究非周期费米子系统中非均匀电荷分布及其相变，发现多体电荷分布总是超均匀（hyperuniform）的，其超均匀性类别取决于费米能级附近单粒子态的局域化性质，并且超均匀性类别的转变对应一个三级相变（third-order phase transition）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索非周期费米子系统中是否存在不同的非均匀电荷分布，以及它们之间是否存在相变，并寻找一种有效的分类手段来描述这些电荷分布的全局均匀性。

Method: 以广义Aubry-André模型为具体研究对象，利用超均匀性（hyperuniformity）这一量化工具来分类和分析不同填充分数、势能强度和势能形状下的多体电荷分布。

Result: 在所有考察的参数条件下，多体电荷分布总是表现为超均匀，但其超均匀性类别取决于费米能级附近单粒子态的局域化性质，而非高能态的性质。超均匀性类别的变化对应非均匀多体态之间的相变，且该相变为三级相变。

Conclusion: 非周期费米子系统中电荷分布的超均匀性类别可作为区分不同非均匀多体态并标识相变的有效判据，费米能级附近单粒子态的局域化性质在其中起决定性作用。

Abstract: We show the existence of distinct inhomogeneous charge distributions and a phase transition between them in aperiodic fermion systems. Using a generalized Aubry-André model as an example, we obtain various types of charge distributions, which we classify by means of hyperuniformity, a general mean to quantify and classify the global uniformity of spatial distributions. Examining various cases of filling fraction and potential strength and shape, we find that the many-body charge distribution in this model is always hyperuniform, i.e., showing an anomalously suppressed long-range fluctuation, while its hyperuniformity class depends on the localization properties of the states around the Fermi energy, irrespective of those of high-energy states. Namely, the change in the localization properties of these single-particle states leaves a signature in the hyperuniformity class of many-body charge distribution. We further show a change of the hyperuniformity class corresponds to a phase transition between inhomogeneous many-body states, and that it is of the third order.

### [88] [Replica theory for the rate functional of the empirical spectral distribution function of diluted Hermitian matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17868)
*Edgar Guzmán-González,Isaac Pérez Castillo*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 稀疏随机矩阵（sparse random matrix）谱统计的涨落行为缺乏系统的解析描述，尤其是对大偏差（large deviations）尺度下的率泛函缺乏有效的计算框架。

Method: 基于副本方法（replica method）构造缩放累积量生成泛函（scaled cumulant-generating functional）；在副本对称（replica-symmetric）鞍点假设下推导率泛函候选形式；通过泛函导数提取累积量；以未加权的埃尔代什-雷尼随机图（Erdős-Rényi random graph）邻接矩阵作为示例应用。

Result: 导出了经验谱分布函数前两个累积量的显式表达式，指出了更高阶累积量的泛函导数求法；计算了傅里叶系数的率函数（rate function），等价于选定线性谱统计量（linear spectral statistics）的率函数；副本对称预测与精确数值对角化在可达涨落区间内吻合良好。

Conclusion: 所提框架为研究稀疏随机矩阵系综（sparse random matrix ensembles）中谱可观测量的率泛函（rate functional）提供了一个系统基础。

Abstract: We develop a replica-based framework for the scaled cumulant-generating functional of the empirical spectral distribution function $i_C$ of diluted Hermitian random matrices. Within a replica-symmetric saddle-point assumption, this construction yields a candidate rate functional for fluctuations of $i_C$. As an illustrative application, we consider adjacency matrices of unweighted Erdős-Rényi random graphs with mean degree $c$. We derive explicit expressions for the first two cumulants of $i_C$, indicate how higher cumulants can be obtained from further functional derivatives, and compute the rate function of Fourier coefficients, equivalently of selected linear spectral statistics. The replica-symmetric predictions are tested against exact numerical diagonalization and show good agreement in the accessible fluctuation regime. The approach provides a basis for studying rate functionals of spectral observables in sparse random matrix ensembles.

### [89] [Finite and disordered Kitaev chains: a large deviation study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17881)
*Clément Fortin,Kai Wang,Tami Pereg-Barnea*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文利用大偏差理论（large deviations theory）研究无序Kitaev链中拓扑边界态（topological edge states）的有限尺寸效应（finite-size effects），发现Lyapunov指数（Lyapunov exponent）的涨落呈现不对称性（asymmetry），使得马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero modes）的强边界局域化比弱局域化指数级更可能出现，这种不对称性为拓扑边界态提供了额外的抗无序保护，并可用来确定满足拓扑量子计算约束的最小系统尺寸。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑边界态以其抗无序的鲁棒性著称，但无序与系统尺寸之间的相互作用（interplay）尚不清晰。传统中心极限定理（central limit theorem）无法捕捉有限尺寸下的稀有涨落行为，因此需要新框架来定量描述有限尺寸效应对拓扑边界态的影响。

Method: 采用大偏差理论（large deviations theory）作为分析框架，研究静态和周期驱动（periodically driven）无序Kitaev链中的Lyapunov指数（Lyapunov exponent）涨落，并分析其大偏差统计特性。

Result: 发现Lyapunov指数涨落存在不对称性（asymmetry），使得马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero modes）的强边界局域化比弱局域化指数级（exponentially）更可能出现。这种不对称性并非拓扑相（topological phase）所特有，且在多种无序分布（disorder distribution）下均成立。

Conclusion: 该涨落不对称性为拓扑边界态（topological edge states）提供了额外的抗无序保护（additional protection against disorder）。基于所提框架，可以确定满足拓扑量子计算（topological quantum computing）约束所需的最小系统尺寸（minimum system size）。

Abstract: Topological edge states are celebrated for their robustness against disorder, yet the interplay between disorder and system size remains poorly understood. We use large deviations theory as a framework to study finite-size effects beyond the central limit theorem. We analyze Lyapunov exponent fluctuations in the static and periodically driven disordered Kitaev chain and find an asymmetry in the large deviations statistics that makes stronger edge localizations of Majorana zero modes exponentially more likely than weaker ones. We demonstrate that this fluctuation asymmetry is not tied to the topological phase. This asymmetry endows topological edge states with an additional protection against disorder and persists across a broad class of disorder distribution. We show how to use our framework to find the minimum system size required to satisfy topological quantum computing constraints.

</details>


### [90] [Learning Dynamics of Chain-of-Thought State Tracking in a Solvable Transformer Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18164)
*Niklas Forner,Marcel Kühn,Matthias Thamm,Bernd Rosenow*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文通过统计力学平均场描述，解析了一个简化单块Transformer在链式思维（Chain-of-thought）状态追踪任务中的训练动力学，揭示了注意力（attention）检索与MLP逻辑模块的分阶段协同学习机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 链式思维生成能将多步计算转化为局部可检查的状态更新序列，但Transformer如何通过训练获得这种更新能力的动力学机制尚不清楚。

Method: 研究在可解设定下进行：采用由置换合成生成的状态序列，训练一个简化单块Transformer进行监督式下一个词元预测（next-token prediction）。架构将固定延迟动作检索（由旋转位置编码RoPE注意力实现）与专用MLP逻辑模块分离。利用统计力学平均场描述，推导出三个序参量（order parameters）——注意力检索、教师矩阵对齐和离目标逻辑重叠——的动力学方程。

Result: 动力学方程在序参量层面与模拟结果定量匹配；结合对数几率分布近似后，能定性预测最终展开准确率中的尖锐相变（sharp transition）。分析揭示了分阶段学习现象：逻辑模块首先学习混合启发式策略，随后注意力锁定到相关动作，使MLP对齐得以高效进行。

Conclusion: 这些结果提供了一个受控的机制性解释，阐明了基于注意力的检索与基于MLP的逻辑在链式思维状态追踪过程中如何协同发展。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought generation can turn a multi-step computation into a sequence of locally checkable state updates, but the training dynamics by which transformers acquire such updates remain poorly understood. We study this question in a solvable setting: a simplified one-block transformer trained by supervised next-token prediction on state sequences generated by composing permutations. The architecture separates fixed-lag action retrieval, learned by RoPE attention, from a specialized MLP logic module that applies the retrieved permutation to the current state. Using a statistical-physics mean-field description, we derive dynamics for three order parameters measuring attention retrieval, teacher-matrix alignment, and off-target logic overlap. These equations quantitatively match simulations for the order parameters and, combined with a logit-distribution approximation, qualitatively predict the sharp transition in final rollout accuracy. The analysis reveals staged learning: the logic module first learns a mixed heuristic; attention then locks onto the relevant action, enabling efficient MLP alignment. Together, these results provide a controlled mechanistic account of how attention-based retrieval and MLP-based logic co-develop during chain-of-thought state tracking.

</details>

Method: 利用核心坍缩超新星（core-collapse supernovae, SNe）中大量产生的mCPs；利用mCP质量导致的飞行时间（time-of-flight, ToF）延迟，在中微子暴信号过后开辟一个干净的搜索窗口；计算在XENONnT、JUNO、DUNE和Hyper-Kamiokande探测器中mCP引发的电子反冲（electron-recoil）信号。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了一种有前景的mCP探测新途径，有望显著提升对毫电荷粒子的探测灵敏度。

Abstract: This work proposes a new terrestrial probe for millicharged particles (mCPs) and demonstrates promising discovery prospects. mCPs can be copiously produced in core-collapse supernovae (SNe), and a fraction may escape, travel to Earth and yield distinct signals. The mCP mass induces a time-of-flight (ToF) delay relative to the SN neutrino burst, opening a clean search window after the neutrino signal has passed. We compute the mCP-induced electron-recoil signals at XENONnT, JUNO, DUNE, and Hyper-Kamiokande for benchmark SN scenarios, and find that for $\varepsilon = 10^{-9}$ and sub-MeV to MeV-scale masses, more than 10 events per year can be detected. This search can improve upon existing SN cooling bound on $\varepsilon$ by up to an order of magnitude.

### [92] [Are neutrinos Majorana? Fixed-target and high-energy astrophysical searches decide](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17132)
*Gabriela Barenboim,Mauricio Bustamante,Qinrui Liu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通过重中性轻子（HNL）探测中微子马约拉纳性质的新方法，结合SHiP实验与中微子望远镜的联合信号，可绕过无中微子双贝塔衰变的盲区，区分中微子是狄拉克费米子还是马约拉纳费米子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中微子是狄拉克费米子（Dirac fermion）还是马约拉纳费米子（Majorana fermion）仍是基本开放问题；传统无中微子双贝塔衰变（neutrinoless double beta decay）探测存在盲区（blind spots），需提出互补性新探针。

Method: 利用重中性轻子（heavy neutral lepton, HNL）引发活性中微子味混合（flavor mixing）的高能偏移，该偏移仅在中微子为马约拉纳费米子时发生。对GeV能标HNL，通过束流倾注实验SHiP直接探测；对TeV–PeV能标，利用天体物理中微子散射探测味比例偏移，不依赖源处味成分。

Result: SHiP可发现HNL并测量其与活性中微子味的混合；中微子望远镜可探测到天体物理中微子到达地球时味比例的偏移；该味偏移对μ子和τ子味扇区最敏感，可绕过无中微子双贝塔衰变的盲区。

Conclusion: 若SHiP与下一代中微子望远镜观测到关联信号，则证明中微子是马约拉纳费米子；若无信号，则支持中微子为狄拉克费米子。

Abstract: Determining whether the neutrino is a Dirac or Majorana fermion remains a fundamental open question. Conventional searches rely on neutrinoless double beta decay, but this electron-only channel suffers from blind spots. We propose a new, complementary probe to overcome this limitation. A heavy neutral lepton (HNL) triggers a high-energy shift in how the active neutrino flavors ($ν_e$, $ν_μ$, $ν_τ$) mix -- but only if the neutrinos are Majorana. For GeV-scale HNLs, the upcoming beam-dump experiment SHiP can discover the HNL and measure how it mixes with the active flavors. Separately, the scattering of TeV--PeV astrophysical neutrinos can resolve the HNL, revealing a shift in the proportions of each flavor arriving at Earth that could be detected by neutrino telescopes, regardless of the unknown flavor composition at the astrophysical neutrino sources. Because this flavor shift is most sensitive to the muon and tau sectors, it bypasses the blind spots of neutrinoless double beta decay. A correlated signal at SHiP and next-generation neutrino telescopes would prove that neutrinos are Majorana; its absence would point to them being Dirac.

### [93] [Quantum decoherence of hyperon spin correlations in QCD hadronization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17240)
*Feng Liu,Zhoudunming Tu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个受量子信息科学启发的框架，认为强子化（hadronization）过程中量子色动力学（QCD）真空激发的正反夸克对继承了其量子数，产生自旋纠缠（spin entanglement），而弦断裂（string breaking）则引入环境自由度导致自旋态的量子退相干（quantum decoherence），从而解释了Λ超子自旋关联实验数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统林德弦模型（Lund string model）在半经典层面成功描述了强子化过程，但未能回答“量子性在强子化中去了哪里”这一根本问题。该研究旨在从量子信息科学的角度建立强子化与量子纠缠和退相干之间的量化联系。

Method: 提出一个基于量子信息科学的框架：(i) 从QCD真空中激发的正反夸克对继承真空的量子数，在其产生时形成自旋纠缠；(ii) 随后的弦断裂过程产生环境自由度，诱发自旋态的量子退相干。

Result: 该框架同时描述了在RHIC [Nature 650, 65-71 (2026)] 和LHC测量的Λ超子自旋关联数据。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了QCD真空、自旋纠缠与退相干、以及强子化过程之间的定量联系。

Abstract: Hadronization, the transition of quarks and gluons into hadrons, lies beyond the reach of perturbative quantum chromodynamics (QCD) and is commonly described by the semiclassical Lund string model. Yet this very success raises a fundamental question: where does the quantumness go during hadronization? In this Letter, we propose an approach inspired by quantum information science, in which (i) quark-antiquark pairs excited from the QCD vacuum inherit its quantum numbers, giving rise to spin entanglement at their creation, and (ii) subsequent string breaking generates environmental degrees of freedom that induce quantum decoherence of the spin state. This framework simultaneously describes the $Λ$ hyperon spin-correlation data measured at RHIC [Nature 650, 65-71 (2026)] and at the LHC, establishing a quantitative connection between the QCD vacuum, spin entanglement and decoherence, and hadronization.

</details>


### [94] [Semi-analytical results for $e^+e^-\to J/ψ+ X_{{\rm non\,}c\bar{c}}$ up to $\mathcal{O}(α_s v^2)$ at B factories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17827)
*Cong Li,Hao-Yang Liu,Xu-Dong Huang,Wen-Long Sang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文在非相对论QCD（NRQCD）因子化框架下，首次计算了B工厂中$e^+e^- \to J/ψ + X_{{\rm non\,}c\bar{c}}$过程的$\mathcal{O}(α_s v^2)$修正，并验证了该阶次下NRQCD因子化的有效性。通过微分方程方法获得了高精度短距系数渐近展开，预言的总截面与Belle实验测量一致，但角分布参数与实验值存在超过$2σ$的偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 精确检验NRQCD因子化框架在高阶修正下的有效性，并系统研究B工厂能量下$J/ψ$非伴随产生过程的微扰QCD（perturbative QCD）和相对论修正，以解释实验测量中可能存在的理论—实验偏差。

Method: 在NRQCD因子化框架内计算色单态（color-singlet）贡献，分别计算$\mathcal{O}(α_s)$、$\mathcal{O}(v^2)$和$\mathcal{O}(α_s v^2)$修正；采用微分方程方法（differential equation method）将短距系数（short-distance coefficients）展开为$r = m_c/\sqrt{s}$的渐近级数至$r^{40}$阶。

Result: 首次获得$\mathcal{O}(α_s v^2)$修正，并验证该阶次下NRQCD因子化的有效性；渐近展开在B工厂能量下达到极高精度，截面相对误差约$10^{-14}$，角分布相对误差约$10^{-7}$。$\mathcal{O}(α_s)$修正达到领头阶截面的约50%，而$\mathcal{O}(v^2)$和$\mathcal{O}(α_s v^2)$修正意外地小。考虑$ψ(2S)$馈入贡献后，预言总截面$0.530_{-0.113}^{+0.122}$ pb与Belle测量一致。

Conclusion: 总截面预测与实验吻合，但角分布参数$0.120_{-0.019}^{+0.027}$与Belle实验值$5.71\pm 2.51$存在超过$2σ$的显著偏差，表明当前理论框架对角分布描述可能仍不充分，需要进一步的实验和理论研究。

Abstract: Within the NRQCD factorization framework, we investigate the color-singlet contribution to $e^+e^- \to J/ψ+ X_{{\rm non\,}c\bar{c}}$ at B factories, computing the $\mathcal{O}(α_s)$, $\mathcal{O}(v^2)$, and $\mathcal{O}(α_s v^2)$ corrections to both the unpolarized cross section and the $J/ψ$ angular distribution. The $\mathcal{O}(α_s v^2)$ correction is obtained for the first time, and the validity of NRQCD factorization at this order is explicitly verified. Using the differential equation method, the short-distance coefficients are obtained as asymptotic expansions in $r = m_c/\sqrt{s}$ up to $r^{40}$, which reproduce exact results with high precision at B factory energies, achieving relative errors around $10^{-14}$ for the cross section and around $10^{-7}$ for the angular distribution. Notably, with the same input parameters, our $\mathcal{O}(α_s)$ and $\mathcal{O}(v^2)$ corrections are consistent with those reported in the literature. Phenomenologically, the $\mathcal{O}(α_s)$ correction (with $μ_R=\sqrt{s}/2$) reaches about $50\%$ of the leading-order cross section, while the $\mathcal{O}(v^2)$ and $\mathcal{O}(α_s v^2)$ corrections are accidentally small. After including feeddown contributions from $ψ(2S)$, the predicted cross section $0.530_{-0.113}^{+0.122}$ pb agrees with the {\tt Belle} measurement within uncertainties. However, the predicted angular distribution parameter $0.120_{-0.019}^{+0.027}$ deviates from the experimental value $5.71\pm 2.51$ by more than $2σ$, calling for further experimental and theoretical investigations.

### [95] [Fourier-Preconditioned Path Deformations for Multi-Field Vacuum Tunnelling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17485)
*Suriyah R. Kannagi,Aadarsh Singh,Sudhir K Vempati*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 提出了一种端点安全的傅里叶方法（endpoint-safe Fourier method），用于多场真空隧穿（multi-field vacuum tunnelling）路径的优化与求解。该方法将隧穿路径表示为直线内插加正弦模式形变，利用JAX自动微分框架实现有限维路径优化，既可作为独立变分拟设，也可作为现有弹跳解算器（bounce solver）的预处理手段。在多个基准测试中，该方法在亚百分水平与现有算法一致，并可显著加速高维计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多场真空隧穿问题的数值求解在高维场空间（high-dimensional field space）中面临计算效率瓶颈，现有弹跳解算器（bounce solver）在不同场景下各自存在缺陷。作者希望开发一种兼具解析拟设的简单性与全数值算法的精度的方法，并能作为预处理工具降低现有求解器的计算成本。

Method: 将场空间（field space）中的隧穿路径写为假真空（false vacuum）与真真空（true vacuum）之间的直线内插（straight-line interpolation）加上在端点处消失的正弦模式形变（sine-mode deformation），从而将问题转化为有限维路径优化问题。该优化在JAX数值框架中通过自动微分（automatic differentiation）实现；同时比较了多种端点安全基函数（endpoint-safe basis family），并验证了傅里叶正弦模式（Fourier sine mode）作为默认选择的鲁棒性。

Result: 在OptiBounce基准势（$N_φ=3,\ldots,20$）及嵌套随机系数势族（$N_φ=50$）上，该方法与FindBounce、OptiBounce和CosmoTransitions在常规基准情形下符合至亚百分水平（sub-percent level），且仅需少量模式。作为初始化工具时，在CosmoTransitions中减少了后续路径形变的步数；在FindBounce点注入测试中，高维情形下运行时间最多降低90%。

Conclusion: 端点安全的傅里叶路径（endpoint-safe Fourier path）在简单的解析路径拟设（analytic path ansatz）与全数值的多场弹跳算法（multi-field bounce algorithm）之间建立起了一座有效的桥梁，兼具拟设的灵活性与数值求解的效率改进。

Abstract: We present an endpoint-safe Fourier method for multi-field vacuum tunnelling. The field-space tunnelling path is written as a straight-line interpolation between the false and true vacua, plus sine-mode deformations that vanish at the endpoints. This gives a finite-dimensional path optimisation problem, which we implement using automatic differentiation in the JAX numerical framework. The method is studied both as a standalone variational ansatz for curved tunnelling paths and as a preconditioner for existing bounce solvers. On the OptiBounce benchmark potential for $N_φ=3,\ldots,20$ and on a nested random-coefficient potential family up to $N_φ=50$, the Fourier result agrees with FindBounce, OptiBounce, and CosmoTransitions at the sub-percent level in the regular benchmark cases, while requiring only a modest number of modes. We also compare several endpoint-safe basis families and find that Fourier sine modes provide a robust default for smooth tunnelling paths. When used as an initialiser, the Fourier path supplies useful geometric information to existing solvers before the final bounce calculation is carried out. In the CosmoTransitions tests, this reduces the number of steps in subsequent path deformation, while in the FindBounce point-injection tests, it gives large runtime improvements in the high-dimensional cases up to 90 $\%$. These results suggest that endpoint-safe Fourier paths provide a useful bridge between simple analytic path ansätze and fully numerical multi-field bounce algorithms.

</details>

### [96] [Retrocausal capacity of a quantum channel: Communicating through noisy closed timelike curves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2509.08965)
*Kaiyuan Ji,Seth Lloyd,Mark M. Wilde*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了通过含噪后选闭合类时曲线（postselected closed timelike curve）实现量子信道逆向因果通信（retrocausal communication）的容量问题，完整刻画了单次逆向因果量子容量和经典容量，并证明渐近容量分别等于信道的最大信息量（max-information）与正则化Doeblin信息量（regularized Doeblin information）的平均值和总和，从而赋予这些信息测度新的操作性解释。该刻画可推广至所有完全正映射（completely positive maps），并适用于后选量子隐形传态（postselected teleportation）及黑洞终态模型（black-hole final-state models）等场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究量子信道在逆向因果（retrocausal communication）条件下的通信容量问题，即信息从未来发送者通过后选闭合类时曲线（postselected closed timelike curve）向过去接收者传输的能力。

Method: 通过数学刻画闭合类时曲线为信道模型，完整表征了单次（one-shot）逆向因果量子容量和经典容量，并推导了渐近容量（asymptotic capacities）与最大信息量（max-information）及正则化Doeblin信息量（regularized Doeblin information）之间的等价关系。

Result: 单次逆向因果量子容量和经典容量被完全刻画；渐近逆向因果量子容量等于信道的最大信息量（max-information）的平均值之和，经典容量等于正则化Doeblin信息量（regularized Doeblin information）的总和。该结果对任意完全正映射（completely positive maps）均成立。

Conclusion: 该研究为最大信息量和Doeblin信息量赋予了新的操作性解释，并将信息论极限推广到任意初始和终态边界条件下的后选量子隐形传态（postselected teleportation）机制，涵盖多种黑洞终态模型（black-hole final-state models）。

Abstract: We study the capacity of a quantum channel for retrocausal communication, where messages are transmitted backward in time, from a sender in the future to a receiver in the past, through a noisy postselected closed timelike curve mathematically represented by the channel. We completely characterize the one-shot retrocausal quantum and classical capacities, and we show that the corresponding asymptotic capacities are equal to the average and sum, respectively, of the channel's max-information and its regularized Doeblin information. This endows these information measures with a novel operational interpretation. Furthermore, our characterization can be generalized beyond quantum channels to all completely positive maps. This imposes information-theoretic limits on transmitting messages via postselected-teleportation-like mechanisms with arbitrary initial- and final-state boundary conditions, including those considered in various black-hole final-state models.

### [97] [Canonical regularization of the stationary Coulomb problem and an Aufbau-like spectral ordering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17359)
*Anand Aruna Kumar*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过正则化德布罗意-玻姆表示（regularized de Broglie–Bohm representation）对氢原子进行分析，引入类朗格（Langer-like）逆平方修正，从而打破库仑简并（Coulomb degeneracy），使能级序列遵循Aufbau/Madelung排序规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 静止氢原子在轨道能级间存在库仑简并（Coulomb degeneracy），而Aufbau/Madelung排序是一个基于经验的多电子规则。本文旨在从解析角度探索单中心库仑问题中能谱排序的起源。

Method: 采用正则化德布罗意-玻姆表示（regularized de Broglie–Bohm representation），通过定态振幅流约束（stationary amplitude current constraints）生成可分离的斯图姆-刘维尔分支（Sturm–Liouville branches），并对径向、轨道和磁扇区引入正则化的类朗格逆平方修正（Langer-like inverse square corrections）。

Result: 修正后的边值问题允许解析求解，产生带有正则化径向与角向指标的类氢能谱；径向库仑量子化获得轨道依赖的偏移，从而消除库仑简并，使能级排序遵循Aufbau/Madelung序列；l=0扇区仍保留标准简并里德伯序列（Rydberg sequence）；分离振幅由非整数参数的一般化特殊函数（包括缔合拉盖尔、勒让德和贝塞尔函数）表示。

Conclusion: 该处理旨在作为正则化单中心库仑问题中能谱排序的解析检验，而非替代多电子原子结构理论。

Abstract: The stationary hydrogen atom has Coulomb degeneracy across orbital levels, whereas the Aufbau/Madelung ordering is an empirical, many-electron rule established in atomic physics. We examine the hydrogen atom through a regularized de Broglie--Bohm representation, in which stationary amplitude current constraints generate separable Sturm--Liouville branches. In this formulation, the radial, orbital, and magnetic sectors acquire canonical Langer-like inverse square corrections. The modified boundary value problems allow analytical solutions and produce a hydrogen-like spectrum with regularized radial and angular indices. Consequently, radial Coulomb quantization acquires an orbital dependent shift, lifting the Coulomb degeneracy and producing a spectral ordering that follows the Aufbau/Madelung sequence.
  On this basis, we construct the ordering of the regularized de Broglie--Bohm states and show that the spectral structure retains the standard degenerate Rydberg sequence in the l=0 sector. The separated amplitudes are represented by generalized special function branches, including the associated Laguerre, Legendre, and Bessel functions with non-integral parameters arising from regularized separation. Therefore, the treatment is intended as an analytical examination of spectral ordering in a regularized one center Coulomb problem rather than as a replacement for the many electron atomic structure theory.
  Keywords: de Broglie--Bohm representation; Coulomb spectrum; canonical regularization; Langer correction; Sturm--Liouville equations; Aufbau principle; Madelung ordering; associated Legendre functions; associated Laguerre functions; Bessel functions.

</details>


### [98] [Kinematic properties of the Pauli equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17548)
*E. E. Perepelkin,B. I. Sadovnikov,N. G. Inozemtseva,V. A. Svetovidov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于Wigner-Vlasov形式论研究了Pauli方程的运动学性质，揭示了概率流可分解为对应不同自旋分量的子流叠加，并推导了考虑自旋-磁场相互作用的Hamilton-Jacobi方程和运动方程系统，通过均匀磁场与非对称二次势中的精确解进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子力学框架中，Pauli方程的概率流结构及其与自旋分量的对应关系尚不清晰，且缺乏将自旋-磁场相互作用（spin-magnetic field interaction）纳入Hamilton-Jacobi方程系统的完整表述。

Method: 采用Wigner-Vlasov形式论（Wigner-Vlasov formalism）作为理论框架，对Pauli方程进行运动学分析；通过概率流的分解，导出带有膨胀系数（expansion coefficients）的自旋分量概率流表达式；进一步推导包含自旋-磁场耦合的Hamilton-Jacobi方程组与运动方程，并在均匀磁场与非对称二次势（asymmetric quadratic potential）中求解精确解以说明应用。

Result: 证明了Pauli方程的概率流可表示为两个子流的叠加，每个子流对应旋量（spinor）的一个特定分量，膨胀系数作为权重函数决定各分量的概率贡献；每个自旋投影对应各自的概率流（probability flux）。建立了新的Hamilton-Jacobi方程组和电磁场中的运动方程系统，明确纳入了自旋与磁场的相互作用。

Conclusion: 本文的理论推导拓展了对Pauli方程概率流运动学结构的理解，所获得的方程系统为处理含自旋-磁场相互作用的量子系统提供了新的分析工具；精确解的展示验证了该框架的可行性与有效性。

Abstract: Based on the Wigner-Vlasov formalism, this paper investigates the kinematic properties of the Pauli equation. It is shown that the probability current associated with the Pauli equation can be represented as a superposition of two currents with certain expansion coefficients. Each of these currents corresponds to a particular component of the spinor. The expansion coefficients effectively serve as weighting functions that determine the probability contribution of the corresponding spinor component. Therefore, each spin projection corresponds to its own probability flux. A new system of the Hamilton-Jacobi equations and also a system of motion equations in electromagnetic fields are obtained, taking into account the interaction between the spin and the magnetic field. To illustrate how these equations can be applied we have investigated the quantum system kinematics in detail using an exact solution of the Pauli equation in the presence of a uniform magnetic field and an asymmetric quadratic potential.

</details>


### [99] [On the entanglement induced by the deformation of phase-space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17587)
*Shilpa Nandi,Shatarupa Maity,Pinaki Patra*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了非对易（noncommutative）相空间变形所诱导的纠缠现象，将正偏转置（PPT）可分离性判据推广至一般Bopp平移类，发现变形参数θ和η会诱导纠缠，并针对各向异性二维谐振子进行了具体应用。同时，提出了一个思想实验（gedankenexperiment），通过协方差矩阵检测输出光电流来识别相空间非对易性——即量子引力（quantum gravity）的信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多数量子引力理论认为时空基本概念与非对易空间相容，但如何通过纠缠现象探测相空间非对易性仍缺乏系统研究。本文旨在建立相空间变形与纠缠之间的理论联系，并提出可行的实验验证方案。

Method: 将正偏转置（PPT）判据（用于双粒子高斯态可分离性）推广到一般Bopp平移类；同时考虑位置-位置非对易性（参数θ）和动量-动量非对易性（参数η），对二维各向异性谐振子应用Peres-Horodecki可分离性条件。

Result: 变形参数θ和η均能诱导纠缠；双粒子高斯态在变形空间中几乎总是纠缠的；Peres-Horodecki条件给出了谐振子在非对易空间中的参数约束方程。

Conclusion: 通过协方差矩阵测量输出光电流的思想实验可以检验：若在通常对易空间中本应可分离的高斯态实际表现为纠缠态，则纠缠由中间背景的非对易空间产生，这将成为量子引力量子性质的信号。

Abstract: Most quantum gravity theories propose that the fundamental concept of space-time is mostly compatible with quantum theory in noncommutative (NC) space. In the present paper, we revisit the notion of entanglement induced by NC deformations of phase space. The positive partial transpose (PPT) criterion for separability of bipartite Gaussian states is extended to a general class of Bopp's shift. In particular, we have considered both the position-position and momentum-momentum noncommutativity, with deformation parameters $θ$ and $η$, respectively. It turns out that $θ$ and $η$ induce the entanglement. We have directly applied the formalism for an anisotropic two-dimensional harmonic oscillator. Peres-Horodecki separability condition leads to a constraint equation for the parameter values of the oscillator in NC space. It turns out that the bipartite Gaussian state is almost always entangled in deformed space. To implement the theoretical idea, we provide an outline for a gedankenexperiment to identify the signature of phase-space noncommutativity, i.e., quantum gravity. In particular, the gedankenexperiment is devised to test the separability of supposedly separable Gaussian states in the usual commutative space, through the covariance matrix, which is constructed via measured output photocurrents after interaction of input Gaussian states and reference states. If the experiment shows that the supposedly separable states are actually entangled, then the entanglement is created through the intermediate background noncommutative space, which is a signature of the quantum nature of gravity.

### [100] [Quantum Computing Algebra (QCA), the theory and implementation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17621)
*Jaroslav Hrdina,Dietmar Hildenbrand,Oliver Rettig*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于实几何代数（real geometric algebra）的框架QCA，通过分裂符号差构造直接转换狄拉克形式（Dirac formalism）为几何代数表示，并利用GAALOP软件实现量子门和多量子比特系统的高效计算，在量子博弈论（quantum game theory）中展示了实代数表述的计算优势。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用分裂符号差（split-signature）构造的实几何代数框架QCA，直接将狄拉克形式转为几何代数表示；并基于GAALOP软件实现量子门和多量子比特系统的计算生成。

Result: 在量子博弈论（quantum game theory）中，实代数表述为纠缠策略（entangled strategies）和量子相互作用的建模提供了计算优势。

Abstract: We present a real geometric algebra framework designed for the direct translation of the Dirac formalism into geometric algebra representations. Unlike previous approaches based on positive-definite signatures, QCA employs a split-signature construction that enables a natural realization of quantum states and operators while simplifying computational implementation. We further present an implementation of QCA using the \textit{GAALOP} software and show how quantum gates and multi-qubit systems can be efficiently represented and generated computationally. As an application, we demonstrate the use of QCA in quantum game theory, where the real-algebraic formulation provides computational advantages for modeling entangled strategies and quantum interactions. The proposed framework establishes a practical bridge between the abstract formalism of quantum computation and efficient geometric algebra implementations.

### [101] [Induced Resource Theories and Harvesting via Quantum Probes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17287)
*Ron Nyström,Simone Cepollaro,Nicola Pranzini,Stefano Cusumano,Alioscia Hamma,Esko Keski-Vakkuri*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个理论框架，用于分析当一个具有明确定义资源理论（resource theory）的量子系统（探针）与一个缺乏资源理论描述的环境（如量子场）相互作用时，能否以及如何通过探针中资源的获取来推断环境的状态。研究确定了将探针中的资源生成解释为环境存在资源的条件，从而为环境引入了有效的资源概念。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有资源理论通常要求系统具有明确的自由操作（free operations）和资源态定义，但在探针-环境相互作用场景中，环境往往缺乏这种资源理论描述；此外，探针与环境的相互作用可能本身不是自由操作，或自由操作的概念根本无法定义。因此，需要澄清在这种不对称或非标准条件下，能否以及如何从探针的资源变化中推断环境的状态。

Method: 提出一个通用框架，系统性地定义了在探针-环境相互作用下，将探针中的资源生成解释为环境存在资源的精确条件（precise conditions）。该框架超越了完全受控的资源理论设定，允许在不要求环境具有完整资源理论描述的情况下分析资源获取（resource harvesting）过程。

Result: 明确了在何种意义上可以认为资源是从环境中“获取”的，并给出了使这种解释成立的条件。结果表明，即使在探针-环境相互作用不是自由操作或无法定义自由操作的情况下，探针中的资源生成仍可被用作环境中存在资源的证据，从而为环境引入了一种有效的资源概念（effective notion of resources）。

Conclusion: 该工作为分析超越完全受控资源理论场景下的资源获取过程提供了系统化的方法，并可能为更一般地理解不同量子资源之间的相互作用（interplay of different quantum resources）迈出一步。

Abstract: We consider scenarios in which a quantum system with a well-defined resource theory is used as a probe to interact with an environment, such as a quantum field, for which a resource-theoretic description is absent or incomplete. We clarify if and how the harvesting of a resource in the probe can tell us about the state of the environment. This is particularly ambiguous when the probe-environment interaction is not a free operation, or the concept of such free operations cannot be defined altogether. We propose a framework and precise conditions under which it becomes possible to interpret resource generation on the probe as evidence of resources in the environment, thereby introducing an effective notion of resources for the latter. Our results clarify in which sense resources can be said to be harvested from the environment and provide a systematic way to analyse such processes beyond fully controlled resource-theoretic settings. More generally, this work may provide a step towards a more general understanding of the interplay of different quantum resources.

</details>


### [102] [Emergent de Sitter Space and Non-Unitary Tensor Networks from Non-Hermitian Quantum Criticality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17983)

Abstract: Extending the holographic principle to de Sitter (dS) spacetimes remains one of the most vital open frontiers in quantum gravity, where a microscopic, bottom-up tensor-network framework that relates boundary quantum data to emergent de Sitter spacetime is still lacking. In this work, we first show the emergence of de Sitter spacetime from boundary entanglement by formulating a non-unitary continuous multi-scale entanglement renormalization ansatz (cMERA) for a concrete non-Hermitian critical fermion chain. Within this emergent spacetime, we analyze the associated geodesics and show that they act as extremal Ryu-Takayanagi (RT) surfaces undergoing a smooth timelike-to-null transition. Remarkably, we demonstrate that this continuum trajectory dictates a distinct tensor-network architecture in which the bond-counting contribution naturally truncates at the discrete timelike-to-null transition toward the deep infrared. In the resulting architecture, the null ray along the horizon is represented by zero-cost links, since the associated cut severs no tensor legs. This network structure successfully reproduces the logarithmic scaling of non-unitary critical entanglement entropy, offering a bond-counting picture for the de Sitter RT formula. Our results provide the long-sought dS/(c)MERA correspondence at the level of both emergent spacetime and discrete holographic entanglement.

### [103] [Projected logical ensembles in surface codes via the random-matrix theory of quantum dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17140)
*Mircea Bejan,Jan Behrends,Max McGinley,Benjamin Béri*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了拓扑纠错码在执行确定性幺正门后，通过综合征提取和最大似然解码产生的测量后逻辑态统计性质，提出了“投影逻辑系综”（projected logical ensemble, PLE），并将其与介观物理中量子点的散射矩阵系综建立同构关系，发现在特定条件下PLE趋近于一种受对称性和解码器约束的最大随机系综，对应Altland-Zirnbauer类D或DIII。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究聚焦于受均匀单量子比特泡利-X旋转（Pauli-X rotations）作用的表面码（surface codes）。在执行综合征提取（syndrome extraction）和最大似然解码（maximum-likelihood decoding）后，定义了一个Born权重系综——投影逻辑系综（projected logical ensemble, PLE）。通过证明具有单一逻辑量子比特的码的PLE与从二维马约拉纳网络模型（2D Majorana network model）中得到的介观量子点散射矩阵系综同构，从而利用随机矩阵理论进行分析。

Result: 发现了量子点呈现混沌行为的参数区间，其散射矩阵可用随机矩阵理论很好地描述。在此区间内，PLE趋近于一个在对称性和解码器约束下最大随机的普适系综。对称性约束由稳定子（stabilizer）和逻辑算子（logical operator）权重决定，实现了Altland-Zirnbauer类D或DIII，文中对两者均进行了说明。

Conclusion: 研究结果建立了介观物理、量子多体系统和量子纠错中涌现普适性概念之间的基本联系。

Abstract: Measurements underpin active quantum error correction (QEC) and have been recognized as a source of novel measurement-induced many-body phenomena. Here, we study the statistical properties of post-measurement logical states arising in QEC on topological codes subject to deterministic transversal unitary gates. Upon syndrome extraction followed by maximum-likelihood decoding, a Born-weighted ensemble arises which we dub the "projected logical ensemble" (PLE). Focusing on surface codes subject to uniform single-qubit Pauli-$X$ rotations, we characterize the measurement-induced randomness of the PLE. To this end, we show that for a code with a single logical qubit, the PLE is isomorphic to an ensemble of scattering matrices describing mesoscopic quantum dots obtained from a 2D Majorana network model with suitable boundary conditions. We uncover regimes where these quantum dots are chaotic such that their scattering matrices are well-described by random matrix theory. In these regimes, the PLE approaches a universal ensemble that is maximally random up to symmetry and decoder-induced constraints. The symmetry constraints, set by stabilizer and logical operator weights, realize Altland-Zirnbauer classes D or DIII, which we both illustrate. Our results establish a fundamental connection between emergent universality concepts in mesoscopic physics, quantum many-body systems, and QEC.

### [104] [Fermionic Hamiltonian engineering with local control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17158)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一种基于共轭（conjugating）系统哈密顿量下的自由演化与实验可行的局域费米子幺正（local fermionic unitary）操作序列的新框架。通过线性规划（linear program）高效获取所需的序列和自由演化时间，将系统演化与这些局域幺正操作交错进行，从而实现目标哈密顿量下的有效时间演化，并对有限脉冲时间误差（finite-pulse-time error）具有内在鲁棒性。

Result: 该方法能够实现任意复杂隧穿系数（complex tunnelling coefficient），仅受底层系统哈密顿量的连接性（connectivity）约束。在1088模晶格上的非相互作用Harper-Hofstadter模型以及具有复杂隧穿系数的相互作用Fermi-Hubbard链上展示了该方法的动力学工程能力。

Conclusion: 所提方法在构造上避免了Floquet工程（Floquet engineering）中固有的连续能量吸收（continuous energy absorption）问题，为费米子系统的哈密顿量工程提供了一种高效且鲁棒的实现途径。

Abstract: Quantum simulators enable the exploration of complex quantum phenomena in condensed-matter systems by reproducing their dynamics on controllable quantum devices. However, experimental constraints often restrict the class of Hamiltonians that can be realized natively. Hamiltonian engineering addresses this limitation by expanding the set of accessible target Hamiltonians from a fixed system Hamiltonian defined by the hardware. We introduce a new framework for fermionic Hamiltonian engineering based on conjugating free evolution under the system Hamiltonian with sequences of experimentally feasible local fermionic unitaries. The required sequences and free-evolution times are obtained efficiently via a linear program. By interleaving system evolution with these local unitaries, our method realizes effective time evolution under a broad class of target Hamiltonians, with intrinsic robustness to finite-pulse-time errors. In particular, we demonstrate that arbitrary complex tunnelling coefficients can be realized, constrained only by the connectivity of the underlying system Hamiltonian. We illustrate this capability by engineering the dynamics of the non-interacting Harper-Hofstadter model on a 1088-mode lattice and an interacting Fermi-Hubbard chain with complex tunnelling coefficients. By construction, our approach avoids the continuous energy absorption inherent to Floquet engineering.

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明柱形约束下的狄拉克（Dirac）本征态具有确定的螺旋守恒流纹理，即使是在零轨道角动量（l=0）通道中。由此导出的自旋选择性耦合由狄拉克流纹理与标量手性势（chiral scalar potential）共同产生，形成一种几何选择定则，为手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）等自旋极化现象提供了最小化的静态狄拉克几何核（static Dirac-geometric kernel）描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在手性诱导自旋选择性（chirality-induced spin selectivity, CISS）等自旋极化现象中，狄拉克方程在约束几何下的基本响应机制尚不清晰。本文旨在识别在标准狄拉克理论框架内、无需外磁场或自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）的情况下，由约束狄拉克模式自身流纹理产生的最小静态自旋选择核（spin-selective kernel）。

Method: 理论推导。首先分析柱形约束下狄拉克本征态（Dirac eigenstates）的流纹理结构，包括其螺旋守恒流（helical conserved-current）和零轨道角动量通道（l=0）中的非零 azimuthal 分量。进一步推导静态手性标量势（static chiral scalar potential）作用于约束 l=0 狄拉克模式时产生的通道分辨矩阵元核（channel-resolved matrix-element kernel）。

Result: 柱形约束中狄拉克本征态即使在 l=0 通道也具有确定的螺旋流纹理，最低约束模式中狄拉克流（Dirac current）包含非零 azimuthal 分量与纵向输运分量，且在两个自旋分辨扇区（spin-resolved sectors）中呈现相反手性。由此推导出的自旋选择耦合满足几何选择定则：对角通道（diagonal channels）消失，而离对角转换通道（off-diagonal conversion channels）存活。耦合强度由内部采样流重叠积分 J_chi(k) 控制，该积分度量手性径向分布与自旋向上 azimuthal 狄拉克流密度（spin-up azimuthal Dirac-current density）的空间重叠。

Conclusion: 本文在标准狄拉克理论（standard Dirac theory）内识别出描述自旋选择性响应的最小静态狄拉克几何核，建立了一个基线结构（baseline structure），可由此系统地发展动力学介质（dynamical-medium）、散射（scattering）和输运（transport）形式，以全面描述 CISS 等自旋极化现象。

Abstract: We show that exact Dirac eigenstates in cylindrical confinement carry a definite helical conserved-current texture even in the zero orbital angular momentum channel l = 0. For the lowest confined mode, the Dirac current contains a nonvanishing azimuthal component together with longitudinal transport and exhibits opposite handedness in the two spin-resolved sectors. The structure also persists into the evanescent region.
  We further derive the channel-resolved matrix-element kernel generated by a static chiral scalar potential acting on the confined l = 0 Dirac modes. The resulting spin-selective coupling arises from the Dirac current texture and the scalar chiral potential, and yields a geometric selection rule in which diagonal channels vanish while off-diagonal conversion channels survive. The coupling strength is governed by an internal sampled-current overlap Jchi(k), defined as the integral from 0 to R of f(rho) times jphi_up(rho, k) times rho d rho.
  This quantity measures the spatial overlap between the chiral radial profile and the spin-up azimuthal Dirac-current density. The mechanism is fully local and texture-based, without external magnetic fields or spin-orbit coupling.
  Within standard Dirac theory, this work identifies the minimal static Dirac-geometric kernel underlying spin-selective response, establishing a baseline structure from which dynamical-medium, scattering, and transport formalisms can be systematically developed toward a complete description of spin-polarization phenomena such as CISS.

### [107] [Cavity method for permutation models on Cayley trees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17751)
*Masayuki Ohzeki*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究 Cayley 树上的置换统计模型，利用对称群上的类函数性质对边卷积算符进行不可约表示下的对角化，推导了均匀顺磁空腔解的线性稳定性判据，并通过数值迭代验证了该判据的正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 假设配对相互作用仅依赖于相对置换（relative permutation）的循环类型（cycle type），从而将 Boltzmann 权重写为对称群上的类函数（class function）。该性质使边卷积算符（edge convolution operator）在不可约表示（irreducible representation）扇区中对角化。对于循环因子化权重（cycle-factorized weights），特征值可表示为 Schur 函数（Schur functions）的特化。

Result: 线性稳定性由特征值的特征比（character eigenvalue ratios）控制；导出了不稳定性判据（instability criteria），并通过直接数值迭代空腔方程（cavity equation）验证了其有效性。

Conclusion: 所提出的类函数方法有效地将 Cayley 树上的置换模型问题转化为表示论中的特征值计算，为随机张量网络等领域的相变分析提供了理论工具。

Abstract: Motivated by permutation statistical models arising in random tensor networks, we study permutation models on a Cayley tree whose variables take values in the symmetric group $\Sn$. The pair interaction is assumed to depend only on the cycle type of the relative permutation. Then the Boltzmann weight is written as a class function on $\Sn$. This property diagonalizes the edge convolution operator in irreducible representation sectors. As a result, the linear stability of the uniform paramagnetic cavity solution is controlled by the character eigenvalue ratios. For cycle-factorized weights, these eigenvalues can be expressed as specializations of Schur functions. We derive the instability criteria and also verify their validity by comparison with direct numerical iterations of the cavity equation.

### [108] [Manipulation of Topological Corner States via Subchiral Symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17975)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 以二维Benalcazar-Bernevig-Hughes模型为例，将传统的手征对称性（chiral symmetry）分解为四个子手征对称性，每个子对称性对应一个零能角态。通过受控的胞间跳跃（intercell hoppings）选择性打破这些子对称性，逐步将四重简并角态流形降阶为孤立模式；进一步设计绝热协议（adiabatic protocols），实现单个角态或两个角态叠加态在选定角位间的转移，并在IBM量子处理器上进行了实验验证。

Result: 数值模拟和IBM量子处理器实现均表明，所提出的协议可以高保真度执行，实现了对高阶拓扑角态的可编程操控。

Conclusion: 子手征对称性为可编程的高阶拓扑态操控提供了一条有效路径。

Abstract: Higher-order topological phases provide robust corner modes, but their use requires controllable creation, isolation, and transfer of individual modes and their superpositions. Here we demonstrate, using the two-dimensional Benalcazar-Bernevig-Hughes model as an example, that subchiral symmetry provides a general control principle for manipulating topological corner modes. The conventional chiral symmetry decomposes into four subchiral symmetries, each associated with one zero-energy corner mode. By selectively breaking these subsymmetries with controlled intercell hoppings, we reduce the fourfold corner-state manifold step by step to single isolated modes. We further design adiabatic protocols that transfer either a single corner state or a superposition of two corner states between selected corners, while preserving the relative phase in the latter case. Both numerical simulations and IBM quantum-processor implementations show that the proposed protocols can be executed with high fidelity, establishing subchiral symmetry as a route to programmable higher-order topological state manipulation.

### [109] [Quantum statistical enhancement of collective behaviour in a bosonic active Ising model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18091)
*Kian L. Assent,Emil Strauch,Sabine H. L. Klapp,André Eckardt,Alexander Schnell*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于全同玻色子（ideal bosons with spin）引入并研究了主动伊辛模型（AIM）的一维量子晶格变体，发现玻色子量子统计显著增强了经典模型中群聚（flocking）和星形凝聚（aster formation）两种集体行为，与基于硬核玻色子的量子推广模型形成对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 集体行为（collective behaviour）如群聚和星形凝聚主要是在经典主动系统（active systems）中研究的，其量子统计效应尚未被充分探索。本文旨在引入量子统计效应（玻色子统计）到主动伊辛模型中，探究其对集体行为的影响。

Method: 引入并研究了一维（1D）量子晶格变体的主动伊辛模型，该模型基于具有自旋自由度的全同玻色子（ideal bosons），并与基于硬核玻色子（hard-core bosons）的量子推广模型进行对比。

Result: 玻色子量子统计显著增强了经典一维模型中的群聚和星形凝聚行为；这一现象与基于硬核玻色子的量子推广模型（Khasseh et al., 2025）形成对比，后者未观察到量子统计稳定化效应及星形凝聚态。此外，横向外磁场（transverse external magnetic field）诱导的量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）会抑制这些集体相。

Conclusion: 玻色子量子统计能够显著稳定经典主动系统中的集体行为，但这一稳定化效应会受到横向磁场诱导的量子涨落的竞争与抑制。

Abstract: Collective behaviour such as flocking (the collective motion of a spontaneously formed group along a common direction) or aster formation (the binding of opposing flocks, inhibiting each others motion) are intriguing emergent phenomena in active systems with local alignment rules. Until recently, their occurrence was mainly studied for classical systems, a prime example being the active Ising model (AIM), which translates the main ingredients of flocking and aster formation (i.e., alignment and self-propulsion) to a lattice framework. Here we introduce and study a one-dimensional (1D) quantum lattice variant of the AIM, based on ideal bosons with a spin degree of freedom. We find that both the collective behaviours of the 1D classical model, flocking and aster formation, are markedly enhanced by the bosonic quantum statistics. This contrasts with a recent quantum generalization of the AIM based onto hard-core bosons [Khasseh et al., Phys. Rev. Lett. 135, 248302 (2025)], where flocking, but neither its quantum-statistical stabilization nor aster states were observed as a consequence of interactions. Moreover, we investigate the competition of this quantum statistical stabilization of collective phases with their suppression by the quantum fluctuations induced by a transverse external magnetic field.

# cs.CE [[Back]](#toc)

### [110] [Online Spectral Deflation for State Constrained Optimal Control Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17971)
*Teeratorn Kadeethum,Francesco Ballarin,Youngsoo Choi,Sanghyun Lee*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出一种可复用的谱消融（spectral-deflation）策略，用于加速含逐点状态约束的参数化偏微分方程约束最优控制（parametric PDE-constrained optimal control）问题中的非活跃集（inactive-set）线性系统求解。该方法基于一个全域参考Schur补矩阵，预先计算低阶参考特征模态，在线阶段将其限制到当前非活跃集上，并作为A-DEF2消融基用于Jacobi预处理共轭梯度法（CG）中。实验表明，该方法在多个基准问题上将CG迭代次数减少约55%–98%，且在GPU上相比CPU稀疏直接法和代数多重网格基线获得墙钟时间收益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 参数化PDE约束最优控制问题中，每个参数实例对应的非活跃集系统虽为对称正定，但其活跃集（active set）随参数非光滑变化，导致系统维度、稀疏模式和谱分布剧烈变化，使得稀疏分解、多重网格层次和Krylov子空间信息的复用受到严重限制。现有求解器结构需针对每个参数实例重建，计算开销高昂。

Method: 提出一种可复用的谱消融策略：仅需一次预计算，提取一个全域参考Schur补矩阵的低阶特征模态（参考模态）；在线阶段，将参考模态限制（restrict）到当前参数对应的非活跃集上，构造为A-DEF2消融基，结合Jacobi预处理CG进行求解。框架支持POD（Proper Orthogonal Decomposition）扩充、Rayleigh-Ritz重新选择、粗网格或解析参考模态以及条件数保护措施。该方法保持高保真的非活跃集系统，仅加速线性代数求解，而非用代理模型替代最优控制求解。

Result: 在扩散问题、对流扩散问题、非线性热传导问题和共轭传热问题等基准测试中，消融策略将CG迭代次数减少约55%–98%。GPU部署相比CPU稀疏直接法和代数多重网格基线获得墙钟时间收益，因为参考基仅构建一次而竞争求解器结构需重新构建。粗网格或解析模态可在单次参数扫描内摊销离线成本；细网格特征求解仍受限于预计算开销。

Conclusion: 谱消融策略能够有效复用参考模态信息加速参数化非活跃集系统的求解，显著降低线性代数迭代次数和计算时间。方法的泛化性通过多种扩展（POD扩充、Rayleigh-Ritz重选、粗网格/解析模态）得到支持。消融非活跃集线性求解核本身，不涉及减少活跃集外层循环的优化。

Abstract: Parametric PDE-constrained optimal control with pointwise state constraints requires repeated solution of restricted Schur-complement systems on parameter-dependent inactive sets. In a primal active-set method, each inactive-set system is symmetric positive definite, but the active set can change nonsmoothly with the parameter. The resulting operator may vary in dimension, sparsity pattern, and spectrum, limiting reuse of sparse factorizations, multigrid hierarchies, and Krylov information. We propose a reusable spectral-deflation strategy anchored to one full-domain reference Schur complement. Low reference eigenmodes are computed once, restricted online to each inactive set, and used as an A-DEF2 deflation basis for Jacobi-preconditioned CG. The framework also supports POD enrichment, Rayleigh-Ritz reselection, coarse-grid or analytical reference modes, and conditioning safeguards. Given the active set, the method preserves the high-fidelity inactive-set system and solves it to the prescribed CG tolerance; it accelerates the linear algebra rather than replacing the optimal-control solve with a surrogate. We explain the method through a spectral-coherence view, motivated by interlacing and perturbation arguments and assessed with principal-angle diagnostics. Across diffusion, convection-diffusion, nonlinear thermal, and conjugate-heat-transfer benchmarks, deflation reduces CG iterations by about 55 to 98 percent. GPU deployments also show wall-time gains over CPU sparse-direct and algebraic-multigrid baselines, because the reference basis is built once whereas competing solver structures are rebuilt per instance. Coarse-grid or analytical modes amortize the offline cost within a single parameter sweep; fine-grid eigensolves remain more precompute-limited. Timings isolate the inactive-set linear-solve kernel; reducing the active-set outer loop is outside the present scope.

</details>

### [111] [Mechanism of production and deviation from the standard Gutenberg-Richter law of the big earthquakes (An analysis of big earthquakes)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17103)
*Bogdan Felix Apostol*

Main category: physics.geo-ph

TL;DR: 本文描述了震源中两种自复制能量累积机制，它们在大地震区域修正了古登堡-里克特定律（Gutenberg-Richter law）。第一种机制在大临界震级区域左侧减缓能量累积并可能产生前兆，第二种机制在右侧加速能量累积且前兆可能缺失。两种机制均降低了累积频率分布，并在临界区域附近引入震级间隙和分支。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 修正古登堡-里克特定律在大地震区域的适用性，解释大震级区间的能量累积行为异常，并为“自抑制地震”（self-arresting）与“龙王地震”（dragon-king earthquake）概念提供理论支撑。

Method: 通过引入两种自复制能量累积机制，并在古登堡-里克特经验分布中增加一个临界震级区间（critical-magnitude region/range）作为额外拟合参数，以描述震级概率密度在临界区左右两侧的不同变化。

Result: 两种机制均降低了古登堡-里克特累积频率分布。在临界区左侧，震级概率密度保持不变；在临界区右侧，概率密度降低。两种机制可能在大地震之间引入震级间隙（magnitude gap），并在临界区附近产生累积频率分布的两个分支。

Conclusion: 本文提出的临界震级区间作为额外拟合参数，有助于理解大地震的两种类型（自抑制地震与龙王地震）之间的差异，并为震级间隙和能量累积行为提供了新的机理解释。

Abstract: We describe two self-replicating mechanisms of energy accumulation in the seismic focus, which modify the Gutenberg-Richter law in the region of the big earthquakes. The first mechanism acts for magnitudes smaller than a narrow region of large critical magnitudes; it slows down the energy accumulation and may produce precursors. The second mechanism acts above that region, and accelerates the energy accumulation; the precursors may be absent. Both mechanisms reduce the Gutenberg-Richter excedence distribution. On the left of the critical region the Gutenberg-Richter magnitude probability density is unchanged, while on the right the probability density is reduced. The procedure described in this paper introduces a critical-magnitude region (range) as an additional fitting parameter. The results may bear relevance upon the recent concepts of "self-arresting" and "dragon-king" earthquakes. The two self-replicating mechanisms may introduce a magnitude gap between the two types of big earthquakes, and two branches in the excedence law, in the vicinity of the critical region.

</details>


### [112] [A Fixed Representation Probe Reveals Morphology-Space Organization in Non-Gaussian Elastic Transients](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17061)
*Jose Sanchez-Andreu*

Main category: physics.geo-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出使用冻结的卷积编码器（frozen convolutional encoder）作为固定探针，通过潜在几何（latent geometry）和扰动响应（perturbation response）比较不同物理系统中非高斯弹性形态（non-Gaussian elastic morphology），并在花岗岩声发射实验中成功区分了两种断裂组织模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 间歇性能量释放驱动的弹性系统会产生非高斯瞬态信号，这些信号包含爆发、振铃、脊线和聚类能量包等特征，但尚不清楚这些特征是否构成跨物理系统可比较的可测量形态。

Method: 使用一个在富含瞬态信号的干涉噪声上预训练的冻结卷积编码器，不对目标域进行微调、再训练或重新校准；将信号映射到公共时频表示，通过潜在几何和扰动响应进行比较，包括L2归一化嵌入、累积角路径、相位随机化和时间顺序扰动。

Result: 花岗岩声发射实验中，该方法区分了两种断裂组织：分布式损伤演化和局部化破裂模式；后者累积角路径更大，对相位随机化和时间顺序扰动退化更严重。合成对照和地震形态破坏实验表明，该响应无法仅由边际频谱能量解释。

Conclusion: 冻结的富含瞬态表示可以作为固定测量探针，用于跨异构物理系统比较非高斯弹性形态。

Abstract: Elastic systems driven by intermittent energy release generate non-Gaussian transients across domains such as brittle fracture, seismicity, rotating machinery and interferometric instrumentation. These signals often contain bursts, ringdowns, ridges and clustered energy packets, but it remains unclear whether such motifs define a measurable morphology comparable across physical systems. Here we use a frozen convolutional encoder trained on transient-rich interferometric noise as a fixed probe of non-Gaussian elastic morphology. The encoder is not fine-tuned, retrained or recalibrated on any target domain. Signals are mapped to a common time-frequency representation and compared through latent geometry and perturbation response rather than task-specific classification. In granite acoustic-emission experiments, L2-normalized embeddings define trajectories on a latent hypersphere. The cumulative angular path provides a derivative-free observable of morphological reorganization. This geometry distinguishes two fracture organizations: a more distributed damage evolution and a more localized rupture regime. The localized regime accumulates a larger angular path and degrades more strongly under phase randomization and temporal-order perturbation, consistent with a more phase-sensitive and sequence-dependent rupture morphology. Synthetic controls and seismic morphology-destruction experiments indicate that the response is not explained by marginal spectral energy alone, while random-weight attribution controls show that visual localization is insufficient without quantitative perturbation tests. These results support frozen transient-rich representations as fixed measurement probes for comparing non-Gaussian elastic morphology across heterogeneous physical systems.

*Gabriele Taricco,Andrea Tosin*

TL;DR: 本文针对有限图上的齐次玻尔兹曼型方程（homogeneous Boltzmann-type equations）建立模型，用以描述社交网络等“部分对部分”（some-to-some）的优先交互系统，并严格推导了当代理数量趋于无穷大时的稠密图极限（dense graph limit），同时在线性成对交互情形下，刻画了极限方程的长时间行为及其与经典“全对全”（all-to-all）设定下均衡分布的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统动理学理论（kinetic theory）中“全对全”交互假设源于气体分子碰撞，但该假设不适用于描述社会交互等具有优先连接特征的相互作用。

Method: 考虑有限图上齐次玻尔兹曼型方程以建模网络化的优先交互，并严格推导当代理数量趋于无穷时的稠密图极限；在线性成对交互情形下分析极限方程的长时间行为。

Result: 成功推导了有限图上齐次玻尔兹曼型方程的稠密图极限，并在线性成对交互情形下刻画了极限方程的长时间演化行为，获得了涌现的均衡分布（emergent equilibrium distributions）。

Conclusion: 将经典“全对全”交互的均衡分布与基于图结构的新模型下的均衡分布进行了对比，揭示了二者之间的关联。

Abstract: In kinetic theory, interactions between particles are typically assumed to be "all-to-all", meaning that any pair of randomly selected particles may, in principle, interact. This assumption originates from the theory of colliding gas molecules; however, it may be less appropriate for describing other forms of interaction, such as social interactions. These are more naturally characterised as "some-to-some", reflecting the existence of preferential connections between agents. In this paper, we consider homogeneous Boltzmann-type equations on finite graphs that model such networks of preferential interactions, and we rigorously derive their dense graph limit as the number of agents tends to infinity. We also investigate the long-time behaviour of the limiting equation in the case of linear pairwise interactions, characterising the emergent equilibrium distributions and relating them to their counterparts in the classical "all-to-all" setting.

### [114] [Semiclassical Analysis of Tunneling in Graphene under Nonuniform Electrostatic and Magnetic Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17689)
*Maria V. Perel*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个狄拉克费米子（Dirac fermion）穿过单层石墨烯（monolayer graphene）中n-p-n结的准经典隧穿理论，在垂直磁场作用下，通过准经典近似将散射问题简化为简并点的连接问题，给出了反射与透射系数的显式表达式，并分析了Fabry-Pérot共振与“魔角”条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究局限于恒定磁场和精确可解的静电势分布，本文旨在处理一般静电势形成的n-p-n结和任意磁场下的散射问题，以推广准经典隧穿理论。

Method: 假设静电势和磁场为单一空间坐标的光滑函数，且仅在有限区间内非零；在准经典近似（semiclassical approximation）下，结合对入射角（incidence angle）的附加假设，将问题转化为一对简并点（degeneracy points）的连接问题，并利用先前工作的结果进行求解。

Result: 获得了反射与透射系数（包括相位）作为能量和入射角函数的显式表达式；推导了Fabry-Pérot共振（Fabry-Pérot resonances）和“魔角”（magic angles）的准经典条件，并分析了干涉图样；数值结果展示了磁场引起的透射角依赖性。

Conclusion: 本文建立的准经典理论框架可处理一般n-p-n结与任意磁场下的隧穿问题，拓展了此前限于精确可解情形的研究范围，并为理解磁场诱导的透射角依赖性提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We develop a semiclassical theory of tunnelling of Dirac fermions through an n-p-n junction in monolayer graphene subjected to a perpendicular magnetic field. Electrostatic and magnetic fields are assumed to be smooth functions of a single spatial coordinate, supported on a finite interval, vanishing outside it, and thus ensuring asymptotically free states. In contrast to earlier studies restricted to constant magnetic fields and exactly solvable electrostatic potential profiles, we consider a general electrostatic potential forming an n-p-n junction and an arbitrary magnetic field, and formulate the corresponding scattering problem. Within the semiclassical approximation, and under an additional assumption on the incidence angle, the problem reduces to a connection problem for a pair of degeneracy points, treated using results from our earlier work. We obtain explicit expressions for the reflection and transmission coefficients, including their phases, as functions of energy and incidence angle. Furthermore, we derive semiclassical conditions for Fabry-Pérot resonances and "magic" angles, and analyse the resulting interference pattern. Numerical results demonstrate the angular dependence of transmission induced by the magnetic field.

### [115] [Moment generating function of the tacnode process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17771)
*Taiyang Xu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了 tacnode 过程（tacnode process）在多个区间上的计数函数生成函数，给出了积分表示，推导了大间隙渐近（large gap asymptotics）至常数项，并建立了计数函数期望、方差、协方差以及联合波动的中心极限定理（central limit theorem），将原有的单点理论推广到多区间多间断点情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: tacnode 过程是非相交粒子系统与随机平铺模型中出现的普适行列式点过程（determinantal point process），此前仅有单区间（1-point）理论研究，缺乏对多区间多间断点（multi-interval setting with multiple discontinuities）情形的系统分析。

Method: 通过哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）控制一组 $8m+4$ 个耦合微分方程，给出 $m$ 点生成函数（$m$-point generating function）的积分表示；结合哈密顿量的微分恒等式（differential identities）推导大间隙渐近。

Result: 获得了大间隙渐近的显式公式（含常数项）；得到了计数函数期望、方差和协方差的渐近公式；建立了计数函数联合波动的中心极限定理。

Conclusion: 成功将 tacnode 过程的单点理论推广至多区间多间断点情形，为更一般的不相交粒子系统和随机平铺模型提供了普适性分析工具。

Abstract: The tacnode process is a universal determinantal point process arising in non-intersecting particle systems and random tiling models. In this paper, we study the generating function for the counting functions of the tacnode process on a union of $m$ intervals, $m\in\mathbb{N}^{+}$. Our first result provides an integral representation for the $m$-point generating function in terms of the Hamiltonian governing a system of $8m+4$ coupled differential equations. Combined with several differential identities for this Hamiltonian, the representation yields the large gap asymptotics, up to and including the constant term. As further applications, we obtain asymptotic formulae for the expectations, variances, and covariances of the counting functions, and establish a central limit theorem for their joint fluctuations. These results extend the previously known $1$-point theory for the tacnode process to the multi-interval setting with multiple discontinuities.

### [116] [When Volumetric Growth Selects Surface Growth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17774)
*Rohn Abeyaratne,Roberto Paroni,Marco Picchi Scardaoni*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在线弹性力学（linearly elastic solids）的优化驱动框架下，证明了体积生长（volumetric growth）的最优分布会奇异地集中于边界或内部界面，从而在特定条件下以变分机制（variational mechanism）实现表面生长（surface growth）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索体积生长与表面生长之间的关系，并建立一种优化驱动的理论框架，使生长分布由约束优化问题（constrained optimization problem）决定而非通过演化律（evolution law）预设。

Method: 在一维和轴对称（axisymmetric）设置下，以外部载荷做功最小化为驱动过程，推导生长分布的显式解析解（explicit analytical solutions）。初始将生长表述为分布式的体积生长应变张量（distributed growth strain tensor），随后分析其最优分布形式。

Result: 最优生长分布是奇异的（singular），集中出现在边界或内部界面上。体积生长在一定条件下变分地等价于表面生长。

Conclusion: 提出了一个变分机制（variational mechanism），解释了表面生长为何可以作为体积生长的一种最优实现形式被选择出来。

Abstract: We investigate the relationship between volumetric and surface growth within a recently proposed optimization-driven framework for linearly elastic solids. In this approach, growth is not prescribed through an evolution law; instead, the growth distribution is determined as the solution of a constrained optimization problem.
  Focusing on processes driven by the minimization of the work performed by external loads in one-dimensional and axisymmetric settings, we derive explicit analytical solutions for the resulting growth distributions. Although growth is initially formulated as a volumetric process through a distributed growth strain tensor, we show that the optimal growth distributions are singular and concentrate on boundaries or internal interfaces.
  These results provide a variational mechanism through which, under certain conditions, surface growth is selected as the optimal realization of volumetric growth.
