### [117] [Counterexamples to the $L^1$ and $L^{\infty}$ boundedness of the one-dimensional wave operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17898)
*Sisi Huang,Xiaohua Yao*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过构造反例，证明一维薛定谔算子（Schrödinger operator）的波算子（wave operators）在一般情形（generic case）及满足特定条件的例外情形（exceptional case）下，在端点 $p=1,\infty$ 上无界，从而完整刻画了一维波算子的 $L^p$ 有界性图景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已知一维波算子 $W_{\pm}(H,-\Delta)$ 在 $1<p<\infty$ 上一致有界，且在例外情形的端点也有界性结论，但一般情形下端点 $p=1,\infty$ 的无界性长期缺乏严格证明。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 通过构造非零、有界且紧支撑的势函数 $V$，对一般情形以及满足 $\lim_{x\rightarrow-\infty}f_+(0,x)\neq 1$ 的例外情形，分别证明波算子在 $L^1(\mathbb{R})$ 和 $L^{\infty}(\mathbb{R})$ 上的无界性；在后者中还证明从 $L^{\infty}(\mathbb{R})$ 到 BMO（Bounded Mean Oscillation）空间的无界性。

Result: 在一般情形下，波算子在 $L^1(\mathbb{R})$ 和 $L^{\infty}(\mathbb{R})$ 上无界；在例外情形且 $\lim_{x\rightarrow-\infty}f_+(0,x)\neq 1$ 时同样无界，且从 $L^{\infty}(\mathbb{R})$ 到 BMO 空间也无界。

Conclusion: 结合已有结论，本文提供的反例完整刻画了一维波算子的 $L^p$ 有界性图景，解决了长期悬而未决的端点情形问题。

Abstract: It is well established that the wave operators $W_{\pm}(H,-Δ)$ for the one-dimensional Schrödinger operator $H=-Δ+V(x)$ are bounded on $L^p(\mathbb{R})$ for all $1<p<\infty$ in both generic and exceptional cases. They are also bounded on $L^1(\mathbb{R})$ and $L^{\infty}(\mathbb{R})$ in the exceptional case with $\lim\limits_{x\rightarrow-\infty}f_+(0,x)=1$. For the remaining endpoint cases, it has long been expected that they are generally unbounded at the endpoints $p=1,\infty$ due to the presence of the Hilbert transform in the low energy part, yet a rigorous proof has been missing.
  In this paper, we show that even for a bounded and compactly supported non-zero potential $V$, the wave operators $W_{\pm}(H,-Δ)$ are unbounded on $L^1(\mathbb{R})$ and $L^{\infty}(\mathbb{R})$ in the generic case, as well as in the exceptional case with the condition $\lim\limits_{x\rightarrow-\infty}f_+(0,x)\neq1$. Moreover, in the latter case, they are even unbounded from $L^{\infty}(\mathbb{R})$ to ${\rm BMO}(\mathbb{R})$ (Bounded Mean Oscillation space). Hence together with those known results, our counterexamples complete the picture of the $L^{p}$ boundedness of one-dimensional wave operators.

</details>


### [118] [Average entropy of Bogoliubov-Kubo-Mori random state ensemble](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17960)
*Sohail,Lu Wei*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本研究推导了由Bogoliubov-Kubo-Mori (BKM)度量诱导的随机量子态系综的平均纠缠熵精确显式公式，该方法无需关联核，仅利用系综归一化常数性质，为计算高阶累积量奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机态在量子科学多个分支中具有基础性作用，而由von Neumann熵通过Bogoliubov-Kubo-Mori (BKM)度量诱导的新随机态系综（BKM系综）尚缺乏精确的平均纠缠熵公式。现有方法通常依赖关联核（correlation kernel）进行平均熵计算，亟需新的框架以处理BKM系综。

Method: 研究仅利用BKM系综归一化常数（normalization constant）的性质，绕开了关联核的使用，推导出平均纠缠熵的精确显式公式。

Result: 成功推导出BKM系综平均纠缠熵的精确显式表达式，该推导完全不依赖于系综的关联核。

Conclusion: 所建立的框架不仅解决了BKM系综的平均纠缠熵计算问题，还为计算该系综的平均值（average）之外的高阶累积量（higher-order cumulants）开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Random states play a foundational role in different branches of modern quantum science. In this work, we study a recently proposed random state ensemble induced from von Neumann entropy through the Bogoliubov-Kubo-Mori (BKM) metric. In particular, we derive an exact yet explicit formula of average entanglement entropy over BKM ensemble. In obtaining the formula, we only make use of properties of normalization constant of the ensemble in the absence of its correlation kernel, contrary to average entropy computation of other ensembles. This new framework paves the way for calculating higher-order cumulants of BKM ensemble beyond the average.

</details>

### [119] [Directing Open-Ended Evolution in Artificial Life via Multi-Scale Path Divergence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17091)
*Mikhail Akhtyrchenko,Mikhail I. Katsnelson,Andrey Ustyuzhanin*

Main category: cs.NE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种受重整化群启发的显式标量指标——多尺度路径散度（MSPD, denoted D_P），用于量化局部转移法则在时间多尺度上的异质性组织。该指标既可作为无梯度适应度函数驱动开放式进化（OEE），又可作为事后分析透镜揭示局部动态，在多种人工生命基质上均有效，建立了从人工生命到物理复杂性理论之间的桥梁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人工生命中的开放式进化（open-ended evolution, OEE）通常依赖不可解释的黑箱神经网络复杂度指标，导致类生命系统与物理复杂性理论脱节。本文旨在提出一个具有物理基础的显式复杂度度量，以弥合这一鸿沟。

Method: 提出了多尺度路径散度（Multi-Scale Path Divergence, MSPD, denoted D_P），这是一个受重整化群（renormalization group）启发的标量指标。MSPD定义在群体层面，是已实现轨迹的泛函，通过窗口化有限分辨率估计量计算，且两者之间的一致性以命题形式陈述。该指标兼具无梯度适应度函数与事后分析透镜的双重角色。

Result: MSPD优化的参数在保持出复杂度分数上高于来自同一基底的匹配随机参数。高H_Δt态对应对外部干预更不稳定的状态，表明该指标追踪的是底层动态的生物学特征而非噪声。较高的MSPD对应更强的尺度依赖阻挫（scale-dependent frustration）：高复杂度系统在不同空间尺度上的动力学表现出更大差异。该协议可迁移至Life-like元胞自动机和Particle Life++等基质。

Conclusion: 单个显式公式既能引导开放式进化，又为复杂度提供了通向物理理论的有原则的桥梁，这是黑箱驱动方法所无法实现的。

Abstract: Open-ended evolution (OEE) in artificial life is typically driven by uninterpretable, black-box neural-network complexity metrics, leaving life-like systems disconnected from physical theories of complexity. We introduce MSPD (Multi-Scale Path Divergence, denoted DP ), a renormalization-group-inspired scalar that quantifies the temporal multiscale organization of heterogeneity in local transition laws. MSPD is defined at the population level as a functional of the realised trajectory and is computed as a windowed finite-resolution estimator, with consistency between the two stated as a proposition. The metric is an explicit formula and plays a dual role: as a gradient-free fitness function and as a post-hoc analytical lens on any simulation that exposes local transition laws. Empirically, MSPD-optimized parameters produce higher held-out complexity scores than matched random parameters from the same substrate. High-$H_{Delta_t}$ states correspond to states with higher instability to external interventions, so the metric tracks the biology of the underlying dynamics rather than noise. Higher MSPD corresponds to stronger scale-dependent frustration: high-complexity systems exhibit larger differences between the dynamics expressed at different spatial extents, linking MSPD directly to the frustration criterion of biological complexity in the sense of Vanchurin et al. [ 23 ]. The same protocol transfers beyond the primary Flow-Lenia substrate to Life-like cellular automata and Particle Life++, where C1, C2 and C5 all hold. A single explicit formula thus both directs open-ended evolution and provides a principled bridge to the physics of complexity that black-box drivers do not.

</details>

### [120] [Toward Controllable Catalyst Inverse Design via Large-Scale Autoregressive Pretraining](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17445)
*Dong Hyeon Mok,Jonggeol Na,Seoin Back*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于生成式预训练Transformer（Generative Pretrained Transformer, GPT）架构的条件催化剂生成模型，通过在1.33亿个催化剂结构上预训练并在约46万个优化结构上微调，实现了对催化剂结构的高效条件生成，显著提升了筛选效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 异质催化剂（heterogeneous catalysts）的逆向设计因催化剂表面结构复杂且耦合表面-吸附物相互作用（coupled surface-adsorbate interactions）而极具挑战性；传统筛选方法效率低下，而基于机器学习的筛选在面对巨大搜索空间时效率也会下降，因此需要能够直接生成目标性质催化剂的生成模型（generative model）。

Method: 基于生成式预训练Transformer（GPT）架构，引入数值嵌入层（numerical embedding layer），在单一自回归框架（autoregressive framework）内实现同时基于类别属性（categorical properties）和连续属性（continuous properties）的条件生成。模型先在1.33亿个催化剂结构上预训练，随后在约46万个优化结构上微调。

Result: 模型实现了98%的结构有效性（structural validity）和95%的优化有效性（optimization validity）；在吸附物类型和组成的条件匹配率为93%；在结合能（binding energy）条件匹配率约为20%，是基线训练分布的四倍；生成分布系统性地向目标值偏移，使反应靶向催化剂发现的筛选效率提升了1.5至4倍。

Conclusion: 大规模自回归预训练（large-scale autoregressive pre-training）结合显式属性条件化（explicit property conditioning），为可控催化剂生成和加速催化剂发现提供了一条实用路径。

Abstract: Inverse design of heterogeneous catalysts remains challenging because catalyst surfaces exhibit substantial structural complexity with coupled surface-adsorbate interactions across a vast chemical space that is difficult to explore efficiently through conventional screening alone. Although machine learning-based high-throughput screening has accelerated catalyst discovery, its efficiency inevitably declines as the search space grows, motivating the development of generative models that can directly construct catalysts with target properties. Here, we present a conditional catalyst generative model based on the Generative Pretrained Transformer architecture with a numerical embedding layer that enables the generation of catalyst structures conditioned on both categorical and continuous properties within a single autoregressive framework. The model was pretrained on 133 million catalyst structures and subsequently fine-tuned on approximately 460,000 optimized structures with associated categorical properties and binding energies for conditional generation. The resulting model achieved 98% structural validity, 95% optimization validity, and high categorical condition fidelity, with a 93 % joint match rate for adsorbate type and composition. For binding energy conditioning, the match rate of approximately 20% represents a four-fold improvement over the baseline training distribution, and the generated distributions shift systematically toward the target values, enabling a 1.5 to 4-fold improvement in screening efficiency for reaction-targeted catalyst discovery without additional fine-tuning. These results show that large-scale autoregressive pre-training, combined with explicit property conditioning, provides a practical route toward controllable catalyst generation and accelerated catalysts discovery.

</details>

Method: 利用NA64固定靶实验中电子与原子核相互作用产生的$Z'$玻色子，通过共振$e^{+}e^{-}$湮没产生道增强对$m_{Z'}\in[200,300]$ MeV质量范围的灵敏度，分析完整电子束数据集（2016–2022年，约$9.4\times10^{11}$电子打靶），统计量为先前工作的约三倍。

Result: 对于未破缺的$U(1)_{B-L}$情形，新上限超越了专用中微子散射实验的约束，成为亚GeV质量区间$g_{B-L}$最严格的实验室界限。在$Z'$耦合暗物质的场景下，衰变宽度由不可见道主导，可从NA64不可见模式分析直接导出排除限。

Conclusion: NA64实验以更大统计量显著提升了$g_{B-L}$的约束强度，为亚GeV能区$U(1)_{B-L}$模型提供了当前最严格的实验室界限，并可通过不可见衰变模式进一步约束暗物质耦合情形。

Abstract: Extensions of the Standard Model featuring an additional $U(1)_{B-L}$ gauge symmetry provide a compelling framework linking the origin of neutrino masses to possible dark matter candidates. The associated gauge boson, $Z'$, couples directly to Standard Model fermions and can be produced in fixed-target experiments through electron-nucleus interactions. In this work, we present new constraints on the coupling constant $g_{B-L}$ obtained with the NA64 experiment using the full electron-beam dataset collected between 2016 and 2022, corresponding to $(9.4\pm0.5)\times10^{11}$ electrons on target. The analysis includes the resonant $e^{+}e^{-}$ annihilation production channel, which enhances sensitivity in the mass range $m_{Z'}\in[200,300]$ MeV. The larger dataset provides approximately three times the statistics of previous analyses, thereby improving sensitivity. For the unbroken $U(1)_{B-L}$ case, the new limits exceed those from dedicated neutrino-scattering experiments, providing the most stringent laboratory bounds on $g_{B-L}$ for sub-GeV masses of the new boson. In scenarios where the $Z'$ couples to dark matter, the decay width is dominated by invisible channels, and the corresponding exclusion limits can be directly derived from the NA64 invisible-mode analysis.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缪子磁异常（muon magnetic anomaly）a_μ=(g_μ-2)/2是粒子物理标准模型（Standard Model）的关键精密检验量，实验值与理论值的潜在偏差可能暗示新物理（new physics）的存在。本工作的动机是在费米国家加速器实验室（Fermi National Accelerator Laboratory, FNAL）以更高的统计精度完成最终测量，减少实验不确定性。

Method: 测量基于缪子储存环磁场中反常自旋进动频率（anomalous spin precession frequency）与屏蔽质子进动频率（shielded proton precession frequency）的比值，并结合已知精度达22 ppb量级的外部常数。数据分析使用了2021至2023年收集的正缪子（positive muons）新数据集，其统计量是先前结果的2.5倍以上。

Result: 新数据集独立给出a_μ=1165920710(162)×10^{-12}（139 ppb）；与先前结果合并后得到a_μ=1165920705(148)×10^{-12}（127 ppb）。新的实验世界均值为a_μ^Exp=1165920715(145)×10^{-12}（124 ppb），主要由FNAL的测量结果主导。

Conclusion: 该项工作完成了Muon g-2实验在FNAL的最终缪子磁异常测量，以更高的统计精度（124 ppb）确立了新的实验世界平均值，为将来与标准模型（Standard Model）理论预言值的比对提供了基准。

Abstract: This report details the final measurement of the muon magnetic anomaly, $a_μ=(g_μ-2)/2$, by the Muon $g-2$ experiment at Fermi National Accelerator Laboratory (FNAL), using positive muons collected from 2021 to 2023. The value of $a_μ$ is determined from the ratio of the anomalous spin precession frequency to the shielded proton precession frequency in the muon storage ring magnetic field, combined with external constants known at the 22 ppb level. The new dataset, containing over $2.5$ times the statistics of our previous results, yields $a_μ=116\,592\,0710(162)\times 10^{-12}$ (139 ppb), or $a_μ=116\,592\,0705(148)\times 10^{-12}$ (127 ppb) when combined with our previous results. The new experimental world average, dominated by the measurements at FNAL, is $a_μ^{\text{Exp}}=116\,592\,0715(145)\times 10^{-12}$ (124 ppb).

### [123] [Better Queries, Cheaper Attention: Adapting Transformers for Efficient Sparse Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17631)
*Philippa Duckett,Samuel Van Stroud,Max Hart,Gabriel Facini,Tim Scanlon*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出一种几何感知的动态查询解码器（geometry-aware dynamic-query decoder），结合输入条件化的查询构建与结构化稀疏交叉注意力，用于高多重度稀疏传感器测量数据中的目标重建。在简化高亮度大型强子对撞机探测器中的带电粒子径迹重建任务上，该方法相比固定查询基线将重建效率从94.1%提升至98.1%，假率降低超过一半，端到端推理延迟降低近50%，峰值内存分配降低超过10倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于查询的Transformer解码器（query-based transformer decoder）在从稀疏科学传感器测量中进行目标重建上有效，但其固定、与输入无关的查询集以及代价高昂的解码器交叉注意力限制了向高多重度数据的可扩展性。

Method: 引入几何感知动态查询解码器（geometry-aware dynamic-query decoder），将输入条件化的查询构建与结构化稀疏交叉注意力（structured sparse cross-attention）相结合。解码器查询从选定的编码器级测量表示中初始化，作为候选径迹种子，使查询内容和查询多重度均取决于输入。局部间隔交叉注意力（Local Strided Cross-Attention, LSCA）利用由此诱导出的几何顺序，将学习到的掩码门控交叉注意力替换为几何定义的局部支持，从而将注意力限制在物理上合理的查询-击中相互作用上，并暴露稀疏性以支持块稀疏执行。

Result: 在简化高亮度大型强子对撞机探测器的带电粒子径迹重建任务中：动态查询（DQ）架构将重建效率从94.1%提升至98.1%，假率降低超过两倍；DQ+LSCA模型将端到端推理延迟降低近50%，峰值分配推理内存降低超过10倍。

Conclusion: 几何感知的动态查询解码器通过输入依赖的查询构造和结构化稀疏注意力，显著提升了高多重度场景下目标重建的性能与效率。

Abstract: Query-based transformer decoders are effective for object reconstruction from sparse scientific sensor measurements, but their scalability to high-multiplicity data is limited by fixed, input-independent query sets and costly decoder cross-attention. We introduce a geometry-aware dynamic-query decoder that couples input-conditioned query construction with structured sparse cross-attention. Decoder queries are initialised from selected encoder-level measurement representations that serve as candidate trajectory seeds, making both query content and query multiplicity input-dependent. Local Strided Cross-Attention (LSCA) exploits the induced geometric ordering by replacing learned mask-gated cross-attention with a geometry-defined local support that restricts attention to physically plausible query-hit interactions and exposes sparsity for block-sparse execution. We study this architecture for charged-particle trajectory reconstruction in a simplified High-Luminosity Large Hadron Collider detector, where thousands of trajectories must be reconstructed from tens of thousands of sparse measurements. In the nominal configuration, the dynamic-query (DQ) architecture increases trajectory reconstruction efficiency from 94.1% to 98.1% and reduces the fake rate by more than a factor of two relative to the fixed-query baseline. The DQ+LSCA model reduces end-to-end inference latency by nearly 50% and peak allocated inference memory by more than a factor of 10 relative to the fixed-query baseline.

</details>

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于BESIII探测器收集的20.3 fb⁻¹ e⁺e⁻对撞数据，在质心能量3.773 GeV处首次对D⁺→π⁺ηη衰变进行振幅分析（amplitude analysis）。唯一显著的过程是D⁺→a₀(980)⁺η, a₀(980)⁺→π⁺η，其分支比为(3.67±0.12_stat±0.06_syst)×10⁻³。研究发现，a₀(980)⁺η产生的π⁺η质量谱线形与此前在D_(s)→a₀(980)π和D⁰→a₀(980)⁻e⁺ν_e衰变中观察到的线形存在显著差异。传统振幅模型（Flatté、色散修正Flatté、T-矩阵、K-矩阵参数化）及其扩展均无法同时满足线形拟合质量和a₀(980)物理极点位置的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 通过首次对D⁺→π⁺ηη衰变进行振幅分析，研究其中间共振态a₀(980)的性质，以加深对轻标量介子（light scalar meson）结构的理解。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器在√s=3.773 GeV处采集的20.3 fb⁻¹ e⁺e⁻对撞数据，对D⁺→π⁺ηη衰变进行振幅分析。采用Flatté、色散修正Flatté（dispersively modified Flatté）、T-矩阵和K-矩阵参数化（K-matrix parameterization）等多种模型描述a₀(980)振幅。

Result: 唯一显著的过程是D⁺→a₀(980)⁺η, a₀(980)⁺→π⁺η，分支比为(3.67±0.12_stat±0.06_syst)×10⁻³。a₀(980)⁺η产生的π⁺η质量谱线形与D_(s)→a₀(980)π及D⁰→a₀(980)⁻e⁺ν_e衰变中观察到的线形存在显著差异。所有传统模型及其扩展均无法同时拟合该线形并保持a₀(980)在K\bar K阈值附近的物理极点位置。

Conclusion: 传统直接产生振幅模型（conventional direct-production amplitude model）在拟合质量与物理极点位置之间存在张力，表明当前对a₀(980)的描述仍不完善，需要进一步的理论和实验研究。

Abstract: Using $20.3~{\rm fb}^{-1}$ of $e^+e^-$ collision data collected with the BESIII detector at $\sqrt{s}=3.773~{\rm GeV}$, we perform the first amplitude analysis of the decay $D^+\toπ^+ηη$. The intermediate process $D^+\to a_0(980)^+η$, $a_0(980)^+\toπ^+η$, is observed as the only significant component in the amplitude analysis, and its branching fraction is measured to be $(3.67\pm0.12_{\rm stat}\pm0.06_{\rm syst})\times10^{-3}$. The $π^+η$ mass spectrum associated with $a_0(980)^+η$ production exhibits a line shape that differs substantially from those observed in $D_{(s)}\to a_0(980)π$ and $D^0\to a_0(980)^-e^+ν_e$ decays. We examine several conventional descriptions of the $a_0(980)$ amplitude, including Flatté, dispersively modified Flatté, $T$-matrix, and $K$-matrix parameterizations. With reference $a_0(980)$ parameters, neither these models nor their extensions including additional small resonant or non-resonant amplitudes reproduce the observed line shape satisfactorily. When the $a_0(980)$ parameters are allowed to float, satisfactory fits can be obtained, but the pole mass is driven well above the $K\bar K$ threshold, inconsistent with the near-threshold character of the $a_0(980)$. The results reveal a tension between fit quality and the physical pole position in conventional direct-production amplitude models.

# physics.optics [[Back]](#toc)

### [125] [Multipolar optical binding in focus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17694)
*Ashutosh Shukla,Sneha Boby,G V Pavan Kumar*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文利用广义多粒子米氏理论（generalized multiparticle Mie theory）计算了一对金纳米颗粒（AuNPs）在米氏散射区（Mie regime）的光学结合力（optical binding force）分布与刚度，揭示了多极等离激元模式（multipolar plasmonic modes）对零力节点和机械刚性的影响，为可编程超流体（metafluids）和可重构微机械（reconfigurable micromachines）提供了力学框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统研究多在瑞利极限（Rayleigh limit）下使用偶极近似（dipole approximation）研究金纳米颗粒的光学结合，但该领域正转向100–500 nm粒子的米氏区（Mie regime），其中偶极近似已不充分，必须考虑复杂的多极共振（multipolar resonances）景观，用以设计更复杂的光学物质（optical matter）形式。

Method: 采用广义多粒子米氏理论（generalized multiparticle Mie theory）对一对金纳米颗粒（AuNPs）的光学结合力（optical binding force）进行数值计算；在电偶极（electric dipole）、四极（quadrupole）、八极（octupole）模式各自散射峰对应的共振波长处，计算总光学结合力及机械阱刚度（mechanical trap stiffness, $dF_i/di$）。

Result: 等离激元模式对称性（plasmonic mode symmetry）显著影响零力节点（zero-force nodes）的空间分布以及光学结合二聚体（optically bound dimer）的刚性。

Conclusion: 通过将多极现象与标准实验配置对齐，本研究为可编程超流体（programmable metafluids）和可重构微机械（reconfigurable micromachines）提供了力学框架，弥合了基础电动力学（electrodynamics）与可重构纳米操控（reconfigurable nanomanipulation）之间的鸿沟。

Abstract: The optical binding of gold nanoparticles has conventionally been explored within the Rayleigh limit using dipole approximations. But the field is increasingly focusing on the Mie regime for particles in the 100-500 nm range, where the dipole approximation is insufficient, and a complex landscape of multipolar resonances must be considered. This can be leveraged to engineer more complex forms of optical matter. To this end, we computationally study the optical binding force landscapes experienced by a pair of AuNPs using generalized multiparticle Mie theory. We calculate the total optical binding forces and mechanical trap stiffness values ($dF_i/di$) at the specific resonance wavelengths where the electric dipole, quadrupole, or octupole modes reach their respective scattering peaks and dominate the mechanical response. We demonstrate that the plasmonic mode symmetry greatly influences the spatial distribution of zero-force nodes and the rigidity of the optically bound dimer. By aligning these multipolar phenomena with standard experimental configurations, this work provides a mechanical framework for programmable metafluids and reconfigurable micromachines, bridging the gap between fundamental electrodynamics and reconfigurable nanomanipulation.

</details>

# physics.plasm-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [126] [Time-dependent Trapped Plasmas: Nonlinear Dynamics, Symmetries and Invariants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17237)
*Thonimar V. Alencar,Luiz Gustavo Ferreira Soares,Ronaldo Thibes*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究单组分等离子体（single-component plasma）在时间依赖简谐陷阱（time-dependent harmonic trap）中的非线性动力学，从对称性和不变量函数（invariant function）角度出发。通过高斯假设（Gaussian ansatz）将偏微分方程组约化为常微分方程组，分析微分算子的代数结构与诺特对称性（Noether symmetry），识别各物理情形下的守恒量，揭示等离子体内部动力学与陷阱时间调制之间的耦合关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索时间依赖简谐陷阱中单组分等离子体的非线性动力学行为，特别是系统的对称性结构和守恒量（conserved quantity）的识别，以理解内部等离子体运动与外部陷阱调制之间的相互作用机制。

Method: 将系统描述为等熵绝热（isentropic adiabatic）条件下的流体，建立偏微分方程组（PDEs）。采用高斯假设对粒子数密度分布进行变量替换，将系统约化为常微分方程组（ODEs），随后分析相应微分算子的代数结构，并在特定物理情形下研究诺特对称性。

Result: 在各研究情形下识别出合适的守恒量（invariant）。获得的守恒量捕捉了等离子体内部动力学与陷阱时间调制之间的相互作用，对系统的演化施加了严格的限制条件。

Conclusion: 时间依赖陷阱中的单组分等离子体动力学受对称性支配，守恒量的存在显著约束了系统的演化路径，表明内部动力学与外部调制的耦合具有深刻的代数结构根源。

Abstract: We investigate the nonlinear dynamics of a single-component plasma confined in a time-dependent harmonic trap regarding aspects of symmetry and invariant functions. The system is described as a fluid in an isentropic adiabatic regime by a system of partial differential equations. A convenient change of variables, with a Gaussian ansatz for the number density distribution, allows a consistent mathematical description in terms of ordinary differential equations, from which we follow up with an analysis concerning the corresponding differential operators algebraic structure and Noether symmetries in specific physical regimes. For each studied case, proper invariants are identified. The obtained conserved quantities capture an interplay between the internal plasma dynamics and the time modulation of the trap, resulting in a sharp restriction for the system evolution.

</details>

### [127] [Probing the QCD Phase Structure with Dileptons from SIS to LHC Energies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17764)
*Adrian William Romero Jorge,Taesoo Song,Qi Zhou,Elena Bratkovskaya*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文通过准粒子模型（DQPM）和离壳部分子-强子-弦动力学（PHSD）输运方法，系统研究了相对论性重离子碰撞中强相互作用物质在有限温度和重子化学势下的性质，重点分析了双轻子探针与QGP相结构的关系。结果表明，在低碰撞能量下热QGP辐射可超过粲衰变产生的双轻子，为直接观测QGP电磁辐射提供了新的窗口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解有限温度和重子化学势下强相互作用物质的性质，并利用双轻子（dilepton）作为探针研究QGP相结构（QCD phase structure）在宽能量范围内的表现。

Method: 平衡态QGP采用动力学准粒子模型（Dynamical QuasiParticle Model, DQPM）描述，该模型复现了格点QCD状态方程并提供依赖于重子化学势（$μ_B$）的准粒子性质、输运系数及热双轻子产率（包含弹性和非弹性部分子过程）；动力学演化由离壳部分子-强子-弦动力学（off-shell Parton–Hadron–String Dynamics, PHSD）输运方法模拟，统一传播部分子和强子自由度并纳入手征对称性恢复效应。

Result: 宽能量范围内的相对论性重离子碰撞时空演化表明，在$\sqrt{s_{NN}}\simeq 3.5$ GeV处即可出现小尺寸的解禁闭QGP核心。首次在PHSD框架下展示了QGP热双轻子辐射对重子化学势的依赖性，该影响在低碰撞能量下更为显著。热QGP辐射的激发函数显示，在$\sqrt{s_{NN}}\lesssim 25$–$30$ GeV的中央Au+Au碰撞中，其强度可超过关联粲衰变产生的双轻子。

Conclusion: RHIC-BES和FAIR能量区间因重子化学势较高且热QGP辐射贡献显著，在扣除重味和Drell-Yan背景后，特别有利于直接观测QGP电磁辐射（electromagnetic radiation）。

Abstract: We study the properties of strongly interacting matter at finite temperature and baryon chemical potential in relativistic heavy-ion collisions, with emphasis on dilepton probes of the QCD phase structure. The equilibrium QGP is described within the Dynamical QuasiParticle Model (DQPM), which reproduces the lattice-QCD equation of state and provides $μ_B$-dependent quasiparticle properties, transport coefficients, and thermal dilepton rates, including elastic and inelastic partonic processes. The dynamical evolution is modeled with the off-shell Parton--Hadron--String Dynamics (PHSD) transport approach, which consistently propagates partonic and hadronic degrees of freedom and incorporates chiral-symmetry restoration effects. We discuss the space--time evolution of heavy-ion collisions over a broad energy range and show that a small deconfined QGP core can already emerge at $\sqrt{s_{NN}}\simeq 3.5$ GeV. We present, for the first time, the baryon-chemical-potential dependence of QGP thermal dilepton radiation in PHSD and demonstrate that its influence increases toward lower collision energies. The excitation function indicates that thermal QGP radiation can exceed dileptons from correlated charm decays in central Au+Au collisions at $\sqrt{s_{NN}}\lesssim 25$--$30$ GeV, making RHIC--BES and FAIR energies particularly promising for the direct observation of QGP electromagnetic radiation after subtraction of heavy-flavor and Drell--Yan contributions.

### [128] [A First Post-Friedmann Extension of the Schrödinger Approach to Cosmic Structure Formation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16521)
*Yiwen Deng-Huang,Daniele Bertacca,Sabino Matarrese*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文将薛定谔方法（Schrödinger approach）在大尺度结构形成中的应用从牛顿极限拓展至第一后弗里德曼（first post-Friedmann, 1PF）阶，提出了包含相对论修正的薛定谔型框架，其中有效矢量势由横向速度场决定，并包含了与参考系拖曳效应（frame-dragging）相关的度规矢量扰动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准薛定谔-泊松系统（Schrödinger--Poisson system）虽然有效描述了自引力无压流体的动力学，但仅对应后弗里德曼领头阶（即牛顿极限），忽略了在视界尺度及高精度宇宙学巡测中变得重要的下一阶相对论修正。

Method: 从平坦ΛCDM背景下的1PF连续性方程和欧拉方程出发，识别与协变质量守恒相关联的守恒密度变量，分析速度场的横向1PF分量，引入有效矢量势以构造薛定谔型表述。

Result: 在1PF阶，完整的质量流不能被标量相位的梯度单独表示；薛定谔型表述需要由横向速度分量决定的有效矢量势，该势包含后弗里德曼度规矢量扰动（涉及相对论参考系拖曳效应）以及由零涡度条件所需的非线性标量项。在标量形式下，这些修正表现为有效势的虚部贡献。

Conclusion: 该系统的领头阶还原为标准的薛定谔-泊松公式，1PF阶则提供了冷物质动力学薛定谔描述的相对论扩展。

Abstract: We extend the Schrödinger approach to large-scale structure formation beyond the Newtonian regime by working at first post-Friedmann (1PF) order. The standard Schrödinger--Poisson system gives a useful reformulation of the dynamics of a self-gravitating pressureless fluid, but it corresponds to the leading post-Friedmann, or Newtonian, limit. It therefore misses the relativistic corrections that enter at next-to-leading order and become relevant on horizon scales and for high-precision cosmological surveys. Starting from the 1PF continuity and Euler equations in a flat $Λ$CDM background, we identify the conserved density variable associated with covariant mass conservation. In terms of this variable, the continuity equation takes a Newtonian-like conservative form. However, even for vanishing covariant vorticity, the spatial velocity field in the cosmological frame contains a transverse 1PF component. Thus the full 1PF mass flux cannot be represented solely by the gradient of a scalar phase. We show that the Schrödinger-like formulation at 1PF order requires an effective vector potential fixed by this transverse velocity component. This vector potential contains the post-Friedmann metric vector perturbation, related to relativistic frame-dragging effects, together with nonlinear scalar terms required by the zero-vorticity condition. Equivalently, when the equation is written in scalar form, these corrections appear as an imaginary contribution to the effective potential. At leading order our system reduces to the usual Schrödinger--Poisson formulation, while at 1PF order it provides a relativistic extension of the Schrödinger description of cold matter dynamics.

</details>


### [129] [Damped Harmonic Oscillator Dark Energy and the Hubble Tension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17550)
*Saddam Hussain,Simran Arora,Qiang Wu,Tao Zhu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种由阻尼谐振子方程控制的暗能量状态方程，涵盖欠阻尼、临界阻尼和过阻尼三种解。通过与Planck CMB、DESI BAO、BBN、宇宙计时器以及三组Ia型超新星数据集的联合约束发现，欠阻尼解可将哈勃常数提升至约70–72 km/s/Mpc，使与SH0ES的张力降至约1.4σ；但Pantheon+数据集强烈偏向近临界阻尼解且给出较低的H₀值，揭示超新星数据集间存在显著系统性张力。贝叶斯证据表明，相对于ΛCDM模型，该模型在降低H₀张力时未付出统计代价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前宇宙学中，Planck CMB数据与SH0ES局部测量之间在哈勃常数H₀上存在显著张力（Hubble tension），亟需超越ΛCDM标准模型的暗能量模型来缓解这一矛盾。

Method: 采用阻尼谐振子方程（damped harmonic oscillator equation）描述暗能量状态方程（dark-energy equation of state），解得欠阻尼（underdamped）、临界阻尼（critically damped）和过阻尼（overdamped）三类解，并与Planck CMB、DESI BAO、BBN、宇宙计时器以及三组Ia型超新星数据集（DESY5、Union3、Pantheon+）进行联合约束，通过贝叶斯证据（Bayesian evidence）比较模型表现。

Result: 欠阻尼解对DESY5数据给出H₀ = 70.9 ± 1.1 km/s/Mpc，对Union3给出H₀ = 72.0⁺¹·⁴₋₂·₁ km/s/Mpc，将与SH0ES的张力降至约1.4σ；Pantheon+则强烈偏好近临界阻尼解，给出正w₀和H₀ = 66.23 ± 0.85 km/s/Mpc，揭示超新星数据集间存在显著系统性张力。贝叶斯证据相对ΛCDM模型不具决定性。

Conclusion: 欠阻尼暗能量模型在DES和Union3数据集下可实现H₀张力缓解，且相对于标准模型ΛCDM未产生统计代价，但超新星数据集间的系统差异需进一步厘清。

Abstract: We investigate a dark-energy equation of state governed by a damped harmonic oscillator equation, admitting underdamped, critically damped, and overdamped solutions. Confronting the model against Planck CMB, DESI BAO, BBN, Cosmic Chronometers, and three Type~Ia supernova compilations, we find that the underdamped solution yields $H_0 = 70.9 \pm 1.1$ km/s/Mpc, with DESY5 and $H_0 = 72.0^{+1.4}_{-2.1}$ km/s/Mpc with Union3, reducing the tension with SH0ES to $\sim\!1.4σ$, while Pantheon+ strongly favors a near-critically damped solution with positive $w_0$ and $H_0 = 66.23 \pm 0.85$ km/s/Mpc, revealing a significant systematic tension among supernova datasets. Bayesian evidence relative to $Λ$CDM is inconclusive for DES and Union3 data, demonstrating that $H_0$ tension alleviation is achievable at no statistical cost relative to the standard model.

</details>


### [130] [Joint reconstruction of $H(z)$ and $fσ_8(z)$ with physics informed neural networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17614)
*Konstantinos F. Dialektopoulos*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于物理信息神经网络（physics informed neural network, PINN）联合重构哈勃参数 H(z) 与结构增长率 fσ₈(z) 的方法，通过广义相对论线性增长方程在训练中耦合二者，并利用宇宙时钟、重子声学振荡和红移空间畸变数据验证了可行性与鲁棒性，结果揭示了与 ΛCDM 模型的偏离及 σ₈ 张力的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通常分别重构哈勃参数 H(z) 与结构增长率 fσ₈(z)，再事后检验两者的一致性；作者希望直接在训练过程中通过广义相对论的线性增长方程（linear growth equation）耦合二者，实现联合重建并提高物理自洽性。

Method: 采用物理信息神经网络（physics informed neural network, PINN），网络包含一个共享骨干网络（shared backbone）与两个独立输出头，分别输出 H(z) 和 fσ₈(z)；通过自动微分（automatic differentiation）在配置点处计算线性增长方程的残差作为额外损失项，并引入物理耦合权重 λ∈{0, 0.01, 0.1, 1.0}；在 50 个 H(z) 和 63 个 fσ₈(z) 观测数据上训练 100 个独立种子网络构成的集成，并使用 SH0ES 和 Local Distance Network 两种局域 H₀ 先验进行归一化锚定。

Result: 采用任一种局域 H₀ 先验时，哈勃常数 H₀ 均被精确恢复为先验值，两种重建在 fσ₈(z) 上不可区分；重建的 fσ₈(z) 在所有红移处系统性地低于 ΛCDM 预测，与 σ₈ 张力（σ₈ tension）一致；Om(z) 零检验（null test）显示低红移处显著偏离平坦 ΛCDM 预期。

Conclusion: 在训练过程中通过增长方程耦合两个可观测量是可行且有益的；重建结果对于两种局域 H₀ 测定值的选择具有鲁棒性。

Abstract: We present a proof of concept for the joint reconstruction of the Hubble parameter $H(z)$ that assumes no dark energy equation of state and the growth rate of large scale structure $fσ_8(z)$ using a physics informed neural network. Rather than fitting these two observables separately and checking their consistency post hoc, we couple them through the linear growth equation of general relativity directly during training, using the equation residual evaluated at collocation points via automatic differentiation as an additional loss term. The network employs a shared backbone feeding two independent output heads, one per observable. We train an ensemble of 100 independently seeded networks on a compilation of 50 $H(z)$ measurements from Cosmic Chronometers and Baryon Acoustic Oscillations and 63 $fσ_8(z)$ measurements from Redshift Space Distortions, and study four values of the physics coupling weight $λ\in \{0,\,0.01,\,0.1,\,1.0\}$. We then anchor the $H_0$ normalization using two independent local distance scale determinations: the SH0ES result $H_0 = 73.04 \pm 1.04$\,km\,s$^{-1}$\,Mpc$^{-1}$ and the Local Distance Network consensus $H_0 = 73.50 \pm 0.81$\,km\,s$^{-1}$\,Mpc$^{-1}$. With either prior the Hubble constant is recovered exactly at the prior value, and the two reconstructions are indistinguishable in $fσ_8(z)$. The reconstructed $fσ_8(z)$ sits systematically below the $Λ$CDM prediction at all redshifts, consistent with the $σ_8$ tension, while the $\mathrm{Om}(z)$ null test shows a marked departure from the flat $Λ$CDM expectation at low redshift. The results establish that coupling the two observables through the growth equation during training is both feasible and beneficial, and that the reconstruction is robust to the choice between the two local $H_0$ determinations.

</details>


### [131] [Synergy between CSST and future gravitational-wave detectors: Probing primordial black holes by cross-correlating dark sirens with galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17617)
*Ya-Nan Du,Ji-Yu Song,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出通过引力波（GW）成团偏袒（clustering bias）作为统计观测量，区分天体物理黑洞与原始黑洞（PBH）的并合事件。结合中国空间站巡天望远镜（CSST）的测光星系巡天与未来引力波探测器网络（ET2CE和BDET2CE）的模拟目录，发现BDET2CE网络凭借更精准的定位能力可将PBH可探测阈值从约40%降低至约20%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波事件和星系都示踪宇宙物质分布，但天体物理黑洞与原始黑洞（primordial black holes, PBHs）的并合倾向于分布在不同的环境中，因而具有不同的成团偏袒（clustering bias）。利用这一统计差异，可以区分两类并合事件群体。

Method: 将中国空间站巡天望远镜（Chinese Space-station Survey Telescope, CSST）的测光星系巡天与两个未来探测器网络的模拟引力波目录进行互相关分析：第三代地面网络ET2CE（爱因斯坦望远镜和两个宇宙探索者探测器）以及多频段网络BDET2CE（在ET2CE基础上增加空间基站的Decihertz干涉引力波天文台）。

Result: CSST结合10年ET2CE观测可在PBH占总体并合率超过约40%时揭示其贡献；BDET2CE凭借显著更优的定位精度，将这一阈值降低至约20%。改进源于恢复了小尺度成团信息，而定位误差原本会抹除这些信息。

Conclusion: 将未来引力波探测器网络与CSST星系成团观测相结合，提供了一条有前景且基本独立的统计路径来识别原始黑洞。

Abstract: Gravitational-wave (GW) events and galaxies both trace the cosmic matter distribution, but the mergers of astrophysical black holes and primordial black holes (PBHs) are expected to populate different environments and therefore to cluster with different biases. The GW clustering bias is thus a statistical observable that can separate the two populations. We assess how well this can be done by cross-correlating the photometric galaxy survey of the Chinese Space-station Survey Telescope (CSST) with mock GW catalogs from two future detector networks: the third-generation ET2CE network (the Einstein Telescope and two Cosmic Explorer detectors) and the multi-band BDET2CE network, which adds the space-based baseline Decihertz Interferometer Gravitational-Wave Observatory. We find that CSST combined with 10 years of ET2CE observations can reveal a PBH contribution once its fraction in the total merger rate exceeds about $40\%$, while the much sharper sky localization of BDET2CE lowers this threshold to about $20\%$. The improvement comes from recovering the small-scale clustering information that localization errors would otherwise erase. These results show that combining future GW detector networks with CSST galaxy clustering offers a promising and largely independent route to identifying PBHs statistically.

### [132] [Alleviating the Hubble tension with the $Λ_{ω_s}$CDM model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17749)
*Youri Carloni*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出 $Λ_{ω_s}$CDM 模型，通过在早期宇宙引入一个亚主导的“带压物质”（barotropic fluid）项来缓解哈勃常数（Hubble constant）张力。利用 Planck 2018 CMB、DESI DR2 及 Pantheon+SH0ES 数据进行的马尔可夫链蒙特卡罗（Markov Chain Monte Carlo）分析表明，该模型可将哈勃常数提升至 $H_0 = 71.51^{+0.72(1.43)}_{-0.74(1.46)}$ km/s/Mpc，有效缓解了哈勃张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准 $Λ$CDM 模型在晚期宇宙表现良好，但面临日益显著的哈勃张力（Hubble tension），即早期宇宙（CMB）与晚期宇宙（超新星等）对哈勃常数的测量值存在约 5σ 的不一致。作者旨在不破坏晚期 $Λ$CDM 成功的前提下，通过在早期引入额外组分来缓解这一张力。

Method: 作者将 $Λ$CDM 扩展为 $Λ_{ω_s}$CDM 模型，在早期宇宙添加一个称为“带压物质”（matter with pressure）的项——一种随宇宙膨胀而亚主导于尘埃和辐射的 barotropic 流体，使得模型在晚期恢复 $Λ$CDM 行为。通过马尔可夫链蒙特卡罗（MCMC）方法，结合 Planck 2018 CMB、DESI DR2 以及 Pantheon+SH0ES 数据进行参数约束。

Result: Barotropic 因子和新增流体的归一化密度分别为 $ω_s = 0.294_{-0.004(0.023)}^{+0.014(0.015)}$ 和 $10^{5}Ω_s = 1.62_{-0.56(0.91)}^{+0.36(1.02)}$。引入这两个额外参数后，哈勃常数提升至 $H_0 = 71.51^{+0.72(1.43)}_{-0.74(1.46)}$ km/s/Mpc，从而有效（de facto）缓解了哈勃张力。

Conclusion: $Λ_{ω_s}$CDM 模型通过在早期宇宙引入一种亚主导的带压流体，能够在不破坏晚期 $Λ$CDM 成功描述的前提下，显著提高哈勃常数的推断值，从而缓解哈勃张力。该工作为修改早期宇宙物理以解决哈勃张力提供了一条可行路径。

Abstract: We formulate a novel extension of the $Λ$CDM model, named $Λ_{ω_s}$CDM, in which we consider an additional term at early times in order to alleviate the Hubble tension. This additional component, referred to as \emph{matter with pressure}, indicates a barotropic fluid that is subdominant to dust and radiation as the Universe expands, thereby recovering the $Λ$CDM paradigm at late times. We constrain the $Λ_{ω_s}$CDM cosmology by performing a Markov Chain Monte Carlo analysis with Planck 2018 CMB, DESI DR2, and Pantheon+\texttt{SH0ES} data. The results suggest that the barotropic factor and the normalized density of the new fluid are given, respectively, by $ω_s=0.294_{-0.004(0.023)}^{+0.014(0.015)}$ and $10^{5}Ω_s=1.62_{-0.56(0.91)}^{+0.36(1.02)}$. With these two additional parameters, the Hubble constant is increased to $H_0 = 71.51^{+0.72(1.43)}_{-0.74(1.46)}$ km/s/Mpc, alleviating \emph{de facto} the Hubble tension.

### [133] [Constraints on the Sum of Neutrino Masses from ACT DR6 and DESI DR2 Considering Isocurvature Initial Conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17994)
*Hongsheng Hou,Sai Wang,Zhi-Chao Zhao,Xin Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文评估了在放松纯绝热初始条件假设的情况下，中微子质量和（∑mν）的宇宙学约束。结合CMB-SPA、DESI DR2重子声学振荡数据和DES第五年超新星样本，发现在ΛCDM和CPL动力学暗能量模型中，引入中微子密度等曲率（NDI）分量后，∑mν的上限变化微弱，NDI振幅与零一致。研究进一步揭示，该上限对暗能量状态方程和统计先验高度敏感，采用物理上合理的质量等级先验后上限显著提升。当前数据未发现NDI模式的证据，中微子质量约束的稳健性需解决先验依赖和暗能量不确定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往的中微子质量宇宙学约束通常假设纯绝热（adiabatic）初始条件，但这一假设可能过于理想化。本研究旨在系统性评估在允许存在中微子密度等曲率（neutrino density isocurvature, NDI）分量时，中微子质量和（∑mν）约束的稳健性，并揭示先验选择和暗能量模型对约束结果的影响。

Method: 采用CMB-SPA联合数据集（包含Planck 2018、ACT DR6和SPT-3G）、DESI DR2重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillation, BAO）数据以及DES第五年超新星样本，在ΛCDM和CPL动力学暗能量（dynamical dark energy）模型下，同时约束绝热模式和NDI分量，并对比不同先验下界对∑mν上限的影响。

Result: 在ΛCDM模型中，95%置信上限从纯绝热时的∑mν＜0.052 eV轻微放宽至包含NDI时的＜0.057 eV，NDI振幅与零一致。在CPL动力学暗能量模型中，绝热上限为＜0.111 eV，含NDI时变为＜0.115 eV，等曲率模式同样未被探测到。值得注意的是，纯绝热ΛCDM下的0.052 eV低于正常中微子质量等级（normal neutrino mass hierarchy）所要求的最小和0.05878 eV，表明该界限是统计先延展至零的人为产物；采用质量等级先验后上限提升至＜0.092 eV。

Conclusion: 当前数据未显示NDI模式存在的证据，中微子质量上限对此扩展具有稳健性。然而，要获得明确的、模型无关的界限，必须处理先验依赖性和暗能量状态方程的不确定性。本研究首次利用完整的CMB-SPA+DESI DR2+DES数据集给出了∑mν与NDI的联合约束。

Abstract: We present a robust assessment of cosmological constraints on the sum of neutrino masses ($\sum m_ν$) when relaxing the standard assumption of purely adiabatic primordial initial conditions. Allowing for a neutrino density isocurvature (NDI) component alongside the adiabatic mode, we analyse the latest CMB-SPA combination (Planck 2018, ACT DR6, and SPT-3G), DESI DR2 baryon acoustic oscillation data, and the DES Year 5 supernova sample. Within the $Λ$CDM model, the 95\% upper limit weakens only marginally from $\sum m_ν< 0.052$ eV (purely adiabatic) to $< 0.057$ eV (including NDI), with the NDI amplitude consistent with zero. In the CPL dynamical dark energy model, the adiabatic limit is $< 0.111$ eV, shifting to $< 0.115$ eV with NDI, yet the isocurvature mode remains undetected. While these limits are robust against the inclusion of isocurvature perturbations, they are highly sensitive to both the assumed dark energy equation of state and the prior lower bound on $\sum m_ν$. Notably, the adiabatic $Λ$CDM limit of $0.052$ eV lies below the minimum sum required by the normal neutrino mass hierarchy ($0.05878$ eV), indicating that this bound is an artifact of the statistical prior extending to zero. Imposing a physically motivated hierarchy-informed prior raises the limit to $< 0.092$ eV. Our results demonstrate that current data show no evidence for NDI modes and that the inferred neutrino mass upper limit is robust against this extension, but a definitive, model-independent bound requires addressing prior dependencies and dark energy uncertainties. This work provides the first joint constraint on $\sum m_ν$ and NDI using the full CMB-SPA+DESI DR2+DES dataset.

</details>


### [134] [Large primordial non-Gaussianity from transient turns in Higgs-$R^2$ inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18095)
*Flavio Pineda,Luis O. Pimentel*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了多场Higgs-R²暴胀中瞬态转弯轨迹对原初非高斯性的影响，发现其能高效产生局域非高斯性，对Higgs非最小耦合参数具有敏感约束力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多场暴胀模型中，场空间流形（field space manifold）的双曲几何可能导致非平凡轨迹动力学，进而影响原初扰动。本文旨在厘清瞬态转弯如何将等曲率扰动（isocurvature perturbations）转化为绝热模并产生非高斯性（non-Gaussianities）。

Method: 不依赖慢滚近似（slow-roll approximation）或局域近似（local approximation）计算完整的三点函数（bispectrum），并跟踪曲率扰动与等曲率扰动的超视界（superhorizon）演化。

Result: 瞬态转弯能高效转移等曲率涨落至绝热扇区，产生显著局域非高斯性。在基准参数（ξ_h=0.1, λ=10^{-10}）下获得f_NL^loc≈−17.7；随Higgs非最小耦合增大，转弯率受抑制，模型趋近有效单场吸引子，Maldacena一致性关系恢复（f_NL→0.0159）。

Conclusion: 原初非高斯性（primordial non-Gaussianity）是Higgs非最小耦合的敏感探针，能显著限制模型可行参数空间，并与当前CMB约束对比给出更强限制。

Abstract: We investigate the generation of primordial non-Gaussianities in multifield Higgs--$R^2$ inflation, focusing on the effects of transient turning trajectories in the hyperbolic field space manifold. We compute the full bispectrum without relying on slow-roll or local approximations and follow the complete superhorizon evolution of curvature and isocurvature perturbations. We show that transient turns efficiently transfer isocurvature fluctuations into the adiabatic sector, generating sizeable local non-Gaussianities. For a benchmark Higgs nonminimal coupling $ξ_h = 0.1$ and quartic coupling $λ= 10^{-10}$, we obtain $f_{\rm NL}^{\rm loc}\simeq -17.7$. As the Higgs nonminimal coupling increases, the turning rate is progressively suppressed and the model approaches the effective single-field attractor, recovering the Maldacena consistency relation $f_{\rm NL}\rightarrow 0.0159$. Comparing our predictions with current CMB constraints, we find that primordial non-Gaussianity provides a sensitive probe of the Higgs nonminimal coupling and can significantly restrict the viable parameter space of the model.

</details>


### [135] [Pushing the Primordial Frontier: Exact Linear Solutions in Multifield Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18248)
*Javier Huenupi,Claudio Muñoz,Gonzalo A. Palma,Spyros Sypsas*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文给出了双场暴胀系统中曲率扰动与等曲率扰动线性动力学的精确解析解，该解对任意熵质量与耦合强度均有效，并首次推导了原初功率谱的封闭形式振幅表达式，为研究强耦合多场可观测效应提供了分析基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双场暴胀系统中，曲率扰动ζ与等曲率扰动σ之间存在耦合，尤其在强耦合（strongly coupled）区域（通常与快速转向暴胀相关）解析控制困难。现有研究多依赖数值或近似手段，缺乏适用于任意耦合强度与熵质量的精确解析框架。

Method: 在准德西特（quasi-de Sitter）背景中，针对包含熵质量μ与无量纲相互作用强度λ的双场暴胀系统，求解曲率扰动ζ与等曲率扰动σ耦合的线性动力学方程，获得精确解析解。

Result: 给出了原初功率谱（primordial power spectrum）振幅的封闭形式表达式，该表达式能够统一插值描述弱耦合（weakly coupled）、强耦合（strongly coupled）、轻场（light-field）和重场（heavy-field）四个不同区域的行为。

Conclusion: 该解析框架为超越功率谱的多场可观测量的解析研究开辟了道路，可应用于非高斯性（non-Gaussianity）、粒子产生（particle production）以及圈图修正（loop corrections）等课题。

Abstract: We present exact analytic solutions for the linear dynamics of a two-field inflationary system in which the primordial curvature perturbation $ζ$ is coupled to an isocurvature perturbation $σ$ of entropy mass $μ$. The solutions are valid for arbitrary values of $μ$ and the dimensionless interaction strength $λ$, within a quasi-de Sitter background. They therefore provide analytic control over the strongly coupled regime in which $ζ$ interacts with light isocurvature fields, commonly associated with rapid-turn inflation. As a first application, we derive the amplitude of the primordial power spectrum in closed form, obtaining an expression that interpolates between the weakly coupled, strongly coupled, light-field, and heavy-field regimes. These results open the way to analytic studies of multifield observables beyond the power spectrum, including non-Gaussianity, particle production, and loop corrections.

### [136] [Planck mass gravitinos in Einstein-Maxwell backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17139)
*Artur Krawczyk,Krzysztof A. Meissner,Hermann Nicolai,Bartłomiej Sikorski*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了带电大质量自旋-3/2场（charged massive spin-3/2 field）与电磁耦合时的不一致性问题，表明引力的引入可以抵消电磁导致的非双曲性、非因果性和幺正性丧失。通过Rarita-Schwinger场在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦（Einstein-Maxwell）背景下的分析，推导出质量-电荷-宇宙学常数之间的不等式，并利用Stückelberg自旋子（Stückelberg spinor）重新表述系统，得到可重整化传播子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 带电大质量自旋-3/2场长期以来被认为存在问题，因为其与电磁的耦合通常导致双曲性丧失、非因果传播及幺正性丧失。然而，分数电荷的超大质量引力微子（gravitino）在超出标准模型的新物理方案中作为暗物质候选起着核心作用，因此亟需解决这一明显矛盾。

Method: 重新审视Deser和Waldron的结果，在爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦背景下对最小耦合的Rarita-Schwinger场进行分析。通过Rarita-Schwinger约束的可解性和特征行列式（characteristic determinant）重新推导不等式，展示爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦应力张量如何补偿纯电磁病态；进一步采用Stückelberg自旋子重新表述系统，分析螺旋度-1/2（helicity-1/2）扇区，并讨论相应的传播子与鬼场（ghost）系统。

Result: 一致性要求质量、电荷与宇宙学常数之间存在一个下界不等式；该不等式表明此类粒子必须接近普朗克标度（Planck scale）。基于Stückelberg形式的传播子分析显示可重整化性，并讨论了相应的鬼场系统。

Conclusion: 通常被视为低能带电自旋-3/2现象学严重障碍的条件，反而独立地指示了此类粒子必须存在于普朗克标度附近，与作者此前基于其他论据的结论一致。Stückelberg形式对于获得可重整化传播子至关重要。

Abstract: Charged massive spin-3/2 fields have long been regarded as problematic, because their coupling to electromagnetism generically leads to loss of hyperbolicity, acausal propagation and loss of unitarity. At the same time, fractionally charged supermassive gravitinos play a central role in a recent proposal of two of the present authors, where they are the only fermionic degrees of freedom beyond the Standard Model and provide novel dark matter candidates. We address this apparent tension by revisiting the result of Deser and Waldron, who showed that the inclusion of gravity can compensate the electromagnetic source of the inconsistency. For a minimally coupled Rarita-Schwinger field in an Einstein-Maxwell background, consistency requires a lower bound on the mass in terms of the charge and the cosmological constant. What is usually a severe obstruction to low-energy charged spin-3/2 phenomenology becomes an independent indication that such particles must lie close to the Planck scale, as argued by two of the present authors on other grounds. We rederive the inequality from the solvability of the Rarita-Schwinger constraints and from the characteristic determinant, emphasizing how the Einstein-Maxwell stress tensor compensates the purely electromagnetic pathology. We then reformulate the system using a Stückelberg spinor, showing that the helicity-1/2 sector reproduces the same condition. This formulation is also essential for obtaining a renormalizable propagator. We discuss this propagator and the corresponding ghost system.

### [137] [When Renormalisation Remembers: UV/IR Mixing as an Entanglement Bridge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17147)
*Steven Abel*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过引入Born-Reciprocal Tensor Network (BRTN)将紫外/红外混合（UV/IR mixing）重新诠释为希尔伯特空间中的重整化尺度间关联现象，并证明在特定大体积极限下Wilson重整化群行为可以被恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Wilson重整化假定紫外自由度逐渐退耦，形成自治的红外描述；但在紫外/红外混合理论中，不同尺度间存在持久关联，破坏了这一记忆缺失（memoryless）假设。因此需要发展可以显式处理UV/IR混合的新理论框架。

Method: 本文提出了Born-Reciprocal Tensor Network (BRTN)——一种在相空间对偶性（phase-space reciprocity）下全局对称的新型张量网络（tensor network）构型。在此基础上构造真空态并重现预期的辐射修正（radiative corrections），将UV/IR混合编码为重整化尺度间的交叉纠缠（cross-bridge entanglement）。

Result: 得到的重整化几何（renormalisation geometry）具有记忆效应，其中的桥（bridge）连接了红外的对偶表示。交叉纠缠为有效描述的可行性提供了精确判据。存在一个将基本尺度固定的大体积极限（large-volume limit），在此极限下局域描述的障碍随尺度消失，Wilson行为得以恢复，重整化过程丧失记忆。

Conclusion: BRTN为UV/IR混合提供了一个具体且可计算的平台，揭示了记忆性重整化几何与Wilson式遗忘重整化之间的转换条件。

Abstract: Renormalisation is traditionally understood to be a Wilsonian memoryless process in which ultraviolet (UV) degrees of freedom gradually decouple, leaving an autonomous infrared (IR) description. However this need not be the case: in UV/IR mixed theories correlations between widely separated scales can persist. In this work I recast UV/IR mixing as a Hilbert-space phenomenon, realised as correlations across renormalisation scales. This formulation is implemented using the Born-Reciprocal Tensor Network (BRTN), a new configuration of tensor network that is globally symmetric under phase-space reciprocity. On this network I prepare the vacuum and reproduce the expected radiative corrections. The resulting renormalisation geometry exhibits memory, with a bridge linking reciprocal representations of IR physics, whose cross-bridge entanglement provides a precise criterion for the viability of an effective description. I analyse when this criterion is met, and show that there is a large-volume limit, with the fundamental scale held fixed, in which the obstruction to a local description scales away: Wilsonian behaviour is restored and renormalisation forgets. The BRTN therefore provides a concrete and calculable platform for UV/IR mixing.

</details>


### [138] [Extended Supergravity Needs String Scale Cut-off](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17149)
*Ashoke Sen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究弦论紧化（string compactification）中BPS黑洞的超对称指标（supersymmetric index）在弦耦合（string coupling）下的独立性。通过选择弦尺度（string scale）作为紫外截断（UV cut-off），证明了单圈修正后的指标不依赖于弦耦合，与超对称预期一致；同时讨论了Calabi-Yau流形紧化中欧拉数（Euler number）为零/非零时的情形与未解决难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将引力路径积分中单圈修正的紫外截断尺度设定为弦尺度（string scale），遵循弦论规则；分别分析具有N=8、N=6、N=4超对称的弦紧化情形，以及II型弦论（type II string theory）在Calabi-Yau流形上的紧化，区分欧拉数为零与非零两种情况。

Result: 当截断尺度选择为弦尺度时，超对称指标对弦耦合的依赖消失，与超对称理论预期一致。类似结果适用于欧拉数为零的Calabi-Yau流形紧化；对于欧拉数非零的情形，遇到了一个尚未完全解决的难题（puzzle）。

Conclusion: 在弦论框架下选择适当的紫外截断（弦尺度）可以消除BPS黑洞超对称指标对弦耦合的依赖，符合超对称性要求。欧拉数非零的Calabi-Yau紧化情形仍存在未解决的难题，需要进一步研究。

Abstract: Many string compactifications down to four non-compact space-time dimensions with N=8, N=6 and N=4 supersymmetry have BPS black holes carrying pure D-brane charges and preserving four supersymmetries. The string coupling does not flow in these backgrounds and can be set to any arbitrary value. Therefore the supersymmetric index of these black holes must be independent of the string coupling. On the other hand, explicit computation of one loop correction to the index from gravitational path integral is sensitive to the choice of ultraviolet cut-off. We show that if the cut-off scale is chosen to be the string scale in accordance with the rules of string theory, then the dependence of the index on the string coupling disappears in accordance with the expectation from supersymmetry. Similar results are obtained for type II string theories compactified on Calabi-Yau manifolds with zero Euler number. For non-zero Euler number we encounter a puzzle that we discuss but do not fully resolve.

</details>

Abstract: We develop a geometric framework for non-supersymmetric effective gauge theories based on their nonlinear supersymmetrizations. We construct supersymmetric embeddings for most operators up to dimension six from constrained chiral and vector superfields, and formulate vector bundles using the superfields to systematically organize the operators under field redefinitions in the gauge sector. This formalism manifests a complex geometry underlying gauge operators and accommodates redefinitions across different spins.

### [140] [The Helical SYK Model and Emergent Infrared Integrability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17161)
*Gustavo Valdivia-Mera,Bhavay Tyagi,Eric R. Bittner,Pavan Hosur*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文构造了1+1维螺旋SYK模型（helical SYK model），系统分析了其手征扇区（chirality sectors）层次结构、可积性条件与红外行为，证明在完整相互作用空间下模型在红外极限变为自由可积理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev（SYK）模型在1+1维时空中的螺旋推广形式，研究其在不同对称性约束下的可积性质以及红外极限行为。

Method: 通过手征味空间（flavor-chirality space）中的局域四次相互作用（local quartic interactions）与随机耦合构造螺旋SYK模型；在对称性约束最强的扇区中采用玻色化（bosonization）方法精确求解，在一般情形下利用大N极限（large-N limit）下的短程选择定则（short-distance selection rules）与退火无序平均（disorder averaging）处理，并结合共形微扰论（conformal perturbation theory）围绕自由固定点进行分析。

Result: 四次相互作用可组织为受对称性控制的手征扇区层次结构；密度-密度型扇区（density-density form）可精确求解并具有可积性；完整螺旋相互作用空间破坏了这一可积结构；但整个相互作用空间在共形微扰论意义下为边缘无关（marginally irrelevant），因此理论在红外（IR）极限下变为自由且可积。

Conclusion: 该螺旋SYK模型在红外极限下恢复自由可积性，表明体系中存在一种由对称性和无序共同保护的流动机制，从非可积的高能行为流向可积的低能物理。

Abstract: We construct a helical generalization of the Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) model in $1+1$ dimensions, built from left- and right-moving Majorana fermions with local quartic interactions and random couplings in flavor-chirality space. These interactions organize into a symmetry-controlled hierarchy of quartic chirality sectors. At the most restrictive end of this hierarchy, symmetry forces the quartic structure into a density-density form, which admits an exact solution using bosonization, rendering the theory integrable. Once the full quartic helical interaction space is allowed, including purely chiral, chirality-balanced, and chirality-imbalanced sectors, this symmetry-protected integrable structure is lost. Nevertheless, the large-$N$ infrared limit remains analytically tractable through short-distance selection rules and disorder averaging. Using conformal perturbation theory about the free fixed point, we show that the entire interaction space is marginally irrelevant, and the theory thus becomes free and integrable in the IR.

</details>


### [141] [Thermal One-point Functions and Asymptotic CFT Data: QFT in AdS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17167)
*Ilija Burić,Francesco Mangialardi,Francesco Russo,Volker Schomerus,Alessandro Vichi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用热反演公式（thermal inversion formulas）研究了与AdS₄中有质量相互作用标量场对偶的三维共形场论（CFT₃）的热配分函数和一点函数，分析了谱密度和OPE系数在大算子维度下的渐近行为，并计算了立方和四次体相互作用的微扰修正。结果表明，热反演得到的渐近公式在中等共形权重下仍保持定量准确，且这一特性在引入体相互作用后依然成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索共形场论中与重算子（heavy operators）——即大维度算子——相关的热力学可观测量（thermal observables）的具体行为。该区域即使在广义自由场论（generalised free field theory）中也尚未被充分探索，本研究旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用热反演公式（thermal inversion formulas）分析热配分函数和一点函数，从体（bulk）对偶的角度出发，先考察非相互作用体理论对应的广义自由场，再通过微扰论计算立方和四次体相互作用（cubic and quartic bulk interactions）的一阶修正。

Result: 得到了谱密度和OPE系数在固定自旋（fixed spin）下重算子渐近行为的解析结果；发现热反演导出的渐近公式在远离渐近区域的中间共形权重（intermediate conformal weights）下仍具有定量准确性，且该性质在引入体相互作用后依然保持。

Conclusion: 热反演方法能够为共形场论中的重算子数据提供新的解析控制，即便在包含体相互作用的微扰情形下，其预测的定量可靠性依然保持，表明该方法在研究大维度算子区域方面具有普遍适用性。

Abstract: We investigate the thermal partition and one-point functions of the three-dimensional conformal field theory dual to a massive interacting scalar field in AdS$_4$. Using thermal inversion formulas, we determine the asymptotic behaviour of the spectral density and OPE coefficients involving heavy operators at fixed spin. We first analyse these CFT data for the generalised free field, corresponding to the non-interacting bulk theory. Then we compute the first-order perturbative corrections induced by the cubic and quartic bulk interactions. The thermal observables considered here probe a sector associated with operators of large dimension and, in the bulk description, a regime dominated by states with large particle number. This regime remains comparatively unexplored even in generalised free field theory. Remarkably, the asymptotic formulas obtained from thermal inversion remain quantitatively accurate far from the asymptotic regime, describing CFT data reliably already at intermediate conformal weights. Our results show that this feature survives the inclusion of bulk interactions and provide new analytic control over heavy-state data in conformal field theories.

</details>


### [142] [Black hole equations of state and response functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17171)
*Silvester G. A. Borsboom,Manus R. Visser*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文系统发展了一种基于热力学表示（thermodynamic representations）的平衡态热力学框架，并将其应用于球形空腔内的Schwarzschild黑洞。研究发现，该准局域黑洞的稳定性依赖于热力学表示的选择：大黑洞分支在固定体积下热力学稳定但在等温压缩下力学不稳定，而在固定压力下系统在整个物理状态空间中热力学不稳定。研究还发现热膨胀系数处处为负，等焓膨胀总是使黑洞冷却。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的黑洞热力学缺乏一个系统性的框架，能够统一处理在不同热力学势和独立变量选择（即热力学表示）下的状态方程和响应函数。作者希望建立这样的通用框架，并应用于准局域Schwarzschild黑洞，以揭示其稳定性、热力学响应等性质如何依赖于表示选择。

Method: 论文系统建立了以热力学表示为框架的平衡态热力学形式体系：热力学表示由热力学势（thermodynamic potential）和每个共轭对中选取的一个独立变量共同定义；状态方程（equations of state）来源于势函数的一阶导数，响应函数（response functions）来源于二阶导数。将该框架应用于理想气体及球形空腔内的Schwarzschild黑洞，并将空腔面积及其共轭表面压力解释为全息对偶系统的热力学体积和压力。

Result: 准局域Schwarzschild黑洞的稳定性依赖于热力学表示，即依赖于平衡扰动下哪些变量被固定。大黑洞分支在固定体积下热力学稳定，但在等温压缩下力学不稳定；系统在绝热压缩下处处力学稳定。在固定压力下，黑洞在整个物理状态空间中热力学不稳定。此外，热膨胀系数处处为负，等焓膨胀总是使黑洞冷却。

Conclusion: 该框架为准局域引力热力学（quasi-local gravitational thermodynamics）中广泛的黑洞系统提供了一种系统地推导状态方程和响应函数的途径，有助于深入理解黑洞热力学的表示依赖性及其稳定性特征。

Abstract: We systematically develop a framework for equilibrium thermodynamics in terms of thermodynamic representations, which are choices of thermodynamic potential and independent variables, one from each conjugate pair. In each representation, equations of state arise from first derivatives of the potential and response functions from its second derivatives. We apply this framework to ideal gases and to Schwarzschild black holes in a spherical cavity in various representations, interpreting the cavity area and its conjugate surface pressure as the thermodynamic volume and pressure of a holographically dual system. For this quasi-local Schwarzschild black hole, stability depends on the thermodynamic representation, or equivalently on which variables are held fixed under equilibrium perturbations. The large black hole branch is thermally stable at fixed volume but mechanically unstable under isothermal compression, while the system is mechanically stable under adiabatic compression everywhere. At fixed pressure, the black hole is thermally unstable throughout the physical state space. We also find that the thermal expansion coefficient is negative everywhere and show that isenthalpic expansion always cools the black hole. More broadly, the framework provides a systematic route to deriving equations of state and response functions for a wide class of black hole systems using quasi-local gravitational thermodynamics.

</details>


### [143] [Effective-metric formulation of Casimir energies in nonlinear scalar and electromagnetic theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17221)
*C. A. Escobar*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过有效几何（effective geometry）方法研究了非线性场论中的卡西米尔效应（Casimir effect），证明洛伦兹破缺标量场的结果可推广为适用于非线性理论线性化涨落（linearized fluctuations）的有效度规（effective metric）方案，并在非线性电动力学中通过平行板卡西米尔能（parallel-plate Casimir energy）计算验证了这一方案的正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前述对洛伦兹破缺（Lorentz-violating）标量场的分析表明，常动学背景会通过标度变换和行列式因子修正平行板卡西米尔能。本文旨在揭示这一结构背后的共同数学本质（Schur补结构，Schur-complement structure），并将其推广为一种普适的有效度规方案，用以处理非线性理论在常背景上线性化后的涨落系统。

Method: 通过分析约化格林函数（reduced Green function）的Schur补结构，证明约化二次型同时控制格林函数的分母和能量密度插入产生的分子。将该有效度规方案应用于非线性标量理论和非线性电动力学 $\mathcal{L}(\mathcal{F})$：对于前者，有效张量为拉格朗日量在常梯度背景上的Hessian矩阵；对于后者，常磁场背景将涨落分为普通Maxwell支和异常光学支（extraordinary optical branch）。

Result: 在非线性电动力学中，分别通过直接模式求和（direct mode summation）和分支逐一应用有效度规公式计算平行板卡西米尔能，两种方法结果完全一致。所得能量依赖于磁场背景与板之间的取向，在常规非线性电磁扇区中展现出了具体的各向异性卡西米尔响应（anisotropic Casimir response）。

Conclusion: Schur补结构是理解线性化涨落卡西米尔效应的统一框架，有效度规方案可从洛伦兹破缺标量场推广至非线性场论，为处理非线性理论中涨落诱导的Casimir效应提供了通用工具。

Abstract: We study the Casimir effect in nonlinear field theories through the effective geometries that \mbox{govern} their linearized fluctuations. Previous analyses of Lorentz-violating scalar fields showed that a constant kinetic background modifies the parallel-plate Casimir energy by a rescaling of the plate separation and an overall determinant factor. We show that this structure is not merely a consequence of diagonalizing the reduced Green function. It follows from a common Schur-complement structure: after Fourier reduction parallel to the plates, the same reduced quadratic form controls the spectral denominator of the reduced Green function and the numerator generated by the energy-density insertion. This observation allows the Lorentz-violating scalar result to be used as an effective-metric prescription for regular fluctuation sectors arising from the linearization of nonlinear theories around constant backgrounds. In nonlinear scalar theories, the effective tensor is the Hessian of the Lagrangian evaluated on a constant-gradient background. In nonlinear electrodynamics $\mathcal{L}(\mathcal{F})$, a constant magnetic background splits the fluctuations into an ordinary Maxwell branch and an extraordinary optical branch. For this electromagnetic sector, we compute the parallel-plate Casimir energy both by direct mode summation and by applying the effective-metric formula branch by branch, finding exact agreement. The resulting energy depends on the orientation of the magnetic background relative to the plates, providing a concrete anisotropic Casimir response in a regular nonlinear electromagnetic sector.

</details>


### [144] [Universal structure in the interactions of massless fields on the lightcone](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17380)
*Jin Kozaki,Yasha Neiman*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在光锥形式（lightcone formalism）下，将无质量任意自旋场（massless fields of arbitrary spin）的三次顶点（cubic vertices）从平直时空推广到（反）德西特时空（(Anti-)de Sitter spacetime），证明了自对偶/手征理论（self-dual/chiral theories）仅需三次顶点即可完全自洽，并揭示了顶点可通过线性化曲率（linearized curvatures）的“阿贝尔化”推广来表达。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将光锥形式下无质量任意自旋场的三次相互作用顶点从平直时空推广到（反）德西特时空，并验证自对偶/手征理论在仅含三次顶点时的完备自洽性。

Method: 通过将光锥形式中所有三次顶点表达为线性化曲率的“阿贝尔化”（abelian）推广形式，利用此类线性化曲率的共形不变性（conformal invariance），建立平直时空与（反）德西特时空顶点之间的简洁联系。

Result: 给出了所有三次顶点的简洁显式表达式；证明了自对偶杨-米尔斯（Self-Dual Yang-Mills）、自对偶广义相对论（Self-Dual General Relativity）和手征高自旋引力（Chiral Higher-Spin Gravity）等理论在仅含三次顶点时完全自洽；同时指出所给顶点表达式是非局域的（non-local），但可转化为局域形式。

Conclusion: 光锥形式中任意自旋的三次顶点可统一由线性化曲率的阿贝尔化推广得到，平直与（反）德西特时空之间的简洁对应关系源于线性化曲率的共形不变性；尽管非局域性存在，但可方便地化为局域形式。

Abstract: We consider cubic interactions of massless fields of arbitrary spin in 4 spacetime dimensions, within the lightcone formalism. We extend two key results from flat to (Anti-)de Sitter spacetime. First, we present a simple explicit expression for all the cubic vertices. Second, we prove that the various self-dual/chiral theories, such as Self-Dual Yang-Mills, Self-Dual General Relativity and Chiral Higher-Spin Gravity, are fully consistent with no need for vertices beyond cubic. The key observation behind our results is that all cubic vertices in the lightcone formalism can be expressed as a direct generalization of the "abelian" vertices formed by multiplying linearized curvatures. The simple relationship between flat and (Anti-)de Sitter then follows essentially from the conformal invariance of such linearized curvatures. The price for such simplicity is that our vertex expressions are non-local. It is however easy to bring them into a local form, which we also present.

Method: 基于Manschot和Wang的i\varepsilon-规定（i\varepsilon-prescription）和E_s-正则化模积分框架，构建了闭合有向环面（closed oriented torus）在GSO投影前的正则化扇区泛函。同时采用Baccianti等人的Lorentzian反演重构方法独立交叉验证结果。

Conclusion: 这项工作为Type IIB超弦理论环面真空的未投影扇区提供了首个直接的正则化构造，为后续的弦论真空分析奠定了正则化方法基础。

Abstract: We study the one-loop torus vacuum of Type IIB Superstring theory through sector-resolved modular integrals. Building on the i\varepsilon-prescription and the E_s-regularized modular-integral framework of Manschot and Wang [1], we construct regularized sector functionals for the closed oriented torus before the final GSO projection. The construction keeps the unprojected spin-sector data explicit and fixes the compact-domain and cusp contributions within a single modular prescription. We also independently cross-check the result with the Lorentzian-inversion reconstruction of modular integrals by Baccianti et al. [2] This provides a first direct regularized construction of the unprojected sectors of the Type IIB Superstring torus vacuum.

### [146] [Imprints of dynamical phases in semiclassical entanglement entropy in 2D CFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17625)
*Parijat Dey,Semanti Dutta,Bobby Ezhuthachan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了大c共形场论（CFT）中由sl(2,ℝ)驱动态导致的半经典纠缠熵的时间演化，并在AdS₃/CFT₂对偶框架下，通过计算后反应几何与微扰极小面积，验证了Faulkner-Lewkowycz-Maldacena（FLM）猜想关于全息纠缠熵一阶量子修正的预言。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究驱动共形场论（driven CFT）中纠缠熵的动力学相位特征，并在全息对偶（holographic dual）框架下检验纠缠熵的量子修正是否与边界CFT结果一致，从而验证Faulkner-Lewkowycz-Maldacena（FLM）猜想的正确性。

Method: 在1+1维大c CFT中构造sl(2,ℝ)驱动态，通过改变驱动参数观察纠缠熵的动力学相位；在全息对偶中，以相干态（coherent state）中能动张量（stress tensor）的期望值作为源项求解爱因斯坦方程（Einstein's equation），得到后反应几何（backreacted geometry）；在短距近似（short distance approximation）下，计算O(G_N^0)阶的微扰极小面积（perturbed minimal area）与体纠缠熵（bulk entanglement entropy）。

Result: 驱动参数变化时，纠缠熵呈现驱动CFT动力学相位的特征；全息计算得到的体纠缠熵与边界CFT纠缠熵在O(c^0)阶相匹配。

Conclusion: 该匹配结果为Faulkner-Lewkowycz-Maldacena（FLM）猜想关于全息纠缠熵一阶量子修正的部分提供了非平凡检验（nontrivial check）。

Abstract: We study the time evolution of semiclassical entanglement entropy in a class of $sl(2,\mathbb{R})$ driven states in a large $c$ conformal field theory (CFT) in $1+1$ spacetime dimensions. Upon varying the parameters of the drive, we find that the entanglement entropy exhibits the signature of the dynamical phases of the driven CFT. We further study the holographic dual of this CFT where the excited states of a minimally coupled scalar in $AdS_3$ induce a backreaction that modifies the background geometry. We compute the back reacted geometry by solving Einstein's equation with the expectation value of the stress tensor in the coherent state as the source term. Subsequently, we calculate the time evolution of the perturbed minimal area and the bulk entanglement entropy at $O(G_N^0)$, up to the sub-leading order in short distance approximation. These results match the CFT entanglement entropy in the boundary at $O(c^0)$, and serve as a nontrivial check of the Faulkner-Lewkowycz-Maldacena (FLM) conjecture for the first quantum correction of holographic entanglement entropy. The details of the check has been provided in the accompanying ancillary notebook.

### [147] [Hamiltonian formalism for Bose excitations in a plasma with a non-Abelian interaction: plasmon bremsstrahlung](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17670)
*Yu. A. Markov,M. A. Markova,N. Yu. Markov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种描述高能色荷粒子在热夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）中碰撞时产生等离子体轫致辐射（plasmon bremsstrahlung radiation）的经典哈密顿波理论，通过推广李-泊松括号（Lie-Poisson bracket）并引入四组玻尔兹曼型（Boltzmann-type）动力学方程，在固定色荷近似下获得了等离子体数密度无色分量和有色分量的精确解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能色荷粒子在热夸克-胶子等离子体中的碰撞伴随着等离子体轫致辐射，这一过程需要系统的理论描述。现有理论框架尚缺乏对涉及两个独立玻色子场分量和两个非阿贝尔色荷（non-Abelian color charge）的热QCD（quantum chromodynamics）介质的完整哈密顿处理。

Method: 提出经典哈密顿波理论，将李-泊松括号推广至热QCD介质情形，引入两个独立的玻色子正规场变量分量$a^{\phantom{\ast}(1)a}_{\bf k}$和$a^{\phantom{\ast}(2)a}_{\bf k}$以及两个非阿贝尔色荷$Q^{\,a}_1$和$Q^{\,a}_2$。构建包含软集体激发和两个硬检验粒子色荷自由度的正则变换（canonical transformations），并以新正规场变量$c^{\,a}_{\bf k}$的分量$c^{\phantom{\ast}(α)a}_{\bf k}$和新色荷${\mathcal Q}^{a}_α$的积分-幂级数形式给出六阶最一般结构。采用多时间尺度微扰理论（multiple-time-scale perturbation theory）构建动力学方程。

Result: 引入等离子体数密度${\mathcal N}^{\,(α,α^{\prime})aa^{\prime}_{\phantom{1}}}_{\bf k}(τ)$，该量在有效色空间和有效双粒子空间中均为非平凡矩阵。得到了考虑硬粒子平均色荷时间演化的自洽四组玻尔兹曼型动力学方程系统。在固定色荷近似下，获得了定义无色分量$N^{(1)}_{\bf k}$、$W^{(1)}_{\bf k}$和有色分量$N^{(2)}_{\bf k}$、$W^{(2)}_{\bf k}$的动力学方程系统的精确解。

Conclusion: 该经典哈密顿波理论为描述热夸克-胶子等离子体中高能色荷粒子碰撞导致的等离子体轫致辐射提供了系统框架。四组玻尔兹曼型动力学方程及其在固定色荷近似下的精确解，为理解等离子体数密度的无色和有色分量的动力学行为奠定了基础。

Abstract: The classical Hamiltonian wave theory describing plasmon bremsstrahlung radiation occurring upon collision of high-energy color-charged particles in a hot quark-gluon plasma is proposed. A generalization of the Lie-Poisson bracket to the case of a hot QCD medium, involving two independent components $a^{\phantom{\ast}(1)a}_{\bf k}$ and $a^{\phantom{\ast}(2)a}_{\bf k}$ of the bosonic normal field variable $a^{\phantom{\ast}a}_{\bf k}$ and two non-Abelian color charges $Q^{\,a}_1$ and $Q^{\,a}_2$ is suggested. The canonical transformations including both bosonic degrees of freedom of the soft collective excitations of the hot quark-gluon plasma and degrees of freedom of two hard test particles related to their color charges are written out. The most general structure of the canonical transformations in the form of integro-power series in the components $c^{\phantom{\ast}(α)a}_{\bf k},\,α= 1, 2$, of the new normal field variable $c^{\,a}_{\bf k}$ and in the new color charges ${\mathcal Q}^{a}_α$ up to the terms of sixth order is presented. To construct kinetic equations the multiple-time-scale perturbation theory is used. The notion of the plasmon number density ${\mathcal N}^{\,(α,α^{\prime})aa^{\prime}_{\phantom{1}}}_{\bf k}(τ)$, which is a nontrivial matrix both in the effective color space and in effective two-particle space, is introduced. The self-consistent system of four Boltzmann-type kinetic equations taking into account the time evolution of the averaged color charges of the hard particles is obtained. In the approximation of the fixed color charges of two interacting particles the exact solution of the system of kinetic equations defining the dynamics of the colorless $N^{(1)}_{\bf k}$, $W^{(1)}_{\bf k}$ and color $N^{(2)}_{\bf k}$, $W^{(2)}_{\bf k}$ components of the plasmon number density, is obtained.

### [148] [Monopoles, Center Vortices, Confinement in (3+1)d, and the Lens-Space Twisted Partition Function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17708)
*Yui Hayashi,Yuya Tanizaki*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出利用 $\mathbb{Z}_N^{[1]}$ 对称性扭曲配分函数（twisted partition functions）来定义中心涡旋凝聚（center-vortex condensation）和单极子凝聚（monopole condensation）的规范不变判据；通过分析这些配分函数在伴随希格斯相（adjoint Higgs phase）中的行为，揭示了两者之间的内在关系，并证明中心涡旋凝聚必然伴随单极子凝聚，进而超越了传统的 Wilson-'t Hooft 分类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论中缺少一种规范不变（gauge-invariant）的方式来判定中心涡旋凝聚和单极子凝聚，这使得对非阿贝尔规范理论（non-Abelian gauge theory）中禁闭（confinement）机制的理解不够精确。本文旨在建立基于拓扑对称性（topological symmetry）的严格判据，并澄清这两种凝聚之间的逻辑关系。

Method: 利用 $\mathbb{Z}_N^{[1]}$ 对称性（一种高阶形式对称性（higher-form symmetry））构造扭曲配分函数：以环面（torus）扭曲配分函数表征中心涡旋凝聚，以透镜空间（lens space）扭曲配分函数表征单极子凝聚。通过拓扑场论（topological field theory）技术分析这两类配分函数在伴随希格斯相中的领头阶贡献，并推导凝聚之间的关联。

Result: 环面扭曲配分函数和透镜空间扭曲配分函数的领头非平凡贡献分别来自中心涡旋和单极子，验证了所提判据的有效性。进一步证明，具有中心涡旋凝聚的有能隙相（gapped phase）必然也呈现单极子凝聚。在中心涡旋模型（center-vortex model）中，高阶电荷单极子凝聚（higher-charge monopole condensation）展现了对称性分数量子化（symmetry fractionalization）现象，超出了传统的 Wilson-'t Hooft 分类框架。

Conclusion: 本文建立的规范不变判据为研究非阿贝尔规范理论中的禁闭与拓扑序（topological order）提供了新的工具。中心涡旋凝聚对单极子凝聚的必然蕴含关系表明，这两种凝聚并非相互独立，而是具有层次结构。对称性分数量子化的发现则拓展了对规范理论相图（phase diagram）的理论理解。

Abstract: We propose the gauge-invariant criteria of center-vortex condensation and monopole condensation using the $\mathbb{Z}_N^{[1]}$-symmetry twisted partition functions: The torus twisted partition function characterizes the center-vortex condensation, and the lens-space twisted partition function characterizes the monopole condensation. To justify our proposal, we study how these twisted partition functions behave in the adjoint Higgs phase and show that their leading nontrivial contributions come from the center vortex and monopole, respectively. Using the techniques of topological field theories, we uncover the relation between the center-vortex and monopole condensations, and in particular, we prove that the gapped phase with the center-vortex condensation necessarily shows the monopole condensation, too. We then study a center-vortex model with monopoles as an illustrative example, and the higher-charge monopole condensation gives an example of the symmetry fractionalization, which goes beyond the conventional Wilson-'t Hooft classification.

</details>


### [149] [Aspects of Witten Diagrams for Holographic Defects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17719)
*Dean Carmi,Sudip Ghosh,Trakshu Sharma*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文通过分裂表示方法，研究了存在共形缺陷（conformal defect）的全息CFT中Witten图的共形块分解（conformal block decomposition），得到了树图级别OPE系数的显式表达式以及交叉核（crossing kernel）的闭式解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在缺陷共形场论（defect CFT）的背景下，尚缺乏对Witten图中共形块分解系数的系统解析结果，这些系数对于发展bootstrapping方法至关重要。

Method: 采用适配于探针膜（probe brane）设置的AdS传播子分裂表示（split representation），对接触图、树图交换图以及单圈两点Witten图进行直接道（direct channel）共形块分解，并推导树图交换的交叉道块展开递推关系。对于交叉核，利用体道（bulk channel）Lorentzian反演公式导出闭式表达式。

Result: 给出了树图Witten图直接道分解中OPE系数的显式表达式；建立了两点树图交换图的交叉道块展开系数递推关系并计算了种子系数；针对零维缺陷（d=2,4）和面缺陷（d=4,6），导出了缺陷到体道交叉核的闭式表达式。

Conclusion: 所得树图块分解系数可用于发展缺陷CFT中体算符两点函数的解析bootstrapping方法；交叉核的闭式结果为理解缺陷CFT中的道交叉关系提供了精确描述。

Abstract: In this paper, we study the conformal block decomposition of Witten diagrams for $d$-dimensional holographic CFTs in the presence of a $p$-dimensional conformal defect. The holographic dual in this case contains a probe AdS$_{p+1}$ brane embedded inside AdS$_{d+1}$. In particular, we focus on contact, tree-level exchanges and some one-loop two-point Witten diagrams, which contribute to the two-point function of CFT bulk scalar operators. We also consider a tree-level exchange diagram for a three-point function involving one CFT bulk scalar operator and two scalar operators localized on the defect. Employing the split representation of AdS propagators, adapted to the probe brane setup, we perform the direct channel conformal block decompositions of these diagrams. In the case of tree-level diagrams, we obtain explicit expressions for the OPE coefficients in the direct channel decompositions. For two-point tree-level exchange diagrams, we derive recursion relations for the coefficients in the crossed-channel block expansions and compute the seed coefficients which serve as inputs for these relations. Our explicit results for the block decomposition coefficients for tree-level Witten diagrams are potentially useful for further developing the analytic functional approach to bootstrapping two-point functions of bulk operators in general defect CFTs. We also study the crossing kernel, which encodes the bulk channel partial wave expansion of a defect channel partial wave. Using the bulk channel Lorentzian inversion formula for defect CFTs, we derive closed form expressions for this defect-to-bulk channel crossing kernel for zero-dimensional defects in $d=2,4$ dimensions and surface defects in $d=4,6$ dimensions.

</details>


### [150] [A Double--Scaling Large--\(d\) Saddle of BFSS/BMN Matrix Quantum Mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17758)
*Badis Ydri*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文对质量变形玻色子BFSS矩阵量子力学的大d动力学进行了研究，通过Hubbard-Stratonovich变换局域化Yang-Mills相互作用，识别出一个关联双标度极限（double-scaling limit），在该极限下系统在低温和高温区间分别呈现BFSS₂型和IKKT型动力学行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索质量变形玻色子BFSS矩阵量子力学在大d极限下的非平庸动力学行为，特别是通过引入关联双标度极限来平衡Yang-Mills相互作用和显式质量变形（mass deformation），从而在二者之间实现参数化的竞争与插值。

Method: 采用Hubbard-Stratonovich变换局域化Yang-Mills相互作用，将矩阵坐标积分后得到关于辅助伴随核（auxiliary adjoint kernel）的有效作用量；引入交换对称鞍点（commuting-symmetric saddle）及其最大对称化特例，通过单个动态生成的质量偏移（mass shift）k₀编码相互作用；最终系统化为具有自洽频率s²=m+k₀的规范矩阵谐振子（gauged matrix harmonic oscillator），该频率由能隙方程（gap equation）确定。

Result: 在低温度X空间物理、holonomy有效作用量及Yang-Mills可观测量方面给出了相结构分析。识别出一个关联双标度极限d→∞、m→∞且κ=m^{3/2}/d固定，在此极限下系统插值于对易子主导的BFSS区域与质量主导的高斯区域之间。低温区间能隙增强抬高退禁闭标度，打开参数化大均匀holonomy区域；高温区间高斯描述保持自洽，而对易子贡献被参数化压制。

Conclusion: 双标度理论在低温下表现为弱耦合BFSS₂型规范谐振子扇区行为（均匀holonomy区域扩大），在高温下表现为几乎对易矩阵的IKKT型行为，从而实现了两种矩阵模型动力学行为之间的平滑过渡。

Abstract: We study the large--\(d\) dynamics of the mass--deformed bosonic \(\mathrm{BFSS}_{d+1}\) matrix quantum mechanics using a Hubbard--Stratonovich localization of the Yang--Mills interaction. After integrating out the matrix coordinates, the theory reduces to a holonomy--dependent effective action for an auxiliary adjoint kernel. We introduce a commuting--symmetric saddle and its maximally symmetric specialization, in which the interaction is encoded in a single dynamically generated mass shift \(k_0\). The resulting large--\(d\) description is a gauged matrix harmonic oscillator with self--consistent frequency \(s^2=m+k_0\), fixed by a gap equation.
  We analyze the low--temperature \(X\)-space physics, the holonomy effective action, the Yang--Mills observable, and the associated phase structure. We then identify a correlated double--scaling limit in which \(d\to\infty\), \(m\to\infty\), and \(κ=m^{3/2}/d\) is held fixed. In this limit the Yang--Mills interaction and the explicit mass deformation remain parametrically balanced: the theory interpolates between the commutator--dominated BFSS regime and the mass--dominated Gaussian regime.
  The double--scaled theory exhibits two complementary large--\(d\) regimes. At low temperature, the enhanced gap pushes the deconfinement scale upward and opens a parametrically large uniform--holonomy region, where the bulk dynamics behaves as weakly coupled \(\mathrm{BFSS}_2\)--type gauged harmonic--oscillator sectors. At the same time, the high--temperature branch reveals an overlap window in which the Gaussian description remains self--consistent while the commutator contribution per matrix pair is parametrically suppressed. The resulting dynamics is therefore \(\mathrm{BFSS}_2\)--like in its enlarged uniform--holonomy sector and IKKT--like in its almost--commuting matrix behavior.

*Daichi Takeda*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从全息对偶的角度推导了高温区全息布朗运动的林布拉德（Lindbladian）描述，验证了其完全正性与迹保持性，并分析了在BTZ黑洞和AdS$_5$黑膜背景下的动力学行为，包括相空间矩的时间演化、能量弛豫和稳态特征。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于拖尾弦端点（trailing string endpoint）的影响泛函，推导出对应的量子主方程（quantum master equation），并证明其满足完全正性（complete positivity）和迹保持性（trace-preserving）。随后在两套全息背景——BTZ黑洞（BTZ black hole）和AdS$_5$黑膜（AdS$_5$ black brane）——下显式求解林布拉德系数，后者仅考虑沿$x^1$方向的端点涨落。

Result: 成功构造了高温区全息布朗运动的林布拉德描述，给出了BTZ黑洞和AdS$_5$黑膜背景下的林布拉德系数显式表达式，并展示了相空间矩的时间演化、能量弛豫（energy relaxation）以及稳态（steady states）的分析结果。

Conclusion: 全息布朗运动可在高温极限下被严格地纳入林布拉德形式，这为利用开放量子系统工具研究全息系统的非平衡动力学提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We derive a Lindbladian description of holographic Brownian motion in the high-temperature regime. Starting from the influence functional for a trailing string endpoint, we identify the corresponding quantum master equation and prove that it is completely positive and trace-preserving. We determine the coefficients of the Lindbladian explicitly for two holographic backgrounds: the BTZ black hole and the AdS$_5$ black brane, restricting in the latter case to the endpoint fluctuation along the $x^1$-direction. We then analyze the time evolution of phase-space moments, energy relaxation, and steady states.

### [152] [Single-valued polylogarithms for higher genera](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17911)
*Konstantin Baune,Johannes Broedel,Yannis Moeckli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将亏格一黎曼曲面上的单值多对数函数（single-valued polylogarithms）构造推广到更高亏格的带单穿孔黎曼曲面，建立了与Enriquez联络及D'Hoker-Hidding-Schlotterer多对数函数的联系，并在该框架下识别了Arakelov Green函数。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前亏格一（genus one）情形下的单值多对数函数构造已被建立（arXiv:2511.15240），但更高亏格的穿孔黎曼曲面（once-punctured Riemann surfaces of higher genera）上的推广尚未完成，这限制了该类函数在更一般几何背景下的应用。

Result: 成功将单值多对数函数的构造从亏格一推广到更高亏格的带单穿孔黎曼曲面，所得函数具有平凡的单值表示，因而可降为曲面上的良定义函数；并在该框架下识别出Arakelov Green函数（Arakelov Green's function）。

Conclusion: 本文为更高亏格穿孔黎曼曲面上的单值多对数函数提供了统一的构造方案，并通过与已有构造的对比及Arakelov Green函数的识别，验证了该方法的兼容性与理论价值。

Abstract: We extend the construction of single-valued polylogarithms at genus one from arXiv:2511.15240 to once-punctured Riemann surfaces of higher genera. The resulting functions have a trivial monodromy representation with respect to the fundamental group, hence they descend to well-defined functions on the surface. Our construction of single-valued polylogarithms is based on Enriquez' connection and relates them to the polylogarithms from D'Hoker-Hidding-Schlotterer. Finally, we identify the Arakelov Green's function within our framework.

Conclusion: 全息Schwinger-Keldysh方案在禁闭相与解禁闭相中均可有效应用，为研究夸克-反夸克系统及其非平衡动力学提供了统一的全息框架。

Abstract: The holographic Schwinger-Keldysh (SK) prescription proposed by Skenderis and van Rees (SvR) has the advantage of being applicable whether or not the gravity dual contains a black hole. Taking advantage of this feature, we derive the quadratic effective action for a quark-antiquark pair in the confinement phase within the holographic SK framework of SvR. We also apply the SvR prescription to derive the quadratic effective action for a single heavy quark moving at a constant velocity in a nonequilibrium steady state in the deconfinement phase.
