### [154] [UV/IR mixing as an artifact of non-covariant quantisation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17964)
*Kilian Hersent,Flavio Mercati*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究标量场在非交换闵可夫斯基时空（noncommutative Minkowski spacetime）上的路径积分量子化（path integral quantisation），指出量子化方案依赖于非交换泛函导数（noncommutative functional derivative）的选择，并区分两种自然方案：一种保留未形变统计（undeformed statistics），重现标准方案并导致UV/IR混合与形变庞加莱协变性（deformed Poincaré covariance）破缺；另一种采用辫统计（braided statistics），获得协变且无混合的n点函数。作者论证UV/IR混合并非非交换性（noncommutativity）的固有特征，而是对称性破缺量子化的产物。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清非交换场论中UV/IR混合的起源，区分其是由非交换几何本身导致，还是由不恰当的量子化方案所引入。

Method: 通过分析标量场在量子齐性空间（quantum homogeneous space）上的路径积分量子化，引入两种非交换泛函导数选择，比较它们在形变庞加莱协变性（deformed Poincaré covariance）和UV/IR混合方面的表现，并将形式体系应用于T-闵可夫斯基模型（T-Minkowski models）、欧几里得三维量子引力模型（Euclidean three-dimensional quantum gravity model）和量子二球面（quantum two-sphere）。

Result: 保留未形变统计的方案重现标准量子化，产生破缺形变庞加莱协变性并伴有UV/IR混合；而采用辫统计的方案则获得协变的n点函数且无UV/IR混合。外部动量与环路动量在非平面贡献（non-planar contributions）中的交织被确认为协变破缺和混合的共同来源。

Conclusion: 在所述模型中，[8]中报告的UV/IR混合并非非交换性的本质特征，而是由破缺形变对称性的量子化方案所引入的人为产物（artifact）。协变性由量子化方案决定，有限性由传播子独立决定，二者可被解耦分析。

Abstract: We study the path integral quantisation of a scalar field on a generic noncommutative deformation of Minkowski space, built as a quantum homogeneous space of a deformed Poincaré group. We show that the procedure depends on the choice of noncommutative functional derivative, and we isolate two natural choices, distinguished by the space in which the Leibniz rule remains undeformed. The first, which carries the undeformed statistics, reproduces the standard scheme and yields n-point functions that break the deformed Poincaré covariance and exhibit the UV/IR mixing of [8]. The second, which adapts the functional calculus to the braided statistics of the fields in the spirit of [20], yields covariant n-point functions free of this mixing. We trace both the covariance breaking and the mixing to a single source, the intertwining of external and loop momenta in the non-planar contributions, and conclude that, in the models considered, the UV/IR mixing of [8] is an artifact of a quantisation that breaks the deformed symmetry rather than a feature of noncommutativity itself. We further disentangle covariance, fixed by the quantisation scheme, from finiteness, fixed independently by the propagator, and illustrate the formalism on the T-Minkowski models, the Euclidean three-dimensional quantum gravity model, and the quantum two-sphere.

</details>


### [155] [Generalised Symmetries and Manifest Duality II: Curved Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18013)
*Subhroneel Chakrabarti,Arkajyoti Manna,Madhusudhan Raman*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将自对偶规范场论的对偶势表述（potential-based formulation）推广至弯曲时空，通过Sen形式论的度规依赖线性映射实现引力耦合，并在AdS₅×S⁵上验证了全息边界贡献与超引力RR四形式势的局部壳上等同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用Sen形式论（Sen's formalism）中度规依赖的线性映射（metric-dependent linear map）编码引力耦合；保留高阶h-规范对称性（higher-form h-gauge symmetry），通过不同规范选择恢复Sen的通量表述或势表述；导出D=4n环面约化理论与任意维多重形式表述（polyform formulation）的引力映射显式形式。

Result: 无需费米子化（fermionisation）即可重现二维手征玻色子（chiral boson）的Álvarez-Gaumé-Witten引力反常，以及十维自对偶五形式的同类反常；在AdS₅×S⁵上，物理壳上作用量（on-shell action）无需手动添加边界项即给出全息原理所需的非零边界贡献；建立了与超引力RR四形式势（RR four-form potential）的局部壳上等同关系。

Conclusion: 该势形式表述在弯曲时空下自洽地包含引力耦合、反常与全息边界项，为对偶规范场论在引力和弦理论中的应用提供了统一框架。

Abstract: We extend the potential-based formulation of self-dual and duality-symmetric gauge theories developed in \cite{Chakrabarti:2025gyt} to curved spacetime. The gravitational coupling is encoded by the same metric-dependent linear map of Sen's formalism. The parent new action retains the higher-form $h$-gauge symmetry, and different gauge choices reproduce either Sen's flux-based formulation or a potential-based description in which the shadow sector decouples directly at the level of the action. We also derive explicit form of the gravitational map for the toroidally reduced theory in $D=4n$ and for a polyform formulation in arbitrary dimension, both of which apply equally to ours as well as Sen's formalism. As non-trivial checks, we reproduce the Álvarez-Gaumé-Witten gravitational anomalies of the two-dimensional chiral boson without fermionisation, and of the ten-dimensional self-dual five-form. Finally, on $\mathrm{AdS}_5\times S^5$ the physical on-shell action yields the non-vanishing boundary contribution required by holography without adding a boundary term by hand. We also establish a local on-shell identification with the textbook supergravity RR four-form potential.

</details>

### [156] [Spin effects in the particle current of Bose-Einstein condensates in synthetic gauge fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17248)
*Hugo Bencomo Martín,Antonio Muñoz Mateo*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究报道了非相对论性理论中自旋（spin）的效应——粒子流密度中的自旋项，通过赝自旋-1/2玻色子的玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）构建的合成霍尔系统（synthetic Hall system）进行观测，并分析了相互作用强度对该自旋项的影响及其与Aharonov-Bohm相移（phase shift）的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋虽非相对论性量，但其效应在非相对论性理论框架（non-relativistic theoretical framework）中并不总是显式体现；本文旨在揭示其中一个被忽略的效应——粒子流密度（particle current density）中的自旋项。

Method: 利用赝自旋-1/2（pseudospin-1/2）玻色子构成的非相对论性玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体搭建合成霍尔系统，通过调节相互作用强度（interaction strength）来观测自旋项对粒子流的影响。

Result: 在无相互作用系统中，自旋项对粒子流的贡献使得经典漂移速度（classical drift velocity）在局域上得以匹配；随着相互作用增强，自旋-轨道流比（spin-to-orbital current ratio）下降。自旋项贡献的变化会改变整体粒子速度及其在回路中的环量（circulation），进而影响其与Aharonov-Bohm相移的关系。

Conclusion: 粒子流中的自旋项在非相对论性系统中具有可观测的物理效应，其贡献随相互作用强度变化，并最终影响与Aharonov-Bohm相移相关的物理行为。

Abstract: Although spin is not a relativistic quantity, its effects are not always manifestly captured within non-relativistic theoretical frameworks. We report on one of these effects: the spin term in the particle current density, which could be observed in the setup of a synthetic Hall system made with non-relativistic Bose-Einstein condensates of pseudospin-1/2 bosonic particles. By tuning the interaction strength, the system can show how the spin term in the particle current is needed for the local matching of classical drift velocity in the ground state of the non-interacting system, whereas for increasing interactions the spin-to-orbital current ratio decreases. In either case, since the overall particle velocity changes with the spin term contribution, so does its circulation in a loop, which in turn has physical consequences for its relationship with the Aharonov-Bohm phase shift.

</details>


### [157] [Vorticity Induced by Non-frontal Collisions of Quantum Droplets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17498)
*J. E. Alba-Arroyo,Santiago F. Caballero-Benitez,Rocio Jáuregu*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文在扩展Gross-Pitaevskii方程框架下，理论分析了超冷碱金属原子构成的量子液滴（quantum droplets）因非正面二元碰撞所引发的旋转动力学。数值实验揭示了系统中存在多种稳定的拓扑激发（topological excitations），包括涡旋环（vortex rings）、位错线（dislocation lines）和单物种涡旋（vortices in one species）。这些拓扑缺陷的自发产生依赖于韦伯数（Weber number）和碰撞参数（impact parameter），并提出了一种利用相互作用斜坡（interaction ramps）在实空间和傅里叶空间探测涡旋的实验方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究超冷原子量子液滴非正面碰撞诱导的旋转动力学，探索在不可压缩区（incompressible regime）下异核量子液滴碰撞中自发产生的拓扑激发及其鲁棒性，为实验观测提供理论基础和可行的探测方案。

Method: 采用扩展Gross-Pitaevskii方程（extended Gross-Pitaevskii equation）框架进行理论研究，数值实验模拟由$^{41}$K和$^{87}$Rb原子组成的异核量子液滴在不可压缩区的非正面二元碰撞过程，分析碰撞参数和韦伯数对拓扑缺陷产生的影响。

Result: 非正面碰撞导致动力学不稳定性，可自发产生涡旋环、位错线和单物种涡旋等拓扑激发，这些拓扑缺陷对测量具有鲁棒性。其出现与否取决于韦伯数和碰撞参数。

Conclusion: 提出了一种利用相互作用斜坡在实空间和傅里叶空间进行涡旋探测的实验方案，为拓扑激发在超冷原子量子液滴体系中的实验研究提供了可行途径。

Abstract: The rotational dynamics induced by the non-frontal binary collisions of quantum droplets composed of ultracold alkali atoms are analyzed. A theoretical study is presented within the extended Gross-Pitaevskii equation framework, using experimentally feasible conditions. Numerical experiments elucidate a rich landscape of possible topological excitations in the system that are robust towards measurements. The collision of heteronuclear quantum droplets composed of $^{41}$K and $^{87}$Rb atoms in the incompressible regime, gives rise to dynamical instabilities that spontaneously generate topological defects: vortex rings, dislocation lines, and vortices in one species. Their presence depends on the Weber number and the impact parameter. An experimental proposal for vortex detection in both real and Fourier space using interaction ramps is described.

### [158] [Universal scaling and relaxation in decaying turbulence of Bose gases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18059)
*Arnol D. García-Orozco,Michelle A. Moreno-Armijos,Sarah Sab,Amilson Fritsch,Vanderlei Salvador Bagnato*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本短评综述了孤立量子系统中湍流玻色气体的普适弛豫动力学，重点讨论了非热固定点（nonthermal fixed points）与波湍流（wave turbulence）中的自相似标度行为，以及通过普适标度解从有限动量分布数据中提取普适指数的方法。实验展示了三维囚禁玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose–Einstein condensate）中正反级联（direct and inverse cascades）的观测结果，揭示了由普适标度律支配的不同弛豫阶段，表明湍流在远离平衡态动力学及热化过程中起到关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解孤立量子系统的弛豫动力学是非平衡物理领域的核心挑战，但目前对远离平衡态下量子多体系统的普适行为认识仍不充分，亟需统一的理论框架与实验验证。

Method: 采用短评综述形式，综合理论分析与实验观测；理论方面聚焦非热固定点与波湍流中的自相似标度行为，并介绍一种通过微分方程的普适标度解从有限动量分布区域提取普适指数的方法。

Result: 在三维囚禁玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中观测到直接级联与逆级联，揭示了由普适标度律支配的不同弛豫阶段。

Conclusion: 湍流在远离平衡态动力学中扮演关键角色，为理解量子多体系统中的输运过程与热化提供了统一视角。

Abstract: Understanding the relaxation dynamics of isolated quantum systems remains a central challenge in nonequilibrium physics. In this short review, we discuss recent experimental and theoretical advances in universal dynamics of turbulent Bose gases, with particular emphasis on nonthermal fixed points and wave turbulence in our experimental system at the São Carlos Institute of Physics of the University of São Paulo. We highlight the emergence of self-similar scaling behavior and its connection to particle and energy transport across momentum scales. In addition, we discuss an approach in which a differential equation has a universal scaling solution, providing a practical framework for extracting universal exponents from limited regions of the momentum distribution. Furthermore, we recap experimental observations of direct and inverse cascades in a three-dimensional trapped Bose--Einstein condensate, revealing distinct relaxation stages governed by universal scaling laws. These results demonstrate that turbulence plays a key role in far-from-equilibrium dynamics, offering a unified perspective on transport processes and thermalization in quantum many-body systems.

Method: 研究利用XENONnT探测器（一种双相液氙时间投影室（dual-phase liquid xenon time projection chamber））采集的$^{220}\mathrm{Rn}$和$^{222}\mathrm{Rn}$校准数据，测量了$^{212}\mathrm{Pb}$和$^{214}\mathrm{Pb}$的$\beta$衰变分支比。

Conclusion: 这些结果有助于改进暗物质和中微子实验的本底建模（background modeling），进而提升对太阳中微子及超出标准模型物理的探测灵敏度。

Abstract: We present precision measurements of $^{212}\mathrm{Pb}$ and $^{214}\mathrm{Pb}$ $β$ decay branching ratios using $^{220}\mathrm{Rn}$ and $^{222}\mathrm{Rn}$ calibration data from the XENONnT detector, a dual-phase liquid xenon time projection chamber. Characterizing these isotopes is critical, as they lead to significant low-energy backgrounds in rare-event searches. We report ground-state branching ratios of $(14.75 \pm 0.20(\mathrm{stat}) ^{+0.14}_{-0.40}(\mathrm{sys}))\%$ for $^{212}\mathrm{Pb}$ and $(9.8 \pm 0.3(\mathrm{stat}) ^{+0.8}_{-0.2}(\mathrm{sys}))\%$ for $^{214}\mathrm{Pb}$, providing the most precise direct measurements of these transitions to date. These results contribute to enhancing background modeling for dark matter and neutrino experiments, improving sensitivity to solar neutrinos and physics beyond the Standard Model.

### [160] [Perfect fluids revisited: an action principle approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17084)
*Kostas Tzanavaris*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在微分形式（differential forms）的明显协变框架下重新审视了相对论性理想流体的变分原理（variational principle），重点分析了类时流和类零流所需的边界条件。对于类零流，运动方程强制焓密度为零，导致应力-能量张量分解为具有可变压力的真空能项与零性尘埃贡献，表明其动力学本质而非运动学。该构造不依赖于引力场方程，可推广至一阶或非度规引力理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在明显协变的微分形式框架下重新审视相对论性理想流体（relativistic perfect fluids）的变分原理，特别关注良定作用原理（well-posed action principle）所需的边界数据，并系统分析将同一变分原理从类时流（timelike flows）推广至类零流（null flows）时面临的困难与物理后果。

Method: 采用微分形式构建明显协变的变分原理形式体系。对于类时流，该方法本质上是Schutz作用原理的几何化重构。对于类零流，直接应用相同的变分原理，通过运动方程分析焓密度（enthalpy density）的约束条件，并分解应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensor）的结构。

Result: 类零流的运动方程强制焓密度为零（$ρ+P=0$），系统并非一般的理想流体。其应力-能量张量分解为两项：一项类似真空能（vacuum energy-like），具有可变压力；另一项为零性尘埃（null dust）贡献。这表明类零流情形下流体推广的障碍是动力学（dynamical）而非运动学（kinematical）的。

Conclusion: 由于物质作用量（matter action）的构建独立于任何引力场方程，该变分原理构造可推广至一阶引力理论（first-order theories of gravity）或非度规引力理论（non-metric theories of gravity）。

Abstract: We revisit the variational principle for relativistic perfect fluids in a manifestly covariant formulation based on differential forms, with particular attention to the boundary data required for a well-posed action principle. For timelike flows, the formalism is largely a geometric reformulation of the Schutz action principle for perfect fluids. We then analyse the extension of the same variational principle to null flows. In that case, the system is not a generic perfect fluid: the equations of motion force the enthalpy density to vanish, $ρ+P=0$. The resulting stress-energy tensor decomposes into a vacuum energy-like term with variable pressure and a null dust contribution. This shows that the obstruction to the naive fluid extension is dynamical rather than kinematical. Since the matter action is formulated independently of any gravitational field equations, the construction can be generalised to first-order or non-metric theories of gravity.

</details>


### [161] [Quantum fate of the Choptuik naked singularity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17135)
*Chih-Hung Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文论证经典临界坍缩（critical collapse）中出现的裸奇点（naked singularity）在量子反作用（quantum backreaction）下会被覆盖：外部分析表明，量子效应会生成有限质量的陷获面（trapped surfaces），将类裸奇点区域隐藏在量子产生的视界之后，从而将可预测性丧失程度降低到与普通黑洞蒸发（black hole evaporation）相同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典临界坍缩中从光滑初始数据演化出裸奇点，这是比普通黑洞奇点更严重的时间预测性（predictability）破坏。本文的动机是检验量子反作用（quantum backreaction）能否消除这种区别，从而缩小经典广义相对论中裸奇点导致的预测性丧失。

Method: 在爱因斯坦-标量场系统（Einstein-scalar system）中，基于半经典内部（semiclassical interior）分析构建外部裸奇点区域的模型。在 $2+1$ 维通过光滑匹配和物理边界条件解析选择真空极化态（vacuum polarization state）；在 $3+1$ 维通过数值视界追踪（numerical horizon tracing）研究量子移位阈值附近的外区行为。

Result: 在 $2+1$ 维中，量子反作用将经典裸区域包裹在量子陷获分支（quantum trapped branch）中。在 $3+1$ 维中，量子移位阈值附近的外区产生有限质量的边际陷获面（marginally trapped surfaces），而非零质量的裸端点。

Conclusion: Choptuik 裸奇点（Choptuik naked singularity）与普通黑洞奇点具有相同命运：量子效应将潜在的柯西视界（Cauchy horizon）推到量子生成的视界之后，将预测性丧失简化至标准黑洞蒸发问题（black hole evaporation problem）的范围。

Abstract: Classical critical collapse provides a dynamical route from smooth initial data to a naked singularity, representing a sharper violation of predictability than ordinary black hole singularities. We argue that this distinction is erased by quantum backreaction. Building on the semiclassical interior analysis, where quantum self-energy of the collapsing matter generates a universal growing mode and a finite mass gap, we study the exterior naked singularity region that determines global visibility in the Einstein-scalar system. We analyze controlled exterior models in both $2+1$ and $3+1$ dimensions. In the former, smooth matching and physical boundary conditions analytically select a vacuum polarization state, whose backreaction cloaks the classically naked region by a quantum trapped branch. In the latter, numerical horizon tracing shows that near a quantum-shifted threshold the exterior develops finite-mass marginally trapped surfaces rather than a zero-mass naked endpoint. These results suggest a global quantum picture in which the Choptuik naked singularity shares the fate of an ordinary black hole singularity: quantum effects push the putative Cauchy horizon behind a quantum-generated horizon, thereby reducing the loss of predictability to the standard black hole evaporation problem.

</details>


### [162] [Improving low-latency multi-messenger follow-up of neutron star-black hole mergers with mode-by-mode filtering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17137)
*Francesco Iacovelli,Digvijay Wadekar,Javier Roulet,Emanuele Berti,Alessandra Corsi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种通过模式滤波（mode-by-mode filtering）处理高阶模式信噪比时间序列的方法，在低延迟下实现中子星-黑洞并合事件的快速参数估计，显著改善光度距离、视角、定位体积和次级质量等关键参数的约束，计算成本仅相当于仅使用四极矩模式的分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中子星-黑洞（neutron star-black hole, NSBH）并合事件的快速参数估计对于决定是否、在何处以及如何开展电磁对应体（electromagnetic counterpart）的后续观测至关重要。现有低延迟分析通常仅使用主导的四极矩（quadrupole）谐波，导致光度距离（luminosity distance）、倾角（inclination）和固有双星参数之间存在强简并（degeneracy），限制了电磁可探测性（electromagnetic detectability）和宿主星系关联（host-galaxy association）的估计精度。

Method: 对引力波信号的 (2,2)、(3,3) 和 (4,4) 模式信噪比（signal-to-noise-ratio, SNR）时间序列进行逐模式滤波（mode-by-mode filtering），在低延迟下实现对高阶模式信息（higher-order-mode information）的边际化（marginalization），计算成本与仅使用四极矩的分析相当。

Result: 在LIGO-Virgo网络设计灵敏度下对模拟NSBH探测事件的应用表明，该方法能够改善光度距离、视角（viewing angle）、定位体积（localization volume）和源坐标系次级质量（source-frame secondary mass）的约束。在已公开的NSBH事件数据验证中，GW190814事件因不对称性（asymmetric）和较高的信噪比而获得最显著的改进。

Conclusion: 所提出的低延迟高阶模式滤波方法能够在计算成本可接受的条件下，显著提升NSBH并合事件关键参数的估计精度，从而改善电磁对应体可探测性和宿主星系识别的判断能力。

Abstract: Rapid parameter estimation for neutron star-black hole (NSBH) mergers is essential for deciding whether, where, and how electromagnetic facilities should follow up gravitational-wave alerts. Current low-latency analyses typically use only the dominant quadrupole harmonic, leaving strong degeneracies among luminosity distance, inclination, and intrinsic binary parameters. We show that mode-by-mode filtering of the $(2,2)$, $(3,3)$, and $(4,4)$ signal-to-noise-ratio (SNR) time series enables low-latency marginalization over higher-order-mode information at a computational cost comparable to quadrupole-only analyses. Applied to simulated NSBH detections in a LIGO-Virgo network at design sensitivity, our method improves constraints on luminosity distance, viewing angle, localization volume, and source-frame secondary mass, thereby sharpening crucial estimates of electromagnetic detectability and host-galaxy association. We also validate the approach on public data for previously detected NSBH events, finding the largest improvement for the asymmetric, higher-SNR event GW190814.

</details>


### [163] [Boundary conditions and Hilbert spaces in no-roll quantum cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17163)
*Steffen Gielen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在极端慢滚动暴胀极限下构造了闭合宇宙微超空间量子宇宙学的希尔伯特空间，发现物理希尔伯特空间维数取决于标量场势能（相当于宇宙学常数）是否固定：固定时为一维，对应于Vilenkin隧穿波函数；可变时则为无限维，且自伴性要求引出一族边界条件，其中一种近似选出Hartle-Hawking波函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在极端慢滚动暴胀（extreme slow-roll inflation）极限下，将标量场近似为常数，构造闭合宇宙微超空间量子宇宙学（minisuperspace quantum cosmology）的希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space），并探讨势能项（等效于宇宙学常数）对物理态空间维数及波函数选择的影响。

Method: 在标量场恒定的近似下，将势能视为依赖于初始条件的积分常数（integration constant），等价于单模引力（unimodular gravity）中的宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）。通过固定或放开该常数的取值，分析Wheeler-DeWitt方程的解及其内积结构，并引入哈密顿量的自伴性（self-adjoint）要求来约束奇点处的边界条件。

Result: 若固定积分常数，Wheeler-DeWitt方程有两个独立解，自然内积选出具有正范数的Vilenkin隧穿波函数（tunnelling wavefunction），物理希尔伯特空间为一维。若势能自由，理论允许无限维希尔伯特空间，对应有效哈密顿量的能量本征态。自伴性要求导出一族边界条件，推广了DeWitt波函数消失判据（DeWitt criterion），该条件总导致Hartle-Hawking波函数（Hartle-Hawking wavefunction）与隧穿波函数的混合，但某一特定选择可近似选出Hartle-Hawking波函数，带有指数压低的修正。

Conclusion: 势能项（宇宙学常数）是否固定决定了物理态空间维数与主导波函数形式：固定时支持隧穿波函数和一维态空间，可变时则允许无限维谱并经由边界条件近似选定Hartle-Hawking波函数。该结果与量子引力中关于闭合宇宙的最新讨论一致。

Abstract: We construct Hilbert spaces for the minisuperspace quantum cosmology of a closed Universe in the limit of extreme slow-roll inflation, in which the scalar field is approximated as constant. In this setting, the potential energy in the scalar field is an integration constant depending on initial conditions, equivalent to the cosmological constant as it appears in unimodular gravity. If one fixes the value of this integration constant, the Wheeler-DeWitt equation admits two independent solutions, and a natural inner product picks out one of them (essentially Vilenkin's tunnelling wavefunction) with positive norm. The physical Hilbert space is then one-dimensional, in agreement with some recent discussions of closed universes in quantum gravity. However, if the potential energy is left arbitrary, the theory allows for an infinite-dimensional Hilbert space corresponding to energy eigenstates of an effective Hamiltonian. Requiring that this Hamiltonian be represented as a self-adjoint operator leads to a one-parameter family of boundary conditions at the singularity, generalising the DeWitt criterion of a vanishing wavefunction. The boundary condition always leads to a mixture of Hartle-Hawking (no-boundary) and tunnelling wavefunctions, but a particular choice "almost" singles out the Hartle-Hawking wavefunction, with exponentially suppressed corrections.

</details>


### [164] [Exciting the Vacuum: Non-Thermal Particle Bursts and Multi-Messenger Signals from Binary Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17178)
*Sohrab Rahvar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究了双黑洞系统动态弯曲时空中的粒子产生，发现了一种非热、幂律形式的发射谱，区别于热谱的霍金辐射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将弯曲时空量子场论（quantum field theory in curved spacetime）中的粒子产生机制（如霍金效应（Hawking effect）和安鲁效应（Unruh effect））推广到双黑洞系统引起的时变引力扰动中。

Method: 将无质量标量场（massless scalar field）耦合到双黑洞度规，采用Bogoliubov变换方法和S矩阵形式（S-matrix formalism），并在度规扰动$h_{μν}$的领头阶进行计算；扰动由标准四极矩形式（quadrupole formalism）建模，保留时域四极矩（$\ell=2$）贡献。

Result: 在弱场、大间距旋进（inspiral）区间，粒子发射呈现非热、幂律（power-law）形式，辐射能量速率满足$dE/dt \propto M^{10/3}ω^{16/3}$，与热谱的霍金辐射截然不同。

Conclusion: 双黑洞旋进阶段产生的粒子谱是非热而非热谱；将该分析推广到包含并合阶段、使用数值相对论度规（numerically-relativistic metric）的工作留待未来。

Abstract: We investigate particle production in the dynamical curved spacetime of a binary black hole system. Particle production is a well-known feature of quantum field theory in curved spacetime, underlying the Hawking and Unruh effects. Here we extend it to the time-varying gravitational perturbation sourced by a binary black hole. Treating a massless scalar field coupled to the binary metric, we compute the particle flux and radiated energy to leading order in the metric perturbation $h_{μν}$, using both the Bogoliubov transformation method and the S-matrix formalism. The perturbation is modeled with the standard quadrupole formalism, retaining the time-domain quadrupolar ($\ell=2$) contribution that dominates gravitational-wave emission. Our calculation is valid in the weak-field, large-separation inspiral regime and is not expected to capture the strong-field, nonlinear merger phase. In this regime we find a characteristic non-thermal, power-law emission with $dE/dt \propto M^{10/3}ω^{16/3}$, in contrast to a thermal Hawking spectrum. Extending the analysis through merger that uses the numerically-relativistic metric
  is left to future work.

</details>


### [165] [CASPER: Interpretable ResNet based Classifier with FastShap Explainer for Gravitational Wave Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17214)
*R. Rai,R. Verma,Somya*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出CASPER端到端流水线，将残差卷积神经网络（Residual CNN）分类器与FastSHAP解释器相结合，用于引力波（Gravitational Wave, GW）检测。该模型在真实探测器噪声（H1和L1）下，在信噪比（SNR）7-42范围内对260个真实事件进行分类，AUC达到91%，并通过Focal Loss和Platt Calibration改善泛化能力。FastSHAP归因图可完整恢复啁啾形态（chirp morphology），实现可解释分类决策，且整体参数量少于标准深度学习模型，仅需标准CPU即可运行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统匹配滤波（matched filtering）依赖预计算波形模板，且无法提供分类决策由何种信号驱动的信息；现有深度学习方法虽然灵敏度较高，但存在类别重叠（class overlap）、类别权重不平衡（imbalanced class weighting）、样本多样性有限以及训练-测试不匹配（train-test mismatch）等系统性偏差，导致在真实探测器噪声中泛化能力不足。因此，需要一种兼具高检测性能与可解释性的轻量级替代方案。

Method: 构建CASPER端到端流水线，核心组件为残差卷积神经网络（Residual CNN）分类器与FastSHAP解释器。网络使用Focal Loss优化决策边界，并采用Platt Calibration（Platt标定）改善概率输出的泛化能力。数据来自引力波开放科学中心（Gravitational Wave Open Science Centre）的260个真实事件，覆盖H1和L1两个探测器且信噪比（SNR）范围为7-42，未使用任何合成数据增强。

Result: 分类器在模型整体上的AUC（Area Under Curve）达到91%，且具有较低的误报率。FastSHAP生成的归因图能够完整恢复啁啾形态（chirp morphology），提供详细的视觉分类决策解释。整个流水线参数量少于标准深度学习模型，且无需GPU等专用硬件，仅需标准CPU即可运行。

Conclusion: CASPER作为轻量级端到端流水线，在真实条件下实现了有效的引力波检测，通过引入可解释性（归因图）弥补了传统方法在决策可解释性上的缺陷，同时解决了现有深度学习方法在泛化性上的部分问题，为实际引力波探测提供了一个高效且可解释的替代方案。

Abstract: Traditional matched filtering has been the standard for Gravitational waves (GW) detection ever since LIGO was established, even though it requires pre-computed waveform templates and provides no accounts of information about which signal drove the decision of classification. Deep-learning alternatives showed competitive sensitivity, but system biasesincluding class overlap, imbalanced class weighting, limited sample variation, and traintest mismatchcontinue to cause problems with generalisation in real detector noise. We introduce CASPER-Classification with Attribution via ShaPlEy in Residual neural networks, an end-to-end pipeline combining residual convolutional neural network (CNN) classifier with a FastSHAP explainer. 260 distinct events from the Gravitational Wave open Science Centre were fetched across SNR range of 7-42 from both H1 and L1 detectors with no synthetic augmentation. The classifier achieves AUC (Area Under Curve) of 91% across the model with a low false alarm rate. Focal Loss and Platt Calibration were used to improve decision boundary and generalisation. FastSHAP attribution maps recover the complete chirp morphology and provides detailed maps for a visual interpretation of the decision. The complete pipeline contains fewer parameters than standard deep learning models and requires no hardware except a standard CPU making our model an effective lightweight pipeline for Gravitational Wave Detection under real life conditions.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用几何光学近似（geometric-optics approximation）推导光子球半径、临界碰撞参数及阴影半径；通过Bozza方法导出描述强场偏转角对数行为的领先系数$\bar{a}$；利用事件视界望远镜（EHT）对M87*和SgrA*的观测数据约束模型参数。

Abstract: We study the shadow and strong-field optical properties of a static, spherically symmetric dyon-like dilatonic black hole. The photon sphere radius, critical impact parameter, and shadow radius are obtained and analyzed in terms of the charge $Q$ and the dilatonic coupling parameter $a$. We show that increasing these parameters decreases the photon sphere and shadow radii, leading to a smaller apparent shadow. The predicted angular diameter is compared with the observational data for M87$^{*}$ and SgrA$^{*}$, and the model parameters are constrained. We also estimate the high-frequency energy emission rate in the geometric-optics approximation and derive the leading Bozza coefficient $\bar{a}$, which characterizes the logarithmic behavior of the deflection angle in the strong-field regime. Astrophysical implication of the obtained outcomes are discussed.

### [167] [Acceleration-induced spectral blind spots in stimulated atomic transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17396)
*Jiawei Hu,Hongwei Yu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文发现均匀加速可以将原子对光子的受激跃迁响应转换为特定频率下的无响应现象，即“光谱盲点”（spectral blind spots），在该点上受激吸收和加速诱导激发同时被抑制。该效应源于加速原子对量子真空涨落（quantum vacuum fluctuations）的非平凡响应，并作为Unruh效应（Unruh effect）的一种新型标志，表现为受激跃迁的缺失而非增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索加速能否将光-物质相互作用中常见的受激跃迁（stimulated transitions）响应改变为一种频率选择性的无响应现象，并揭示其与Unruh效应的联系。

Method: 通过理论分析研究均匀加速原子与具有横向动量分量的入射光子之间的受激跃迁概率，识别出使该概率为零的离散频率条件；并基于电子在组合电场和磁场中的自旋劈裂（spin splitting）给出数量级估计。

Result: 当入射光子动量存在垂直于加速度方向的分量时，受激跃迁概率在一组由加速度、原子跃迁频率和光子传播角度决定的离散频率上消失。在这些频率点上，普通受激吸收和加速诱导激发均被抑制。数量级估计表明，基于电子自旋劈裂的实验方案可进入所需的参数区间。

Conclusion: 该结果揭示了一种尚未被探索的、由加速度修正的光-物质相互作用形式，并将光谱盲点确立为Unruh效应的一种新表现——以受激跃迁的缺失为特征，而非传统预期的增强。

Abstract: Stimulated transitions are among the most fundamental processes in light-matter interaction, underlying resonant absorption and emission in atomic systems. Here we show that uniform acceleration can convert this familiar response into a frequency-selective absence of response. Specifically, when an incident photon has a nonzero momentum component transverse to the acceleration, the stimulated transition probability vanishes at a discrete set of frequencies fixed by the acceleration, the atomic transition frequency, and the photon propagation angle. At these spectral blind spots, both ordinary stimulated absorption and acceleration-induced excitation are simultaneously suppressed, rendering the atom effectively unresponsive to the incident radiation. The effect arises from the nontrivial response of accelerated atoms to quantum vacuum fluctuations and provides a distinctive signature of the Unruh effect through the absence, rather than the enhancement, of stimulated transitions. We further provide an order-of-magnitude estimate showing that an electron-based implementation with spin splitting in combined electric and magnetic fields could access the required parameter regime. These results reveal an unexplored form of acceleration-modified light-matter interaction and identify spectral blind spots as a new manifestation of the Unruh effect.

### [168] [The Pre-geometric Origin of Geometric Trinity of Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17580)
*Salvatore Capozziello,Giuseppe Meluccio*

TL;DR: 本文展示了预几何引力（pre-geometric gravity）如何通过自发对称性破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）机制，统一地导出引力几何三分体（Geometric Trinity of Gravity）——即基于曲率（curvature）、挠率（torsion）和非度规性（non-metricity）的三种等价引力表述（GR、TEGR、STEGR）——在作用量和规范选择两个层面上的一致性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从Yang–Mills形式的规范理论出发，引入类似Higgs场的预几何场，通过自发对称性破缺机制生成有效度规及经典引力动力学。在未破缺相中分别推导预几何作用量和预几何规范固定条件（pre-geometric gauge-fixing conditions）的适当表达式，并分析它们在破缺相中如何映射到几何三分体的不同表述。

Result: 在自发破缺相中，预几何引力同时与引力几何三分体的三种作用量表述以及仿射联络（affine connection）的多种规范选择保持一致。这一普适结果通过未破缺相中预几何作用量和规范固定条件的分析得到严格证明。

Conclusion: 预几何引力为引力几何三分体提供了统一的生成机制，自发对称性破缺可以一致地导出GR、TEGR和STEGR三种等效表述，从而在更基础的层面上统一了基于不同几何特征的引力理论。

Abstract: The so-called Geometric Trinity of Gravity is based on three distinct geometric features of spacetime, i.e.\ curvature, torsion and non-metricity, which give rise to equivalent dynamics for General Relativity (GR), Teleparallel Equivalent of General Relativity (TEGR) and Symmetric Teleparallel Equivalent of General Relativity (STEGR). Pre-geometric gravity, on the other hand, offers a unifying framework from which all metric-affine theories can emerge. Starting from a gauge formulation \textit{à la} Yang--Mills with a Higgs-like field, a mechanism of spontaneous symmetry breaking can give rise to an effective metric as well as to the classical dynamics of the gravitational field. In particular, the emergence of gravity in the spontaneously broken phase is shown to be consistent with all the different formulations of the Geometric Trinity of Gravity, in terms both of actions and of gauge choices for the affine connection. This general result is achieved by deriving and analysing suitable expressions in the unbroken phase for pre-geometric actions and for pre-geometric gauge-fixing conditions respectively.

### [169] [Action based approach to dissipative relativistic fluid systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17686)
*G. L. Comer,N. Andersson,T. Celora,I. Hawke*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个用于描述含耗散的相对论两流体系统的作用量原理（action principle），以粒子和熵为具体组分，通过将耗散性与协变散度非零相联系，从几何视角自上而下地构建模型。该作用量模型能够恢复因果性热传播的Cattaneo方程，并在单流体极限下导出Tolman红移条件的动力学推广，最终通过三个示例展示了其对相对论Navier-Stokes方程预期项的复现能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有相对论耗散流体力学模型在描述非线性系统时面临结构复杂性不足的问题，且缺乏一种几何化的、自上而下的作用量构建方法。本文旨在提出一种基于作用量原理的新框架，以粒子和熵构成的两流体系统为切入点，统一描述耗散效应并保证因果性。

Method: 将耗散性定义为通量的协变散度（covariant divergence）非零；取粒子通量保守、熵通量耗散。在拉格朗日量（Lagrangian）中引入物质空间度规（matter space metric）的固有时导数项以产生体粘滞和剪切粘滞，并加入新的速度项。通过将熵的四速度锁定为物质组分的四速度，实现单流体极限下的约化。

Result: 作用量模型恢复了相对论Cattaneo方程，确保热传播具有因果性。在单流体极限下，导出一个约束方程，该约束导致了标准Tolman红移条件（Tolman red-shift condition）的动力学推广。三个示例作用量（复杂度递增）在单流体极限下复现了相对论Navier-Stokes方程中的预期项。

Conclusion: 基于作用量的方法能够为非线性耗散相对论流体系统提供远更丰富的结构，可能用于构建更真实的耗散相对论流体模型。该框架在单流体极限下与已知理论兼容，同时允许更一般的几何化拓展。

Abstract: We develop an action principle for a relativistic two-fluid system with dissipation. The specific constituents of the model - which serves as a proof of principle - are particles and entropy. The linchpin of the action is the assertion that a given flux is dissipative if its covariant divergence is non-zero. For our model, the particle flux is taken to be conservative while the entropy flux is dissipative. This allows for a "top-down" approach where the general question is geometric. Previous work has shown that new terms (the proper time derivative of matter space "metrics") must be included in the Lagrangian in order to produce equations of motion with terms representing bulk and shear viscosity. In addition to including these terms we show that further terms - interpreted as velocities - can be included. The new action-based model recovers known relativistic formulations of the Cattaneo equation, which results in causal heat propagation. We further advance our understanding by exploring the single-fluid limit by locking the entropy four-velocity to that of the matter component. This reduces the system to a single field equation along with a constraint equation. We show that this constraint leads to a dynamical extension of the standard Tolman red-shift condition. Finally, we provide three example actions (of increasing complexity) which demonstrate that the model is able to reproduce (in the single-fluid limit) the anticipated terms from the relativistic Navier-Stokes equations. In the general case, the action based approach allows for a much richer structure, which may be relevant for realistic models of non-linear dissipative relativistic fluid systems.

### [170] [Intrinsic handedness in O1-O4a black-hole mergers: probing orbital precession, remnant retention in dense environments and cosmological mirror asymmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17752)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双黑洞并合过程通常会因并合动力学破坏镜像对称性（mirror symmetry），从而产生左右手引力波的不平衡。作者希望利用一个与观测者无关的物理量来量化这种内禀手性（intrinsic handedness），并探索其在轨道进动、并合反冲、层次并合以及宇宙学镜像对称性等领域的统一探测价值。

Method: 采用引力波光学Stokes参数的类比量V_GW作为与观测者无关的手性度量；基于LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA在O1至O4a运行期间观测到的91个双黑洞并合事件进行分析；利用V_GW与并合残余黑洞反冲（recoil）之间已建立的定量关系来约束并合残骸在致密星团中的保留比例。

Result: 91个事件中92%倾向于非零V_GW，表明进动动力学（precessing dynamics）在事件中占主导地位；最多仅8%的并合残骸可能被束缚在球状星团或核星团中从而参与层次并合（hierarchical merger）；V_GW的宇宙学分布在V_GW→-V_GW变换下保持对称，平均值为⟨V_GW⟩=-1.9^{+6.1}_{-6.6}×10^{-3}（90%置信度），与无优先手性和大尺度统计各向同性预期一致；O4a数据的加入使⟨V_GW⟩的不确定性比O1-O3数据降低约40%。

Conclusion: 双黑洞并合手性可作为一个统一探针（unified probe），同时用于研究轨道进动、并合反冲、层次并合形成以及宇宙学镜像对称性。本研究首次将V_GW的观测与并合残骸保留约束以及宇宙学手性分布检验相结合，展示了该方法的广泛适用性。

Abstract: Precessing binary black-holes generically produce an imbalance of right- and left- handed gravitational waves, reflecting the breaking of mirror symmetry by the merger dynamics. We study this phenomenon using the observer-independent quantity $V_{\rm GW}$, a gravitational analogue of the optical Stokes parameter that quantifies the intrinsic handedness of the emitted radiation. Using 91 LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA black-hole mergers from the O1-O4a observing runs, we find that $92\%$ of the analyzed events favour non-vanishing $V_{\rm GW}$, indicating a predominance of precessing dynamics across the events. Through a recently established relation between $V_{\rm GW}$ and the remnant black hole recoil, we further constrain the retention of merger remnants in dense stellar environments, finding that at most $8\%$ could remain gravitationally bound to globular or nuclear star clusters and subsequently participate in hierarchical merger channels. We finally investigate the cosmological distribution of black-hole merger handedness. The observed $V_{\rm GW}$ distribution is consistent with symmetry under $V_{\rm GW}\rightarrow -V_{\rm GW}$, and yields an average value $\langle V_{\rm GW}\rangle=-1.9^{+6.1}_{-6.6}\times10^{-3}$ ($90\%$ credibility), consistent with the absence of a preferred handedness and with expectations from large-scale statistical isotropy. In particular, the inclusion of O4a events reduces uncertainties in $\langle V_{\rm GW} \rangle$ by $\sim 40\%$ with respect to O1-O3 events. These results establish black-hole merger handedness as a unified probe of orbital precession, remnant recoil, hierarchical formation, and cosmological mirror symmetry.

</details>


### [171] [Quasi-topological gravity for 4-dimensional Taub-NUT, near-horizon extreme Kerr, and swirling symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17784)
*Aimeric Colléaux,Ivan Kolář,Tomáš Málek*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文对四维引力理论进行了分类，识别出那些具有与准拓扑引力（quasi-topological gravity）类似可积性（integrability）的理论，但针对的是具有球对称、双曲对称和平面对称的Schwarzschild、Taub-NUT解及其双重Wick旋转对应解、近极端Kerr解、旋涡宇宙（swirling universe）以及Eguchi-Hanson瞬子等度规对称性的情形。研究表明，对于这些度规，只有场方程为三阶（平凡积分后为二阶）的理论才能在黎曼张量（Riemann tensor）中解析；同时，在每个曲率阶上存在唯一的场方程为一阶（平凡积分后为代数方程，可积性与广义相对论相同）的理论，并构建了由无穷高阶高能修正构成的规则静态黑洞解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分类具有可积性（integrability）的四维引力理论，这些理论对具有多种对称性（球、双曲、平面Schwarzschild、Taub-NUT等）的度规具有与准拓扑引力类似的性质，从而填补对高曲率修正引力理论系统分类的空白。

Method: 利用对称临界性原理（principle of symmetric criticality），考虑具有4个Killing矢量场和3维轨道（3-dimensional orbits）的度规，在仅依赖于黎曼张量（Riemann tensor）的理论框架下，通过分析场方程的阶数和解析性条件进行分类。

Result: 对于所考虑的对称性度规，只有场方程为三阶（平凡积分后为二阶）的理论能在黎曼张量中解析；在每个曲率阶上，存在唯一一种场方程为一阶（平凡积分后为代数方程）的理论，且可积性与广义相对论相同。从无穷高阶高能修正中构造了规则静态黑洞，并对所有对称性得到了闭式解（closed-form solutions）。

Conclusion: 所分类的理论具有清晰的物理解释，为在高曲率修正下构造具有可积性的引力模型提供了系统框架，并推广了准拓扑引力（quasi-topological gravity）的可积性概念。

Abstract: We classify 4-dimensional gravitational theories with integrability properties analogous to quasi-topological gravity, but for metrics with the symmetries of spherical, hyperbolic, and planar Schwarzschild and Taub-NUT solutions, their double-Wick-rotated counterparts - the B-metrics, the near-horizon extreme Kerr, and the swirling universe - and the Eguchi-Hanson instanton. These are the symmetries that allow consistent reductions (principle of symmetric criticality) with 4 Killing vectors and 3-dimensional orbits. Considering theories depending only on the Riemann tensor, we show that, for these metrics, only those with third-order equations (second-order after trivial integration) can be analytic in the Riemann tensor. We show that there is a unique theory with first-order field equations (algebraic after trivial integration, with the same integrability as general relativity) at each order in curvature and construct regular static black holes from infinite towers of these high-energy corrections to general relativity. For these theories, we obtain closed-form solutions for all the symmetries listed above, which we analyze to ensure they have a clear physical interpretation.

### [172] [Stability of regular spherically symmetric solutions in scalar-tensor gravity coupled to nonlinear electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17843)
*Rustam Ibadov,Najibullokhon Shukurullokhon*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类标量-张量引力非最小耦合非线性电动力学（NLED）中的新型正则黑洞，通过纯磁NLED源规避了“不可行”定理，证明其具有去Sitter真空核心、无奇点、奇偶宇称扰动下动力学稳定，且存在极端质量下限，从而为黑洞信息丢失悖论提供了热力学残骸框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过引入纯磁NLED源构造标量-张量引力中的正则黑洞解；采用奇数宇称（axial）线性引力扰动分析动力学稳定性；使用数值时间域积分与半解析WKB近似（WKB approximation）独立验证；基于质量-半径关系进行热力学分析。

Result: 几何分析表明中央Penrose奇点被完全消除，替换为能量密度全局有界的正则de Sitter真空核心；Regge-Wheeler型有效势在事件视界外严格正定且凸起；数值与WKB分析共同确认无快子不稳定性（tachyonic instability），呈现稳定准正则振铃（quasi-normal ringing）后指数衰减；质量-半径关系揭示严格质量间隙，对应极端构型（M ≥ M_min），表明Hawking蒸发终止于该极端极限。

Conclusion: 该正则黑洞在动力学上稳定，且半经典Hawking蒸发终止于极端质量下限，留下大质量热力学残骸（thermodynamic remnant），为黑洞信息丢失悖论（black hole information loss paradox）提供了一种理论解决框架。

Abstract: We investigate the geometric, dynamical, and thermodynamic properties of a novel class of regular black holes in scalar-tensor gravity non-minimally coupled to nonlinear electrodynamics (NLED). By incorporating a purely magnetic NLED source, we circumvent the classical "no-go" theorems that prohibit regular configurations for purely electric fields under the weak energy condition. The geometric analysis demonstrates the complete resolution of the central Penrose singularity, replacing it with a regular, de Sitter-like vacuum core characterized by a globally bounded energy density ($ρ_c < \infty$). To assess the physical viability of these configurations, we analyze their dynamical stability against odd-parity (axial) linear gravitational perturbations. The derived Regge-Wheeler-like effective potential is strictly positive and convex outside the event horizon. Numerical time-domain integration, independently corroborated by the semi-analytical WKB approximation, confirms the total absence of tachyonic instabilities, revealing a stable quasi-normal ringing phase followed by an exponential decay. Furthermore, our thermodynamic analysis of the mass-radius relation reveals a strict mass gap corresponding to an extremal configuration ($M \ge M_{min}$). This indicates that the semi-classical Hawking evaporation must terminate at this extremal limit, leaving behind a massive thermodynamic remnant, thereby providing a theoretical framework toward resolving the black hole information loss paradox.

### [173] [Hybrid Stars with Post-Merger Rotation Profiles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17875)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用四参数唯象差动旋转律（phenomenological rotation law），将最大角速度位置从中心偏移；针对准环型（type C）和准球型（type A）两类差动旋转解，分析相变对全局性质和角速度轮廓的影响。

Result: 1. 存在准环型混合星构型，其中解紧闭夸克物质形成围绕质心的环，强子物质位于中心和外层；2. 角动量增加时，$J=const$序列的转折点向低能量密度方向移动，相变存在的区域显著收缩；3. A类和C类解中，角速度轮廓在能量密度不连续的情况下依然连续；4. 不同状态方程（equation of state）的质量-半径曲线交叉点处，旋转轮廓非常接近，尽管能量密度轮廓差异显著。

Abstract: We study the effect of differential rotation on hybrid stars with the first-order deconfinement phase transition from hadronic to color superconducting quark matter. The differential rotation is introduced within a realistic, four-parameter phenomenological rotation law, in which the maximum angular velocity of the rotating configuration is shifted away from the center. We focus on two classes of differentially rotating solutions, namely quasi-toroidal (type C) and quasi-spherical (type A), and study the changes in the star global properties and angular velocity profiles due to the presence of a phase transition. Thus, we demonstrate the existence of quasi-toroidal hybrid star configurations in which deconfined quark matter forms a ring around the center of mass, while hadronic matter remains at the center and outer layers. Furthermore, we show that when increasing the angular momentum $J$ the turning points of the $J=const$ sequences shift towards lower energy densities, shrinking considerably the region where differentially rotating neutron stars with phase transitions exists. Interestingly, for both type A and type C solutions, the angular velocity profile is continuous throughout the star despite the discontinuity in the energy density. Moreover, we show that at the crossing points where the mass-radius curves for different equations of state intersect, the rotational profiles of the solutions are very close despite large differences in the energy density profiles. This reveals a possible degeneracy between the post-merger remnant properties for models with and without phase transitions, emphasizing the need for complementary multi-messenger observables to distinguish between them.

### [174] [Long-Lived Ringing of Near-Extremal Kerr Black Holes Resonantly Driven by Extreme-Mass-Ratio Inspirals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17883)
*Wen-Biao Han*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文证明极端质量比旋近（EMRI）能够共振驱动近极端克尔黑洞的零阻尼模（ZDM），通过频域Teukolsky振幅识别出源支持的轨道谐波，其频率落在基本引力ZDM的极点半宽内，从而在复频响应中增强极点贡献，并通过复响应断层扫描从实频轨道数据中恢复已知的克尔极点，为测量黑洞视界面引力提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近极端克尔黑洞支持零阻尼模（zero-damped modes, ZDMs），其时域阻尼率极小，使其成为探测近视界区域的理想长寿命探针。本文旨在探索极端质量比旋近（extreme-mass-ratio inspirals, EMRIs）能否在真空广义相对论中共振驱动这种响应。

Method: 利用偏心倾斜克尔测地线的频域Teukolsky振幅，识别出源支持的轨道谐波，其实数频率落入基本引力ZDM的一个极点半宽（pole half-width）内。通过复响应断层扫描（complex-response tomography）从实数频率轨道数据中恢复克尔极点，并减去平滑非极点分量后分析残余相位行为。

Result: 找到了一个源支持的轨道谐波，其实频落入基本引力ZDM的极点半宽内；在复响应中，极点贡献因该半宽较小而增强；复响应断层扫描从实频轨道数据中恢复了独立计算的克尔极点；残余信号表现出相干简单极点的相位缠绕（phase winding），极点贡献与非极点部分相当；被驱动的分支处于超辐射区（superradiant regime）并携带负视界通量（negative horizon flux）。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了EMRI共振驱动的、极点可分辨的ZDM响应，恢复的极点半宽为测量黑洞视界面引力（horizon surface gravity）提供了一种新途径。

Abstract: Near-extremal Kerr black holes support zero-damped modes (ZDMs), whose small time-domain damping rates make them long-lived probes of the near-horizon region. We show that bound extreme-mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) can resonantly drive this response in vacuum general relativity. Using frequency-domain Teukolsky amplitudes for eccentric-inclined Kerr geodesics, we identify a source-supported orbital harmonic whose real frequency falls within one pole half-width of the fundamental gravitational ZDM. In the complex response, the pole contribution is enhanced by this small half-width, while complex-response tomography recovers the independently computed Kerr pole from real-frequency orbital data. After subtracting the smooth non-pole component, the residual exhibits the phase winding of a coherent simple pole, with a pole contribution comparable to the smooth non-pole part of the EMRI-sourced Teukolsky amplitude. The driven branch also lies in the superradiant regime and carries negative horizon flux. These results establish a pole-resolved, resonantly driven ZDM response by EMRIs and make the recovered pole half-width a route to measuring the horizon surface gravity.

### [175] [Sensing the Inflationary Production of Scalars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17963)
*A. J. Foraci,C. Litos,R. P. Woodard*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文回顾了德西特暴胀（de Sitter inflation）期间物质场圈对引力子自能（graviton self-energy）的贡献机制，利用自能量子修正线性化爱因斯坦方程，并通过格林函数方法得到引力辐射平面波模函数的一圈修正。共形耦合物质仅在对视界穿越后模函数虚部趋于零的速率产生对数增强，而经历暴胀粒子产生（inflationary particle production）的无质量最小耦合标量场则导致模函数实部趋于常数的速率大幅增强，该效应可被解释为暴胀哈勃参数（Hubble parameter）的移动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究德西特暴胀期间物质场圈如何通过自能机制修正引力子的传播行为，以深入理解暴胀时期量子效应对引力辐射的影响。

Method: 通过物质场圈贡献计算引力子自能，进而量子修正线性化爱因斯坦方程；采用格林函数方法（Green's function method）获得引力辐射平面波模函数（plane wave mode functions）的精确一圈修正，并利用重整化群（renormalization group）的变体对修正进行理解和求和。

Result: 共形耦合物质仅对模函数虚部在视界穿越（horizon crossing）后趋于零的速率产生对数增强（logarithmic enhancement）；无质量最小耦合标量场则对模函数实部趋于常数的速率产生更强的增强效应。

Conclusion: 无质量最小耦合标量场导致的显著增强效应可被解释为暴胀哈勃参数的移动（shift of the inflationary Hubble parameter）。

Abstract: We review the mechanism by which loops of matter fields contribute to the graviton self-energy during de Sitter inflation. The self-energy is used to quantum-correct the linearized Einstein equations. A Green's function method is employed to obtain exact 1-loop corrections to the plane wave mode functions of gravitational radiation, subject to the usual ambiguity in the initial state. Conformally coupled matter, which does not experience inflationary particle production, makes only a logarithmic enhancement of the rate at which the imaginary part of the mode function goes to zero after horizon crossing. These corrections can be understood, and even summed up, using a variant of the renormalization group. However, massless, minimally coupled scalars, which experience massive inflationary particle production, induce a much stronger enhancement of the rate at which the real part of the mode function approaches a constant. One interpretation of this effect is as a shift of the inflationary Hubble parameter.

### [176] [The free boundary problem in general relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18128)
*Kostas Tzanavaris,Latham Boyle,Neil Turok*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文提出将时空奇异性视为自由边界（free boundary），通过作用量原理（action principle）导出了奇点处需满足的边界条件（boundary conditions）。该条件排除了Kasner-like或BKL时空，但允许由流体（0 ≤ P < ρ）驱动的共形正则时空（包括FLRW模型）。标准热大爆炸FLRW宇宙学的线性扰动在奇点处满足反射边界条件，与大规模宇宙学观测一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法通常将时空奇异性视为固定边界或需要额外正则化手段，缺乏从变分原理（variational principle）出发的统一处理方案。论文旨在建立一个自洽的作用量框架，将奇异性作为自由边界处理，从而导出内在的边界条件。

Method: 将奇异性视为自由边界（free boundary），其中变分不受约束；通过要求作用量在这种自由变分下取驻值（stationary），推导出奇点处须满足的（在壳）边界条件。该方法适用于爱因斯坦引力耦合物质的一般情况。

Result: 导出的边界条件排除了Kasner-like或BKL类型的时空，但允许由满足0 ≤ P < ρ的流体驱动的共形正则时空（包括FLRW模型）存在。对于标准热大爆炸FLRW宇宙学，线性（标量、矢量、张量）扰动在奇点处满足反射边界条件，这与大规模宇宙学观测相符。

Conclusion: 将奇异性视为自由边界的变分框架是可行的，并能给出具有物理意义的边界条件，有效筛选出符合观测的宇宙学模型及扰动模式。

Abstract: We study the action principle for space-times whose boundary is singular. We suggest that it is natural to treat the singularity as a {\it free} boundary, where the variation is unconstrained. Demanding that the action is stationary under such free variations then implies certain (on-shell) boundary conditions at the singularity. We derive these boundary conditions for the case of Einstein gravity coupled to matter and show that, when applied to an initial spacelike singularity, they exclude Kasner-like or BKL space-times, but admit conformally regular space-times (including FLRW models) sourced by fluids satisfying $0 \leq P < ρ$. For standard hot big bang FLRW cosmologies, the admissible linear (scalar, vector, tensor) perturbations satisfy reflecting boundary conditions at the bang, in agreement with large-scale cosmological observations.

</details>


### [177] [Beyond Plane Waves: Coherent Network Response to Collimated Gravitational-Wave Wavepackets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18184)
*S. D. Campos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于准直引力波暴的傍轴波包（paraxial wavepacket, PWM）模型，推导了探测器网络对该结构化信号的相干响应。研究表明，在现有LIGO-Virgo基线中，PWM波形与标准正弦-高斯暴（sine-Gaussian burst）不可区分，验证了平面波近似的有效性；但在第三代探测器网络中，有限横向结构会产生不可忽略的几何相位偏移。通过蒙特卡洛模拟，采用PWM先验的统计量在固定虚警率下将探测效率提升了约3-4倍，同时保持了对平面波类信号的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波暴的探测通常依赖平面波近似，但该近似在更高灵敏度的下一代探测器网络中可能不再成立。本文旨在引入傍轴波包模型来刻画引力波暴的有限横向结构，并评估其对探测器网络相干响应的影响，进而探索是否可以利用结构信息提升探测效率。

Method: 提出傍轴波包（PWM）模型描述准直引力波暴，并推导探测器网络的相干响应。通过解析失配估计和重叠积分比较PWM波形与标准正弦-高斯暴的差异。采用基于事件级的玩具蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟，对比标准暴搜索排序统计量与受PWM模型约束的统计量，后者对跨探测器的几何不一致性施加惩罚。

Result: 在LIGO-Virgo基线中，PWM波形与平面波近似不可区分，验证了平面波近似的有效性。在第三代网络中，有限横向结构会引入显著的几何相位偏移。玩具蒙特卡洛模拟显示，PWM先验约束的统计量在固定虚警率（false-alarm rate）下，探测效率提升约3-4倍，且对平面波类信号保持原有性能。

Conclusion: 傍轴波包模型为处理下一代引力波探测器网络中因有限横向结构产生的几何相位效应提供了理论框架，并有望通过几何一致性约束显著提升引力波暴的探测效率。

Abstract: We present a paraxial wavepacket model for collimated gravitational-wave bursts and derive the coherent response of detector networks to these structured signals. For current LIGO-Virgo baselines, analytic mismatch estimates and overlaps show that PWM waveforms are effectively indistinguishable from standard sine-Gaussian bursts, validating the plane-wave approximation. We then identify a regime relevant to third-generation networks in which finite transverse structure produces non-negligible geometric phase shifts. A toy event-level Monte Carlo compares a standard burst-search ranking with a paraxial wavepacket model-constrained statistic that penalizes geometric inconsistencies across detectors; in this controlled setup, the PWM prior yields a factor of $\sim3$-$4$ gain in detection efficiency at a fixed false-alarm rate, while maintaining performance on plane-wave-like signals.

</details>
